jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvaliḥ
 namo gurubhyaḥ śāstrakṛdbhyaśca 
 nibandhakartṛparicayaḥ
bhāratīyadārśanikeṣu jñānaśrīnāmnā prasiddhau dvāvācāryāvāstām  tayoḥ kāśmīrā
bhijanaḥ pramāṇaviniścayavyākhyātā bhūyasāṃ bauddhaśāstragranthānāṃ bhoṭabhāṣānuvāda vidhāyako
jñānaśrībhadro'nyataraḥ itaraśca gauḍadeśodbhavo vikramaśīlācārya suvikhyātakītirjñāna
śrīmitraḥ  anayodvitīyo'trādhikṛtaḥ  kutracidasya jñānaśrīnāmnā nirdeśaḥ kutracicca
jñānaśrīmitranāmnā  svagranthapuṣkiāsu tu mahāpaṇḍitācāryajñānaśrīmitrapāda ityupādhi 
maṇḍitaṃ tasya nāmadheyamāyāti  vaṅgamagadhamaṇḍaleśvareṇa dharmapālena pratiṣṭhite tadanvavāya
saṃbhavairupalālite ca vikramaśīlāmahāvihāre bhāratetaradeśebhyo'pi vidyārthino vividhavidyā
vāptaye samājagmuḥ śāstrāṇi tu sarvāṇi bauddhapramukhānyadhigamya bahuśrutebhya ācāryebhyaste
bhāratavarṣasyādhyātmikasampadā svaṃ svaṃ deśamalaṃcakruḥ  śrūyate ekādaśe sṛṣṭaśatake vidyā
vihāre'tra catvāro dvārapaṇḍitāḥ dvau ca mahāstambhau babhūbuburiti  jñānaśrīmitraśca teṣu
dvitīya mahāstambhapadaṃ bhūṣayāmāsa 
ādāvayaṃ jñānaśrīmitraḥ saindhavasampradāyabhuktaḥ śrāvaka āsīt tadanu ca tantra
yānamāśritavāniti śrūyate  āsīdatra mahāvihāre saindhavānāmatiprābalyam  kadācit
tantragranthā herukapratimā ca kācit tairvahāvāhutīkṛtāḥ  rājñā ca te na daṇḍitāḥ 
eteṣu saindhaveṣu śrīmitranāmadhāriṇo janā dṛśyante  vaṅgadeśodbhavaistantrayānānusāribhire
teṣāṃ vivāda itivṛttaviśruta eva 
bhoṭadeśīya granthebhyo jñānaśrī mitramadhikṛtyaitadanyacca vivaraṇaṃ samupalabhyate  svadeśe
viśuddhabauddhadharmapracāraṇāparāyaṇena bhoṭamahīpena hra lā ye śe od ityākhyena vikrama
śīlācāryaṃ dīpaṅkaramatīśamāmantrayituṃ svajanāḥ preṣitāḥ  parijñāya teṣāṃ vikramaśīlā
gamanakāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca rājopāyanādikaṃ rājasammānalābhāya vā dhanasañcayanārthaṃ vā bhoṭadeśa
gamanaṃ na tadā svīkṛtavānācārya   anantarametadarthaṃ punarāgatebhyo bhoṭadeśīyebhyo rājñastasya
dharmārthaṃ dhanasaṃgrahaparasya śatrubhirbaṃndhanaṃ kārāgāre jīvanāvasānaṃ ca viditvā karuṇāparavaśo
dīpaṅkaraḥ saddharmapracārāya duḥkhasaṅkalāṃ bhoṭadeśayātrāmaṅgīcakāra  ime ca bhoṭadeśīyā
nāropāntasya saṃvardhanāṃ vikramaśīlāyāṃ pratyakṣīcakruḥ  ativṛddho'yamācāryo'tīśasya dakṣiṇaṃprastāvanāṃ
jñānaśrī mitrasya ca vāmaṃ bāhumāśritya śivikāto'vatatāra  bhoṭadeśāya prasthānāt
pūrvaṃ dīpaṅkaro jñānaśrīmitrād guhyamupadeśamadhigamya tadanuṣṭhitavānityapi śrūyate 
etebhyo jñānaśrīmitrasya vikramaśīlāyāṃ maryādātirekaḥ parijñāyate 
dīpaṅkarastūnaṣaṣṭivarṣadeśīya ekacatvāriṃśadadhikaikasahasrata me khuṣṭa saṃvatsare
vasantata bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tatyāja  tatkāle jñānaśromitro'pi svīyapāṇḍityena granthanirmāṇana
ca parāṃ prakhyātimadhijagāmeti śakyānumānam 
upalabhyamānānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ pariśīlanāj jñāyate vācaspatipramukhānāṃ
naiyāyikānāṃ sandarbhāstena nāmagrāhamuddhṛtāḥ khaṇḍitāśceti  vācaspatestu nyāyasūcī
nibandhanirmāṇakālastasyaiva svavacasā vasvaṅkavasuvatsara iti vijñāyate  paraṃ tu vatsa ro'yaṃ
vikramābdaṃ vā nirdiśati śakābdaṃ veti vipratipattisthānaṃ paṇḍitānāmāsīt  adhunā
śakasaṃvatsara eva vācaspatinollikhita iti nipuṇagaveṣaṇayā nirdhāritam 
nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāyāṃ      jarannaiyāyikasya jayantabhaṭṭasya mataṃ
vācaspatinā parāmṛṣṭamiti tātparyapariśuddhāvudayanācāryokti  jayantaśca kāśmīrādhipasya
śaṅkaravarmaṇo'mātyapadamalaṃ cakāreti jayantakṛtādāgamaḍambaranāṭakāt parijñāyate  ayaṃ
śaṅkaravarmā sṛṣṭīyapañcāśītyadhikāṣṭaśatatamāndād prabhṛti dvayadhikanavaśatatamābdaṃ yāvat
kāśmīramahīṃ bhunakti smetītivṛttavidāṃ matam  nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāpariśiṣṭabhūto
nyāyasūcīnibandhastu tadanusāraṃ na vasvaṅkavasumite vikramānde   khuṣṭadhabde 
janimarhati paraṃ tu tatsaṃkhyakaśakasaṃvatsare   vṛḥ  iti draṣṭavyam  vācaspatinā
svagranthānāmanukramo bhāmatyāṃ pradarśitaḥ  tadanusāraṃ nyāyagranthadvitayānantaramapi tena 
tattvakaumudī tattvavaiśāradī bhāmatī ca vinirmitā iti parijñāyate  ato jñānaśrīmitreṇa
prathame vayasi ācāryasya vācaspate vidyāvibhūtiḥ pratyakṣīkṛteti vāḍhaṃ saṃbhāvyate 
jñānaśrīmitraśca svaśiṣyeṇa ratnakīrtinā sahodayanācāryakṛtiṣu khaṇḍita ityagre
pradarśanīyamasmābhiḥ  ratnakīrtiḥ svagurorgranthānāṃ sārasaṅkalanaṃ kṛtavāniti tannibandha
bhūmikāyāṃ pradarśitam  ataevodayano'nayoḥ kanīyān samakālikaśceti saṃbhavet 
suvikhyātayornyāyācāryayorvācaspatyudayanayoścāntarā jñānaśrīmitra setubandhanaṃ cakāreti
mahattvātiśayastasya tadgranthānāṃ ca  tasya granthanirmāṇakālastu sṛṣṭīyaikādaśaśatakasyādi
me'rdhe saṃbhavet 
prastāvanā
āstikaśāstreṣu bauddhagrantheṣu ca sutarāṃ niṣṇāta āsīdayaṃ jñānaśrīmitra iti
tannibandhapāṭhād vijñāyate  tasya prākpradiṣṭaṃ tantrayānānugatvaṃ tu na granthaparyālocanātaḥ
spaṣṭībhavati  pramāṇavārtikasthailokaviśeṣa  vyākhyāvasare svagurortamapi pradarśita
metena  suvarṇadvīpavāsino dharmapālācāryasya śiṣyatvasvīkāropya'sya śrūyate  svasampradāya 
paricāyakastatkṛtaślokastu tadīyasākārasiddhī
āryāsaṅgamanaṅgajinnayavaho yadbhūpatīśo'nvaśād
ācāryo vasubandhurudhuramatistasyājñayādidyutat 
dignāgo'tha kumāranāthavihitāsāmānyasāhāyaka
stasmin vārtikabhāṣyakārakṛtinoradyānavadyā sthitiḥ 
iti  atra svavacasānena maitreyanāthopajñayogācāravijñānavādasampradāye prajñākarapravartite ca
dharmaprasthāne'sthāntarbhāva iti sphuṭīkṛtam  prācāryeṇa sthiravratakena Stcherbatsky
prajñākarānuyāyināṃ tredhā vibhāga pradarśitaḥ  teṣu vibhāgeṣu jino ravigupto yamāriśca
pravaktāraḥ saṃjātāḥ  prajñākara śiṣyo ravigupto jñānaśrīsamakālaṃ kāśmīreṣūvāsa  yamāriśca
kāśmīrakasya jñānaśriyaḥ śiṣyaḥ kāryakṣetraṃ cāsya vaṅgeṣviti tena pratipāditam  atha
raviguptakṛtijinena svagranthe khaṇḍitā jinakṛtiśca yamāriṇā iti tata eva śrūyate 
jñānaśrīmitrastu kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasyāntime bhāge kañcanācārya ravināmānaṃ dvedhā
nāmagrāhaṃ sasammānaṃ collikhati  etaṃ viṣayaṃ manasi nidhāya raviguptajñānaśrīyamāriṇāṃ
parasparasaṃbandhaḥ punarvivecanamarhati  sarvaṃ ime vaṅgamagadhapracalite prajñākarīye prasthāne'nta
rbhūtā na veti raviguptayamāryorantarā ca jñānaśrīmitrasya sthānamuta jñānaśrībhadrasyeti ca
punaravekṣaṇīyam  atra nirṇayastu jñānaśrīmitranibandhaiḥ saha bhoṭabhāṣānuvādanibaddhābhyāṃ
raviguptasya yamāreśca kṛtibhyāṃ sādhyena tulaneneva saṃbhāvyate 
 upalabdhanibandhaparicayaḥ
upalabdhānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ kaścit paricayo'trāpekṣita iti kṛtvā
svalpaparisareṇaiva sa prastūyate prastāvanā
 kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyākhyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vastūnāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaparo mukhyatamo jñāna
śrīmitranibandhaḥ  eṣa ca granthāntarasyādhyāyaviśeṣa iti na mantavyam  etasyaiva catvāraḥ
paricchedāḥ santi  atra nyāyavedistambhabhūtānāṃ śaṅkarabhāsarvajñatrilocanavācaspatīnāṃ
matāni samunmūlya svamataṃ sthāpitamiti granthakṛtā kaṇṭhata evāpāditam  dṛśyate cātra
tattanmatāni proddhṛtya bāhulyena khaṇḍitānīti 
yat sat tat kṣaṇikaṃ yathā jaladhara  santastu bhāvā ime
sattā śaktirihārthaṃkarmaṇi miteḥ siddheṣu siddhā na sā 
nāpyekaiva vidhānyadāpi parikṛnnaiva kriyā vā bhaved
dvedhāpi kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃgatirataḥ sādhye ca viśrāmyati 
ityādimaśloke śāstrārtha saṃgṛhītaḥ  tataścaturṣu paricchedeṣu pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekā
hetukavināśādhikārākhyeṣu sthiravādaṃ dīrghaviśleṣaṇena khaṇḍayitvā svamataṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam 
vicāraścātra pūrṇāṅgo mārmikaśca 
 vyāpticarcā tu bauddhopajñavyāptisvarūpa pradarśanaparo nibandha  vyāptiśca
bhāratīyadarśanaprasthāneṣu cārvākān prahāya sarvaiḥ svīkriyate  kiṃ tu tasyā mūlaṃ svarūpaṃ
cādhikṛtya teṣu matabhedo vartatetarām  naiyāyikā vyabhicārājñānaṃ sahacārajñānaṃ ca
vyāptiniścayopāya iti kathayanti bauddhāśca tādātmyatadutpattibhyāmabhāvena ca vyāptimupa
pādayanti  atra tu prāsaṅgike vicāre trilocanavācaspatiprabhṛtīnāṃ matānyuddhṛtya
khaṇḍitāni  ante ca pratyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavaiva hetuphalabhāvasvabhāvavyāptisiddhiriti
niṣkarṣaḥ pradattaḥ 
 jñānaśriyo nibandhāvalau bhedābhedaparīkṣā hastratamā  jñānajñeyayoḥ saṃbandha
vicāro'syā viṣaya iti bhāti  tayorbhedameke āmananti aikyaṃ cāpare  pakṣayorubhayorapi
doṣāḥ pradiṣṭā itītare bhedābhedapakṣamurarīkurvanti  bhedasvīkāreṇābhedapakṣasya abhedāva
lambanena ca bhedapakṣasya doṣā apayantīti teṣāmāśaya  siddhāntastu jñānaśriyo'bheda
pakṣapātī bhedābhedasvīkāre ubhayapakṣaparidṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ sannipātāpatteḥ 
 anupalabdhirahasyamapi kṣudramākāreṇa bauddhadārśanikasvīkṛtāyā anupalabdhe
laṃkṣaṇaṃ bhedāśca samāhṛtya śāstragranthebhyo'tra carcitāni 
prastāvanā
 sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā tvanupalabdhi rahasyasya khilarūpeṇa svīkāramarhati
śabdasāmānyābhāve kāryānupalabdhisāmarthya vivecanāt  śabdasāmānyābhāve ca na siddhā
tino vimatiḥ prastute kāryānupalabdhisthale svabhāvānupalabdhipratiṣṭhāpanamevātra tasya
kṛtyam 
 apohaprakaraṇaṃ bauddhasiddhāntānusāraṃ śabdārthavivecanaparamatīva gambhīrārthakam 
śabdestāvanmukhyamākhyāyate'rtha
stanāpohastadguṇatvena gamyaḥ 
arthaścaiko'dhyāsato bhāsato'nyaḥ
sthāpyo vācyastattvatto naiva kaścit 
iti prakaraṇārthasaṃgrāhakaḥ iloko jñānaśrīmitrasya  eṣa grantho bāhulyena khaṇḍita udayanā
cāryeṇa tadanusāriṇā ca śaṅkaramiśreṇeti bauddhādhikāracarcāniratairavadheyam 
 īśvaravādastu viśvanirmātunityasya parameśvarasya khaṇḍanaṃ vidadhāti  prathame
paricchede śaṅkaravācaspativittokabhāsarvajñatrilocanaśatānandānāṃ jagatkartṛsādhakāni
matāni tattadvacasā samupasthāpya dvitīye bauddhadṛśā sāmānyatastatkhaṇḍanam  tṛtīye ca
vistaravyākhyānam 
dharmakīrtikṛtapramāṇavārtikastheśvarakhaṇḍanaparasya ślokasaptakasya
tṛtīyo'pi paricchedastredhā vibhakto granthakāreṇa 
 svasiddhāntānusāraṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvanirṇaya kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhī vihito
jñānaśrīmitreṇa  trikapañcakacintetyasyāparaṃ nāmadheyam  dharmayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvasthāpana
dharmottarasya
vidhāvupalambhānupalambhānāṃ saṃkhyā nirṇayamadhikṛtya bauddheṣu matavirodhaḥ 
pañcakapakṣaḥ jñānaśrīmitrasya tu trikapakṣaḥ  gadyapadyanibaddhe'tra granthe kārikāsu siddhāntaḥ
pradarśitaḥ gadyabhāge ca tadarthako vicāraḥ  jñānaśrī mitra nibandhe vayameka eva bhoṭabhāṣāyā
manūdito'bhūt 
 yoginirṇayaprakaraṇe yogisvarūpaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ ca bauddhasammataṃ vivecitavānā
cāryaḥ 
 advaitabinduprakaraṇaṃ sākāravijñānavādavyākhyānaparam  atra jñānajñeyayo
stāttvikabhedanirāśaḥ kṛtaḥ 
 sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākāravijñānavādameva mahatā āḍambareṇa prapañcayati 
dharmaṃkītirasya vādasya pravartaka iti śrūyate  prajñākareṃṇāyaṃ viśadīkṛtaḥ  atra śāstre
prastāvanā
vādasyāsya vyākhyānaṃ nāgārjunamaitreyanāthāsaṅgādiprācīnācāryasammatipradarśanapuraḥsaraṃ
samupalabhyate  dharmakīrteḥ prajñākarasya ca matāni pradarśitāni  ṣaṭsu paricchedeṣu vibhakta
midaṃ śāstram  prathame nirākārajñānavādavivecanam dvitīye saṃkleśavyavadānacarcā tṛtīye
madhyamāvatārapradarśanam caturthe citrādvaitaprapañcanam pañcame svasaṃvedanavicāraḥ ṣaṣṭhe ca
yogācāravijñānavādena mādhyamakasiddhāntasya maulikamaikyaṃ samāgacchanti 
 sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ tāvat sākārasiddhiśāstrasya padyātmakaḥ sārasaṃgrahaḥ 
atra tu catvāraḥ paricchedāḥ  teṣveva śāstrasthānāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ paricchedānāṃ viṣayāḥ
samāhṛtāḥ 
 prastutanibandhānāṃ kartṛtvavicāraḥ
atra kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyaṃ vihāyaikādaśanibandhā mātṛkāmekāmavalambyaiva sampāditāḥ 
bahutra ca granthakṛnnāmanirdeśa puṣpikāyāṃ nāyāti  ataeva prastutanibandhānāmekakartṛttva
svīkārakāraṇaṃ spaṣṭīkaraṇīyam 
   kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye puṣpikāsuna granthakārollekha  antimaśloke tenastāt
parapāragastribhuvane jñāna śriyo'yaṃ jana ityatra tasya saṃketa iti pratibhāti  ratnakīryudayana
vādidevādibhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasthāḥ ilokā jñānaśrīnāmnā samuddhṛtāḥ 
   vyāptinirṇayastu jñānaśrī mitrakṛtireva puṣpikāyāṃ tathā nirdeśāt 
 bhedābhedaparīkṣāpi jñānaśrīmitranirmitā tadīyasākārasiddhau tathā kathanāt 
  anupalabdhi rahasyasya sarvaśabdābhāvacarcāyāśca kartā nollikhitaḥ na
vetaratra tadupalambhaḥ 
 apohaprakaraṇastha sandarbho vādidevena jñānaśromitrasyaiveti nāmagrāhaṃ gṛhītaḥ
syādvādaratnākare 
 īśvaravādakartureva granthāntaraṃ trikapañcakacinteti īśvaravāde nirdiṣṭam 
sākārasiddhiśāstre ca tatkartubṛhadīśvaravādaḥ samullikhitaḥ 
 trikapañcaka cintāparākhyā kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrakṛtiriti tasya
granthasya bhoṭabhāṣānuvādāt parijñāyate 
prastāvanā
 ratnakorte sarvajñasiddherādhārabhūto yoginirṇaya iti bhāṣāsāmyād viṣaya
sāmyācca samāyāti 
 sākārasiddhī jñānaśrī mitra granthatvenādvaitabinduprakaraṇasyollekho dṛśyate 
 sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ ca puṣpikānirdeśāj jñānaśrīmitra
kṛtī eva 
etat sarvaṃ manasi nidhāya ekāṃ śailī sarvatra cāvalokya vimṛśya caikamātṛkāyāṃ
sarveṣāṃ samupalambhaṃ dvādaśa ime granthā jñānaśrī mitranirmitā iti nirṇayaḥ svata evāpatati 
ebhiḥ sahānupalabdhā sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrasya samullekhamarhati  sāpi ratnakīrtinā
svasarvajñasiddhau vyavahṛteti pratibhāti  sākārasiddhau vyāpticarcāyāṃ ca jñānaśrī mitreṇa
sarvajñasiddhiḥ kācidullikhitā yoginirṇaye ca jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiḥ sarvajñasiddhiḥ anyatra
yoginirṇaye sarvajñasiddheḥ ślokārdhoddhāro dṛśyate  ekaiva sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrīmitrakṛtā
sarvatrāmṛṣṭeti pratibhāti 
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye 'hetuphalagrahaṇe vyavasthitapratisandhātṛvādastu prastoṣyate'nekānta
cintāyām' iti nirdeśadarśanena jñāyate jñānaśrīmitrasyābhipretamanekāntavādamālambya
granthāntaramāsīditi  sā tvanekāntacintā nirmitā na veti na parijñāyate 
 prastutanibandhānāṃ kālakramaḥ
saṃskaraṇe'tra mātṛkādṛṣṭagranthakrama evānusṛtaḥ  itaretarollekhadarśanāt kutracidanyathā
bhāvasaṃbhave'pi mātṛkāyā ekatvād viparivartanamatra na yuktiyuktam  na ca pūrṇo grantha
kramo'nyataḥ kutaścidāgacchati  nibandhāścātra parasparanirapekṣāḥ  udayanācāryakṛte
ātmatattvaviveke jñānaśrīmitramatakhaṇḍana vidhāvapi nibandhanirmāṇakramo nānusṛta iti lakṣyate 
itaretarollekhadarśanabalena prāptaṃ granthakramavivaraṇamatra prastūyate 
anupalabdhi rahasyam sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ ca
nibandhāntare nāmagrāhaṃ nopāttāni  ato jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiṣu teṣāṃ kramikasthāna nirdeśo
na śakyakriya  vyāpticarcāyām apohaprakaraṇe īśvaravāde coddeśāt tebhyaḥ prāk

tātparyapariśuddhau kusumāñjalo ca yathāprāptaṃ bauddhamatakhaṇḍanaṃ na tirohitaṃ vidvallocanebhyaḥ

vā na śakyakriya āsīt

cakāra 
ādhunike kāle kṣīṇo'pi nyāyagranthānāṃ saṃpradāyo vartate na tu bauddhagranthānām

udayanakṛtagrantheṣūpalabhyamāneṣvātmatattvaviveka eva prathamaḥ  tatra tvādita ārabhya

ityatra

iti īśvaravāda pṛ   sthajñānaśrīmitraślokaṃ samuddiśatīti bhāti

dṛṣṭastāvadayaṃ ghaṭo'tra ca patan dṛṣṭastathā mudgaro

mādhavācāryakṛte sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe  pṛ   kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagato yat sat tat
kṣaṇikam ityādiśloko jñānajñīmitranāmollekhapuraḥsaraṃ samuddhṛto dṛśyate  atra saṃgrahe
bauddhadarśana paricchede jñānaśrī mitraprabhāvo'nyatrāpi prasphuṭaḥ 
jñānaśrīmitranibandheḥ śaṅkaramiśrasya pratyakṣaparicaya āsīt  ātmatattvavivekakalpa
latāyāṃ tenāpohaprakaraṇādvaitabindusākārasiddhisākārasaṃgrahebhyaḥ ślokāḥ gadyasandarbhācoddhṛtāprastāvanā

smṛtaḥ śaṅkareṇa śaṅkarasya kāle bauddhaśāstrasya dhārā niruddhā babhūva tataḥ pūrvameva bauddha
vidyāvihārāṇāṃ tadgranthasampradāyasya cocchedāt 
jayarāmanyāyapañcānano'pi nyāya siddhāntamālāyāṃ vādivinodadṛṣṭāṃ bauddhācāryanāmāvalīṃ
samuddharati  tasya jñānaśrīmitra nibandhaparijñānamāsīdityatra tu pramāṇaṃ nopalabhyate

nyāyāvatāra ṭippana ke devabhadrakṛte kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagataṃ sattvalakṣaṇaṃ samuddhṛtam  jñāna
śrīmitraśca nāmnā samuddiṣṭaḥ 
malliṣeṇanirmitāyāṃ syādvādamañjaryāṃ jñānaśrīkṛtāpohaprakaraṇasthasya etāsu pañca
svavabhāsinīṣvityādiślokasya samuddharaṇaṃ dṛśyate  paṇḍitāśokakṛtāyāṃ sāmānyadūṣaṇadika
prasāritāyāmapyeṣa śloka āyāti  paṇḍitāśokasya jñānaśrīmitrāt prācīnatvaṃ na
sandehātītam  atra tu prastutaślokasya kartṛnirdhāraṇe kṛte sati bhaviṣyati jñānaśriyā
malliṣeṇasya sambandhanirṇayaḥ

śāstrimahodayena prabhācandrasya kālo nirṇītaḥ  sa ca jñānaśrīmitrāj jyāyāniti
pratibhāti  ataeva kanīyaso jñānaśriyaḥ ślokasyoddhāro'pi tasyāsambhava eva 
yaśovijayācāryasyāpratyakṣa paricayo jñānaśrīmitreṇāsīt  anekāntavyavasthā 
prakaraṇe tena jñānaśrīmitrakṛtaḥ śloka uddhṛtaḥ  nyāyakhaṇḍakhādyasya tasyātmatattvavivekena
saha saṃbandhaḥ suviditaḥ  ato jñānaśrīmatāni tatra paramparayā āgacchanti  na ca kutrāpi
jñānaśrīmitro nāmadheyenollikhito yaśovijayena  nārāyaṇācāryakṛtā ātmatattvaviveka
vyākhyā raghunāthaśiromaṇerātmatattvavivekadīdhitiḥ guṇānandavidyāvāgīśakṛtaścātmatattva
vivekadīdhitiviveko bahudhā samuddhṛtā yaśovijayena  etebhya eva jñānaśrīmataparijñānaṃ
tasya bhavet  nārāyaṇāderapi jñānaśrīnibandhaparijñānaṃ nāsīditi bhāti āsīt

jagajjāyeta 
atha sattvalakṣaṇaṃ tāvad bhavatāmarthakriyāsāmarthya meveti cet  tat kimidānīṃ
samayasiddhena lakṣaṇena pratyakṣabādho'bhidheya    tad yadi bhavato'pi lakṣaṇadoṣa evānena
krameṇa vaktumiṣṭo'bhidhīyatām  asmākaṃ tu na tallakṣaṇaprasādhanāya parikarabandhaḥ
kiṃ tu tallakṣaṇena' kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanāya  atastallakṣaṇānavadhāraṇaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhipratibandha
mādadhīta kārye  kāryāntaradarśane tu tatrāpi tadanumānaprasavaḥ krameṇa kena vāryate  idānīṃ
tvarthakriyāsamarthasyaiva pakṣīkaraṇāt pakṣabahibhū te sādhyasādhanayorasiddhāvapi na kaścid doṣa
ityuktaprāyam' 
tasmāt sāmayikalakṣaṇakṣatāvapi ki punaraniścayamātre paṭutarapratyakṣabalāvalambita
vastubhāve aṅkarādivastuni vastudharmasya kāryatvasya virodha' iti  tadapekṣayā bījā
dikamarthakriyāsāmarthyasamarthanasahameva kathamasiddhiḥ 
nanvarthaṃkriyāsāmarthyamitaradvā vastulakṣaṇamaspṛśatendriyajñānena kathaṃ vastutvamupa
sthāpitamityucyate  tadapi yat kiñcit anubhave pramāṇāntaracintāyā niravakāśa
tvāt  dṛśyate hi śāstrīyalakṣaṇānullekhepyabhyāsabhāvitapratyakṣodayamātrād vastutvamavasāya
pravṛttiravisaṃvādabhāginīti kimatra kriyatām  evaṃ tu syāt  yadi paramārthato'rthakriyā
sāmarthyameva vastutvaṃ tadā idamato jāyata iti janmādhiraṇaṃ vastūlikhatā 'adhyakṣeṇārtha 
kriyāsāmarthyamevollikhitam  athānyadeva vastulakṣaṇaṃ tadā tadevollikhitam  yathā
'triguṇamayatvamitaradvājnullikhitā tadabahirbhūtaṃ nīlaṃ nīlagrāhiṇā 'gṛhītamevātatsiddham
adhyakṣeṇaṃ vastutvamaṅkurā kāryatāvāde'pi kāryāntarādarśane'pi kāraṇasya
 sādi paṭi a  no'santaḥ ra  halasya a  tāvaditi nāsti ra  dhovidheya ra
 neti nāsti a  sādhanopapari ra
 kṣaṇe a
 prāyaḥ a   tāvastu ra ā
 naṃ varodha ā   sāmarthanasahameva ā   matarad ra   mavasthāyitaṃ ā  bharita ā
 kriyātā a dhyeṣaṇārtha ra ā  ṇīmayatva ā ra  meva tatsi a mevā ra
 nastattamaṅkurādeḥ ra  kāryatāmasvāmi ajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
bījāderarthasāmarthyamavasthāpayatīti  kāryaṃvat tarhi bījādikamapi pratyakṣodayādevāstu
vastusat' kimarthaṃ sāmarthyagaveṣaṇeneti cet  na vai vastuvyavahāre pratyakṣapāṭavaṃ paribhūyārtha
śaktimanusarāma tasyā api pratyakṣādhīnatvāt  kiṃ tu kṣaṇabhaṅgamaṅgīkārayitum 
pratyakṣakṛto hi vastuvyavahāra uktakrameṇa tadatallakṣaṇasādhāraṇoṃ na kṣaṇikatvasādhā
niyamena prabhavati  arthakriyāsāmarthyaṃ tu vastulakṣaṇamabhavadapi yatra svayaṃ vartate tatrāvaśyaṃ
tadanupanīya na svarūpasattāmā viśati  tataḥ sādhanatvenāsya prastāvo'tra na vastulakṣaṇa
tveneti sthitam 
evaṃ jñāne'pi svarūpasaṃvedanaṃ sattvāvyabhicārīti sarvaṃ pūrvavat  tadanenāpi viṣayasya
sāmarthyasiddhiravyāhateti veditavyam  pareṇa hi paravedane bhrāntiśaṅkāvakāśaḥ 
svarūpavedane punaḥ sarvathā tadabhāva eva  atha svavedane vipratipadyeta tadaikārthasamavāyināpi
jñānena vedanasvīkāre'ṅkurādivadeva' pareṇāpi svarūpopadhānānna kaścid doṣaḥ  anyathā
dṛṣṭārthavyavahārahāniḥ sarvathā prasajyeta 
nanu viṣayajñānayorhetuphalabhāva eva kathamavagantavyaḥ upalambhāt pūrva viṣayasyā
nupalambhāt  vyatirekabalāditi brūmaḥ  sati ca bāhye'rthe sthiretaratvanirṇayārambhaḥ 
tasmādarthakriyākārikadambakapakṣīkaraṇavat pramāṇagocaracakrapakṣīkaraṇe'pi nāśrayasvarūpa 
dvārā dvividhāpyasiddhirasthirasādhanasya 
athārthaśakteḥ sarvathā sūkṣmavicārāsahatvād a rtha  śaktaṃ sarvamiti kapakṣīkaraṇam
kiṃ vā sādhanamiti cet  nanu bījāderaṅkarādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ nahi dṛṣṭe anupapannaṃ nāma 
sarvasya hi vicāranāmnaḥ pramāṇasthānubhava eva sīmā  kiṃ caivamanicchan prāmāṇikaḥ kathaṃ
dhūmādapi dahanamanumāsyati  jalajvalanayorvātātapaśītātaṃḥ sadṛśīṃ pravṛttimālambeta
apravṛtti vā  bhavāneva kathaṃ vā mithyāśaktimāropayatā pareṇa sādhana upanyaste tadabhāvaṃ
vidvānevaitatparājayāśaṃsī dūṣaṇopanyāsottarito'sti  tatrāpyasiddhayādikameva vaktumādri
yase na tu jātyuttaram'  tadetadāyātam nātmanāpi pratyaya iti  tasmād brūyā kiñcit
kenacit pratāritaḥ  durapahnavā tu śaktirartheṣu  sābhāsā cet  saṃvṛttyā na paramārthena 
astu yathā tathā saṃvṛttyā paramārthena vā kimatra nirbandhena 
 prastuptaṃ a vāstukimartho ra  sādhanīya ra  svarūpatāmā ra  sādhanake ra
 viṣayasāma ā  hīti nāsti ra  parato vedane ra  jñānenāsvīkāre'ṅkurādivade va ra
svīkārāṅkurādiva a  jātyuttaraḥ a ttaraṃ ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ
matiḥ
atha 'bhāvasāṃvṛtaśaktisamanvayinī kṣaṇikatāpi sāṃvṛtī syānna pāramārthikīti
 tatrāpyucyate  iha tattvābhyāso'bhyudayaniḥśreayasaphalaheturiti
nityānityādivicāramā rabhante santaḥ tadaniścaye'bhyāsānupapatteḥ  sa cābhyāso
nityeśvarādidattasāhāyakastannirapekṣo vā tatphalahetu syāditīdṛśi prakaraṇe pramāṇa
parīkṣādakṣāṇāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgāvatāraḥ  atra yadi paramapuruṣārthasādhanamaniṣṭaparihāreṇa
śaktisthitināntarīyakatayā saṃvṛtireveyam kṣaṇikatāpi saṃvṛtirevāstu paramapuruṣārtho
payogenaiva kṣaṇikatāyāmādarāt  kimasmākaṃ paramārthacintayā yatra na pramāṇaprameya
vibhāga sādhyasādhanavyavahāro vā kaścit  atha paramārthe'pyevaṃ saṃbhavati tadā tadā 
kṛṣṭaḥ śaktisambhavaḥ tadanvayī ' vā kṣaṇabhaṅgo na pāramārthikatvamāpatati  pramāṇaprameya 
vibhāgādyabhāve tu sarvathā caitanyavyāvṛttau svacinmātravyavasthitau vā pakṣadharmatvādya
bhāvaniścayakālavat kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirabhavantyapi na pīḍayati  tatra kṣaṇikatāsiddhira
tāttvikīti yastrāsayati sa svargāpavargaphalaprāptirapāramārthikīti kiṃ na trasyati 
tasmād yāvat sādhyasādhanabhāvavyavahāraḥ tāvat parīkṣākṣamamityeva pāramā
thiṃkatvam mūladūṣaṇaṃ  prati sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāsatkalpatvāditi  alamativistareṇa 
etena yadasthānābhiniveśinā nyāyabhūṣaṇakāreṇa bhāṣyakārīya kāryakāraṇa
bhāvadūṣaṇaprabandhamutthāpya varṇitam tat sarvaṃ nirupayogamiti pratipāditam  tathāhi
yadyetāvata śramasyāsiddhatodbhāvanāyāmevopayoga kimanena kartavyam  asiddhidha
parihṛtā puruṣārthasamīyā 'vastutattvanirūpaṇapravṛttasya śaktisiddhināntarīyaka
vyāpāratvāt  tata eva tathā kramākramābhyāṃ kāryotpattirvyāptetyetadapyasiddhamiti
yaduktaṃ tadapi niravakāśam  yadapyanena tattadāśaṅkayottarābhimānāt paryaṃnte sāṃvṛtatvārtha
kriyāpātāt
arthaṃkriyāsamarthaṃ yat tadatra paramārthasat 
pra vā  
 atheti nāsti a  bhāva iti nāsti ra  syāditi nāsti ra  atrāpyu ra  sadāra
 dṛśī a  tava yadi ra  śaktimiti ra  neti nāsti ra  sambhavatasta a
 sveti nāsti ra   siddhiśva pīḍayanti ra  tatrā a  parīkṣākṣamamiti nāsti a
 bhāṣiṇaṃ ā ra  bhāṣyakārya  ā  bhramasyā a  vastutva ra  kāryopapatti ra
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
'ityuktiveyathyaṃmudbhāvya likhitam  yathā saṃvṛtyārthakriyāsamartha tathā tat paramārthasaditi
cet  sāmānyāvayavisaṃyogādeḥ kiṃ na tathā sattvamiṣṭam  tasya saṃvṛttyāpyasāmarthya miti
cetna anvayavyatirekapratibhāsasyobhayathā tulyatvāt  tathāhi yatra yatra cakṣuḥ pravartate
tatra tatra taimirikakeśādivanna stambhādipratibhāso bhavatīti stambhāde sāmarthyagatiḥ 
tathā mahiṣādiṣu gavādyanvayabuddhirna bhavati  paramāṇumātreṣu saṃyogādirahiteṣu
cāvayavisaṃyogabuddhirna bhavatīti sāmānyāderapi sāmarthyagatiriti  tadapyasāram 
nahi saṃvṛtirityeva parigrahastyāgo vā bālasaṃvṛterapi grahaṇaprasaṅgāt  paṇḍitasaṃvṛterapi
paramapuruṣābrthasādhanapravaṇāyāstyāgaprasaṅgāt  avicāritaramyā hi pratītiḥ
saṃvṛtiḥ  asti ca bālakasya darpaṇatalāvalīnasatyavadana graho vicāravidhuraḥ puruṣārtha
sādhanagraho vā paṇḍitānāṃ tvadvicāreṇa vidhurito na ca tyājyaḥ tatparityāge kṣaṇabhaṅga
parīkṣānapekṣāyā iṣṭatvāt 
atha bauddhasyāyaṃ vicāro mama tvatrāniṣṭireva'  tato bauddhasyaiva' siddhānta 
virodhaḥ sādhanasya ca vādyasiddhatā doṣa iti cet  sa tāvadayaṃ vicāra pramāṇam
apramāṇaṃ vā  pramāṇatve tavaivāyaṃ na mameti vibhāgānupapattiḥ  pratyuta pramāṇād
bahirbhāvasvīkāre nādhikāra  prativāde'pi tavetyāyātam  athāpramāṇam tadā yadi
nāmāgamapradeśapratipādito'rthaḥ kaścinna samartha  ' prakṛtasya tu na kṣatiḥ  tadetadāyātam 
yadi kiñcit kacicchāstre na yuktaṃ pratiṣidhyate 
bruvāṇo yuktamapyanyaditi rājakulasthitiḥ 
pra vā  
iti  sautrāntikasamayasthitasya hi kṣaṇabhaṅgaṃ prasādhayataḥ sthityantaravirodho na
bādhakaḥ  anyathā
ākāśaṃ dvau nirodhau ca nityaṃ trayamasaṃskṛtam
 abhidharmakośe 
ityanena kiṃ navābhidhānam  naiyāyikasya copamānaṃ pramāṇamicchato vaiśeṣikā
pekṣayā kathaṃ na siddhāntavirodha  bhinnaprasthānatvaṃ tu samānam  śaktisaṃśrayaśca na
 iti vyakti ra   miti cetara anvaya ra  vattasta ra  tathā hi ra  govālaṃ sa  
vṛte ra  pramāṇāyā ra   syaivāyaṃ ra  riva ra   syāya ra  tavāya ra  māyama ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ
sautrāntikanītimatikramya '  yadi tu tatrāpi na syāt śaktisthitiḥ tadā svapratibhāsa
mātramācaṣṭe na bauddhasiddhāntasthita iti syāt  tasmānnayāntaravirodhe'pi na siddhānta
virodhayogaḥ nāpi vādyasiddhiḥ  na ca vastubalapravṛttānumāne śāstrānurodhaḥ kaścit 
tadvicāraprāmāṇye tu sāṃvṛtatve'pyathaṃśakteravaśyābhyupagantavyatayā tadupanītakṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhi
bādhitanityābhimatasāmānyasamavāyādikalpanamadharasaṃvṛtitvād bālasaṃvṛtivannopādeyam
arthakriyāśaktau  aśaktī sva viṣayajñānajanane'pyayogyasya sattvābhyupagama saṃvṛtirastu
kiṃ tvadharato'pyadhareti niścayaḥ  ataevādharādharasaṃvṛtyapekṣayottarottarāsu paramārthatvena
'vyavasthāpyamānāvaśyābhyupagantavyā niruttarārthakriyaiva saṃvṛti paramārtha iti tathā sat
paramārthaṃsaducyate  tathāhi bālasya darpaṇatale vadanagrahamapekṣyāsadeva vadanamatra
khyātīti' paramārtha iti ucyate  tadapekṣayā ca darpaṇapratihativyāvṛttyā netrāṃśavaḥ
svamukhameva gṛhṇātīti paramārtha  evamuttarottaraparikalpeṣu' balavatsu pūrvapūrvaḥ saṃvṛtiruttaro
ttaraḥ paramārtho yāvadarthakriyāsthitiḥ  tadatikrame hi grāhyagrāhakabhaṅgādāyātaṃ pratibhāsa
mātravyavasthānamiti kva saṃvṛtervārtā  tasmāt saṃvṛtīnāma antimārthakriyāśaktireva
paramārthaṃśabdavācyeti na saṃvṛtimātratvena sāmānyādisaṃvṛtistatkalām adhirohati 
tadvicāraprāmāṇyaṃ tu 'gajanimīlikayāvadhīrya tattvatta eva śaktiḥ paramārthastatra tatro
cyate sāmānyādayaśca saṃvṛtisanta iti  evamavayavisaṃyogādayo'pi saṃvṛtisantastadva
dubhayathā veditavyāḥ śakte paramārthatayā nityatābhyupagamatvāt kṣaṇasthitidharmatāyāḥ 
aṇava eva hi viśiṣṭotpannā dravyadvayaṃ vā saṃyogaśunyaṃ tattadbuddhisādhanamiti kimavaya
vyādinā  tat kathaṃ sāmānyādiparigrahaḥ saṃvṛtimātratvenārthakriyā samīkriyate 
yadi ca tāvataiva sāmyaṃ kimupapattighoṣaṇena  mā bhūdhara saṃvṛtitvamiti niyamo
panyāsaḥ  tacca śaktisamanvayinaḥ tadādhārasya vā kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgamena dunivāram  yathoktaṃ
prākśaktisamanvayābhāve tadādhārasthāpi saṃvṛtisattve kutastaddharmasya 'sāmānyāderadhara
saṃvṛtitvaparihāra  tasmāt saṃvṛtimātratvameva sāmyam  tatra cokto doṣaḥ  yā
ceyamupapattirbuddhivyatireko nāma sāpyapohe cintayiṣyate 
 kramasya ra  stayā a  māviṣṭena a  sveti nāsti a  rtha kena ra
 vyamānāvasva ra vyasāmarthavaśyā a  ucyate iti nāsti ra  itīti nāsti a
 nirvikalpeṣu a  bhutkandhā ra   nimīlitena ra  aṇava hi ra  samāyate a
  panyāsaḥ a  tinyāpanyāsā ra   kti samarthārthāyina  ra  samarthabhāve ra
 radharaṃ sa ra  sādhya ṣyate iti nāsti ra  sāpi kṣīṇā nahi buddhimātra
vyatirekeṇa vyatirekavastusiddhikramaḥ  ki tarhi vastvantarākāraparihāreṇa
yatrākāra viśeṣo
buddheḥ sphuṭataravastutasya yadā nārthasya bāhyavastugrahaḥ tadvaghatirekavyatireka vastukathanamjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
yaccedamūce  kiṃ ca yadyanirūpitatattvā pratītiḥ saṃvṛtiḥ tata eva kāryakāraṇavyava
sthitiriṣṭā tathā satyakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ sarvavyavahāriprasiddho'nvartho
jñeyaḥ' kiṃ tatra sūkṣmavicāreṇeti  tadapyayuktam  tathāhi yastāvat tattvata eva
kṣaṇabhaṅgurabhāvagrāmasādhanāya sādhanamāha sautrāntikaḥ svacinmātrāsthitau sādhana
dūṣaṇāvadhānābhāvāt tasya tāttvikameva sāmathyaṃ trividhaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhopalabhyam  kathaṃ
tasyāyamupālambhaḥ  paraviṣayapramāṇopasthāpitamanyaṃ vā parihṛtya kathamāsitumasau
samartha  tāvatā ca tāttvikī kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ sāṃvṛtamupa
pādayati iti kimasyāṅgīkaraṇaprayāsena  na ca vicāra parisphuranneva parihatu' śakya
chāyādravyatādiniṣedheśvarasiddhayādiṣvapyanādaraprasaṅgāt  tadaniṣṭavādinaḥ pratīta
syāpi vicārasya sūkṣmatvāditi kṛtamidānīṃ śāstraparamparāpariśrameṇa  tataśca kiṃ tatra
sūkṣmavicāreṇeti vimucya vicāraśvārurasau na bhavati yenākṣaṇikakṣepa' iti vaktumucitam 
tacca na pratijñāmātreṇa sidhyati  asmābhistu nityamatyetuṃ sādhanamupanyastam  na ca tatra
doṣaḥ 
atha prastutasūkṣmavicārādare sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāpyavakāśaprasaṅgo doṣa eva
yadāha  sūkṣmekṣikayā hi kāryakāraṇabhāvād bheda eva syāt tvaduktāt nyāyāditi 
idamapi śraddhājaḍasyaiva śobhate  yāvaddhi bhāvānāmarthakriyāśaktiparityāgaṃ na sahāmahe
tāvadavyāhataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgāṅgīkāro nityanigrahaśca  yadā tu śaktivivecana vib
cārāntare ca balavati cetaḥ kramiṣyate tadā kṣaṇikatāvimokṣamapītyakṣamaḥ  samāna
svāddaṇḍasya  na caivaṃ śakterupagamo nityatāmanityatāṃ ca pratyujjīvayituṃ śaknoti asādhā
raṇatvāt  tathāhi na khalu śaktiriti pramāṇaśūnyameva kiñcit kacit kadācid astī
tyavimokṣaḥ  ki tarhi  etadvījādikamaṅkarādisamarthamityanenākāreṇa pratyakṣa prativedyata
yaiva  tacca pratyakṣaṃ yathānvayavyatireke pramāṇamiṣṭaṃ tathā kāryāṇāṃ 'kramītaratvepītyevaṃ prakāreṇa
nyāyena śakti kṣaṇikatāyāṃ viśrāmyantī na nityasādhāraṇīti kathamubhayorapi
na caivamādhārarūpavyatirekeṇa rūpanirbhāsa  sāmānyādevikalpamātrasya tu kalpite sāmānye kvāpi
sāmābhyaṃ sāmānya miti  iti prānte kenacid yojitam  a 
 ddho'bhyanujñeyaḥ ra   trividha ra  manvarthā a  śakyate ra  tāni ra
 dviṣvanā ra  apīti nāsti ra  nākṣaṇikatvakṣe ra  nityamityetuḥ a 
prasaṅga ra
 bhāvoccheda ra  syai va śobha ra  vivecini ā  cakāro nāsti a  bhramiṣyate a
 dhimokṣamaya ra  pratyavayituṃ a  bhramī a  śaktikṣaṇikatāyā ra
 ranī kathaṃ a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāra
pratyujjīvanam  tadevaṃ balavati 'hetuphalatā bhraṃśaśaṃsinī vicāre śaktisiddhā kṣaṇika 
vāsti  sā saṃvṛtiḥ  nityatā 'tvadharasaṃvṛtireveti sāmānyavad bhāvyam  tadvicāra
balane tu na kiñcidāśaṃkāsthānamiti siddhaiva śaktiḥ 
tatkathamucyatetathāpyasiddhatvānna sattvena kṣaṇikatvasiddhi  nāpyarthakriyāyāḥ
kramākramābhyāṃ vyāptisiddhiriti sāṃvṛtaśaktipakṣe'pi nirvāhasya darśitatvāt 
nanu yathā saṃvṛtau paramapuruṣārthaṃ prārthayamānasyopāyānveṣaṇapravṛttasya nārthaśaktimanā
śritya sthātuṃ śaktiḥ tathā mayā tatphalalābhinā bhāvyamityupāyānveṣaṇānnityatāgraho'pya
vaśyamāyāta iti nityo'pi satsaṃvṛtisanna bhavatu kathamadharasaṃvṛtiviṣaya  nityātmā tu
cintāntaramarhati  na ca tanmātreṇopagamārhaḥ yataḥ saṃvṛtiviśeṣaviṣaya syāt  evaṃ

bādhakasya
kiṃ cāyamabādho nāma bādhāviraho bādhānupalabdhirveti vikalpayoḥ kramād

kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'nvayādhikāra
apica māyākaraḥ śirasi nimajjitaṃ golakamāsyena niḥsārayatīti pratya
bhijñā śirasi chidraprasaṅga saṅgatenānumānena bādhyamānā ki nopalabdhā  bādhyamānā
na pratyakṣamiti prastute'pyastu  ataḥ pratyakṣatvakīrtanamasyā yācitakamaṇḍanamātramatrā
ṇam  yathā cāvanatākāśapratibhāsaḥ sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nābādhya eva tathā nāvisaṃ
vādyevetyapi vyaktam  tadvadeva caikatāgrahaḥ a sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nāvisaṃvādī 
nahi tadaparādhyavasāyodayamantareṇa praṇatāmbarasaṃvedane sa evāyamiti pratyaye'paraḥ
saṃvādo'rthaṃkriyādisvabhāva  saṃbhavati  ataśca bādhakābhāve'pi nāmāprāmāṇyavyava
hāro'śakyasādhanaḥ  tadvadeva saṃvādena prāmāṇyamanvaśāsataḥ tadabhāvāt prāmāṇya
vyavahāro'pi kutaḥ pratyabhijñāyā  ubhayaniścayābhāve ca tadubhayāvalambī saṃśayaḥ
siddhaḥ  tallakṣaṇe kadalakāṇḍādau vyabhicāradarśanāt paripuṣṭāniṣṭāṅgaśca' tatkutaḥ
prāmāṇyam 
ki ca ya evamāha visaṃvādinī yā sā pratyabhijñaiva na bhavati tadābhāsatvāditi
tena śabdādau prameyatvaṃ hetukṛtya yat sādhyavyabhicāri prameyatvaṃ tatprameyatvameva na
bhavati tadābhāsatvādityapi vaktavyameva 
atha pramāṇaviṣayatvamātraṃ prameyatvam tacca vyabhicāriṇo'pyakṣīṇam  evaṃ
rtāha pūrvāparekīkaraṇamātraṃ pratyabhijñārtha  tacca vyabhicāriṇyā apyasti  pratyabhijñā
nāma kriyatāṃ mā vā kevalaṃ sā pramāṇameva na ' bhavatīti vaktavyam  prameyatva
mapi yadvyabhicāri tat liṅgameva na bhavatītyapi brūhi  ekalakṣaṇatayā yathaikatra
vyabhicārastathānyatrāpi saṃbhavanna 'nivāryaṃta iti pratyabhijñāne'pi nāśakyam 
nanvagniratretyanumānamananumānaṃ ca hetvābhāsakāle samānākāram  tatkatham
ekatrāśvāso' nānyatra  hetudvāreṇa viśeṣāt  yathā hi ekaṃ trirūpa liṅga niścayajanitam
anyadanyathā yathā kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītireva kācitpariśuddhā yā adhyakṣānupalabdhi
sādhanā kācidanyatheti darśitam  tathā ca sati bhinnalakṣaṇatvāt nāśvāsānāśvāsasaṅkaraḥ
tathā na pratyabhijñāyāṃ śakyam anupahatendriyasyeva tajjñānasya vā vyabhicāriṇyāmapi
vyāpārāt  nāparaḥ parairapi paridīpite viśeṣa  dīrghakālānubandhamātraṃ tu bahala

jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
vyāmohād adṛṣṭādihetuprabhāvād  viparyaya sāmagrīsamavadhānaparilambe'pyupapattimat
yathoktaṃ prāk  yad vā yataḥ kutaścit parokṣārthapratipattimanumānamanumatya yatra vyabhi
cāraḥ taliṅgameva na bhavati anumānaṃ veti nirvṛttimālambamāna pakṣadharmatvādika
liṅgalakṣaṇaṃ tatprabhavamanumānaṃ kimarthamabhidadhyāt 
atha vyabhicāriṇo'pi vyabhicāradarśanamasamartham sāmagrīlābhavilambe
vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa liṅgatvaprasaṅgād vaktavyameva lakṣaṇam yadīkṣaṇānnirvṛttiranī 
kṣaṇādanāśvāsaśca jāyate 
tato na prekṣastadanurūpānuṣṭhāna prārambhamāsāda
yet  santi hi pratyanī kadarśanasthānāṃ sādhanāni 'cirakālābhyāsabhāvitā samasamā
dhibalonmīladadhyakṣagocaravyabhicārāṇi ' kṣaṇikatādisādhanavat  tatkimidānīṃ
vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa bhāvinyā pramāṇānupapatteḥ sādhanānyeva bhavantu tadanurūpā
   nuṣṭhānena vā viphalamāyāsamāviśatu prekṣa  pakṣadharmatvādilakṣaṇe tu tallakṣaṇa
nirūpaṇāyāṃ tadaprāptau tadaiva 'hastakatyāgānnāyāsamāviśati  tallakṣaṇaprāptau vā tadeva
upādadīta  tanna vyabhicārāvalambanaṃ sādhu  vyatirekanirākaraṇāyaiva vivekā
rambhāt  tatkathaṃ lakṣaṇamavācyamiti cet  etat sarvaṃ pratyabhijñāyāmapi ālocayan
yāvanna lakṣaṇabhedaṃ paśyasi tāvannaikasyāṃ vyabhicārādarśī vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇāpara
syāmāśvāsa mekāntena katu marhasi  tasmāllakṣaṇayukte bādhāsaṃbhave tallakṣaṇameva dūṣitaṃ
syāditi sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ  tadiyaṃ pratyabhijñā vyapanayatu vyabhicāraśaṅka kalaṅkitā tayā
na kālāntarasthitimarthasya sthāpayitu prabhavati nāpyanumānamanavakāśayitum  tat
kathaṃ tadapekṣayā pratyakṣabādhitaḥ pakṣa ucyate  sapakṣe vā jaladhare kathamanvayābhāvaḥ 
atha mā bhūt pratyabhijñāyā prāmāṇyam tadanusārī sthiratāniścayo vā  kṣaṇika
tvāvadhāraṇaṃ tu sapakṣīkṛte kathaṃ yataḥ sapakṣe sattvaṃ hetorupapadyate  ucyate
iha jala
dharasya jaladhāraṇakriyāsamarthastāvadekārthasvabhāvo'śakyaparihāraḥ  kṣaṇāntare ca
dvitīyādau tatkriyāyāḥ 'kṛtatvāt punaḥ kartumaśakyatvāt tajjātīyāmanyajātīyāṃ' vā
kuryāt  na kuryād vā kāmapi kriyāmiti pakṣaḥ  evaṃ tat kriyākaraṇakṣaṇāt prāgapi
 a pāṭho ghṛṣṭaḥ vipa rya  ya ra   lambyamāa   diti ra  apīti nāsti ra  rśana
samarthasāmagrī a  tadanumānuṣṭāna ra  kālāghyābhyāsa a  vyabhicārīṇi kṣaṇika 
sabhāṃ saṃviśata prekṣāḥ ra  hehatakatyā ra  u  ta lakṣaṇa a  vyatireke ra  naikasyāvyabhi ra
 vyabhicāradarśī a  pratyabhijñānyāyānayet  vyabhicāraśaṃkātayā ra  stāvadekadāsvabhāvo ra
 kriyeyaṃ ra  anya jātīyāmiti nāsti ra  taditi nāsti a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ
vaktavyam  tatra yadi 'tatkaraṇasamarthasvabhāvo'mbhodharaḥ tatkṣaṇavat kṣaṇāntare'pi
kathaṃ kadācit kriyāviccheda  kṣaṇāntaranivartanīyakriyāsamarthasvabhāvatve vā kṣaṇāntaravat
tatrāpi kṣaṇe sajātīyetarakriyāprasavaprasaṅgaḥ  kṣaṇāntare'pi hi tacchāmarthyasya saṃbhavājjananaṃ
taccānyadāpyakṣīṇam 
kāryāṇi hi vilambante kāraṇāsannidhānataḥ 
samarthahetusadbhāve kṣepasteṣāṃ tu kiṃkṛtaḥ 
 tattva saṃgraha  
etenākaraṇapakṣo'pi pratikṣiptaḥ  yadā vilambo'pyasahyaḥ tadā dūrotsāditam
akaraṇam  asāmarthya vā samīhitasamaye'vyakaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ sadaikasvabhāvatvāt  svabhāva
aṃśe ca pratikṣaṇaṃ kṣayaḥ siddho jaladharasya  tatra prayogaḥ yad yadā yajjananasamarthaṃ tattadā
tajjanayatyeva'  yathā'ntyā kāraṇasāmagrī svakāryam  sa eva vā jaladharastadavasthāyāṃ
vāri dhārayan ' kṛṣībalavilocanotsavādikāryam vārivitaraṇakāle vā tatkriyām
śaktaścāyamubhayadaśāyāmubhayakāryamajitumiti svabhāvahetuprasaṅgaḥ  jananamantareṇa sāmarthya 
vyavasthāyāṃ sarvasya sarvatra śaktivyavahāraprasaṅgaḥ  niyataścāyaṃ pratipanno vyavahāraḥ 
na cāsya jananādanyannimittamupapadyate  tato jananavinābhāve vipakṣe niyamavattvena
a 'kṣaṇavyāpakaviyogenātmasattayā  viyujyamāno janana eva viśrāmyatīti samartha
vyavahāragocaratvamātrānubandhi janakatvaṃ siddhamiti vyāptisiddhiḥ 
kodravaḥ  na karoti ca
evaṃ yad yadā yatkaraṇasamarthaṃ tattadā tatkarotyeva  yathā'ntyā kāraṇasāmagrī 
śaktaścāyaṃ sakalakriyātikramakāle'pīti  anyadā  sarvathā'karaṇapakṣe yojyam 
asamarthasvabhāvatve tu yad yatrāśaktaṃ na tat tatkaroti yathā śālyaṅkaraṃ kodravaḥ 
aśaktaścāyamudavāhano'karaṇakṣaṇavat kṣaṇāntare'pīti vyāpakavirudvopalabdhe na
kadācit kuryāditi hetvarthaḥ 
viparyayaprayogaśca yad yanna karoti na tat tatra śaktam yathā śālyaṅṅkuramakurvan
prathamakṣaṇasādhyāṃ kriyāṃ dvitīyādikṣaṇe dvitīyā dikṣaṇasādhyāṃ
 samartha iti nāsti a  apīti nāsti a  mbhāvādevajanana ra  pākṣīṇaṃ a
 teṣāṃ hi ta sa  kiṃ kutaḥ a  durāt ra  tadā karotyeva a  vāridhāraṇa ra
 ato a  niyamavatve lakṣaṇa a  pāṭho ghṛṣṭa a  bandhe a  sidhyatīti a
 anyadā'karaṇa ra  labdhi ra  na ra 
 jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
vā prathamakṣaṇa iti vyāpakānupalabdhirjaladharasya tattatkriyāsu samarthāsamarthasvabhāvatayā
pratikṣaṇaṃ bhedamutpādayatīti 
evaṃ sarvathā'karaṇāpekṣayā yad yanna karoti na tattatra samartha' yathā śālyaṅkara
makurvan kodravaḥ  na karoti cākaraṇakāle karaṇakālakāryāṃ kriyāmiti  sāmarthyā
pekṣayā yad yat karoti na tat tatrāśaktam antyasāmagrīvat  karoti cāyaṃ' toyadhara
stoyadhāraṇamiti viruddhavyāptopalabdhi rasamarthakṣaṇād bhinatti karaṇasamartham  yathā hi
jananena vyāpyate samarthasthitiyogyatā tathā jananaṃ tayāpi  tadasāmarthyaviruddhaṃ yat
sāmarthyaṃ tena vyāptaṃ karaṇamupalabhyamānasāmarthyaṃ kadarthayatīti samarthāsamarthasvabhāvatayā
svabhāvabhedaḥ siddhastoyadasya  tatkathaṃ sattvādanyadanumānaṃ nāstītyucyate 
atra ca samarthavyavahārayogyatājananayobhinna vyāvṛttikatayā sādhyāviśiṣṭatā
hetorityavāntarai kīrtitaṃ dūṣaṇamanavakāśaṃ veditavyam  tasmādekārthakāriṇaḥ kṣaṇāntarā
pekṣayā samarthetarasvabhāvatayā bheda eveti kṣaṇabhaṅgitā sapakṣatāmāvati  balāhake
sattvasiddhiraviruddhā 
nanu kṣaṇabhedeṣvavatiṣṭhamānasyāpi  bhāvasya sahakārisaṃgamāpekṣayā 'karaṇākaraṇa
mupapadyamānaṃ kathaṃ svabhāvabhedamāpādayituṃ prabhavati  tato yathoktaprasaṅgamaulahetuṣvane
kāntaḥ  kiṃ punarasya' samarthasvabhāvasya sahakāribhiḥ kartavyam yadayamanapekṣya saha
kāriṇo na svakāryakarmaṇi pravṛttimālambate  anupakāriṇyapekṣāyā ayogāt  svayam
asamarthastu sāmarthyamarthayamāna  ' sahakāriṇo'pekṣata iti yuktametat  tato'kiñcitkarāḥ
ca sahakāriṇo'pekṣāgocarāśceti vyāhṛtam 
atra śaṃkaraḥ sahakāriviraho hi tasyāsāmarthyamucyate  taccāsya sahakāri
sākalyahetubhirapanīyate tayorekatra b sahasthitivirodhāt  sākalyahetubhyaśca
vaikalyasyaiva vyāvṛttiḥ na tadvataḥ sākalyasya sahakārivirahavyāvṛttirūpatvāt  na ca
'sahakārisākalyavaikalyayorāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāṃ tadvatastadbhāvasiddhiḥ
tābhyāmanyatvāt  ataeva sahakārivirahavyāvṛttihetorna tadvatastirobhāvasiddhiriti 
tasya
 na  ta  t tatra samarthaṃ ra  kārya kriyā ra  asamarthyāṃ ra  nāyaṃ ra  sa    marthya ra
 samarthyamiti ra   stoyadharasya ra  bhaṅgatayā a  sattve a  bhidyamāna ra
 kāraṇākaraṇa ra  puna  tasya ra  sāmarthyayamāna ra  sakalavai ra  sahakāritvameva
vyāvṛtta heto a 
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ
etadeva nyāyabhūṣaṇakāro'dhyāha sahakāriṇastasya kamupakāra kurvanti yena taivinā
na karotīti cet  kāryameva kurvanti  anyopakārakaraṇe hi sahakāritvameva na syāt 
tathāhi yadi tameva kurvanti tadā tatkāriṇa eva syuḥ na tatsahakāriṇaḥ  tena sahaikaṃ
kāryaṃ kurvanto hiṃ tatsahakāriṇo'bhidhīyanta iti  tathā bhavatu nāmānupakārako'pi
 sahakārī tathā yadi tasya prāgeva śaktirasti kiṃ na karoti  nāsti cet  paścāda
śaktaḥ kathaṃ karoti  paścācchaktaścet  śaktāśaktayoḥ kathaṃ na nānātvam  viruddha
dharmādhyāsasya bhedakatvādityāśaṃkya sahakārisākalyaṃ hi tasya śaktiḥ  tavaikalyaṃ
cāśaktiḥ  tena sahakārivaikalye prāgaśakta ucyate  paścāt sākalye ca śaktaḥ  
dharmadharmiṇośca' bhedaḥ prasādhitaḥ  tena śaktyutpāde'pi nāvaśyaṃ tadutpādaḥ  aśakti
nivṛttāvapi nāvaśyaṃ tadvato nivṛttiḥ pratibandhābhāvāditi 
tadetat sarvamapohaprastāve dharmadharmaṇorabhedapratipādanenaiva nirastaṃ veditavyam
sākalyavekalpayorāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāṃ dharmiṇa eva tathāvasthānāt 
astu vā
dharmadharmaṇorbheda eva  nāpi sahakāriṇāmakiñcitkaratve vipratipadyāmahe  kevalaṃ
na tāvanta eva sahakāriṇaḥ kāryakāriṇaḥ  nāpi sākalyameva kāryamarjati kiṃ tu so'pi
bhāvaḥ  'tadarthaṃ taireva ' prayattamiti na vistareṇopayogaḥ  tasya ca bhāvasya yādṛśaśvarama 
kṣaṇe'kṣapakriyādharmā svabhāvaḥ tādṛśa eva cetu prathamakṣaṇe'pi tadaiva prasahya kurvāṇo
gīrvāṇaśāpenāpi' nāpahastayituṃ śaktaḥ  kiṃ punastavāmunā marmapīḍājanitaviklava
vikrośamātreṇa  yathāhi śaktāśaktatayā bhaṅgaprasaṅgaparihārāya sākalyavaikalyalakṣaṇa
dharmāntarasvabhāve śaktayaśaktī bhinnasvabhāve kalpite tathā na so'pyakṣepa kriyādharmā
svabhāvo bhāvād bhinna evābhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ bhāvasthākartṛtvaprasaṅgāt 
tacca
atha yathā śaktyaśaktī bhinnau dharmo pratijānīmahaṃ na ca tayorudayavyayābhyāṃ
bhāvasya kiñcitu tathā'kṣepakriyādhamaṃtvaṃ kṣepakriyādharmatvaṃ ca dharmāntarameva 
'sahakārisannidhānapratyayabhāvākṣepamudeti vyeti ceti  tathaiva bhāvasya na kiñci
dityucyate

tathāhi yathā na sahakāriṇa eva nāpi sākalyameva janakaṃ tathā sākalye a sati'

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāṃvalau
jātamakṣepakriyādharmatvamapi na prakṛtaṃ bhāvamanapekṣya janakam janakatve'pi svayameva
bhāvasya janakatvasvīkārāt  kiṃ tu ' prakṛto'pi bhāvaḥ kartā strīkartavyaḥ  sa ca
prācīnadaśāto'natiricyamānamūrtiḥ kurvan pūrvamapi kuryāt akurvan vā paścādapi na
kuryāditi tadavastha paribhavaḥ  yadi tu kādācitkaṃ sākalyādivastvantarameva
hetu tadā kāryamapi tadapekṣaṃ kādācitkamiti nyāyyametat  evaṃ yāvad yāvad dharmāntara
parikalpaḥ tāvat' tāvadudāsīno bhāvaḥ  atha akṣepakriyādhamaṃtvaṃ jātaṃ kāryaṃ tu
tato itiko'yaṃ nyāyaḥ  tadavaśyaṃ kāryeṇa janitavyam  taccākṣepakriyā
dharmatvaṃ prāṅtāsoditi kāryodayasyāpi nāvakāśaḥ  evaṃ tarhi kāryātpādanāntaroyaka
makṣetrakāritvama akṣepakāritvanāntarīyakaśca kāryotpāda iti vyaktamitaretarāśrayatvam 
anyathā na yadi kāryotpādanāntaroyakamakṣepakāritvam nākṣepakāritvena
kāryodayākṣepaḥ  'yadi ca nākṣepakāritvanāntaroyakaḥ kāryotpādo'kṣepakāritvāt prāgapi
syāt  ekārthatve tu sākalye jāte 'satyakṣepakāritvaṃ dharmāntaraṃ jātamiti kimanayā
bhāṣayābhihitaṃ kāryamutpanna miti  tathā ca sati na prakṛtadoṣaparihāraḥ  nahi kārya
janmani vivādaḥ yatsvarūpāpekṣastu kāryodaya tasya sarvadā tādavasthyāt kathaṃ kadācitka
teti cintyate 
tasmādakṣepakriyādharmeti janayatīti vā yatsvarūpapuraskāreṇeyamabhikhyā tasya
prāgapi sattve kathamajani kadācit  akṣepakriyādharmakapratyanokasvabhāvasya vā prācyasya
paścādanuvṛttau kathaṃ kadācidapi kāryasaṃbhavaḥ  atha yadi sa evaikaḥ kartā syāt 
yuktametat kiṃ tu sāmagro janikā 'tatsahakāryantaravirahavelāyāṃ balīyaso'pi na kārya
prasava iti kimatra viruddham  ekārthakaraṇācca sahakāritvamukam nopakāreṇeti 
atrocyate  yadi militāḥ santaḥ kāryaṃ kurvate 'tadaikārthakaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ
sahakāritvameṣāmastu ko niṣeddhā  militaireva tu tat kāryaṃ kartavyamiti kuto
labhyate  pūrvāparakaryayorekatve tāvad 'bhāvastra sarvadā jananājananayoranyatara
niyamaprasaṅgasya durnivāratvāt  tasmāt sāmagrī janikā naikaṃ janakamiti sthiravādināṃ
manorathasyānyaviṣaya  dṛśyate tāvadevamiti cet  ataeva na sthairyapakṣa kṣama' iti
 apīti nāsti ra  prakṛtito ra  raṃ naiva a  ntaramapi vikalpa ra  yathā ra
 kāryaṃ ca a  tata iti nāsti ra  pāṭho ghṛṣṭa a  yadi ca nākṣepakāritva nāsti ra
 satyapekṣa ra  tataḥ ra  yadā ra  kuryāt ra  kārya ra  tukārastyaktaḥ ra
 kva ra  kālayo  kārakasvabhāvatvāda ra  jananā nāsti ra  kṣayaḥ ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāra
brūbhaḥ  sarvo hi prasaṅgo viparyayaparyavasānaḥ  tato yadi nityatā syāt janayituḥ janyaṃ
sarvadā syānna vā kadācidapīti  na caivam sākalya eva kadācitkāryotpattiriti
niyamena svabhāvabhaṅgaḥ 
nanu yadi kvacinnityaṃ sarvaṃdā 'kāraṇamupalabdhaṃ syāt tadā kvacinnityatvābhyupa
game sadā kartṛtvaprasaṅgaḥ saṃgacchate yāvatā sarvadā tasyābhāvāt kathametādṛśaṃ
prasañjayituṃ śakyate 
b tadetadapi grāmyam  tathāhi nityatve satīti  asyāyamarthaḥ  parakāla
bhāvī janako yaḥ svabhāvo bhāvasya ' sa eva yadi pūrvakālabhāvī pūrvakālabhāvī vā
yo'janakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa eva yadi parakālabhāvī tadā tadupalabdhameva jananamajananaṃ vā
syāditi  tathā ca sati siddhayorekatvārope siddhameva jananamajananaṃ vā prasajyeta 
na pūrvaparasvabhāvayorekatvasaṃbhavānnityatve satītyucyata iti kimatra viruddham 
atha pūrvaparayorekatvaṃ nopalabdhaṃ kathamāropyata iti manoṣā  evaṃ sati śuktāvapi
rajatāropeṇa na bhāvyam  nahi rajatasvarūpā śuktiḥ kvacidupalabdhigocaraḥ  āropya
rajataṃ kadācidupalabdhameveti nāropakṣatiriti bhavatāmapi kṛtāntaḥ  tathā
māṇaṃ
prastute'pi pūrvāparasvabhāvayorekatvaṃ nopalabhe  āropyamāṇau tu mitha pūrvāpara
svabhāvau siddhāveva  tadārope karaṇākaraṇe api prasajyamāne samañjase eva guñjāpuje
jvalanāropavidhau dāhavat 
tadetadatilāghavamāviṣkṛtamātmanaḥ śaṅkareṇa  tadayaṃ jātyandhānāṃ nolādiprati
vedhavadasaṃbandho niṣedha saugatānāmasanto'kṣaṇikā ityabhidadhānena  tasmāt
sthitametat sthirātmatve militvaiva kāryakaraṇaniyamo bhāgyahīnamanorājya
tathā ca sati sahakārisākalye śaktiśabda samayamapākurvāṇa
sthānīya iti  tathā
O
kamarthaṃ paripuṣṇāti paravyāmohanādanyamanupayuktāprastutābhidhānāt  kṣaṇikatva
vādinā hi śaktāśaktasvabhāvatayā viruddhadharmādhyāsād bhedamāropayatā yādṛśī

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
saṅketena parihāramāracayatīti mahannaipuṇyaṃ yāyikapravarasya  yo hi dhūmādatrāgninā
bhāvyamityāha  tatrāpi yadi kaścid gardabhādau dhūmaśabda saṃketya vahnimapahnavīta na
kaścid doṣaḥ  kṣaṇikavādī hi yajjanayatīti samākhyā  yadanantarabhāvi kāryaṃ

kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ
yaccānumānamāha śaṃkara sthirasiddhau notpattyanantaraṃ vināśī bhāvaḥ prameyatvāt 
vastuvyāvṛttivaditi  avidyamāna vipakṣatvādanvayyeva hetuḥ  prameyatvasya kṣaṇikatvena

katvayoḥ 
atha kāraṇaṃ viṣaya iti jñānāt prāgapekṣitasattāko'rthaḥ kṣaṇāntare'nanuvarta

paro bodhayitavyaḥ

svīkārāt  pṛthagjanāpekṣayā niyama eṣa iti cet  pṛthagjanāpekṣayā tarhi

ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
tena vā svaviṣayaniyatamutpāditaṃ jñānaṃ tadekagrāhi tatkāraṇasāmagrayā vā

janmanī kathamatiprasajyeyātām 
atha sākāravedanavādino hi viṣayādeva tatsvarūpasaṃvitterutpattirabhimatā
tatrātītagrahaṇe'tiprasaṅgaḥ grahaṇakṣaṇānuvṛttī ca sthirasiddhiriti vivakṣitam  tat
kimayaṃ prasaṅgaheturyatparopagamanamanapekṣya na bhavati  tathā ca sati viparyayaparyavasā

ca sati vyaktamanyad bhuktamanyad vāntamiti nyāya  sthiramārabdhaḥ sādhayitu
 tadviparyaṃyeṇa sākārabodhaṃ vidhurayatīti 
atha sautrāntikasyedamubhayamasamañjasamitīyanmātramucyate tadapi nāsti

' viparyayasarūpasvarūpa saṃvedanameva jñānasya viṣayavedanam  evaṃ ca na vartamānānurodha
atīte'pi tatpratyayāsatterapracyuteḥ  na cātiprasaṅgaḥ viṣayāntareṇāpi sārūpya
samarpaṇāt  na ca ' tanmata
nirvāhaḥ prakṛtaḥ'  bhavatastu tanmatāśrayeṇāpi prameyatvahetuḥ
sthirasiddhaye na prabhavatīti siddhamanekāntaparihārāditi  tataḥ sthiravapuṣi pramāṇāntara
 siddheśyogāt vajro'pa pakṣakukṣī nikṣiptaḥ kiṃ punaḥ sphaṭiko varākaḥ  tadayaṃ
sakriyākriyāvasthayobhiṃdyamānaḥ kathaṃ kāmabhedenāvirodhe dṛṣṭāntībhavitumarhatīti 
yacca viṣayabhedeneva kālabhedenāpi śaktyaśaktyoravirodhapratipādanam tadapyanopayikam 
pratiyogī hi dharmo virodhakaḥ sarvatra  na ca svakāryakaraṇasya parakāryākaraṇaṃ pratya
nīkam  kiṃ tu svakāryākaraṇameva  evaṃ parakāryākaraṇasyāpi parakāyaṃkaraṇaṃ pratyanīkam 
na svakāryakaraṇam  svakāryaṃ na karotīti vyavacchettameva hi svakāryaṃ karotītyucyate

karaṇamakaraṇaṃ ca pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na virodhaparihārāya paryāpnoti

na cātra
yacca nyāyabhūṣaṇena pralapitam yadyasya bhinnā śakti śaktimato'bhyupagamyate
tathāpi ' nāvaśyaṃ śaktāśaktayorbhedaḥ  kasmāt  tvanmate'pi dharmabhedād dharmibheda
niyamāsiddheḥ  tathā ca bhinne'pi kārye sahakāriṇāṃ pṛthagupayogaṃ darśayatā'bhihitam
mṛtpiṇḍāde mṛtsvabhāvebhya ityādi hetubindu lekhitvā  yathā ca tatra mṛdātmatādisvabhāva
bhede'pi na kāryabhedaḥ tathā śaktāśaktādisvabhāvabhede'pyabhedo bhaviṣyati abādhita
tvādhyavasāyasya' samānatvāditi tadapyanena pratyādiṣṭam  santi hi dharmā ye paraspara
virodhino'virodhinaśca  na tu dharmā ityeva virodhāvirodha  na hi brāhmaṇyaṃ
vaiyākaraṇatvenāviruddhamiti cāṇḍālatvenāpyaviruddhamityabhidhātuṃ śakyam 
brāhmaṇyavyāptaṃ cāṇḍālatvam  na ca vaiyākaraṇatvenāpi viruddham  yathā cātra svaprati
yogibrāhmaṇyetaratvameva virodhamādhatte na vaiyākaraṇatvena tathā janayadrūpamajananatayaiva
'viruddhabhāvāna vastusantānabhedena  nīlacaturasrāditā tu śvetaparimaṇḍalatādibhi
virodhamāsādayatu na tu kacit kāryakāraṇādibhiḥ  ato yadi virodhagandhā
saṃbhavāt saṃsthānamṛtsvabhāvayorabhinnena dharmiṇā bhāvyam tat kimatyantapratyanīkayo
reka kārya prati janayadrūpetarayorapīti kaḥ sacetanakaścintayet  viruddhāviruddha

cchedaḥ tattena viruddham  na ca mṛnmayamiti vidhānena pṛthūdaratāvyavacchedaśaṅkāpi

tasmād yayordharmayoryathā virodho dṛṣṭaḥ tathaivābhyupagantavya ityevameva viśeṣamabhipretya
yuktaḥ naikakālāpekṣayā samānapramāṇayorapravṛtteḥ  yena hi kālabhedenābhinnameva
vastu sakriyākriyanīlānīlatvādiyuktamabhyupagataṃ yasya vā tadātmani pramāṇaṃ pravṛttaṃ
tasya kacidvivādasaṃbhave kālabhedenāvirodhaḥ tadvatīti yuktam  tacca dvayamapi nāstīti
vyaktam  ata ekatvādhyavasāyasyābādhitaviṣaya viśeṣaṇamasiddham  ekatvādhyavasāya

va
atha naivābhinnātmanaḥ kasyacit svabhāvabheda iṣyate evaṃ tarhi sahakāripṛthagupa
payogakathanaṃ bālonmatta pralapitaṃ syāditi  tena yadi b dharmadharmaṇostādātmya
tiraskāreṇa bhedāpādanamātramiṣṭam tadā na prakṛtopayogi  tathāhi dharmiṇaḥ sakāśād
dharmā bhedabhāgino bhavantu na vā  santi tāvatkecidanyonyavirodhino ye svādhikaraṇaṃ
dharmiṇamabhitvā nocchvasituṃ śaknuvantīti vivakṣitaṃ kṣaṇikavādinaḥ  tatrānena
tādṛśā' dharmā eva na santi santo'pi vā kālādhupādhisāpekṣā bhedasādhava ityeva
vaktuṃ nyāyyam  pṛthagupayogāt sahakāriṇāṃ dharmiṇaḥ pṛthageva ta iti kimanena 
yadi tu svābhāvyabhāja eva bhedakā na bhidyamānā iti samayo'sya syāt
yuktametat  yāvatā valanādayo'pyavalanato bhedakā dṛṣṭā eva  te ca kriyādirūpatvād
bhinnā eva  tasmāt kalpanoparacitavibhāgā bhavantu saugatamatena bhavanmatena vā
tāttvika bhedo dharmaṃdharmiṇo kimidānīṃ naikāntena  prastāvāntaraṃ hi tat  duṣpariharāstu
dharmā' dharmiṇaṃ bhindānā ye virodhasthāyina iti siddhaṃ sādhyam 
atha kāryādabhedaśca  svabhāvānāṃ pṛthak sahakārikāraṇakalāpopayogaviṣayatvaṃ
ceti duḥśliṣṭatāmātramudbhāvyate paranayasya tadāpi prastutakṣaterabhāvāt kimanena 
bhedavatāmapi bhedakatvād dharmāṇāṃ duḥśliṣṭatābhāsatā ca bhinnasamayasthānāṃ paraspara
magaṇiteṣu sthāneṣu saṃbhavati  tattvaṃ tu kīdṛgiti tattatsthāna nirūpaṇe vyaktībhaviṣyati

tatra yadi prastutānupayogiyatkiñcidvistārayatā sthātavyamityabhimatam sarvasya
śakyametat  na caitāvataiva dharmadharmavādaparisamāptiḥ  tat kimasya garbhārbhakamanati
śayānasya nindāvacane nirbaṃndhena  tathā ca sati tasmānna dharmabhedādeva dharmibheda iti
'' nigamanamavyasyāyuktam  bauddhaḥ kila na dharmāṇāṃ bhedamātreṇa dharmibhedamāha 
kiṃ tu virodhena  anyathā kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāmapi dharmabhedamācakṣīta  anenāpi
svayaṃ viruddhadharmādhyāsādityakṣaramutthāpitam  tad yadi virodhabhedamātrayorviśeṣaṃ na
paśyati yuktamāheti kimaparaṃ vaktavyam 
yadapyayamevāha  yo 'hyananta ra kāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ sa kathamādau tat kāryaṃ kuryāt 
atha kuryānna tarhi uttarakāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ  na hi nīlotpādanasvabhāvaḥ pītādikamapi
karoti  na ca prathamottara kāryotpādanasvabhāvabhedāt tadvato'pi bhedaḥ svabhāva
bhedasya vyabhicāritvenoktatvāditi  tadapi niḥsāram  yadi hi svabhāvaśabdena
svalakṣaṇamabhipretam tadā tadbhede bheda eva vastūnām ka vyabhicāravārtā  tasmāt
svabhāvabheda iti kalpitadharmāntvaṃ yuktam  na ca tanmātreṇa dharmabhedamāpādayati
paraḥ  kiṃtu virodhena  na ca tadvirodhe'pi dharmibhedavyabhicāro'sti  virodho hi
na bhedaṃ vyabhicarati  bhedastu virodhaṃ vyabhicaratītyuktaprāyam 
nanu yadi kalpitā eva te dharmā ka virodha ka vā a bheda iti cet 
iha dvividhamabhidheyaṃ kalpitaśabdasya tattadvyāvṛttavastusaṃbhave bhedamātraṃ kalpanāvabhāsi
tadapi kalpitaṃ kuvalayanīlatvādivat  kalpanāmātraniveśi ca kalpitaṃ karikeśaratriguṇī
mayatvādivat  tatra yadyantima kalpitārtha syāt na bhedanirodhāditi yuktam  prācīne
tu kalpitārthe vastusvabhāvasyaivāvyavasānād bhedo virodho vā vyavasthāpyamānaḥ saṃvāda 
mādāyaiva vartata iti na doṣaḥ 
yacvedam uttarakṣaṇe yatkāryaṃ kartumasya svabhāvaḥ tatkathaṃ prathamakṣaṇe kuryāt 
anyathottara kāryakāritaiva' na svabhāvasyeti tadapyaparibhāvya bhāṣitam  sthirasvabhāvatve
hi bhāvasyottarakālamevedaṃ kāryam na pūrvakālamiti kuta etat  tadabhāvāca kāraṇa
mapyuttara kāryakaraṇasvabhāvamiti kutaḥ  arthānurodhinyo hi vācaḥ śobhābhājaḥ na
vāganurodhādarthaṃtathābhāvo rājavat  kiṃ kurmaḥ uttarameva tasya janmeti cet  astu 
 niyamana ra  hyutarakāryaṃ  ra  bhedotatvato ra  tadbheda ra  dharmāṇāṃ nānā ra
 dharmi nāsti a  ceti nāsti ra  bhavato ra  yetara rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau

lambanena' nistaraṇāt  dhūmādatrāgniragnerabhāvād vā neha dhūma ityukte'pi hi
śakyamabhidhātuṃ svabhāva evāyamasya yadidānīmatra niragnirapi dhūma iti  tasmāt pramāṇa
siddhe svabhāvāvalambanam na svabhāvāvalambanena pramāṇavilopaḥ  pramāṇanirṇayaśca
vihita eva  nīlotpādanasvabhāvaśca na pītādika karotītyasamīkṣākhyānam  upādāna

dupayogasyāśakyabādhanatvāt

ca yathā na nīlaḥ pītamutpādayati tathā nottarajanakaḥ pūrvamutpādayati  evaṃ tarhi yaścottara
janakaḥ yaśca nottarajanakaḥ tayorbhedo'pi kiṃ neṣyate yathā yannīlaṃ tannānīlamiti 
tadalamevaṃvidhapralāpeṣu nirbaṃndhena sthitametat parasparaviruddhadharmādhyāsād deśabhedavat
kālabhede'pi janakājanakasvabhāvayorbheda eva 
etena yadapi nyāyamañjarīkāraḥ prāha nanu kāryotpattiheturyeṣāṃ sannidhimapekṣate
te khalvapekṣitasannidhayaḥ sahakāripratyayāstastha ki kurvanti  na kiñcit  kevalaṃ
kāryameva yeṣāṃ bhāvābhāvāvanuvidhattaṃ te kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhayaḥ sannipatantaḥ
tadeva kāryaṃ vivakṣitaṃ hetunā saha kurvantīti sahakāriṇa ucyante na tu yena saha
kurvanti tasyaiva kartāro bhavantaḥ sahakāriṇo bhavitumarhanti  b  tasmādakṣaṇikasya
svakāryanimāṇe dvividhaṃ sāmarthyam ekaṃ nijaṃ sāmarthyam dvitīyaṃ cāgantukaṃ
sahakāryantaram tayorabhāve tatkāryānutpatteḥ  tasmādeva hi dvividhāt sāmarthyāt
kāryotpatterabhyupagamāt  ekamakṣaṇikaṃ gṛhītvā tasmādeva kāryotpatti saṃbhāvayantaḥ
sāmarthyameva hetūnāmavijñātavantaḥ pare  yasmādakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu tāsu tāsvartha
kriyāsu kartavyāsu kramavatsahkāryaṃntarameva sāmarthyamaṅgīkurmaḥ  tathā ca kramavat

ṇākhyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ saṃkhyātamasmanmate  tat kiṃ prāgapi paścādeva veti vikalpya dūṣaṇa
mudīritam  tatra kimanenoktaṃ bhavatīti niveditameva  yattu kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhaya
ityupaskṛtam tadapi nirupayogam  yadi hi kāryameva svajanmani svatantraṃ syāt yukta
metat ' kevalamevaṃ sati sahakāriṇāmapi sāmarthyarūpatākalpanamaphalamiti hetoḥ
sāmarthyamanapekṣya svātantryādeva kāryaṃ kadācid bhavati kadācinna bhavatīti ki hetu
sāmarthyasamarthanavyasanena' vyavahāramātraṃ vā sāmarthyamiti na tu kacit kiñcit samartha

vārtikālaṅkāre 
yadi hi svayaṃ bhavanaṃ bhāvayadeva' kāryaṃ hetuḥ tadā tadabhāvaprayukto'syābhāva
ityapi syāt  yadā tu hetau jananonmukhe'pi svātantryādeva na bhūtamiti kathaṃ tadabhāva 
prayojako'syābhāva iti pratītiḥ  tasmād yadi kāryakāraṇabhāva a tadā niyataṃ

na cāsau bhidyate tadabhedasya' pramāṇasiddhatvāditi 
apūrvo'yamasya dambhārambhaḥ  yadayamakṣepa kriyādharmā' svabhāva śaktiśabda

sahakārisākalyamiti bravīti śaktyaśaktilakṣaṇaviruddhadharmādhyāsād bheda ityabhimatena
kāryabhedāt kāraṇabheda iti samādhatte  kaḥ khalu kāryabhedāt kāraṇabhedaṃ vaktumupakrānto
yatraivamucyate sahakāribhadena yaḥ kāryabhedaḥ sa na kāraṇabheda iti 
api tu yasya yadā
yajjananasvabhāvaḥ so'vaśyaṃ tatkarotyeva  na hi pradīpa eva vijñānādikāryāṇi sakṛt

jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
īṣiṣya  bauddhasādhanavicārastāvat prastuto'yam  tatra ca prastute'neka kāryeṇānekena
bhāvyamiti kena karṇe bhavato niveśitam yataḥ pradīpadṛṣṭāntīkaraṇaṃ bhavataḥ śobheta 
tadidamucyate anyo vyādhiranyadauṣadhamiti 
yadapyāha yadeva ca sahakāribhedena kāryabhede pradīpasyābhedasiddhau sādhanaṃ tadeva
kramavatsahakāribhedena kāryabhede'kramasyāpīti tadapyatyantamasaṃbaddham  advayākāra
mindriyapratyakṣameva hi bhedabhraṃśamāśaṃsati pradīpe  sapratighasya hi pradīpasya naikasthānam 
bhinnadeśasya cātyantasadṛśasthāpi bhedopalakṣaṇamanivārya māyāgolakavat  ata ekākāra
mindriyajñāna mekatāyāmeva pradīpamavasthāpayati  kālabhede hi bhinne'pi vastunyatyanta
sadṛśe pratyabhijñānamupajāyamānamupalabdham  na ca pratyabhijñānādanyadekatāsādhanam 
tatkathaṃ tadeva sādhana miti na plavate  na ca sadṛśatayā kālabhedena pratyabhijñānasya
saṃśayāṅgatvaṃ vyabhicāradarśanāt lakṣaṇabhedavirahāt sakṛdabhedabhāsinyapi pratyakṣe'nā
śvāsaḥ tathā kvacidadarśanāt  indriyajñāne hi  kramadarśane'pi na yogyamarthadvayaṃ
pratighāti ekībhūyopalabhyamānamupalabdham  tatkathaṃ sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ  tasmādanupa
yoga pradīpadṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam 
etadeva rūpaṃ dṛṣṭāntīkṛtyābhiprāyāntaramasya dyotayan nyāyabhūṣaṇe'pi yadāha
api ca yena svabhāvena rūpaṃ rūpāntaraṃ karoti na tenaiva rasādikam rasāderapi
rūpasvabhāvatāprasaṅgāt  tataḥ sarvaṃ rūpakāryaṃ cakṣuṣā gṛhyate  na caitadiṣṭam  tasmād
yathā rūpaṃ rūpāntarotpādanasvabhāvena tadeva karoti vijñānotpādanasvabhāvena vijñāna
meva karoti na rūpādikam  rasotpādanasvabhāvena ca rasam aevaṃ gandha
sparśanajananasvabhāvābhyāṃ tāveva janayati  tadvadakṣaṇiko'pyādyakāryotpādanasvabhāvena
tadeva karoti  taduttarakāryajananasvabhāvena taduttarameva janayati  nādyamuttarottaraṃ vā 
evamuttarottara kāryeṣvananta kālabhāviṣvapi pratiniyatāḥ svabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ  svabhāvā
eva hetatro na svabhāvītyapyayuktam 'rūpasyāhetutvaprasaṅgāt svabhāvānāmeva hetutvāt

atha duṣṭameva tatsādhanam  tathāpi tena yat siddhaṃ tat siddhameva tāvat 
pradīpasya svabhāvabhedo bhavatu mā vā bhūtu tathāpi  kimasyopanyāsena  yacca dīpasya
svabhāvabhedasādhanāya sādhanaṃ kāryāṇāṃ tādātmyaviraho nāma so'pi yadi siddhasva
sādhyapratibandhaḥ tadā tena yadi yugapadapi bhedasiddhiḥ kasyacit tadā tadorṣyayā
kimanena bauddhasādhanena  prayāgavaṭaprayātāyātayoḥ dvitīyamūḍhakarṇāṭeneva svasādhyasādha

pravartate na vā kiñcidapi sādhanaṃ sādhyasādhanāya pravarteta dhūmādisādhanaṃ svasādhya

ru
athedaṃ pradīpasvabhāvabhedasādhanamadhyakṣā vikṣiptaṃ svasādhyapratibandhavidhuraṃ vā
tadā tadeva naśyatu  na tadā bauddhasādhanasya kṣatiḥ  tathāpi kiṃ tasyopanyāsena 
yadi bauddhasparddhayā tadvimarśamasārīkatu mupamānabhūtaṃ vimarśāntaramevedamupanītam'
tadāyamasthitaḥ pakṣaḥ svabhāvabhedo dīpasyeti  evaṃ sati eka evāsau śaktiviśeṣo
yasteṣāmutpādaka iti cet  etadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayābhyupagamyamānamapi na
nītiśīlān prīṇāti  pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānābhāve teṣāṃ sarvatrotpatteradṛṣṭapūrva
tvādityādinā  tathā  svabhāvabhedābhāve ca kāraṇasya kāryabhedabhāve tasyākasmikatvaṃ
prasajyeta  tathā cākaraṇaṃ viśvasya vaiśvarūpyaṃ syādityanena ca kathaṃ svabhāvabhedameva sva
bhāṣayā draḍhayet  na cāyaṃ nyāyyaḥ  tathā hi yattāvaducyate yadi yenaiva svabhāvena
dīpo vartivikāra hetustenaiva jvālāde  tadā jvālāderapi vartivikāratvaprasaṅgaḥ na caivam 
tasmādbhinnenaiva svabhāvena vartivikāre bhinnena ca jvālādau dīpaḥ pravartate iti viparya
yārthaḥ  tatra ca pratyakṣabādhaiva ṣa niraṃśasya dīpādestatra bhāsanāt  anyathā kadamba 
 viraho a  bauddha ra  dṛṣṭa ra  tathāpi tat a  sādhanāya iti nāsti ra  pramā
tārthamāyā ra  pāṭho'spaṣṭa a  kaṃ ra  madhyamo vikṣipta ra  pāṭho'spaṣṭa a   supa
nāma ra   mavisamvādaka ra  praṇati ra  dṛṣṭaṃ parvatayā ra  bādhe ca a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'nvayādhikāra
golakavadanantasvabhāvaparikaritasyābhāsaprasaṅgāt  na cānupalabhyatvameṣāmabhidhātu
śakyam pradīpasvabhāvatve'nupalabhyatāyā virodhāt  yadi ca pradīpasvabhāvatve'pya
dṛśyatvaṃ viruddhamanurudhyase vartivikārakāraṇatve'pi jvālādihetutāṃ kiṃ na saṃbhāvayasi
yataḥ svarūparāśiṃparikalpanavyagro'si  tasmānnānupalabhyamānasya pradīpasvabhāvatā 
a upalabhyatve ca nādhyakṣādhikṣepaparihāraḥ  dīpādanyadeva dṛśyama dṛśyaṃ vā
vastu dīpasvabhāva iti tu nāgalokabhāṣā  ananyarūpe hi svabhāvasvarūpasvalakṣaṇa
śabdāḥ prasiddhāḥ  kalpanopasthāpite tu dharme bhinna ivābhāsamāne'pi tadadhyavasāyādeva
svabhāvaśabdaprayogaḥ yathā nityatvaṃ śabdasya svabhāva iti  tato yadi sahakāriṇi 
śaktiśabdavadbhinne'pi' kvacitu svabhāvaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ tathāpi svabhāvāntareṇa karotīti
vastvantareṇa sahakāriṇā karotīti yāvat  na ca svabhāvinaḥ karaṇavāraṇamabhimatam 
tataḥ svabhāviśabdo bāhyo'rthaḥ  tena svabhāvenābhinnenaiva bhinnāni kāryāṇi karotītyā
yātam  kevalamanekasahakāriparivārita iti viśeṣaḥ  sa ca kasya neṣṭa  na ca saha
kāriṇo'pi svamanīṣikayā kalpanīyāḥ kiṃ tu yāvanto'nvayavyatireka grāhaka pramāṇa
vyāpārāstāvanta eva  sa ca vyāpāra  tejastailavartyādivyatiriktasya nāstīti kimadhika
vidhānena  pratyuta svabhāvaśabdābhidheyānarthān parikalpya ṣaṭpadārthyāmantarbhāvayan kiṃ
viphalamāyāsyasi  yadā caivaṃ paryante svabhāvaśabdābhidheyaṃ nijaṃ rūpamekamevāneka
kārya heturiti upapāditam tadā yadekena rūpeṇa janitaṃ tadekameveti na siddhā vyāptiḥ 
tathā sati prasaṅgavadviparyayasyāpi nānekāntaparihāraḥ  pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānatāpi
teṣāṃ na pradīpasyaiva tāttvikā ne kasvabhāvatayā kiṃ tu 'tatsāmagrayāmapoddhāradvāreṇānvaya
vyatirekābhyāṃ kasyacittailaṃ kasyacid vatiḥ kasyacid dīpa iti kathaṃ sarvatrotpatti
reṣāmupalabhyate 
yattu kāraṇabhedād bheda iti tatra sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇavaijātyāt kāryavajātya
nimittābhyupagamaḥ  tathaiva pramāṇenārpaṇāt  na tu sāmagrathantargatakāraṇanānātva
'mekasyānekasvabhāvatayeti śāstra eva vipañcitam  tadalameṣāṃ pramāṇanirapekṣasvotprekṣā
I
 paritasyā ra   labhyatā ra   bhāsane ra  yadiha kāriṇi ra  śabda iti
nāsti ra  svato vāśabda ra  karaṇa ca kāraṇa ra  yāvatsva a  nainaṃ ra  dheyānnijaṃ a
 pratīpa ra  taditi nāsti ra  sarvatrotpatte ra  kāraṇavaijātyamityupagamaḥ a
  mekasyaivāneka ra jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
mātreṇa vikalpeṣu nirbandhena  na ca taiḥ svabhāvabhedairbhāvikaḥ siddharapyeṣāṃ kācidartha
siddhirityuktamevetyaphala evaiṣa bhāvaḥ 
yathā tarhi trilocanaścaryayati tathānayorapi nīyatāmabhiprāyaḥ  tathā
ca nyāyamañjarī asādhāraṇamapi sattvaṃ mādhyamikanyāyena śakyamudbhāvayitum 
tathā hi kṣaṇavāde'pi pūrvarūpakṣaṇo yena sva bhāvenānantarakṣaṇamutpādayati 
kiṃ tenaiva rasakṣaṇamapyāhosvit svabhāvāntareṇa  yadi tenaiva rasasyāpi rūpatvaprasaṅgaḥ 
na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāma viśvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt  atha sva
bhāvāntareṇa karoti'  yadyevamekasya viruddhaṃ svabhāvadvayaṃ prasajyeta ' rūpajanana
svabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvāntāvyabhicārī'  tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavet
bhavettatraiva tasya bhāvo'bhāvaśca  bhāvābhāvau ca sākṣādviruddhau pūrvakaṃ rūpalakṣaṇaṃ
bhintaḥ  na ca bhinno dṛśyate saḥ 
syādetat  pūrvakasya rūpakṣaṇasya rase kartavye svabhāvāntaraṃ pūrvaka beva
rasakṣaṇo 'na ca viruddhaṃ svabhāvāntaramastīti  yadyevamakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu kārya
vyaktiṣu svabhāvāntaraṃ kramavat sahakāryantarameveti sarva samānamanyatrābhiniveśāt 
tasmādasādhāraṇamupādadānasya svabhāvabhedāpatteḥ kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvam  yena
ca prakāreṇa svabhāvabhedo nirākriyate tasyākṣaṇikatve'pi samānatvāt sattvamakṣa
ṇikānta nivartate  ato vyatirekāsiddheḥ pratibandhāsiddhiriti 
tatra tāvad yogācāraniṣṭhāmanālocayannayaṃ saugatasamayajñānābhimānī mādhyamika
nyāyenetyāha  ubhayorapi hetuphalāpavādasya tatvato'bhimatatvādityadharasiddhimuddhaya
sākārasiddhī darśitameva sthite ca hetuphalabhāve'smākamiyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅga cintetyuktam 
sā ca sthiti grāhakabhāvasya tāttvikatve gṛhīte  tadā ca yadeva yasyānvaya
vyatirekānuvidhāyi tadeva kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca bhavatu bījākaravat  yathā ca kasyaci
dekamanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi dṛśyamānaṃ kāryaṃ tathā yadyanekamapi kasyacidekasyānvaya
 kacida a  carvayati a  tathānayorapanīya a  pūrvo ra  yena svabhāve'ntaramu
pādeyaṃ kṣaṇa ra  prasaṅgaḥ a   vāntara bhaveti ra  prasajyate ra  svabhāvāvyabhi ra
 sākṣādvirupalakṣaṇa ra  pūrvasya a  na tusva a  vyakti iti nāsti ra  cakāro
nāsti ra  tasya kṣaṇi a   raikasiddhaḥ ra  kaditya ra  hetuphalacinte a  yadā
ghara  kāraṇa cetarat bī ra  cakāro nāsti a  ekasya iti nāsti a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'nvayādhikāraḥ
vyatirekāvanuvidhīyamānamupalabhyate tadā kimanekenāpyeka kāryeṇa bhavitavyam 
paravedanāpalāpe hi ekamapyekasya kāryaṃ na syāt  anapalāpe tvanekamapi kāryamekasya
kena vāryate  ataḥ paravedanā pavādivādimatāvatāraṇena na kiñcit  grāhyagrāhakasthitau
tvekavadanekasyāpyeka kāryatānyāyaḥ samānaḥ  tatkathamekātmanā janyamānamekākārameva
bhavediti lavate 
yattūktam  nahyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇātkāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti tadatisāhasam  ki
vāna paśyati pradīpamekaṃ vikārakāriṇamandhakārahāriṇaṃ ca taraṇi vā tamaḥkamalayo
nidhanapravodhavidhāyinam  sarvadāndhakāramagno vā bhavān paśyati vā sahasramaṃśu 
mālina kāryasahasrakāriṇa  ekasvabhāvāt tu kāraṇānna kāryabheda iti samāna
sāmagrathā na kāryavaijātyamityartha  ataeva na viśvasyāhetukatvam  tasmādekasmādane 
kotpattiravirodhinīṃ kāryadvāreṇa tu rūpaṃ rūpakāraṇaṃ rasakāraṇaṃ ceti samuccayena
svabhāvadvayavyavahāraḥ  ataeva na virodhavārtā  nahi samuccaye pramāṇasiddhe virodha
gandhaḥ  vātātapayorivekasminnākāśadeśe 
yattuktam  rūpajananasvabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvatāvyabhicārīti tāvatāpi
bhedamātraṃ sidhyati na tu virodha kṛtakānityavat'  yathāhi nīlābhāvāvyabhicāri
pītaṃ na nīlaṃ bhavitumarhati na tu tanmātreṇa virodha  na hi yad yato bhidyate tadaśeṣaṃ
tena viruddhamabhidhātuṃ śakyam  virodhastu yadyapyekasmin dharmiṇi dvayorasaṃbhavayoniyamaḥ
saca kadācid vastunorekasya bhāve'nyaparyādānād dahanatuhinavat  kadāciddharmayoḥ
svabhāvenaiva ekādhiṣṭhite'tyāsaṃbhavāt bhāvābhāvavat nīlatvānīlatvavad vā tatra
yadi nīlapītadravyayorapyekabhāve'nya 'paryādānamāpādayet sthādeva a sahānava
sthānanāmā virodhaḥ  na tu tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa  bhedamātraṃ tu tāvatā  evaṃ
nīlatvapītatvayorapyabhāvavyabhicāramātreṇa bhedamātraṃ tu na tu virodha  virodhastu
nīlatvasvīkṛte' dharmaṇi svayamevānīlatvabhedasya pītatvasyābhāvāt  anyathā kṛta
katvānityatvādīnāmapi tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodhaprasaṅgāt 
atha kathamatra tadabhāvāvyabhicāra  na hi kṛtakena satā nānityena bhāvya
mityupapattirasti  yadyevaṃ rūpajanakena satā rasajanakena na bhāvyamityatrāpi kopapattiḥ 
 māni a  pyaika a  māna iti nāsti a   vidhinī a  riva kasmin ra
  svabhāvābhāvā a   taka nitva a  kasvabhāve ra  syādeva ra  svīkārāt a
 kṛtakatva a  na nityena a  katvena rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
rūpajanakatvādeveti cet  na ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇe kṣīṇatvādupapatteḥ anyayoga
vyavacchedasyāsiddhatvāt tathāhi ki rūpasya janakameva  atha rūpasyaiva janakamiti
rūpajanakam  tatra prathamapakṣe rūpaṃ pratyajanakatvasyaiva vyavacchedo na punaranyajanakatvasya
vyavacchedo vidhirveti sādhanāntaramapekṣya tenaiva virodhe vyavacchedasyaiva asiddheḥ 
dvitīye tu pakṣe anyajananakṣepa siddhirasandigdhā  kevalaṃ na tatra pramāṇavyāpāraḥ  yathā
hyekasya tannāntarīyakatvaṃ tathā dvitīyasyāpi yadi syānna doṣaḥ pradīpavat  na tu
' rūpajanakamityeva  rasajanakapratikṣepo rūpajanakatvasyāyogavyavacchedenāpi caritārtha
tvāditi na kāpyupapattiratrāpi  kevalaṃ kalpanābuddhī yathārthāntaramiva rūpajanakatvaṃ
pratibhāti tathā tadabhāvāvyabhicāri ca pṛthageva rasajanakatvamavasīyate  yataḥ pṛthak
śabdapramāṇavṛttiḥ apekṣyate tāvataiva virodhamadhyavasyati  sāvagatiḥ kṛtakatvānitya
tvayorapi na vyavasīyate kenāpi  nāpi tatra virodhābhidhānena kaścidupayogaḥ  ekatra
dharmiṇyaparaparihārārthameva hi virodhaḥ sādhyate  tad yadi virodhe'pyekadharma samparkaḥ
kṛtaṃ virodhacintayā  nīlatvānīlatvādiṣu tu prayujyate parasparaparihārātmā virodhaḥ 
nanu parasparābhāvāvyabhicārāviśeṣe'pi kathaṃ keṣāñcid dharmāṇāmeka
dharmiṇyanavasthānātmā virodha keṣāñcit punarbhedamātraṃ na virodha  uktamatra yadvayava
cchedena yasya vidhānaṃ yadvidhānena vā yasya vyavacchedo niyamena tattena pratiyoginā
viruddham  yatra neyaṃ gatiḥ tadaviruddhamityalaṃ punaḥ pariśrameṇa  tadevaṃ rūpajananarasa
jananayoḥ parasparābhāvāvyabhicāre'pi 'kṛtakatvānityatvavad bhedamātraṃ śabdapramāṇāntarā
karṣi na tu virodha iti sthitam 
yattūktam  tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavedityādi  sa tarhi nyāyaḥ kiṃ kṛtakā
nityatvābhyāṃ bibheti'  prasaṅga eva tatrāpi bhavatviti cet  nanu' parābhyupagamena
prasaṅgaḥ na ca mayedamaṅgīkṛtaṃ parasparābhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodha ekatrānavasthāna
heturiti  kiṃ tavaiṣo'bhyupagama pramāṇavṛttirvā  ubhayathā'pi na mamāparādhaḥ  b
sidhyatutarāṃ ca kṛtakatvānityādīnāṃ virodho na caivaṃ tasmātparasparāvyabhicārasya
 tathāhi iti nāsti ra  rūpajanakatva ra  rasajanakatva ra  sā ca sati ra  kṛta
katva ni ra  vyavadhīyate a   bhidhāne kaści ra  nīlatvādiṣu ra  nanva a  paravya
bhicārā ra  kṛtakatva a  vibhāti ra  eṣa ra  nanva a   mātreṇa
vyabhicāra iti nāsti ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'nvayādhikāraḥ
tādātmyaniṣedhe vyāpārāt na kṛtakatvamevānityatvam  aniṣedhe tvekasyaiva kṛtakatvasya
bhāvo'bhāvaśca syāt  yathā vastuno nīlādanīlasyāvyavacchede tasyaiva bhāvo'bhāvaśca
svīkṛtaḥ syādityucyate  nīlamiti hi tasya bhāvaḥ  anolamiti cābhāvaḥ tadabhāva 
vyāptasyānīlasya bhāvo na vyāpakaṃ tadabhāvamanākṛṣya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ bhāvābhāvayośca
virodha prasādhita evetyekardhāmaṇyanavasthānamiti yannīlaṃ tannānīlaṃ pītādivastu tathā
dharmo'pi yatkṛtakatvaṃ tannākṛtakatvamanityatvādi  yadrūpajananaṃ tannārūpajananaṃ rasajana
nādi  anyathaikatra kṛtakatvarūpajananādau  śabdapramāṇapravṛttāvanyatrānityatvarasajananādau
pramāṇāntarānapekṣāprasaṅgaḥ 
na tadādhāratve 
bhāvābhāvadoṣasya
tasmāt tādātmye bhāvo'bhāvaścaikatra syāditi doṣaḥ 
tau hi parasparaṃ bhinnau dharmo yadyekatra syātāṃ kīdṛśo doṣa 
bhedasādhanenaiva caritārthatvāt  śāstre'pi hi viruddhadharmādhyāso bheda ukto na
virodha  virodhalakṣaṇaṃ tvanyat prasiddhameva  tādātmyaniṣedho'pi viśeṣaṇānapekṣa
svabhāvānupalambhādukko na viruddhopalambhāt  tadevaṃ bhāvābhāvalakṣaṇaviruddhadharma
saṃsargāt taddhamitvena bhāsamānau dharmāveva bhinnau bhavata iti na tayorapi dharmivastuno
rnānādharmayogamātreṇa bhedavārtā  yadā punastathā bhidyamānāveva dharmo yathoktaparaspara
pratidvandvinau bhavatastadā taddharmiṇo'pi bhedaḥ 'nīlatvānīlatvabhāvābhāvadharmivat
ekakārya prati 'jananājananavacca  tasmād bhāvābhāvau sākṣād viruddhau rūpajanakatva
rasajanakatvalakṣaṇau dharmāveva svardhāmitvenābhāsamānau bhinta   na tayorapyādhāraṃ
' prācīna virūpalakṣaṇam svayaṃ virodhābhāvāt  ata eva na bhinnau dṛśyate saḥ
ekakāryajanakājanakatve ca svayaṃ pratyanīkatayā svadharmiṇaṃ bhinta eva abhedadarśanaṃ ca
pratyanīkāvasāyena virodhī yata iti anumānavṛttiśceti sarvamanavadyam 
ayaṃ tu svayameva na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti na ca bhinno
dṛśyate sa iti ca bruvannasvastha eva na nirbandhayogyaḥ  tasmānnaikasvabhāvāyāḥ sāmagrayāḥ
kāryavejātyamityavirodhaḥ  na tu svabhāvaparamparārahitāditi  tadevaṃ svabhāvasandehā
 nīlatvasya ra  bhāvena a  pramāṇavṛttā ra  tadātma ra  nānādharmayonama ra
 nīlatvā nāsti a  ekakāryajananā ra  bhinna ra  prācīnarūpa ra  nakāro
nāsti a  dharmaṇiṣṭhinta    ra
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
pohā yaduktam kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvamasādhāraṇamupā dadānasya svabhāva
bhedāpattiriti tannirastam 
kālpanika iva bhedapratibhāso na tāttviko bhedaḥ  kiṃ ca tāttvikasvabhāvabhedā
pattāvapi sattvamasādhāraṇamiti śraddhāvadheyameva  na hi vastūnāṃ parimāṇātirekeṇa
nityādiva kṣaṇikādapi vyāvṛttaṃ bhavati sattvam yato'sādhāraṇamavadhāryeta  svabhāva
bhūmani kaścinnityo'pi syāditi cet  ' tamanupatattaha sattvaṃ ' a sādhāraṇa
manaikāntikamāśaṅkayatām  tacca cintyam  bādhakānāṃ vyāttavadanānāṃ saṃbhavāt 
atha svabhāvaparamparāsaṃbhave bhāvasyeva paribhavāt kasya kṣaṇikatvamiti kṣaṇi
kādapi vyāvṛttamucyate tadapi nāsti  svayameva svabhāvebhyo bhinnasya svabhāvinaḥ
kriyāsamarthana rakṣāvidhānāt  na ca svabhāvabhedasaṃbhave mūlasya kṣayo'pi yuktaḥ
aparimitopādhisaṃbhave'pi tadvato vyayāniṣṭaḥ  asmadarśane'pi yadi nāma vastva
ntararāśerudayaḥ tathāpi prakṛtabhāvasya kīdṛśī kṣayopapattiriti vyaktametat  sa tu
rāśi pramāṇamanviyānnaveti cintyam  bhavatu vā mūlāpalāpaḥ  ye tu svabhāvā
bhāvikā iṣṭāḥ tadātmani magnatvānmūlasyaikaṃ pṛthak sat kṣaṇikaṃ mā bhūt  bhūyāṃsastu
kṣaṇikāḥ santa ityupacaya eva kṣaṇikatāyā   kathaṃ kṣaṇikatāyāḥ sattvavyāvṛttiḥ 
tadevamevaṃvidhāḥ pralāpā grāmjanajanitamahimānasteṣveva śobhante na tarkakarkaśa 
kuśāgrīya buddhiṣu bauddheṣu  yā tu śikṣā svabhāvabhedasādhanāya syādetaditvādi saiṣā
mevāstu anyo'nyasya svabhāva iti svasthasya vaktumaśakteḥ  svabhāvabhedastu sādhanā
saṃbhavādadhyakṣabādhanācca parihṛta eva  na ca bhavannapi prakṛtadoṣasaṃsparśī nāpi
sahakāryantarameva svabhāvāntaramiti dantaniṣkoṣikayā' svabhāvabhedasādhanā hetavo
viparyāsayituṃ śakyante  kṣaṇikavādī hi sahakāriṇa paśyanneva ' prasiddhasvabhāvabheda
sādhanāya sādhanamupanṣasya na kathamapyanena vacasā pratārayituṃ śakyaḥ  tadvaraṃ tatsādhanama
sādhanameveti mukhyamākhyāyatāniṣṭasiddhavyāghātāditi 
 sandeho mohād ra  sattvena ca vastu na vastu dharmiṇāmasā a  tattva ra  tanna ra
 sattvamiti nāsti a  sū    nyasya ra   rāśi ra   rivyakta a  pramāṇe
manvi ra  kṣaṇitāyāḥ a  jana iti nāsti ra  tyādi ra  svabhāvakābhi     bheda

na tarhi bījaṃ tadapekṣaṃ kṣityādīnāṃ janakam tadanapekṣatve teṣāmaṅkarād bhedānupapatteḥ  na
cānupakārakā apekṣanta iti tvayevoktam  na ca kṣaṇasyopakārasaṃbhavo'nyatra jananāt

ca tadvyāpakayorekatvānekatvayoḥ sāpekṣatvānapekṣa vayoḥ prakārayorabhāvāt uktena krameṇa
sattvaṃ nivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikā ntā davyabhicāriṇo liṅgasyānupadarśanādupadarśayitu
maśakyatvācca  bādhakasyaiva vidyamānatvāt  tasmānnāniṣṭamātraghoṣaṇena kiñcit 
 etena nopakāro'pekṣārtha ityanapekṣaiva kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣu nobhayavyāvṛtiḥ 
atha saṃbhūyakaraṇamapekṣārtha  tadapi yadi pūrvasthitasyeti viśeṣaṇāpekṣā tadāpi

rūpāntareṇa taditareṣāṃ janakam  tathā hi bījamakaraṃ janayadupādānam tadvikriyayā
tadutpatteḥ  taditareṣu punarasya sahakāripratyayatā teṣāṃ tu pūrve pavanādayo yathā svamupā
dānāni tadvikriyayā tadutpādāditi cet  nanu sahakāritopādānate kimekaṃ tattvaṃ

 kathaṃ bījasya na nānātvam bhinnatādātmyāt  etayorvekatvamekatādātmyāt

bhedānupapatteḥ  na cānupakārakāriṇo'pekṣanta iti tvayaivoktam  na ca kṣaṇasyopakāra

sāmagrayā bhinnameva kāryaṃ bhavatīti etādṛśameva kāraṇabhedānuvidhānaṃ kāryasya

pakṣastu pratikṣipta evāsmābhiriti na taddūṣaṇaparamparāyāḥ parihārābhiyogaḥ  etacca

bhāvāt

ca
bhāvāt viparyayaparyavasāyitāvirahācca  tadāhi na ca taddeśatvamatastatkāryatva
mapi nāstīti syāt na caivaṃ śakyam  śakyatve'pi nāsmākaṃ mūlaprasaṅgayoḥ kṣatiḥ 
na coktadoṣaḥ yato jananasāmarthyamanyadā paropagamamātreṇaiva na pramāṇāt  viparyaye
