kramākramābhyāmarthakriyāśaktervyāptireveti 
yadapi trilocanaḥ kaścit sahakāripratyayaḥ pratyakṣa  parokṣaścetaraḥ  a tataḥ
pratyakṣaparokṣasahakāripratyayasākalyamasarvavidā pratyakṣato na śakyaṃ pratyetum  tathā ca
sati sādṛśasahakāripratyayasākalyavataḥ kramayogapadyasyātyanta parokṣatvāt tena vyāptaṃ
sattvamapi parokṣameveti kathaṃ pratibandha  pratyakṣeṇa sidhyatītyāha tadapi nirupayogam 
kāryadharmo hi kramākramau pratipāditau  tataḥ kāraṇasāmagrayāḥ sākalyāsākalyaniścayā
bhāve'pi kramayogapadyaniyama kāryāṇāmadhyakṣagocara eva  ekadaiva kāryotpattiranya
dāpi neti kathamagocara  pratyakṣasya  tadāpi ' hi kāryamekamanekaṃ vā syāt  pratyakṣeṇa
vā tathā gṛhītamanekasaṃbhave'pi caiṃka gṛhītamastu sarvathā kramākramābhyāmeva vyāptā
kāryaniṣpatiriti siddhametat 
nanu kṣaṇabhaṅgapakṣe nārthaṃkriyāpratītiḥ nāpi kramākramapratītiriti kathaṃ vyāpti
vyavasthā  tathā ca śaṅkaraḥ kṣaṇikatve sati sarvasaṃvittīnāṃ svabhāvaniyamena hetuphalayoḥ
svarūpānvayavyatirekāsiddhau sarvatra tadbhāvasyāvagantumaśakyatvāt na hi kārya
saṃvittyā tasya hetubhāve bhāvaḥ pratīyate tadā tasya hetoratītatvāt  nāpi hetusaṃvittyā
 niṣṭhāvipūrvāt a  sayordharmo'nu ra  kathañca ni ra  dūṣitvā ra  prakāreṇeti
nāsti a  sasidvamida ra  kramāthita a  vādinā śakyaṃ ra  tātmikā ra
 sahakārivataḥ ra  parokṣeṇa a  madhyago ra  ti anya a  tadapi ra
 sarvadā ra  sarvatra aśakyatvāditi nāsti ra  na ca a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāra
kāryasya tadbhāve bhāvo'vasīyate tadā tasyānupapattereva na cātītānāgatayovaṃtaṃ
mānena siddhiratiprasaṅgāt  nāpi kāryaṃsaṃvityaiva hetusvabhāvasaṃvittiḥ adṛṣṭānvaya
vyatirekasyāpi dhūme'gnijanya
tvaviniścayaprasaṅa gāt  etena hetumātrasaṃvittyāṃ kārya
saṃvittirapāstā  hetuvyatireke tu kāryavyatirekaḥ svasaṃvittivādino manorathasyāpya
viṣayaḥ tasya hetvabhāve kāryābhāvapratipattāvupāyāsaṃbhavāt  nahi tacca nāsti tena ca
pratipattiriti nyāyyam  tadayaṃ kāryasya hetusadbhāve bhāvaṃ tadabhāve cābhāvaṃ pratipadya
māno'vasthitaṃ ' pratisandhātāraṃ prasādhayatīti  evaṃ ca yadyavasthikartṛsiddhiḥ tadā
sādharaṇānekānta eva maula ' sattvahetuḥ kimatra viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsaḥ
kariṣyati  tadaniṣṭī tu vyāptigrahānupapatteḥ sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamubhayorapi 
yathā ca kramiṇī hetuphale pratyetumaśakye evaṃ phale apīti na kramapratītiḥ nāpi yauga
padyasya 
yathāha sa eva nāpi' yaugapadyasya bhinnākāreṇa jñānena pratiniyatākārāṇāṃ
yaugapadyasthāśakyasādhanatvāt  na tāvadbhireva jñāne yaugapadyaṃ pratyetavyam teṣāmitare
tarāsaṃvedyatve santānāntaravat yugapadbhāvasyāsiddheḥ  na caikamanekākāram svabhāva
bhūtākārabhede bhedasyāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāt  bhede tu vijñānasyākārebhyo'rthāntaratvaprasaṅge
na viṣayasya tadākāratvaṃ samarthitaṃ bhaviṣyatīti 
atrocyate pratisandhātṛsvīkārastāvadasaṃbaddhaḥ  pratisandheyābhimatā bhirbuddhibhirbhedā
bhedavikalpākṣamatvāt abhede b hi sa eva vā syād buddhaya eva vā  atra
ca prathamapakṣe karmaṇaḥ pakṣāntare ' karturabhāvāt kaḥ pratisandhānārtha  bhede'pi buddhibhyo
bhidyamānasya jaḍasya kaḥ pratisandhānārtha  buddhiyogād draṣṭavat pratisandhātṛtvamiti
cet  buddhireva tarhi draṣṭrī pratisandhātrī ceti niyatasvīkāre tadyogādanyasya
tathātvamiti kimanena yācitakamaṇḍanena  buddhīnāṃ kartṛtvābhāvāditi cet  tad
dvāreṇāpi tarhi tasyātmano draṣṭṛtvādivyavahārānupapatti  yadi hi buddhirhetoḥ phalasya
vā draṣṭrī syāt tadānantaryapratiniyamasya cānusandhātrī kalpikā tadyogāttasya draṣṭṛtvaṃ
 avasīyate  vartamānena siddhiriti bhāga patita ra  etena hetu vyatireke iti bhāga
patitaḥ ra  sveti nāsti ra  tacca
 bhāvaṃ ta iti nāsti ra  pratī a  maula iti
nāsti ra  panyāsaḥ niṣṭhāviti nāsti  nāsti ra sya śakya ra  ntara eva ra
 yugapada manekā iti nāsti ra  tad bhedasyā ra  atra saṃbaddhaḥ iti nāsti ra
 bhāvāt buddhi iti nāsti ra  kimanena maṇḍaneneti nāsti ra
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
pratisandhātṛtvaṃ vocyata iti syādapi  prativiṣayamalabdhaviśeṣāyāṃ ca buddhau saṃbandho'pi
na viśeṣa vyavahārayitumīśaḥ adhunā nibandhanādhigantā adhunā phalasya idānīṃ
pratisandhāteti  tathāvidhabuddhigata viśeṣasvīkāre tu kimapareṇa kartavyam tāvataiva
paryāptatvād vyavahārasya  sthirātmānamantareṇa  saiva buddhirna syāditi cet 
kenaivaṃ pratārito'si  aho mohamāhātmyaṃ yadīdṛśānapi paravaśīkaroti 
tathāhi nedamidamantareṇeti yaducyate tat khalvanyatra pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ sāmarthyāva
dhāraṇe sati yujyate vahnariva dhūme cakṣurādivad vā dṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagra kāryādarśane
paścād darśane ca kiñcidanyadapekṣaṇīyamastīti sāmānyākāreṇa  ādyaḥ pakṣastāvannā
stīti vyaktam  dvitīyo'pi na saṃbhavī  nahi kāraṇabuddhisamanantaraṃ kāryabuddhau satyāṃ
niścayapravṛttasya idamasthānantaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mayeti pratisandhānamadṛṣṭapūrvaṃ kadācid yato'nyasya
sāmarthyaparikalpanaṃ syāt  evaṃ smaraṇamapyanubhavāt kutaścit paramparayā śaktipariṇāma
dvāreṇa kutaścit sākṣāt tat paripākabalāditi 
ra anyasyānubhave tarhi kathamanyasya na smṛtiḥ 
anyasyeti na saṃbandhī siddhaśrodyaṃ kimīdṛśam 
anubhavādibhyo bhinnasaṃbandhisiddhayadhikaraṇavivādaprakrame tameva siddhamāsthāya
paryanuyoga ityasaṃbaddhametat  tatsiddhau hi vivādaparyavasānāt kā parāpekṣā  tasmādanya
syeti vivādapadatvādapanīyānubhave kathaṃ na smṛtiriti pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na prakṛtopayogi 
evaṃ tu yujyate codyārthaḥ yaddehasaṃbaddho'nubhavastadanyatra dehe kasmānna smṛterudaya iti 
evaṃ ca vadatā yatkṣetrasambandhi bījaṃ tadanyatra kṣetre kiṃ nāṅkurajanmetyuktaṃ bhavati  sa ca
kutastyo nyāyaḥ 
nanu kāryakāraṇabhāvamātrādanubhavasmaraṇayorna kācidaparā pratyāsattiḥ na ca
kāryakāraṇabhāve'ya niyamo yadādhārameva kāraṇaṃ tadādhārameva kāryamiti viṣayādatyanta
dūre'pi jñānakāryadarśanāt  evaṃ tarhi nāṅkarasthāpi kāryatāmātrādaparā pratyāsattiriti
jñānamivāra dūre'pi bījaṃ janayet  nanu bījārambhiṇa a eva paramāṇavaḥ
kecidaṅṅkure samavādhikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyamānāḥ kathaṃ kṣetrāntare'ṅkuramutpādayitumīśate 
 kimapi pareṇa ra   nantareṇa ra  ṇaiveti ra  sāmagrayo ra  anyanyā a
asyā ra   siddhādhi a  parīti nāsti ra  sambandhe a  vapatā a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥ
bhavatastu' tathāvidhapratyāsattivirahāt  vijñānādinā sādhāraṇaṃ kāryatvamasyeti dūre'pi
jananaprasaṅgo'nivāryaṃ iti cet  kasmāt punaraṅkura eva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāya
kāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante na jñānādau kāryatvena sarveṣāmekarasatvāt  tataḥ sarveṣāmaṅṅkuravat
taddeśa eva jananaṃ jñānādivad vāṅkarasyāpi dūre jananaṃ kāryatvenāviśeṣāt'
tadvadevāṅkure'pi nimittakāraṇatvād bījasya 
ekatra
santānavyavasthānamanyatra
nanu yatraiva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāyikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante sa evāṅṅkuraḥ
tat kathamaṅkurādanyatra teṣāṃ samavāyikāraṇatā codyate  evaṃ tarhi kāryatvenaikarasatayā
samavāyikāraṇatāyā duṣpariharatvādakaraikarūpatvaṃ sarveṣāmekadeśatā ca prasahyāyāteti
sthāne phalitaṃ parihārapratyāśayā  yadi ca kāryatvena sarveṣāmaviśeṣaḥ kāryāṇām
kāraṇānāmapi sarveṣāṃ kāraṇatvenāviśeṣa iti viśvasya vaicitryamatrāṇam 
tasmātkāryatve satyapi na rītirekaiva sarveṣāmiti  yathā  nisargabhedāt kacit kiñcit
samavāyikāraṇatvena kacidasamavāyikāraṇatvena kacinnimittakāraṇatvenopayujyate
bhavataḥ tathāsmākamapi kiñcit kāryaṃ samānadeśameva heturutpādayati kiñcid vyavahita 
deśam kāryaṃ ca kiñcinniyamena hetudeśa evotpattidharmakaṃ kiñcidanyathā  tathaikatra kārye
pratyabhijñāsaṃbhavo nānyatra kāryatvāviśeṣe'pi dīpāntaravat jñānavacca'  tādṛk kāryā
tatropādānakāraṇavyavahāro'smāka
pekṣayā ca yatra bhavataḥ samavāyikāraṇavyavasthā
mātmāderanyatra  tathāvidhahetuphalaparamparāyāṃ ca
sahakāritvamātramiti prakriyābhede'pi kāryadvaitaṃ tādṛg 'nisargasiddhamastīti bhavato'pya
śakyamatikramitumiti sthitametat  tathābhūtabhedasaṃbhave ca yatkāryakaraṇādhikaraṇa
evotpattidharmakaṃ tatkathamitaratrotpadyate  kāraṇaṃ vā svādhikaraṇa eva śakyotpādanaṃ kāryaṃ
kathamanyatra janayet  tadayamanubhavo'pi svādhikaraṇajanyaṃ smaraṇamaṅkuramiva bījātra
kathamanyatrotpādayet  smṛtirvānubhavādhikaraṇaniyatotpattiraṅṅkuravat kathamanyatrotpadyeta
yato dehāntare smaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ codyamavakāśamāsādayet  ātmavāde tu duṣpariha rametatu
vyāpinastasya tenaiva smṛtijananarūpeṇa dehāntare'pi sthānāt  adṛṣṭāśrayaṇaṃ ca nitya
syaiveti bījāṅkuravadanubhavasmaraṇayornyāyo nānyavaditi kathamavagantavyamiti cet 
 viti nāsti a  kāryatve viśe a  kāraṇaṃ ra  deśabhāva    a  prasajyā  ra
 sarveṣāṃ savi ra  mātrāṇaṃ a  tathā ra  kiñciditi nāsti a  kvacidasamavāya
kāraṇatveneti nāsti a  tatraikatra ra  tvāna  la  vacca ra  tathāvidhaphala a  nisiddha ra
  kārya kāraṇā ra  bījātmā ra  smaraṇanyāyo rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalī
bījāṅkurayorapi sa nyāyastathā darśanādevāvasīyate  tathā niyamadarśanaṃ cānubhavasmaraṇayo
rapyasti na hyanyadehe'nubhavavati' b anyamūrtiḥ smṛtimatī nāma 
nanu dehaḥ kathamanubhavavān  tadādhāratayā tatkāraṇatayā tena saha samānakāraṇatayā
vā saṃbandhavivakṣāstīti na kṣatiḥ  kiṃ cātmano'pi kathamanubhavavattvam  samavāya
balāditi cet  nanu samavāyo'pīheti buddhiheturiṣyamāṇa ihetibuddhinibandhanakalpana
eva  asti ceha śarīre buddhiḥ ataḥ kiṃ na samavāyakalpanāpi  ayutasiddha
tvābhāvāt śarīrabuddhayoḥ pṛthageva pratīyamānatvāditi cet  nanu pṛthakpratīyamānayoriheda
miti pratītiniyama uparyaṃdhobhāvena hi bhāvadvaye paridṛśyamāne parasparāsaṅkareṇa
saptamīprathama yonirdeśa upapadyeta yadā tu pṛthagdarśanameva nāsti tadā kathamihedamiti
bhedena nirdiśan prekṣāvattāyā na hīyate  samavāyaviṣaye kacidapi bhedasyādṛṣṭeriti
cet  ataeva svayamiheti buddhi vikalpamātratvena icchayā 'nirvartanayogyāmutpādya
samavāyo nāma kalpyate 
iheti buddheḥ samavāyasiddhirihetidhīśca dvayadarśane syāt 
na ca kacittadviṣaye dvayekṣā svakalpanāmātramato'bhyupāyaḥ 
tena cāsaṃvidyamānasyaivātmano buddhimattāvyavahāra iti bandhyāputreṇa turagaśṛṅgasya
kholighaṭanavṛttāntamanuharati  yat khalu yāvatopayogena kalpitaṃ tāvata upayogasya
anyena siddhireva tasyābhāvaḥ siddhaścātmano'pi smṛtyādhupayogo'nyatheti  tasmāt naika
kāyastho'nubhavaḥ kāyāntare smaraṇakaraṇāya prabhavati 
nanu kṣaṇikatve dehāntara eva smṛterudayāt kathamidaṃ śakyaparihāram janmāntara
parigrahe vā tataḥ santānāntaratvenābhimate'pi dehe kiṃ na prasaṅgo'nyatvasthāviśeṣāditi
cet  īdṛśaṃ dehāntaraṃ smṛtijananamātmano'pi duṣpariharam tato'nyatrāpi tatpra
saṅgo'nyatvasyāviśeṣāditi samānam  yadyapi ca kāyasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ neṣṭam āśu
nāśitvaṃ punastairiṣṭameva tataḥ samāno doṣo yadbhayādātmavādasvīkāraḥ  athātmavāde
tasyātmanaḥ karmaṇābhisaṃskṛta eva dehe smṛtijananamiti na doṣaḥ nairātmyavāde tu kasya
tat karma  śārīrātiriktā hi buddhireva kṣaṇikā saṃbhavati  ataeva ca na kartṛkṣaṇasya
  darśanādavasī ra  bhavati a  buddhivataḥ ra  vipakṣe ra  syāpi dṛ a
 icchāni a  nivarttamāna a  vā ra  syāravīṇi ra  vyogina a
 kāryakṣaṇi ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥ
tatkarmasukhaduḥkhādi saṃvartanīyam tasya tadupabhogābhāvāt  yasya ca kṣaṇasyopabhogaḥ
so'karteti kṛtanāśākṛtābhyāgamadoṣastvatirikto bhavatu na tu kasyacit karmasiddhiryataḥ
'prakṛtadoṣa parihāra syāt  na ca santāno'pi gīyamāno bhinnaḥ kaścidasti  na ca
karmāṇi bhinnaṃ bhavatāmastītyabhitti citrakarmaṃ 
tatrādyād
atrocyate  kartṛkṣaṇasya tāvat tatkarma tatphalopabhogābhāve'pi nāpaham 
nahi 'dāhādikamakurvato atpāditena vahninā tadvān na bhavati naraḥ  antima
kṣaṇasyāpi tatkarmopakārakatayā saṃbadhyate paramparayā tata evopabhogabhāgitvāt 
ekakālatā tu kāryakāraṇayorapi na saṃbhavati saṃbhavati ca merumandarayoḥ  tasmādupa
kāradvārakameva ' bhede tasyedamiti ghaṭanam sa copakāro'ntimasya tatkṛto mahānasti
tanmadhyavartināṃ ca tatsantānavartināṃ kṣaṇānāṃ tādṛgantimakṣaṇaprasūtisāmarthya sākṣātparaṃ
parayā vā utata eva karmaṇa ityupakāradvāraka eva teṣāmapi tatsambandhaḥ  evaṃ ca
sarveṣāṃ karmasambandhavyavasthitau sthitāyāṃ tatkarmādhipatyenopanīyamāna eva śarīre
tatkarmābhisaṃbhūtānāṃ buddhidehakṣaṇānāmudayaḥ nānyatra tādṛk pratyāsatterabhāvāt  karma
ca kāmaṃ na bhinnamasti vyatirekīva  ca nirdeśo'pi vyavahārānurodhena  yastu prāktanaḥ
karmasaṃbaddha ityucyate kṣaṇaḥ sa tādṛg viśeṣabhūto jātaḥ yataḥ payaṃnte tatphalopa
bhoktṛkṣaṇaprasavasamarthasantānasaṃbhavaḥ tadanurūpaśarīrasantatisaṃbhavaśva 
viśiṣṭād yau buddhidehakṣaṇau alpatamaviśeṣayogināvupajātau saṃbhūyottarāvalpatara
viśeṣau ' janayataḥ tau cālpaviśeṣāvuttarī janayata ityanayā diśā tāvacchattilakṣaṇa
viśeṣaprakarṣastaratamādibhāvenopacīyate yāvadantimajananasamarthodayastato'ntima iti 
ekasāmagracadhonatayā parasparānubaddhayorbuddhidehayoranyaparamparāṃ prati viśiṣṭayornaikavyati
rekeṇa dvaitīyikaśāvakāśaḥ  janmāntaraparigrahe'pi tadāyuḥ saṃskārakṣīṇe kṣīyamāṇa
mūrtikṣaṇāntarasahakāriṇā manaḥkṣaṇena janitaṃ tasyānurūpaṃ vapuranyat pūrvavanmanasaḥ
sāhāyakamātanotīti na dehāntare smṛtibhoktṛtvacintāvakāśaḥ  na cātra santānanāmnā
bhinnena kiñcit kṣaṇānāṃ karmasaṃbandhasiddhidvāreṇaiva santāne'pi siddherapratibandhāt
 gābhāvāt
 syopabho iti nāsti ra  na tviti nāsti ra  yataḥ yataḥ ra   karma
kurva ra  parasparapāta ra  vvakāraka ra  codakārontimasyā ra  tadeva a  nāpa
nīyamānaṃ ra  saṃskṛtānāṃ ra  nuro iti nāsti ra  bhūṣitā a  santāna iti nāsti ra
 aṇutama ra
 yogiṇā a ra  vaṇutra ra  cāṇuvi ra  kṣīṇe iti nāsti ra
 janitasyā a  siddha prati ra
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
tebhyastasya vyatirekāt  na ca mukhyataḥ santānadvāreṇa siddhāntopakramaḥ kiṃ tu
kṣaṇadvāreṇeti sarvamavadātaṃ mūlapariśodhanāditi 
yaduktam
yasminneva hi santāne āhitā karmavāsanā 
phalaṃ tatraiva badhnāti karpāse raktatā yathā 
iti tat svābhimatasantānalakṣaṇaprasiddhau 
yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇakāra etad dūṣayānnāha  na sādhanadūṣaṇāsaṃbhavāt anvayādya
bhāvānna sādhanam  na hi kāryakāraṇabhāvāt smṛtiḥ karpāse raktatādivadityanvayaḥ
saṃbhavati  nāpi yatra na smṛtiḥ tatra na kāryakāraṇabhāva iti vyatireko'sti  asiddha
tvādyanudbhāvanānna dūṣaṇam  na hi pūrvabuddhadhanubhūte'rthe uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtiḥ saṃbhavati
tato'nyatvāt santānāntarabuddhivadityasya hetoḥ karpāse raktatāvadityanena na kaściddoṣaḥ
pratipādyata b iti  'tadasamīkṣyābhidhānam sādhanārthāparijñānāt  na hīha
iloke kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ smṛtau hetutvenopanyastaḥ pratīyate  kiṃ tarhi  karmavāsanā 
vāsanā hi karmaṇābhisaṃskāra   vasitaṃ hyabhisaṃskṛtamucyate  karmakṛto viśeṣo yatra
santāne utpāditastatraiva bhogādiphalabandho nānyatra  yatra nāsau viśeṣa iti pratijñāya
karpāse raktatā yathā iti vadataḥ saṃskārasantānabhedo vā heturabhipretaḥ sādhyaṃ
cānyatra  bhogādiphalaniṣedhaḥ tatsantāne tatphalayogyatā ca pratīyate  tadayaṃ prayogaḥ
yo yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kacitsantāne āhitaḥ sa tatraiva phaladānayogyo nānyatra  yathā

kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥ
siddheḥ' dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭenāpi hi pramāṇabalāvalambinī vyāptiḥ siddhayati  adṛṣṭena tu
tatsidviśaṅkāpi nāsti  tasmānna sarvātmanā sādhāraṇo dṛṣṭānta iti vārtāyāmapi 
sādhyasādhanābhyāṃ sādhāraṇastāvadavaśyakartavyaḥ  na hi vyāptipradarśanādanyo dṛṣṭāntasya
na caikāvayavi
arthaḥ na cānupadarśitena dṛṣṭānte sādhyena vyāptisādhanamādarśitaṃ bhavati 
siddhayā sādhyaśūnyatāparihāro hārī  śarīrabuddhayādirāśitayā nartakyā'vayavitvā
bhāvāt  śarīrāpekṣayā svavayavidūṣaṇameva jāgati  ātmāpekṣāyāṃ tu so'dyāpi na
sidhyati viparyayabādhakābhāvāñca nānekāntaśāntiḥ  mameti pratisandhānaṃ hi vikalpatayā
anādyavidyāvaśādapi pratyabhijñānavat 'saṃbhavatkathamekasaṃbandhādhīnatāṃ' svīkuryāditi 
tadevaṃ yathāsmṛti karmaphalasaṃbandhādikamaśeṣamavasthātāramantareṇāpi na vipatti
māsādayati' kṣaṇikavādinaḥ tathā kāryakāraṇabhāvabuddhirapīti na sādhāraṇānekānta
śaṅkākalaṅkaḥ 
śaṅkarastu vācāṭatayā kimapi nāṭayati  tathā hi kadācidupalambhapūrvikā
dhūmabuddhiḥ tejaḥkāryamidaṃ kapotakaṇṭhadhūsaraṃ vastviti niścayamutpādayati kadācit
tadubhayopalambhapūrvakastadanupalambhaḥ  anupalambho'pi pratiyogivastūpalambhasvabhāvatayā
adhyakṣarūpa eva anvayaḥ punaranupalabdhiniṣṭhāyāṃ vihita iti tatraivāvadhāryaḥ  anvaya
vyatirekagrāhakapratyakṣānupalambhanītirapi trikapañcakacintāyāṃ darśitetyāstāṃ tāvat
prakṛtaṃ tū brūmaḥ  ubhayathāpi kramabhāvinīṣu buddhiṣu b pūrvapūrvayā saṃskāra
viśeṣādhānādantimā buddhiretasyedaṃ kāryamiti matimutpādayitu pūrvavannivahatīti
nāvasthitasyānurodha pratisandhātuḥ 
yatpunaruktam vyatireko manorathasyāpyaviṣaya iti tadatisāhasam  nahi yade
pratyakṣa vastugrāhi vastudvayanivṛttau tadeva tayorvyatirekamapi gṛhṇātītyucyate ki tu
tadviviktapratiyogivastūpalambhasvabhāvaṃ pratyakṣāntarameva  tato yaduktaṃ tacca nāsti tena ca
pratipattiriti na nyāyyamiti kopayujyate  na caivaṃ svasaṃvittivādopalambhasaṃgatiḥ 
yadapyuktaṃ pūrvottarayo ' kṣaṇayoḥ saṃvittī tābhyāṃ vāsanā tathā hetuphalādhyavasāyī
 nupadarśa ra  masi ra  preti nāsti ra  cānekānta ra  sambhavamatra kathaṃ ra

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
vikalpa iti cet  tat kimidānīṃ yatkiñcidāśaṅkitena vaktavyamityevaṃ 'vidhiranuṣṭhīyate
bhavatā  vikalpo hi gṛhītānusandhānamatadrūpasamāropo vā syāt  na tāvat pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ adṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasya puruṣasya hetuphalabhāvāgrahe'nusandhānapratyaya he torvāsanā
viśeṣasyaivānupapatteḥ  agṛhītasya cānusandhāne'tiprasaṅgāditi 
tadetanna samīcīnamālocitam  yato hetuphalabhūtapūrvottarakṣaṇayoranubhavena
kramiṇāpi svarūpasākṣātkaraṇāt hetuphalatve gṛhīte eva kevalaṃ hetukāle phalābhāvāt
tadviṣayasāmarthyagrahaṇe'pi phalādarśanāt tedavasāya evāpravṛttaḥ kāryadarśane pravartate' 
tathā phalāvalokane'pi tatkāryatā gṛhītaiva vikalpenānusandhīyata iti gṛhītānusandhāna 
rūpa evāyaṃ trikalpaḥ anvayavyatirekagrahaṇaṃ ca pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ pratipāditamiti
yatkiñcidetat 
etena tadapi pratyuktam yaduktaṃ na cādṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasya hetuphalabhāvo
vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau ca sidhyati  tatrāpi paryanuyogasyāviśeṣādanavastheti 
anvayavyatirekadarśanaṃ hi prastutaviṣayaṃ tāvadupapāditameva  vāsanāvikalpa 
yoranvayavyatirekasiddhiradhyakṣānupalambheṣvantimādevā nusandhāna vikalpapravṛtteḥ ekākinaḥ
pratyakṣādanupalambhād vā pravṛttyabhāvāt śaktisvabhāvatvād vāsanāyāḥ kāryamantareṇa
vyavasthānupapatteḥ  tathā vyavasthitāyāśca tasyāḥ svahetunānubhavenāpi sahānvayavyatireka
siddhiḥ kāryānvayavyatirekadvāreṇaiva  na cādyaṃ codyam yāvannānusandhānavikalpaḥ
tāvanna vāsanāyāṃ vāsanā hetau vānvayavyatirekasiddhiḥ yāvacca na vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau
vānvayavyatirekasiddhistāvannānusandhāna vikalpa iti  na hyanusandhānavikalpo vāsanāyāṃ
vāsanāhetī vānvayavyatirekaniścayamapekṣate api tvanubhayavāsanayoranvayavyatireka
vatyoḥ svasantāne sattāmātram tadanvayavyatirekaniścayasa canusandhāna vikalpamapekṣata
evaṃ  tatra yathā dahanendhanaavikārānvayavyatirekaniścayānapekṣastadapekṣaṇīyo dhūma
iti netaretarāśrayastathā prastute'pītyalaṃ bahubhāṣitayā 
atadrūpasamāropapakṣe tu dūṣaṇaprasaṅgāgatamaprastutatayā tadanaṅgīkāreṇāva
tāvat  tasmādavyākulā kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītirasthiratva' iti sthitam 
dhīritaṃ
 vidhe a  darśanādava a  pravṛtte ra  cakārastyaktaḥ  deṣānu ra  cānvaya ra

anyathā
tatsthitau ca kramapratītiranivāritā asmin satīdamasmādupajātamiti pratīte 
kramāvasāyanāntarīyakatvāt  siddhasādhyavibhaktiprayogasya viṣayaniyamā
nupapatteḥ  yasmāddhetuphalayorvā kramapratītiḥ phalayorveti na kaścidviśeṣaḥ kramāpekṣayā  yauga
padye śāpi nāsti aikakālikānekāvalokanānantarameva sakṛdimāni jātānīti
vikalpasya baujādivāṅṅkarasyotpatteḥ  na hi tadaneka kāryodayagrahaṇakṛtaḥ kaścidaparādho
virodho kṣaṇikatāyāḥ  kramikadarśane hi sthirāpekṣā syādapyanusandhānāyāpātataḥ
sakudarśane tu kiṃ sthireṇa  evaṃ tu syāt sakaddarśane'nantaramapi smartānyaḥ prāpnotīti
tacca parihṛtaṃ prāk  tadeva vā vādhyamastu kimadraṇakaṇḍūyāsthānīyena sākāravedanadūṣaṇo
dgīraṇena' aprastutatvāt  grahaṇaṃ cedasti sakṛdanekasya sākāreṇa nirākāreṇa vā
jñānena bhaviṣyati krimidānīmeva sakalatattvaniṣṭhāyā anuṣṭhānam  yadi tu sakṛjjāyamānā
nekagrahaṇameva ' nāstītyabhimatam tadā yathā sākāranirākaraṇaṃ tathā nirākārasthāpyastu 
anyathā tenaiva grahaṇamāśaṅkayeta' 
kiṃ cānekagrahaṇābhāvo'pi sakṛt kathamabhimataḥ  ki sakṛdanekasaṃbhavābhāvāt 
grahaṇaprakārāsaṃbhavād vā 
prathamakalpe tāvat kathaṃ pradīpasya vartivikārāndhakārakṣayādaya tadā kriyante
svayamapi  asmākaṃ punarevaṃ sati prayāsalāghavameva na kṣatiḥ nitye kramadūṣaṇenaiva
sādhyasiddheḥ 
dvitīye tu anekasaṃbhavavyavahāra kiṃkṛto'stu  anumānakṛto'stu  kiṃ tadanu
mānamiti pṛṣṭo yadi vyākaroṣi tadānumānasiddhameva yaugapadyaṃ kramasahāyamarthakriyā
vyāpakamastu kathaṃ prakṛtivirahadoṣa    atha na vyākaroṣi tāvataiva hato'si  yuga
mantaḥkaraṇasya manaso yugapadanekatra' pravṛttyasaṃbhava eva pratipadyatām
kimanena 
athānekākārāne kasaṃvedanasaṃkalayitā eka eṣitavya iti matiḥ  tataḥ kim 
sthirasvīkāro hi kramavān naḥ saṃprati pīḍayati anyathā tu vādānta rāvatāra eṣaḥ  tadvat

pramāṇasiddhaṃ syāt tadā sidhyet anyathopagamamātrasya sukaratyāgatvādanākārasvī

sthiratvāvirodhinaḥ svīkāre'pi krame'vaśyaṃ svīkāraḥ yathā bhinnadeśamabhinnasvabhāvastha
 kāryakaraṇamicchannapi na bhinnakālamicchati  tasmāt krame pratisandhātṛsvīkārārtha

kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥ
arthakriyābhedanāntarīyako hyākārabhedaḥ padārtheṣu  tatra yadyākārabhede'pi nārtha
kriyābhedaḥ hanta pratibhāsamātrabhedānnātiriktaṃ kiñciditi bāhyapadārthāpalāpa eva
prasaktaḥ  tadavaśyamanena bāhyavastuna ākārabhedābheda eva' svīkartavyo buddhibhidyatāṃ
mā vā  nahi samakakṣatāpi dhiyo'dhigantumalam  anyathā svasaṃvedanamanyaprakāśanaṃ
ca bāhyasyāpi prasajyamānaṃ grāhya grāhakabhāvameva viplāvayet  tad yadi pramāṇasiddhaṃ
buddherekatvaṃ citrākārāyāstasyā evāstu bāhyaṃ tu bhinnākāraṃ bhinnameva  bāhyamapi
bhinnākāraṃ kathaṃ bhinnamiti cet  bhavatu tribhuvanamekameva vastu kimasmākaṃ kṣīṇam 
pṛthagarthakarmaniyogādyabhāve tu na gandharvanagarādivat pratibhāsamātratāmatiśayītetyuktam 
kacidekatā kacid bheda iti vibhāgasyāpi naiṣa prastāvaḥ 
atha buddherapyekatvaṃ samayamātraṃ na pramāṇasiddham  tadānīṃ bādhavirodhī
samaya iti sa eva duṣyatu  pramāṇopanītastu prastuto vastubheda parasparavirodhāt kathaṃ
tyājya 
kiṃ ca
hato heturvakkudi samayamāśritya samaye
tavāstveṣa śreyānatha samayacintā pravadituḥ 
na vai śāstre sthitvā vacanamiti vaktuśca samayaḥ
pramāsiddhai rūpairanumitividhau nāgamaguṇaḥ 
api ca na virodhamātraṃ bhedamasmākaṃ kiṃ tu śaktāśaktatvena  taccāvaśyaṃ a
svīkāryam anyathā sādhanadūṣaṇasamarthānusaraṇavisaraṇāt paryavasito vāda iti
kimapareṇa  tasmācchaktyaśaktidvāreṇa bhedo duṣpariharaḥ  tato virodhamātrasya bheda
vyabhicāre'pi prakṛtaviśeṣasya na' vyabhicāraḥ vastumātrasya vahnivyabhicāre'pi dhūma
lakṣaṇavastvavyabhicāravat 
nanu śaktāśaktatvenāpi bhedo virodhādeva sa ca vyabhicārīti cet  dhūmo'pi
vastutvādeva heturgamako vastutvaṃ ca vyabhicārīti samānam  tasmād vastutvādeva dahanasya
 prayuktaḥ ra  ākārabheda eva ra   tābhidaṃ a  dananyā    prakā ra   citrākṣaro
yāsta ra  yathagandhakarma ra  samagramātraṃ a  duṣyate ra  varṇabhedaḥ ra   vaśyasvīkārya  a
 neti vyaktaḥ ra  lakṣaṇamba  vya bhicāravat ra  vyabhicāratvat a
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
gamako dhūma iti na  vastutvaṃ parihṛtyetyarthaḥ  na tu yāvad vastu tāvad' gamakam  evaṃ
śaktāśaktatvaṃ virodhādeva bhedasādhana miti na virodhaṃ vidhūyetyarthaḥ  na tu yāvad
virodhastāvad bhedasādhakaḥ 
āha ca
virodhaśced bhedaṃ vyabhicarati bhedapratipade
viśiṣṭo'sāviṣṭaḥ prabhavati ca śaktetaratayā 
aśakte sāmānye yadi ca viśeṣo'pi balavān
na dhūmādagnyāśā vyabhicarati yadvastu śikhinam 
virodhādevālaṃ balavadabalatvaṃ yadi bhide
na vastutvaṃ hitvā hutabhuji sa dhūmo'pi balavān 
atho vahni vastu vyabhicaratu bhedo'sya tu balī
pramāsiddhāpattiḥ prakṛtaviṣaye'pyeṣa samayaḥ 
abhede hi śaktāśaktayoḥ sakalamākulam trailokyamapravṛttinivṛttikamāsaktamiti
śaktetarayovirodho'vaśyaṃ bhedasādhaka eṣitavyaḥ ākāradvāreṇa bhavatu mā vā 
nanvākārabhedo'pi śaktibhedanāntarīka eveti kiṃkṛto vibhāga  satyam
bāhyeṣu tāvadevameva jalānalādiṣu tathaivopalabdheḥ  anyathā ca na bāhyaṃ nāma kiñcit
pratibhāsamātrāvaśeṣāt  buddhestvākārā na tāvad dāhagāhanādiṣvevopayogino bāhya
kāryatvātteṣām  yatpunaravasāyādikāryaṃ tadapyākārāntareṇa saha bhedābhedavivādārūḍha
meveti kathamekatraikavyāpāro darśitaḥ '  bhavatu vā kiñcidekamapi kāryam tatrāpi
kimapoddhāradvāreṇa ekākāravyāpārakalpanamatha bhedādeveti cintyam  na cāsmākaṃ
citrabuddherekānekatvasādhane nirbaṃndhaḥ icchāpi sākāratāmātre kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhane tu tasyāpi
na kaścidanurodhaḥ 
anāntarīyake cārthe badhite'nyasya kā kṣatiḥ

 nakāro nāsti ra  na virodha yāvad ra  śaktāśaktaṃ ra   dhiṣo    pi ra  bhe bhi  de ra

iti nyāyāt  tasmānnāpratītikṛto'rthasāmarthyasya kramākramasya ca vyāpyavyāpakabhāva
niścayaḥ 
yatpunarucyate yadi krameṇa vyāptam tadā kathamakrameṇa  athākrameṇa na tarhi
krameṇa  kramākramābhyāṃ vyāptamiti bruvatā vyāpterevābhāva  pradarśito bhavati  sā
hi vyāpyasya tatraiva bhāvo vyāpakasya tatra bhāva evetyevaṃrūpā  ubhayorvyāpakatvena sva
rūpaṃ jahāti  na hi bhavatyagnirdhūmadhūmābhāvābhyāṃ vyāpta iti  kimevaṃ vaktari vaktavyam 
'datto hi jalāñjaliramunā krameṇa sakalatārkikavartmani vartamānairātmanā b ca
anena bahudhā ' dattasya vikalpya dūṣaṇarāśeḥ  api nāmaitatprakārāṇāṃ dūṣaṇenā
sattāpratipādanāt tatprameyamasatsyāditi vikalpya dūṣaṇāni pratīyante tatprakārairavyāptau
ca dṛṣyaprameyasya teṣāmabhāve'pi nāsyābhāvaniyama iti dūṣaṇābhidhāne'pi
prāvi saṃśayaḥ tadalamupanyāsena  tatprakārāṇāmabhāve'bhāvaniyame vā sa eva
vyāptyartha iti kasya niṣedha  tathā ca santānasya vastutvamanicchan bhinno'bhinno veti
vikalpya dūṣaṇamārabhate tadubhayābhāvavibhāvane ca nirvṛṇvīteti na bhedābhedābhyāṃ
vastuvyāptimanaṅgīkurvannirvahati  evaṃ trayādivikalpeṣvapīti sthitam  tasmādekaikenā
vyāptiḥ samudāyena tu vyāptireveti nyāyaḥ  yathā yudhiṣṭhirādiṣvanyatamo'bhavan
pāṇḍava eva na bhavati  ekanivṛttau hi tadanyaprakāramāśrityāsīt tattvam  sarva
prakārābhāve tu kāstām  ato niyamavatī' nivṛttirvyāptireva 
yadapyuktam na hi bhavatyagnidhūṃmadhūmābhāvābhyāṃ vyāpta iti tadapi pāpīyaḥ 
kramākramābhyāṃ hi kāryodayavyāptivādino rāśyantaravirahavatā taddharmadvayena vyāptiḥ
prastutā tat kvedamupayujyate  na hi kramākramāviva kāryāṇāṃ vahnarapi dhūmadhūmābhāvo
dharmaḥ  svabhāva eva hi dharmiṇo dharmaśabdavācyaḥ prakṛtaḥ  tad yadi dhūmadhūmābhāvābhyā
miti dhūmavattvādhūmavattvābhyāmiti vivakṣitam tadā kaḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibandha
bodhasya'  na hi dahanastadavasthādvayavirahitaḥ kacidupapannaḥ 
atha yathā yathoktadharmo nāntarīyakatvamagnestathāparabhūte dhūme dhūmābhāvaśabda
 sāmarthyati nāsti ra  kramā iti nāsti ra  rekā ra  sātiśayasya ra  bhāve
ve cetyeva ra  dharmeni ra  bahuvā ra  vikalpa ca dūṣa a  api nātmaṃ a  apīti
nāsti a  na   ta syā ra  prāgevara  pramāṇābhā ra  vidhāne ca ra   na bhedābhyāṃ ra

ki svaparibhāvakatayeti sāmānyanyāyaḥ  ki cāmī svayamavastuni vidhiniṣedhavyavahāra
mātanvanto vyāpakānupalambhaṃ cāpramāṇayantaḥ paraṃ pratikṣipantīti ka eṣa krama 
nyāyabhūṣaṇakāro hi na hyasati dharmiṇi hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvamiti bruvāṇo'vastuni
hetoḥ pakṣadharmatāniṣedhaṃ vyaktamā  kathametaditi yuktigaveṣaṇe ca dharmiṇo'sattvāditi
hetumabhipreti  anyathā ca vacanamātre ka ādara  athākṣaṇikaṃ naiva pratīyate kathaṃ tasya
kramākramābhyāṃ virodho'vagamyata iti bruvāṇaśca vyaktaṃ pratītyaviṣayatvena virodhāvagamā
bhāvamāha  sa cāvastvantarasādhāraṇo dharmo nitye'vyavastusaṃmate āsajyate 
anyatrāvastuni yadyayaṃ na  nyāyo nitye'pi kathamabhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ 
anyathā
śaṅkaropyetadeva sphuṭayati avastuni pratītyaviṣayatvena na virodhāsiddhiriti 
anyathā prabandhavaiyarthyāt 
nanvasya ṣaṣṭhīsaptamīnirdeśābhāvādasatā saha sato na virodha ityabhiprāyāt na doṣa
iti cet  'adyāpyasato'pratīyamānatvāditi svayamabhivyakto heturapekṣaṇīya eveti

tasya pratītiviṣayatvābhāvo hetuḥ  yadi ca tṛtīyānirdeśenāśrayāsiddhiparihāra manumanyate
bhavān kramākramayorapi nityena saha yogābhāvādarthakriyāśakterapi nityena saha yogābhāva
iti na kṣatiḥ  evaṃ pakṣeṇa yoga eva sapakṣeṇaiva yogo vipakṣeṇāyoga eveti hetostrairūpyaṃ
vakṣyāmaḥ  śāntirastvāśrayāsiddhiprahārasya  tasmāt vivakṣāmātrabheda eva na vastubheda
iti kimanena kāyavratena

na hi dhūmaśaṃśapātvādayo'vastuni vasanti  tasmād yatra bhāvadharmaḥ sādhanaṃ tatra

 tavyā  tadanabhidhāne tu vikalpamātragocarito'yaṃ  sandigdhasattāko nirastasattāko

eva nāśrayāsiddhidoṣeṇa dūṣayituṃ śakyaḥ  na hi tasya vastvāśrayāpekṣā avastudharmādeva 
na ca tadādhārasya pratyakṣānumānāpekṣā avastutvādeva  bhāvadharme tu sādhane

sādhyam  kramādiviraho hetuḥ  asya cābhāvadharmatvaṃ nāma svasādhyāvinābhāvitva
mucyate' abhāvānāṃ śaśaśṛṅgādīnāṃ dharmo na bhāvānāmiti kṛtvā  tadanena vacasā

tacca kutra hetāvupalabdhamaneneti na vidmaḥ  yathā cānyatra sādhyanāntarīyakatā anyadā

kramayaugapadyena hi sattvasya vyāptisiddhau sattvasya vyāpyasyābhāvena' kramayogapadyasya

vyāptirūpaṃ tathā pūrvameva niścitaṃ sadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na pakṣe pramāṇāntareṇa sādhyasiddhayā
vyavasthāpyate tathā kramākramābhāvābhāvenāpi sādhyaṃ prasādhya vyavasthāpyata iti naḥ
pakṣaḥ pūrvameva vyavasthāpitatvāt  tat kuta itaretarāśrayatvam

yadi na nityamanādheyātiśayatvādinā' dharmāntareṇa saha pratītigocarībhavet yaugapadyā

nāśasthāpi mudgarādiparihāreṇa kāraṇamanyadevādṛṣṭaṃ kiñcit syāt yato na purā kāraṇā

tadāpi yadi janane sāmathyaṃ tadāvaśyaṃ kenacid rūpeṇa kāryamutpādayan kṣaṇamātrasthāyi
nāpi rūpeṇa ki 'notpādayet  sarvaṃ tu rūpamaspṛśan kāryaṃ kuryāddheturiti kasya
śraddhāviṣayaḥ  tato yathāyaṃ bhāvo niyatadeśo niyatavastusaṃsthānādyāṃkāra svahetoreva
samutpadyate tathā niyatakālo'pīti kimasaṃbhāvyamatra  na ca deśādiniyamena svarūpa
saṃkocamabhāva eva bhāvasya bhāvayatīti vācyam  na hyabhāvo bhāvamutpannaṃ vā
saṅkocayet  kāraṇena saha saṃbhūya saṅkacitameva cotpādayet  atra pakṣe pṛthak pauruṣa
rahitaḥ  kāraṇasāmagrayantarbhūto'bhāvo'pi nāma yadi bhāvasādhakaḥ kaścidupapādayituṃ
śakyaḥ kiṃ naśchinnam  yādṛśī tādṛśī vā kāraṇasāmagrī kāryaṃ kuryāt  yathā tu
niyatadeśākāraṃ kurute tathā ' niyatakālamapi kartuṃ kastasyāḥ śaktivighāta iti brūmaḥ
yatastadarthamarthyate' parotpattiḥ paścāt  prathamapakṣe'pi kiṃ tāvat sa bhāvaḥ svahetoviśva 
rūpa utpanno niyataḥ kriyate'bhāvena  na vā kenāpi rūpeṇa niṣpanna kenacid vā
niṣpanna eva na tu deśākārakālairiti vikalpāḥ 
antyastāvadayuktaḥ  yena hi rūpeṇa niṣpannaḥ sa eva tasyākāraḥ sa ca na kacid
bhāvamantareṇa kacid bhāvo'pi na kadācidabhavata iti kathamākārādiparihāra 
mābhūt tathaivaṃ kevalaṃ kenacid rūpeṇotpādayituṃ śaknuvataḥ svahetoranyatra

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
kāraṇabhāvaḥ rājabprasādo vā  ādye'pi kalpe sakalatribhuvanākāracchedana

kimakāraṇamanyaḥ kālāntarabhāvī kāraṇāntarāpekṣa   siddho ya sthāyī gaveṣyate
ityuktaprāyam 
pratyarthaṃ bhedo'bhāvasyeti cet  sarvathā'nupalabhyasvabhāvatve sāhasametat 
ato vyomādeḥ 'sarvadharma nirmāṇavat sarvato vyāvartanamapi kiṃ neṣyate  na ca prācīna
mevaṃ vyāpārabhāvamanubhavaḥ kṣamate  tasmāt svakāraṇādeva deśādiniyata iva kāla
niyato'pi jāta iti na sthirapakṣavat kṣaṇikapakṣe'pi vīkṣaṇādiprasaṅgaḥ bhāvasyaivābhāvāt 
sthirapakṣe tu sa cāsti tadavasthaśceti na nivartate prasaṅgaḥ padārthāntarotpattāvapi tasya
tatrākiñcitkaratvāt  aprastutābhidhānaṃ ca bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ 'vastvantarodayavarjanāt 
na nu bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ nivṛtterudayo'padiśyate' iti kimaprastutamatra 
na tu tāvadetra nivṛttiḥ prasajyātmā yāvannodayopadeśaḥ  udaye tu tatparyudastavastvantara
vidhānāt punararthāpattyā nivṛttyākṛṣṭiḥ na tu saiva nivṛtirvastutvādeva anyathāti
prasaṅgāt 
yattu śaṅkaraḥ bhāvādbhāvāntaravadarthāntaratvāviśeṣe kathaṃ sa eva tasyaiva nivṛttiriti
cet  atra vastusvabhāvairuttaraṃ vācyaṃ yeṣāṃ svahetubhyaḥ sahasthitivirodhenaivotpattiḥ na
 hyarthāntaratvādanyatra sahasthitivirodhābhāve bhāvatannivṛtyorapi tasyābhāva iti
nyāyyam tayoreva sahasthitivirodhasya pramāṇena siddhatvāt  na hi yathā kaścidarthāntara
tathā anyeṣāmaheturevaṃ svakāryasthāpi mābhūt tādṛgetadapīti 
etadeva nyāyabhūṣaṇo'pi tadapi dvividhasthāpi 'virodhasya ghaṭanādapāstam

pra vā  
iti duratikramo nyāyaḥ 
yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ yadi tasya na kiñcid bhavati tataḥ pratiṣedho'pi na tasya
bhavatītyapratiṣiddhasvarūpastadavasthatvāt prāgivopalabhyeteti prāgeva prarihṛtametat  tathā
hi pratiṣedho'pi na tasya bhavatīti yadi pratiṣedhākhyo'pi padārtho notpadyata ityarthaḥ
tadā satyametat na tu tāvataivāpratiṣiddhasvarūpatvamarthasya 'svahetutaiva kṣaṇāntare prati
ṣiddhatāpratipādanāt a atha vācanikapratiṣedho vivakṣitastadā kastamapahastayati 
kevalamatra pakṣe prāgivopalabhyetetyasaṃbaddham na yo yadā nāsti sa tadopalabhyaḥ  anyathā
kānyakubjasthito'pi pāṭaliputre dṛśyeta  māndhātā'pi vādyopalabhyeta 
nanvadya māndhāturabhāvastena nopalambhaḥ  ko vai anyathā prāha  kevalaṣaṣṭhīnirdeśād
bhedāvasāye'pi na tato bhinnaḥ padārtho vidhīyate yāvānevārthī māndhātādya nāsti
tatkālaniyatasattākatvāt tāvāneva māndhāturadyābhāva iti   na tu samānametadapi
yāvānevārtho māndhāturadyābhāva iti tāvāneva māndhātādya nāstīti 
yadapyucyate  tatkālaniyatasattākatvāditi tatrāpi tatkāla evāstīti kālāntare
abhāva eva pratipādyata iti kimatrādhikamabhihitam  uktamevaitat  tathāpyucyate
bhedābheda nideśayoreka evārthastattvataḥ kevalaṃ yadi bhinnavastusiddhi pramāṇabalāvalambinī
tadādya nāstītyasyāpi vākyasyādyābhāvo'stītyayamevārthaḥ 
atha bhinnavastubādhaiva pramāṇānvayinī tadābhāvo'stīti tāvadastu  adyābhāvo
jāta ityasyāpi vākyasyādya nāstītyevārtho veditavyaḥ  pramāṇānveṣaṇe ca dṛśyatayā
svīkṛtasyādarśanameva bādhakamuktaṃ ca sādhakaṃ ca kiñcinnetyapi  adyānupalambhe'pi

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
tatkālavartinaḥ kālāntare vastvantararūpamaspṛśatā virahamātreṇa siddha tvamityupapā
ditam  na ca virahamātreṇeti karaṇaśaktinirdeśād vastutva pratyāśā vivakṣāparatantratvāt
kriyākārakavyavahārasya
yāti gandharvanagarādeṣa bandhyāsutaḥ padāre 
mṛgatṛṣṇāmbhasi snātvā pitre dātuṃ jalāñjalim

tantratāmātreṇa dṛṣṭāntīkṛtatvāt

ca sādhorapyetatpāṭho'saṃbhavī sarvathā ki tat sādhurnābhidadhīteti tadaśrutavataḥ praśne

naiva vaktavyam  nāpi sarvathā mithyaivedam  tathā māndhātā nāstīti nādya sthīyate

manuharati 
tadevaṃ nābhidhānādhīnamarthatattvavaśenedaṃ tvabhidhānamiti bhedanirdeśa evādya
abhāvo'sya jāta iti bhinnavastūtpattimivāsaṃśan' adyedaṃ nāstītyasya prasajyapratiṣedhamātra
sūcakasyārthe ' sthāpyo na  viparyaye pramāṇāśaraṇatvādasya vibhāgasya  tatkālaniyamena
kālāntare'bhāvābhidhānaṃ ca siddhasādhanam vastvantarotpattireva hi niṣidhyate kālāntare'
b na ca prasajyapratiṣedhavyavahāramātraṃ pratiṣidhyate  tadasya bādhavidhānapratipāda
ne'pi na paramārthasat padārthāntarasiddhiḥ

pra vā  
iti nyāyasya svayaṃ pratijñānāt  sa cābhāvo bhavan' paścādeveti sphuṭataramasya
kādācitkatvāt sahetutvaṃ vastutvaṃ ceti  tathā ca saha evāha yasya bhāvasya paścādabhāva
sa eva nāśa ityucyate  kathaṃ bhāvasya vināśo'nyo vā kaścinnopalabhyate  atha bhāvasya
vināśa ucyate kiṃ tu sa bhavatīti nocyate bhavatītyabhidhāne ko doṣaḥ  bhāva eva
syāditi cet  tatkimidānīmabhidhānādevārthasya rūpaparivarto bhavati  yadi ca
bhavet tato jāyata ityucyatām  janmāpyabhāvasya kuta iti cet  kādācitkatvāt 
akādācitkatve tu pratyutpannāvasthāyāmapyabhāvaḥ syāditi 
atrocyate vyavahāraśabdena tāvadasmākaṃ niścayavacasī abhimate vacanaṃ ca
vikalpena 'sahaika viṣayameva  vikalpasya ca grāhyādhyavasāyabhedena dvividho viṣayaḥ 
tatra yatpratibhāsaṃ vikalpajñānamājāyate tad grāhyamucyate  yadāśraye tu pravṛttinivṛttī

tatkāladeśasvabhāvavastvavasthādhyavasevā yatastadvikalpodaye vināśākhyavastūtpatti

kimatrabhavata a kopena

mātrātmanā pratiṣidhyate  kiṃ tu vasturūpatayā kalpitayā 
nanu vastu na bhavatītyayameva pratiṣedhaḥ tathā ca sā pratyutirasti na veti praśne
yadyasti kathaṃ na vastu  nāsti cet kathamapratiṣedhaḥ  ucyate vastuvirahamātrasya vastu
tvāropa eva niṣedhaḥ  na vastutvaniṣedhastanniṣedhaḥ  tataḥ pracyutirastīti na pracyuti

 kāṣṭhāntaṃ ā  tatreti nāsti ā   mācaranta ā  bhāvī bhinatti iti nāsti ā   siddhi ā
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'hetukavināśādhikāra
yat punarāha vayaṃ tu paśyāma  tatrānavasthā nābhyupagamyate yatrānavasthāyāṃ
kiñcid dṛṣṭaṃ virudhyeta na cātra dṛṣṭaṃ kiñcid virudhyate  yā tāvad  ghaṭasya paṭādibhyo
vyāvṛttiḥ tayaiva ghaṭādibhyo vyāvṛttaḥ siddhaḥ  tatra vyāvṛttyanta rānavasthāyāṃ na kiñcid
vighaṭitam  vyāvṛttivyāvṛttiparamparāgrahaṇopakṣīṇaśaktitvād vastu vyāvṛttaṃ na sidhya
tīti cet na 'viśeṣaṇaviparyastānāmapi grahaṇānabhyupagamāditi  tatrāpyucyate
sahyastu nābhyupagamo'tra ramparāyā
bhāvasya tadgrahaparamparayāstamāpteḥ 
neṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇavedanaṃ cet
nyāya  samāna iti naiṣa tato vibhāgaḥ 
agṛhītamapi kila vilocanaṃ grāhayati rūpamiti tadviśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇamagṛhītamapi
viśeṣaṇaṃ grāhayatīti manyamānasya prathamamapi viśeṣaṇamagṛhītameva grāhayiṣyati
viśeṣyamiti kṛtaṃ tadgrahaṇenāpi  na cāyaṃ viśeṣaṇakramaḥ  tato yathā prathamameva
viśeṣaṇagrahaṇamanapekṣya lakṣayituṃ viśeṣyamaśaktaṃ tathā dvitīyādyapīti' kathamayaṃ vibhāgaḥ
a śobhāmabhyeti  yathā hyabhāvopādhigrahaṇamantareṇa saṅkīrṇagrahaṇabhītiḥ tathā '
so'pyupādhirasaṅkīrṇo'gṛhyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ parabhedako nāma svayaṃ viṣṭambhidravyavat  evaṃ
paramparāpekṣāyāṃ vyāvṛttavastunaḥ kalperapi grahaṇābhāvādastamayo durvāraḥ 
yadi ca viśeṣaṇamabhāvaḥ tadā' svahetoreva bhinnabhāvasaṃbhave bhinnadarśana vikalpana
yorarthāpattyā siddheḥ kimabhāvena  na hi bhinnamabhinna manubhavitavyamabhrāntapratyayena 
anāpi bhinnamanubhūtaṃ bhinnavirodha  athābhāvamantareṇa na bhinnaṃ nābhinnaṃ 
katarhi kārakavyāpāra ityabhāvaḥ kāraka eva svīkṛto bhavati  tathāpi svahetoreva
bhinnotpattau sarvamaviruddhamiti' nopādhivādaḥ saṃvādaviṣayaḥ 
yaccāha  athavā nirvikalpakajñānena vyāvṛttivyāvṛttyānantyamapi gṛhītamiti
tatrāpi
 yattāvad a  viśeṣaṇa iti nāsti ā  viṇānāmapi a  satyantu a  stanāteḥ

 virodhe a  mantareṇa bhinnannabhinna  a  sarvaviruddha a  nantyā ra
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
nirbhāsamāha yadayaṃ hṛdi nirvikalpe
tat 'kauṣikāvaraṇamapyajahādalajjaḥ 
yatraikamapyanupalabhyamabhāvanāmnā
svavyāpinī sphurati tatra parampareti 
mṛṣāvādaścedārabdhaḥ kimatra naibhṛtyenetyanurūpameva nyāyabhūṣaṇasya yadapyayaṃ
likhati nanu svarūpeṇa buddhaṃ vyāvṛttamavyāvṛttaṃ ā  yadi vyāvṛttaṃ tadā'narthikā
'vyāvṛttiḥ  na ced vyāvṛttaṃ vastusaṅkaraprasaṅgaḥ
svarūpeṇeti ko'rthaḥ  kiṃ vyāvṛtti vinā kiṃ vā vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa 
vyāvṛtti vineti na yuktam vyāvṛttenityadharmatvāt  yo hi dharma kadācid bhavati
tena dharmeṇa vinā'pi dharmī vyapadiśyate yathā kuṇḍalena vinā puruṣo'kuṇḍalī nāśāt
prāganaṣṭa iti  na ca vastvantarād vyāvṛttivihīnaṃ vastu kadācit yathā na gotva
vihīno'sti gauḥ nauṣṇyavihīno'gniḥ 
atha vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa vyāvṛttamityabhipretam  tadiṣṭamevāsmākam
bhedābhyupagamāt  na caivaṃ vyāvṛttiranathikā  yadi vyatiriktena dhanena dhanī puruṣaḥ
kimetāvatā dhanaṃ vyarthaṃ bhavet  tasmāditaretarābhāvo'pi bhāvādarthāntarameveti tadapi
vidhūtam  yasmāt na khalu vastusatīṃ vyāvṛttimanumatyānyadarthaṃ codyametat  kiṃtu
vyāvṛttapratyaye'sāmarthyaveyarthyābhyāmanupayogānna taddhanena' vyāvṛttisiddhiriti codyārthaḥ 
tatra  prathamapakṣe vaiyathyamuktam  dvitīye 'tvasāmarthyamabhipretam 
artha cārthaḥ yadi vyāvṛttasvabhāvo bhāvaḥ svahetorudayavān tadā tadupajanitayā
pratīcyā vyāvṛtta eva pratyetavyaḥ  vyāvṛttilakṣaṇamarthāntaraṃ vināpi na hi
vyasanamevaitadarthasya pramāṇena vā kenacidavadhāritam yat mayā pratyayāntarasākalpe'pi
tāmantareṇa na svajñānamutpādanīyamiti  nāpi jñānasya tadutpāditasya tathā vinā
tadagrahaṇagraho nāma tadiyamanayikā vyāvṛtti  vyāvṛttapratyayasthānyathāpi saṃbhavānna
kalpanīyā 
 koṣikā ā  nāmnā ā  dūṣaṇasya ā  nadhikāravyā a  vyāvṛttiriktena a
 dīśyate ā  rūpeṇa svarūpeṇa ā  vidhuta a vipluta  taddbalena a  tat a
 dvitīye tu a  pravṛttyāvṛddhyā ā  na kṣaṇa ra  yaditi nāsti a  cirādagraho
agrahaṇa a  vyāvṛttiriti nāsti ā tadeva yojitam a
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'hetuka vināśādhikāraḥ
atha na b svahetorvyāvṛtta utpanno bhāva utpannaśca tataḥ saṅkīrṇasva
bhāvasyotpannasya vyāvṛttirevāsatī kathaṃ vyāvṛttapratyayamutpādayedityasamarthā  evaṃ
ca codyaprakrame siddhāmeva vyāvṛttimavasthāpya vyāvṛttanityadharmaṃtvādi kutropayogi  na
hyanena prathamapakṣoktavaiyarthyaparihāravārtā  tathā hi vyāvṛttapratyayasāmarthyāda vyāvṛttirnāma
kalpyate sa ca vyāvṛttapratyayo'nyathāsiddha iti kimasyā kalpanayeti codye vyāvṛttiḥ
nityo dharmaḥ atastena vineti na śakyamityuttaravādinaḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam  yāvatā
vyāvṛttivyatireke sthityaiva vyāvṛttapratyayasyānyathānupapattivādasyāyaṃ nāvasara tadvidhūya
siddhāntamātrakathayā kimatra 
na ca vināśāt prāganaṣṭa ityudāhatuṃ yuktam vināśasya bhedāsiddheḥ  na vyāvṛtti
vihīnaṃ vastvityapi vyāvṛttestāttvikābhede siddhasādhanam 'bhedāsiddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte'pi
atadvayāvṛttirūpayorgotvauṣṇatvayorgavāgnibhedena darśayitumaśakyatvāt 
yaccātraiva pakṣe dvitīyaṃ vikalpitamanena kiṃ vā vyāvṛttiriti vyatiriktena vyā
pāreṇeti tadanabhyupagamenaiva gatam svarūpeṇa vyāvṛttaṃ buddhamiti viśvasmād vyāvṛttarūpaṃ
buddhamityetasyārthasya vivakṣitatvāt  na cādyavaiphalyaparihāra ityuktam  nāpi dhanidṛṣṭāntena
bhinnavyāvṛttisiddhiniyamahe torabhāvāt dhanavadvāra saṃyogasamavāyānapekṣo viśeṣaṇāntarasya
daṇḍapāṇḍaratvāderapi saṃbandhavyavahāra syāt  tasmānnetaretarābhāvo nāma kaścit
svahetoreva parasparavyavacchinnasyotpatteḥ 
evaṃ kālāntaravyavacchinnasyāpīti  na vināśahetunā kiñcit  tadayam 
apekṣeta paraḥ kārya yadi vidyeta kiñcana 
pra vā  
iti siddho nyāyaḥ  kimatra piṣṭapeṣaṇena 
nāśo'dya  jāta iti nānyapadārthabhāvo'
bhāvaḥ svakālaniyatastu sa nānyadā'sti 
 vyāvṛttamupra a   tyasamarthā ra  kathyate ā  kiṅkonasaṃhṛtaṃ ā   sthānavasaraḥ ā

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
nāstyanyadetyapi 'parodaya eva yasya
tasya  prasajyaviṣayāstamaye prasaṅgaḥ 
yatpunarayaṃ prasajyaparyudāsayorbhedasādhanārthamabhāvabhāvavyavahāraviṣayatvena vibhāga
pratyapīpadat tad bhavato bhāṣaiva bhāvānyatetyatrāntare tiraskṛtam  na hi nyāyasiddhasya
samayamātreṇa bādhanaṃ sādhu  tathā hi
yajjāyamānamupalakṣitamarthakāri
bhāvātmanā vyavaharanti tadeva santaḥ 
so'yaṃ na yaḥ samayato yadi bhaṅgabhāgī'
bhāvānavasthitiriyaṃ na ca paryudāsaḥ 
yadā hi mūrtāmūrtasapratighāpratighasanidarśanānidarśanadū rāsanna sthūlasūkṣmādiprakāreṣu
kaścid bhāvamabhāvaṃ vā kaścit svecchāvaśādabhidadhīta  vindhyavandhyāsutādikam
abhāvabhāvaṃ vā tadāyātamavyavasthānaṃ bhāvasya  na caivaṃ kṣatiḥ  svasamayānurodhāt
abhidhānabhedasaṃbhavāt  b kevalaṃ kimidānīṃ paryudastaṃ vastu vyavahriyatām 
tasmāt samayānurodhādabhāvaśabdāpravṛttāvapi ekasya kāraṇāpekṣasaṃbhavasyopālambhabhājo
vā anyastādṛgeva padārtha paryudasto vaktavya  tatkathamabhāvaśabdasaṅkatamātreṇa
paryudāsavyudāsaḥ  yadi punarupalambhasaṃbhavāvapyabhāvābhimatasya samayamātratantrāvityucyate
tadā vāstavaḥ prasajyapratiṣedha evāyaṃ na paryudāsa iti na doṣaḥ  anena tu nyāyavinmāninā
nyāyāgataṃ tameva prakāramullaṅghaya saṃbhavopalambhārthakriyāśaktayaścābhāvasya bhāvikya
abhyupagantavyāḥ  paryudāsapratyanīka prasajyapratiṣedhatā ceti kimato'pi vyasanamanavasāna
manyat 
 yaccāyamāha na hyutpattirbhāvasya lakṣaṇaṃ yena nivṛttirbhavantī bhāvaḥ syādanutpatti
matāmaṇyākāśādīnāṃ ' bhāvatvāditi  tatrāpi
pāṇinena nadī gaṅgā yamunā ca sthalī nadī 
abhavannapi bhāvo'sya na bhāvo'sya bhavannapi 
 dityapi a  prajya ā  bhaṅgabhaṅga a   mapratiṣṭhāpratigha ā  kañcitkañcita a
 kaścitkaścit a mabhāvamabhāvamvā a  paryudasto vaktavyaḥ iti nāsti ra  pālambha
a  mattā ra  prāṇi a ra
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye'hetukavināśādhikāra
naraḥ svātantryamāpanno yadicchati karoti tat 
ubhayatra samāno'yaṃ nyāyo nyāyavidāṃ mataḥ 
nadīsaṃjñāniṣedhe'pi nāvagāhasya bādhanam 
' ' bhāvasaṃjñāniṣedhe'pi paryudāso na bādhyate 
upalambhārthaśaktasya kāraṇāpekṣajanmanaḥ 
sarvasya paryudastatvaṃ vastvantaramapekṣya hi 
abhāvasaṃjñāvirahe paryudāsavyavasthitiḥ 
na kāpi sidhyet sarvatra saṃjñāyā ' sulabhatvataḥ 
yaccedaṃ svarūpanivṛttilakṣaṇā cotpattiḥ pradhvaṃsasyeṣyate na tu prāgasataḥ sattā
saṃbandhalakṣaṇā kāraṇasamavāyalakṣaṇā veti tatrāpi
svarūpasyaiva nirvṛttiḥ sarvatrotpattirucyate 
prakṣipya samavāyaṃ tu vimūḍhaiḥ sāpi hāritā 
samavāyasyaivābhāvāt ka sattāsaṃbandhādiḥ  astu vā so'pi
tathāpyapūrvātmalā'
evotpatti dharmādharmāntarāṇāṃ tu bhāvābhāvau na sādhakabādhako  kiṃ ca kāryasyāpya
bhāvasya na prāgasataḥ sattāsaṃbandha iti ko'rthaḥ  kiṃ prāgasanneva na bhavati  atha
paścādapi na sattvamasya  ubhayathāpi kutaḥ kāryatvamākāśākāśa kuśeśayavat  prāgasataḥ
sattvamastu paścānna tu sattāyogaḥ 
nanu sattvaṃ sattetyanarthāntarametat  yogaśca sambandhaḥ  tatra sattvayogo'sti na
sattāyoga iti ko'pyayaṃ nyāya  atha sattā mahāsāmānyamucyate tadabhāve'pi
svarūpasattvamātreṇa paścāt sannityucyata iti cet  tattarhi svarūpasattvaṃ yadi tāttvikam
tāvataiva kāryatvaṃ kimapareṇa kartavyamanyasyāpi kāryasya  athaupacārikam tadā
nāśasyāpi kutaḥ kāryatā  na hi bandhyātanayasya paścādbhāvopacāre kāryatā vāstavī
nāma 
 abhāva ā  saṃjñayāḥ ā  nivṛttilaṃkṣaṇā ā  prakṣepya a  dharmā iti nāsti
a  sādhakāsā a  nakāro nāsti ā  mākāśākuśe ā
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
yaccedaṃ nivṛtterapyādimattvamityucyata' iti tadāpi nādhikaṃ kiñcit  sā ca
' nivṛttira bhāvarūpeṇaiva b ādimatīti punarna sahāmahe kāryāntarasādhāraṇa
tāyā pratipādanāt  ādeśamātrametat bhūbhujāmeva śobhate  bhāvopalambhakāle' tad
rūpānupalambhādityapi paścādrūpopalambhe śobhāmābhajati  sa ca nāsti kumbhāsaṃbhava
vikalpamātraṃ tu saṅke tānurodheneti darśitam 
arthī paṭārthakriyayā ghaṭasyānupalambhane 
na prāvataṃta ityasti nānyadṛk pratiyoginaḥ 
tadalamasya prakriyāmātramavakaraṃ nirūpya svayamūhyadoṣatvāt 
yaccāha nāpyarthaṃkriyāhetutvamātreṇa bhāvatvaprasaktiḥ tvaduktabhāvalakṣaṇānabhyupa
gamāditi tatrāpi paryudāsatvānatikramādityuktam  tasmānna bhāvādarthāntaramabhāvaḥ 
yatpunarāha tvayāpi bhāvābhāvayolaṃkṣaṇabhedo'bhihitaḥ  tat kathamekatvam 
sarvārthānāṃ lakṣaṇabhedādeva bhedavyavasthā tato'pi cenna bhedavyavasthitirna kasyacit
kutaścid bhedasiddhirityadvaitaprasaṅga iti  tadapyaparyālocanaphalam  yo hi naśvarasvabhāva
eva nāśo nāśyatīti bahulādhikārāt kartari ghan taddharmatākalpanayā vā tadvāca
kenābhidhānāt  tannāśaṃ bhāvasvabhāvamicchāmaḥ  tamevāśritya
sattāmātrānubandhitvānnāśasyānityatādhvaneḥ

ityuktam 
tathā cānenaivotthāpitam bhāva eva kṣaṇasthitidharmā nāśa iti tasyābhedameva
brūmaḥ  naśanaṃ nāśa iti prasajyātmā dvidhā vyākartavyaḥ tattvatastāvad vastutvavirahāt
tattvānyatvaśūnya evāsau bhāvo na bhavatīti tadbhāvaniṣedhamātrapātraṃ tu kharaśṛṅgādivat 
saṃvṛttau tu yathā kālabhedena vikalpyamānaḥ kādācitka iti pratibhāti' tathā
'sarvopākhyāviraharūpatayā bhāvādbhinna iva pratibhātīti nāvastutvepi 'lakṣaṇa

 ivābhāti ā  sarvopakṣo ra  kṣaṇabhede ā

parastasya heturbhāvasvabhāvatvāt  tadayaṃ yat

pra vā  
ityata āha tadapi svavacanavirodhādayuktam  tvayā hi bhāvābhāvayostādātmyamuktam
tacca tattvānabhyupagame virudhyate  tattvābhyupagame'pi lakṣaṇabhedo virudhyate  yasya hi
lakṣaṇabhedena bheda ucyate tasya kathaṃ tattvātattva nirvacanīyatvamiti  tatsukhaidhita 
krīḍanaśīlatayā kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ punaḥ kārayati  na khalu bhāvapracyutisvabhāvenābhāvena
bhāvasya tādātmyaṃ brūmaḥ  yastu na bhavatītyabhāva ' uttarakṣaṇāpekṣayā tena kastādātmya

veditavyam 
yadapyāh 'nanvabhāvasya sarvadharmavivekalakṣaṇatvādutpattirna yuktā  sā
hi bhāvadharma eveti na jñeyatvāderbhāvadharmasyābhāve'pi sadbhāvādityādi tadapya
sāram  na hi sādhāraṇadharmaṃyogamātreṇa virodhapratiniyatānāmapi dharmāṇāmavakāśaḥ
hutāśanasyāpi śaityaprasaṅgāt abhāvasyaiva vā sarvatra sadbhāvaprasaṅgāt jñeyatvādīnāmapi
niṣedhāt  utpattiścābhūtvā bhavanarūpatayā bhāvadharma evetyāpāditameva

prāyam 
tatra hi svayamiti hetvantaramanapekṣya svahetunā kṣaṇaniyatasthitirjanita iti

 śyatī tu ā  naśvaraḥ a  tvayā tādātmyamuktamiti prāntayojanā a  sukhoditaḥ ra
 bhāva iti nāsti ā  svabhāvo ā  uttama ā  nanu a  yuktaṃ ā  sahi

jātaḥ  svahetorhi tatsvabhāvo'tatsvabhāvād vyāvṛtta utpannaḥ  sa kathaṃ paścāṃdapyatatsvabhāvaḥ
syāt  na hi laghusvabhāvād vyāvṛttaḥ pāṣāṇaḥ kadācillaghu syāditi  tadapi pla
eva  yathā hi deśāntarasthitivyāvṛtta utpannaḥ tathā kṣaṇāntarasthitivyāvṛtto'pi kathaṃ
kṣaṇāntarasthiteravakāśa ityuktaprāyam 
nanvasaditi na tadeva vastvabhidhīyate vidhiviṣayatvāt 
'anyaccābhāvaśabdā
bhidheyaṃ pratītigocarāpannaṃ tvayā neṣṭam tato nirviṣayaḥ pratiṣedho visaṃvādītyapratiṣiddhaṃ
vastu syāt  naivam pracyuterapi pratipādyatvāt kuto nirviṣayatvam  nāpi visaṃvādaḥ
bhāvasthitau hi pratiṣedhasya visaṃvādaḥ syāt  sa ca nāsti pracyuteḥ pratipāditatvāt 
na cāvastunaḥ saṅkalpaviṣayatāyā apyanupapattirityuktameva

naṣṭatvamabhyupagantavyam

ataḥ

b namo bhagavate vītarāgāya 
iha dahanādinā dhūmādervyāptiradhyakṣānupalabdhisādhana tadutpattilakṣaṇeti vyutpādyate 
pare hi purastanāstāvadagnimati dhūmasya darśanamadarśanaṃ ca tadvirahiṇītyevānvayavyatirekitvaṃ
kalpayāmbabhūvuḥ  tatra darśanādarśanaṃ yādṛcchikamapi sakṛd bhavediti ca bhūyaḥ pravṛtti
mapekṣate  nanu bhūyasāpi pravṛtte darśanādarśane ghaṭakulaṭādāvupalabdho vyabhicāra iti
cet  kimetāvatā tatrāpyanumānamastvityucyate atha tadvad dhūmādāvapi mā bhūditi 
prathamapakṣastāvad vyabhicārādeva nirasta  dvitīyo'pyavyabhicārādeva  na hyanyasya
vyabhicāre dhūmasya kiñcit  na khalu viṣānamaniṣṭamiti bhakṣyāntaramapi heyamastu 
tāvatā ca sarvā nivṛttilabdheti kimutpattiprārthanayā tanni śca yopayoginā vā pratyakṣā
nupalambhena  tadutpattirapi yadi darśanādarśanādeva gṛhyeta kīdṛśo doṣaḥ  anumānameva
ca vibhāgena bhavatviti tadanveṣaṇam  sa ca vibhāgo vyabhicārāvyabhicāradvāreṇa
siddhaḥ  asati ca vyabhicāre tāvataiva gamakatvam anarthakā tadutpattiḥ  vyabhicāre ca
śatamapi tadutpattayo na samarthāḥ  tasmāt sannikarṣeṇa paryeṣaṇaṃ saṃyogenaiva kṛtārtham  ataeva
saṃyogī heturucyate vardhūmo na kāryamiti 
trilocanastvāha pratyakṣānupalambhayoviśeṣaviṣayatvāt kathaṃ tābhyāṃ sāmānyayoḥ
sambandhapratītiḥ  athānagnivyāvṛttenādhūmavyāvṛttasya sambandha  pratīyata eveti nanu
so'pi kasya pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ  na tāvat pratyakṣasya tasya svalakṣaṇaviṣayatvāt 
nāpyanumānasya tasyāpi tatpūrvakatvāt  na ca vyāvṛttaḥ kaścit sambandhaḥ  atha pratyakṣa
pṛṣṭhabhāvī vikalpo dṛṣṭe bhede'bhedamadhyavasyati tadeva sāmānyam  evamapi vikalpānāṃ
na vastveva viṣayaḥ api tu grāhyākāra saca na vastu  vastu tu teṣāṃ parokṣameveti
kathaṃ tenāpi sambandhagrahaḥ  asmākaṃ tu bhūyodarśanasahāyena manasā tajjātīyānāṃ sambandho
gṛhīto bhavati ato dhūmo nāgni vyabhicarati  tadvyabhicāre dhūma upādhirahitaṃ
sambandhamatikrāmediti hetovipakṣaśaṅkānivartakaṃ pramāṇamupalabdhilakṣaṇa prāptopādhiviraha
heturanupalambhākhyaṃ pratyakṣameva  tataḥ siddhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ 
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
vācaspatestu' prapañcaḥ tathā hi dhūmādīnāṃ vahnayādibhiḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ
na tu vahnayādīnāṃ dhūmādibhiḥ  te hi vināpi dhūmādibhirupalabhyante  yadā tu ārdrendhana
sambandhamanubhavanti tadā dhūmādibhiḥ sambadhyante  tasmād vahnayādīnāmārdrendhanādyu
pādhikṛtaḥ sambandhaḥ na tu svābhāvikaḥ  tato na niyataḥ  svābhāvikastu dhūmādīnāṃ
vahnayādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ tadupādheranupalabhyamānatvāt  a kacid vyabhicārasyā
darśanāt  anupalabhyamānasyāpi kalpanānupapatteḥ  na cādṛśyamāno'pi darśanānarhatayā

adṛṣṭapūrvamapi  viśeṣasmṛtyapekṣa eva hi saṃśayo nāsmṛterbhavati  na ca smṛtirananubhūtacare

vyāpticarcā
kasmāt sarvaṃ sarvasmānna bhavati anyatvāviśeṣāt  tataśca sa evātiprasaṃṅgaḥ  yadyucyeta
na bhāvasvabhāvāḥ paryanuyojyāḥ tasmādanyatvāviśeṣe'pi kiñcideva kāraṇaṃ kiñciñca
kāryamiti nanveṣa svabhāvānanuyogo'kāryakāraṇabhūtānāmapi svabhāvapratibandhe tulya
eva  tasmāt yatkiñcidetadapi 
kena puna pramāṇenaiṣa svābhāvika sambandho gṛhyate  pratyakṣasambandheṣu
pratyakṣeṇa  tathā hi yadā tāvat prathamaṃ vahnidhūmayoḥ sahārdrendhanayoḥ sambandhaṃ paśyati
tadā ki dvayorapi svābhāvika sambandha  aupādhiko vā atha dhūmasyaupādhikaḥ vahneḥ
svābhāvika vaheraupādhiko dhūmasya svābhāvika iti ca na śakyaṃ nirdhārayitum 
tatra vahneranārdendhanasya vinā dhūmamayogolakādī darśanādā ndhanopādhirasya dhūmena
sambandho na tu svābhāvika iti niścīyate  dhūmaviśeṣasya tu vinā vahnimanupa lambhā
dupādhibhedasya cānupalabhyamānasya kalpanāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāt viśeṣasmṛtyapekṣasya
saṃśayasyānupalabdhapūrve'nutpādāt  utpāde vātiprasaṅgāt  prekṣāvatāṃ pravṛttyucchedāt
svābhāvikaḥ sambandho'vadhāryate 
tadidamavadhāraṇaṃ na mānasam anapekṣasya manaso bāhyeṣu pravṛttāvandhavadhirābhāva
prasaṅgāt  bhūyodarśanasāpekṣasya ca pravṛttau pramāṇāntarāpātāt  na hi mano nimitta
mityeva mānasam  tathā sati na kiñcinna mānasam pratyayamātrasya b  manonimitta
tattadasādhāraṇakāraṇāpekṣayā ca
tvāt 
tattatpramāṇavyapadeśe'trāpi bhūyodarśanam
asādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇamastīti pramāṇāntaraṃ jātam  tasmādabhijātamaṇibhedattattvavad
bhūyodarśanajanitasaṃskārasahāyamindriyameva dhūmādīnāṃ vādibhi svābhāvikasambandha
grāhīti yuktam 
evaṃ mānāntara viditasambandheṣu mānāntarāṇyeva yathāsvaṃ bhūyodarśanasahāyāni
svābhāvikasambandhagrahaṇe pramāṇamunnetavyāni  vataśca pratibaddhā hetavaḥ svasādhyena
yadi sādhyamantareṇa bhaveyuḥ svabhāvādeva pracyaveranniti tarkasahāyā nirastasādhya
vyatirekasandehā yatra dṛṣṭāstatra svasādhyamupasthāpayantyeva  na ca śyāmatādiṣu
maitratanayatvādīnāṃ svābhāvikapratibandhasaṃbhavaḥ annapānapariṇatibhedasyopādhe śyāmatāyā
maitratanayatvasambandhaṃ prati vidyamānatvena maitratanayatvasyāgamakatvāt  etena pakkānyasya
vṛkṣasyāgravartīni phalāni etadvṛkṣaprabhavatvāt āsvāditaphalavadityādayo'pyaupādhika
sambandhā vyākhyātāḥ tasmād yasya svābhāvikaḥ sambandho niyataḥ so'numānāṅgam
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
yathā dhūmakṛtakatvādiḥ  yasya tvaupādhikaḥ so'numānāṅgaṃ na bhavati yathā tatputra
tvādiriti sthitam 
atrocyate vyāptirnāma vyāpakasya tatra bhāva evaṃ vyāpyasya vā tatraiva bhāva
ityevaṃ kartṛkarmadharmatathā pratīteranvayavyatirekarūpatayā dvidhānumānasamīyā samohitā
anyathānumāne'nupayogāt  yadi hi sādhane satyavaśyaṃ sādhyaṃ bhavatyeveti sāmānyena
siddhaṃ bhavati sādhyābhāve vā sādhanamavaśyaṃ na bhavatīti tadā viśeṣoddeśena sādhanavati
sādhya pratyāśā bhavati sādhyābhāve tadabhāvasya  yadā tu na yathoktaniyamaḥ tadā
sādhanaṃ ca bhavati na ca sādhyamityāśaṅkāyāṃ kathamanumānāvakāśaḥ  tasmādanumāna
micchatā niyataṃ yathoktaiva vyāptirapekṣitavyā  na ca bhūyodarśanamātreṇa tasyāḥ siddhiḥ 
yathā hi yadṛcchayāpi sakṛt saṃvādasaṃbhāvanā tathā katipayavārānapi yadṛcchayaiva bhavataḥ
saṃvādasya niṣedhaḥ yathā ca sakṛt sahacāradarśane vyabhicāra upalabdha iti na sarvatra
sarvadā ca tatsahacāraniyama iti śaṅkā tathā bhūyodarśane'pi vyabhicāradarśanādeva
bhavantī na śakyaniṣedhā 
yat tu vyabhicāra
darśanādananumānamuktam tanna yuktam  tathā hi kasya punariha
vyabhicāradarśanamanumānavighnāya prayojakam  kiṃ pratipattureva atha śāstrakārasya
yasya kasyacid vā  antyapakṣe pratipattuḥ kimāyātam yato nānumānamayaṃ kuryāt 
anyathānyasya tattadviṣayapratyakṣīkāreṇaiva so'pi kṛtārtha iti kimanumānamavaśya
manveṣate  śāstrakāraṃ ca pṛṣṭā adṛṣṭasambandho'pi dhūmādagnimanumāsyate ityalokikam 
a  pratipattustu nāvaśyaṃ sannapi vyabhivāro gocarobhavati  na hi yatra vyabhicārastatraiva
tāvati kāle deśe vāvaśyaṃ pratītimavatarati  apratīyamānaśca nāstyeveti na śakya
mavasātum ātyantikakālavyavadhāne'pi vā darśanāt anupajātabādhabuddhīnāmapi
nidhanasannidheravarodhācca  tataśca satyapi vyabhicāre pratipattudarśanaṃ saṃbhāvyate  bhavati
cāvyabhicā re'numāna manyathā netyupadiṣṭasya smaran kimasāvavyabhicāra
niścayādanumāne
pravartatām nivartatāṃ vā'darśanamātreṇa niścayāyogādavyabhicārāsiddhaḥ sandigdhā
siddhahetuvat  tatrādyapakṣe karabhādapyanumānaṃ kuryāt  dvitīye tu na dhūmādapi  na hi
vidyamānasyāvidyamānasya vā vyabhicārasthānavalokanakāle kaścid viśeṣaḥ  tato yadi
bhūyāṃsamapi sahopalambha karabhagadaṃbhayoryādṛcchikamāśaṅkate tathā dhūmadahanayorapi kasmānneti
samānam  atha pratyāsannayorapi karabhagardabhayoḥ svātantryeṇopalakṣyamāṇayoḥ paśyāmi
vyāpticarcā
tāvat kimekamapasāryamāṇamanyo'nudhāvati dhenumiva vatsa iti jijñāsayā tathānutiṣṭhanna
tathā pratipadyate  vahnī tvapasārite dhūmāpagamameva pratyeti vahnisannidhāne vā dhūma
saṃbhavam 
ataḥ saṃbhāvyate vyabhicāraḥ karabhasyānyadāpi na dhūmasyeti cet  viśiṣṭameva
tarhi darśanādarśanaṃ dhūme utpattigrāhakaṃ ca yādṛśaṃ tādṛśaṃ na karabhe  tathāhi yadāgnathabhāve
dhūmābhāvaṃ pratyeti tadā sahopalambhapūrvakamagnimātrābhāve dhūmādarśa namupayuktaṃ pratibandha
siddhau  anyathā sahadarśanābhāve tāvadaṅgā rā viśeṣa citrabhānumātrāpasāraṇaṃ ca dhūmadha
nāstyeva karabhavad gardabhābhāva iti ka sambandhabodha  sahadarśane'pi yadi vastvantara
sahitahutāśāpasāraḥ tadā pūrvamasya sattā kiṃ hutāśasya vastvantarasya vā sattayā prayukteti
na niścayaḥ hutāśamātrābhāve tu tadbhāvaprayukta eva prāgasya bhāva iti sulabham  yadāpi
pāvakamātrasannidhau dhūmasattā tadāpi pūrvamubhayādarśanapūrvakamagnimātropadarśane darśanaṃ
dhūmasyopayuktam anyathāgnimātramānītaṃ dhūmaśvāstyeveti karabhavat kutra pratibandhasiddhiḥ
vastvantarasahita hutāśanānayane'pi kasyābhāvena prayuktaḥ prāgabhāvo dhūmasyeti na niścayaḥ 
hutāśamātropalambhe tu tadabhāvaprayukto yuktaḥ 
tadevaṃ pūrvadarśanāpekṣaniyataikādarśanapūrva cānyādarśana viśiṣṭamucyate  tadapi
prācīnadarśanamautarakālikayathoktādarśanadvayāpekṣayā viśiṣṭam  evamadarśanapūrva ke'pi
darśane viśeṣa ūhitavyaḥ yadabhāvāt karabhādau nāśvāsaḥ  tameva darśanādarśanayoviśeṣa
māśritya b pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāravyavahāra tadviṣayaśca bhāvadvayasvabhāvaḥ kārya
kāraṇabhāva ityucyate 
yaccāyattamanāyatte paratra tat tatra tadutpattyā pratibaddhamityapi  tathā hi tanmātrā
panayane dvitīyasāhityasyāpi niṣedhād vyaktaṃ tadāyattaṃ tat  evaṃ tanmātrāpasāraṇe'pi
bīddhavyam anyathā dvitīyāpasāraṇāpekṣaṇāt kutastannātrāpasāraṇamiti tadutpattyaiva
pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanayā vyāptiruktā bhavati na tadviśeṣavirahiṇā darśanādarśanamātreṇa 
tadviśeṣāpekṣaṇe ca sakṛdeva pravṛttau nirvṛttilābhānna bhūyaḥ pravṛttyapekṣā  yathā hi sakṛd
darśanādarśanena pratītasahacāramātrādanāśvāsa karānnāparamapareṇa pratyayam tathā sakṛt
pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ pratītaviśiṣṭajātidvayahetuphalabhāvasambandhānnāparamparābhyāṃ pratyeya
miti tāvataiva nirvṛttiḥ  yadi na sādṛśyādinā jātyantare  tadadhyavasāya puruṣasyeti
nipuṇena pratipattrā bhavitavyam  sahacāramātre tu tajjātāveva saṃśayaḥ anyatra
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
sahacāramātre vyabhicāradarśanaṃ ca puṣṭaṃ bījamasya  na cātra viṣānnadṛṣṭāntaḥ śāntaye
viṣānnād bhojyāntarasya bhinnajātīyatvāt  atra tu yaḥ prayojako bhāgo bhūyaḥ
sahacāralakṣaṇastenaikajātīyatvameva dhūmasya na tu viṣadigdhatvaṃ dadhibhaktāde sādhāraṇa
miti vaiṣamyam  tadutpattimantareṇa cāvyabhicārasyaivābhāvād bhede avyabhicārasyaiva
tadutpattirūpatvāt  avyabhicārāpekṣayā kṣepastadutpatterayukta eva  tasmāt kāryameva
hetudhū mo dhūmadhvajasya tadutpattyāvyabhicārākṣepāt na saṃyogī sahacāramātrollekhāt 
kathaṃ tarhi karabhagadaṃbhodāharaṇamasaṃyogāt  dāsīkalasasaṃyogadarśanabhūmnā santoṣo'stu 
karabhagardabhayorapi vā jalabalākayoriva tāvati kāle deśe'vasthitiniyamastathā
darśanādastviti na kiñcidetat  tasmādarthāntare gamye kāryahetuḥ tadbhāvasiddhiśca
pratyakṣānupalambhāditi sthitam 
trilocanacodye tu brūmaḥ viśeṣaviṣayaṃ pratyakṣamiti ki viśeṣo'pi viṣayo'sya
atha viśeṣa eva  ayogavyavacchedapakṣe na sāmānyaviṣayatāpratihatiriti kathaṃ na
pratyakṣānupalambhāvakāśaḥ sāmānyadvaye  anyayogavyavacchedastu kimasmatsiddhāntāśrayeṇa
ucyate vastuvṛttyā vā  asmākaṃ tāvadubhayamubhayamapi pramāṇamubhayaviṣayam grāhyādhya
vasāyabhedena  yaddhi yatra jñāne pratibhāsate tad grāhyam yatra tu tatpravartate tadadhyavaseyam 
tatra pratyakṣasya svalakṣaṇaṃ grāhyamadhyavaseyaṃ ca sāmānyam  anumānasya tu viparyayaḥ  tatra
sādhanapratyakṣaṃ tadaivārthakriyārthinaḥ kṣaṇavokṣaṇe'pi santānāpekṣayā sāmānya viṣayam 
vyāptigrahaṇaprakaraṇe a punarekavyaktidarśane'pi sarvasajātīyavyaktiviṣayatvena sāmānya
viṣayam  pratyakṣeṇa mayā agnijanmā dhūmaḥ paricchinna iti sakalatadanyāpoḍhavyakti
jātamantarbhāvyaiva tadvalotpannasyādhyavasāyasya saṃvedanāt  yathā rūpamātradarśane rūparasa
gandhasparśa samudāya viśeṣātmani ghaṭe dṛṣṭāvyavasāyāt tadviṣayatvaṃ pratyakṣasya 
na ca sāmānya nāma kiñcidanyadeva kiṃtu svalakṣaṇānyeva parasparamavivecitabhedāni
sāmānyamucyante  bhedavivecane tu pratyekaṃ svalakṣaṇamiti svaśabdenaiva vyavahāraḥ  tato
yadyapi paravilakṣaṇāśeṣasvalakṣaṇānāmapratibhāsānna grāhyatvena viṣayatvam tathāpyadhya
vaseyatvena dunivāramiti kathamanyayogavyavacchedaḥ  vikalpānāmavastveva viṣaya ityapi
parakṛtāntānabhijñatayaivocyate anusandhānānumānayoradhyavasāyāpekṣayāvastuviṣayatvāt 
śeṣaṃ siddhasādhanam  atha vastuvṛttyeti pakṣa  so'pyayuktaḥ sarvajñānānāṃ grāhyādhya
vaseyabhedena viṣayadvaividhyasya duratikramāt  pramāṇasya hi prāmāṇyamevātiricyate
vyāpticarcā
viṣayadvaitaṃ tu sarvatra siddham  tatrānumāne tāvavastuno'pratibhāsādadhyavayameva
svalakṣaṇam grāhyastu svākāraḥ  evaṃvidhaṃ nirloṭhitamasmābhirapohaprakaraṇe iti na
prastūyate  yadyapi ca buddherākāro neṣṭastathāpi vastubalādāyātaḥ kathamapohituṃ śakyaḥ 
na hyapratibhāse jñānaṃ nāma pratibhāsi cānumāyāṃ na vastviti sthite niyataṃ svākāraḥ 
alīkamastviti cet  tathāpi tatpratibhāse grāhyamavaseyaṃ ca bāhyamiti viṣayadvaita siddhī
ki nirbandhena  evaṃ pratyakṣe'pi kācideva vyakti pratibhāsinī grāhyā  sarvā tu
sajātīyādhyavaseyā pratibandhabodhakāle asphuraṇe hi yadyavasāyo'pi syāt pratyakṣeṇa
sambandhabodhaprasiddhigandho'pi nirdhūtaḥ syāt 
yattu mānasena bhūyodarśanajanitasaṃskārasahāyenendriyeṇa vā grahaṇamuktam tatredaṃ
vicāryate  asti tāvadagnidhūmavyaktyoḥ punaḥ punarupalabdhiraindriyī  asti ca tatkṛta
saṃskārajanmā vimarśa ayametatsahita evopalabhyate tat kimanayoḥ sadātano'yaṃ
sahacāraḥ atha suhṛdayasyeva sātyaya iti  parāmarśadurbalasya hetunāntarīyakapratītirapi
bhavati  tadanurūpaṃ cānuṣṭhānam  na punaratrāparo jñānavivataḥ saṃvedyate  tato
bhūyodarśanaṃ tāvat saṃskāradvāreṇa sahāyameva kṛtam na tatprastutamabhidhātuṃ śakyam
tadantimamekajātikāśeṣavyaktiviṣayaka ityapi manorathamātram tadvayaktīnāṃ nirbhāsā
bhāvāt  saṃśayo'pi tadanantaraḥ saṃśayatvādeva na niścāyaka sambandhasya  paścimaśca
niścayākāratve'pi parāmarśaśūnyasyaiveti pratyakṣābhikhyayāpi tadupasthāpite prameye ka
āśvāsa  aliṅgajasya hi vikalpasya pūrvapravṛttadarśanavyāpārānusārādevārthaṃtathā
bhāvasambhavo na svātantryāt b atiprasaṅgāt pūrvapravṛttāni ca darśanāni sahacāra
mātrasākṣīṇi vātātapādisahacāravat kañcid viśeṣamanāviśanti kathamasya yathārthatāṃ
samarthayitumīśate  tathābhāve'pi tānyeva tatra pramāṇam idaṃ tu smaraṇaṃ pramāṇatvena
nirdiśyata iti sādhu  vātātapayoḥ paścāt sahacāravighaṭanāsti viśeṣa iti na vācyam
vyabhicārādarśanakālāpekṣayābhedasya vivakṣitatvāt atrāpi avighaṭananaścayānupa
patteścokkatvāt  yāvadeva vahivyāpārāt pūrvaṃ dhūmānudayo hṛdayasaṃvāsī tāvadeva hi
sahacārāntarād bhedavimarśaḥ tata eva tadvyabhicāre dhūma upādhirahitaṃ sambandhamati 
krāmediti śobhate  anyathā pūrvaṃ sahacāramātropalabdhau yathā dhūmamantareṇānala vilokane
analasya dhūmena sambandhe upādhikalpanaṃ sāmānyena tathā dhūmasyāpi vahnimantareṇa
bhāvasaṃbhāvanāyāmupādhyantarakalpanaṃ bhaviṣyati ataḥ kasya kenaupādhikaḥ svābhāviko
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalī
vā sambandha syāt  na hi suhṛdorekavyatirekeṇānyadarśane'vyatirekeṇāpi taddarśana
saṃbhāvanā na bhavati  kevalaṃ caitramantareṇāpi maitrasya bhāvāvirodhād bhūdharavivara
praviṣṭasyāpi na darśanayogyatā vigalati dhūmasya tu niyataṃ vinā vahnimudaya eva nāstīti
na saṃbhāvanā tāvatā ca tadutpattireva śaraṇīkṛtā bhavati  sā ca na bhūyodarśanā
dityuktameva 
ata eva gogotvayorapi na svābhāvikaḥ sambandho'bhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ
tadutpattipratītivirahe'nyasmāt sahacāriṇo viśeṣābhāvāt  na ca sahacāradarśana
mapyasti pratyakṣeṇobhayabhāgānullekhāt  tat kimatra svābhāvikopādhikavādaprakṣepeṇa
vibhāgena  gamakatvaṃ ca sāmagrayāḥ kāraṇatvādekaṃ kāraṇamanyāpekṣameva janakamityaniyamaḥ 
kāryaṃ tu sāmagrīniyatatvena pratyekaṃ niyatamiti tadeva liṅgaṃ na kāraṇamiti siddham 
aāgnerindhanasannidhau dhūmadarśanād viśeṣoddeśenaiva siddha upādhirindhanam  dhūmasya
punaragninā sambandhe tadupādhirbhavan dṛśya eva bhavet anupalabdhastu nāstītyucyate 
tat kimindhanameva paramupādhiryena dṛśyatāniyamaḥ sambandhe hi vivakṣyate apekṣaṇīya
marthāntaraṃ svabhāvaviśeṣa eva copādhirabhidheyaḥ  na cārthāntaraṃ dṛśyatāniyatam  tataśca
dhūmasyāpi hutāśena saha sambandhe syādupādhiḥ na copalakṣyata iti kathamadarśanānnāstyeva
yataḥ svābhāvikasambandhasiddhi 
atha yadyapekṣaṇīyamarthāntaraṃ syāt kathaṃ dhūma ityeva pāvakasya sattāniyama iti
cet  nanvidameva cintyate kiṃ dhūme sati avaśyamagniḥ sambhavī na veti 
kadācidarthāntaramupādhimapekṣya dhūmo'pi syāt nāgniriti kimatra niṣṭaṅkakāraṇam 
tasmāt pāvakaparādhīnodayo dhūmaḥ pariniṣṭhataḥ kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi bhāvaṃ svīkuryādityeva
sādhu  asiddhā a ceyamupādhyanupalabdhiḥ yathā hi dahano nendhanena vinā dhūmena
saṃbadhyate tathā dhūmo'pi na tena vinā'gniā saṃbadhyata iti samānamupādhitva
atha siddhasyāgnerindhanasāhityena dhūmalābha ityupādhivyavasthā
asiddhasya tu dhūmasya tannimittātmalābhatayā tadavyabhicārāt svābhāvikaḥ sthāpyata iti
cet  evamapi saiva tadutpattirāyātā saiva ca svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ  na ca yathokta
mānasādigrāhyaḥ  na copādhidṛśyānupalabdhibādhya ityaupādhikaśaṅkāyāṃ na vipakṣānni

vyāpticarcā
vācaspatye tu prabandhe'gnerdhūmena saṃbandhe indhanamupādhidṛśya ukta eva  dhūmasya tu
vahninā sambandhe svābhāvikatvamupādheranupalabdhimātreṇa ca bādhaḥ  tatra ca kacid
vyabhicārasyādarśanāditi hetuḥ  tatredamālocyate kimayaṃ heturupādhyanupalabdhisādhakaḥ
atha saivāsya sādhikāyaṃ svābhāvikatvasya bhūtānupalabdheradāṭhyaṃśaṅkayopādhereva bādhakaḥ 
prathame nirupayogaḥ na hi buddherbhāvābhāvī hetvantarasādhyau svasaṃvedyavedanāntarasvabhāva
tvāt  nāsti copādherupalabdhiriti siddhevānupalabdhiḥ  evaṃ vyabhicārādarśane'pi
hetvanupayogo vācyaḥ  vyavahārasādhanamupayoga iti cet na vimaterabhāvāt
apratītimātrasya siddhatvāt  tṛtīyo'pi na yuktaḥ  ekasthā dṛśyaviśeṣaṇarahitāyā
niṣedhasādhanāśaktau dvitīyasyāḥ kīdṛśī śakti  vyabhicāro dṛśya eva vivakṣita iti
cet  tarhi na sarvatra sarvadā vā  tataśca na kacid vyabhicāra ityataḥ svābhāvika
tvamayuktam  kacit tu na dṛṣṭo vyabhicāra ityevaṃ tatkalpanamanalasyāpi dhūmena prasajyeta 
caitramaitrādīnāṃ vā parasparam  sati caivaṃ svābhāvikasambandhe'pyanāśvāsa ityāyātam 
tasmāt sarvatraivāvyabhicāra paryeṣaṇīyaḥ  tato'numānaviṣaye'pi yāvanna sādhyaṃ
pratyakṣeṇopasthāpayati tāvannāvyabhicāraṃ pratīyāditi kṛtamanumānena  kiṃ ca tadutpatti
vādeṣyaṃyā dhūmasyānekāntaparihārāya svābhāvikavāda āśritaḥ anekāntaśca vyabhicārā
śaṅkayā  tataḥ svābhāvikatvāvyabhicāraḥ sarvatra  sarvatrāvyabhicārāca svābhāvika
tvamitītaretarāśrayaḥ  yasya tu sakṛdekajāteranyajātyadhīnotpattipratītireva sarvatrā
vyabhicārapratītiḥ tasya nāyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ bhūyodarśanāpekṣāyāmeva tadavatārasya nyāyaprāpta
tvāt  yathā hyekadā darśane śaṅkāyāmanyāpekṣā tathānyadāpi śaṅkāpekṣā  parasparākṛṣṭa
eva sarvatra darśanākṣepaḥ  yadi tu tatrāpi vārasaṃkhyāniyamaṃ darśayet yathāsmākam 
prāgadṛṣṭī kramāt paśyan vetti hetuphalasthitim 
b dṛṣṭau vā kramaśo'paśyannanyathātvena ca sthitiḥ 
iti pratyakṣānupalambhayorvāratrayaniyamo'vayave samudāye tvekavārasya tadā tāvataiva

tadaśakyatve ca na kacidanumānamayaṃ kuryāditi lakṣaṇaśāstramanarthakam  smaraṇe tu

pra vā  
iti durlaṅghayametattadutpattyanāśrayaṇe  na caivaṃ prāmāṇikalokamaryādātikramopālambhaḥ  na hi
pramāṇagocare kaścidaniścayamācaṣṭe pramāṇābhāve vā niścayam yathā bhavānupādherbādhika
pramāṇābhāve'pyabhāvaniścayam  ata eva na saṃśayapiśācasya sarvatrāvakāśa pramāṇābhāva
evānumatatvāt  pramāṇaviṣaye'pi kiñcivaktuṃ śakyata iti cet  yadi mukhamastīti
vaktavyamucyatām  kevalaṃ yadi svīkṛtapramāṇadharmo vakti tadā sudānamuttaram  athetaraḥ
tadetareṇaiva vaktavyam nāsmākamavasaraḥ  svīkṛtapramāṇasya hi niścayaphalatvāt
pramāṇasyāvipratipannapramāṇaviṣaye niścayasvīkāranāntarīyaka eva tatsvīkāraḥ kathaṃ sarvatra
śaṅkāpiśācī labdhāvakāśā bhavet  kevalaṃ tvatpraṇītalakṣaṇaṃ na pramāṇamiti brūhi 
tacca vicāryamāṇameva vartate  athādṛśyamāno'pyupādhidhūme śamayata iti prāmāṇika
lokayātrātikrama iti cet na prāmāṇikairevāyogyānupalabdherbādhādhikārapratiṣedhāt 
anyatheśvarasvargasādhanāderdatto jalāñjaliḥ  anumānāgamapramāṇasiddhernāyaṃ doṣa iti
cet na pūrvamanupalabdhyā bādhite'numānāde sādhakasyāpravṛtteḥ sarvajñasiddhī prasādhita 
tvāt 
tasmāt pūrvāparaparāmarśavivekaphalame tadanupalabdhimātraṃ niścayasādhanamiti 
tataḥ pramāṇaviṣaye saṃśayānavakāśāntrāyaṃ kacitpravartetetyasaṃbaddham  na ca śaṅkatyeva na
pravṛttiḥ arthasaṃśayena pravṛtteranivāryatvāt snigdhānnapānavat  etat tvanarthaka saṃśayenodā
harato'rthānarthaṃ saṃśayaviṣayo'pyajñāta iti kimataḥ paraṃ vācyam  na caitat prakṛtam
pramāṇavṛttau saṃśayo'stu na vetyasya prakṛtatvāt tatra coktameva  athedamākūtamanekadhā
dhūmasya dhāmanyavyabhicāradarśanāt kadācit tadantareṇa dhūmo bhaveditīyamanarthaśaṅkā 
sā ca nivṛtyaṅgamiti tāmavadhūya svābhāvikasambandhabodha eva vidhīyatāmityarthaḥ 
yathānnapāne maraṇaśaṅkāṃ nirasya pravṛttireveti  yadyevamarthasaṃśayo'pi pravṛttyaṅgamiti yuktam 
bhūyaḥ sāhityadarśanādavyabhicāra eva b hi prāyika annapāne jīvanavat  athedṛśa
manarthasaṃśayameva brūma iti cet  sa tarhi pravartaka eva  tat kathaṃ nāyaṃ kacit pravarteta
ityucyate  kathaṃ vānarthakasaṃśayo'pi nivṛtyaṅgam  etacca kadācid vyabhicāre'pi
samānam kādācitkādānamānavayācanavaditi sādhvī dhūmasya svābhāvikasambandha
siddhiḥ  yathādṛṣṭāśaṅkanaṃ ca prāgeva pratipāditam  ataeva viśeṣetyādi siddhasādhanam

bādhājñāne tvanutpanne nāśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā
tula lo vā 
iti  yadhulikhyamānasyārthasya bādhajñānamutpannaṃ sādhakaṃ vā pramāṇam tadā śaṅkāyāḥ
kāvakāśa  tasyāḥ saṃśayarūpatvāt sādhakabādhakasya caikāntāvasāyasādhanatvāt 
athendriyeṣu timirādibādhajñānānutpattirvivakṣitā tadaprastutam  na hi dhūmādī svarūpasyā
siddhirāśaṅkitā kiṃtu vyāpteriti 
ko vā'rtho niṣpramāṇikā iti yadi sādhakapramāṇaviraha iṣṭaḥ tat kiṃ śaṅkāyāḥ 
yad vā śaṅkayollikhyamānasyārthasya tasyāpi tatraivānyatra vā  anyatrāpi sajātīye
anyamātre vā  prathamapakṣastāvanna prastāvānurūpaḥ  bhavatu vā tathāpi tadanyajñāne
sādhanamekārdhasamavetaṃ mānasamarthāpattiḥ svasaṃvedanaṃ vā tanna kṣīṇamasyā  śaṅkitasya
prastute sādhakapramāṇābhāvastu śaṅkāsādhaka evetyuktam  anyatra sajātīyena pramāṇā
bhāvasya tvayamarthaḥ yad dhūme vahnayanāyattatvaṃ śaṅkayate tat tajjātīye pramāṇena
nāvagatam tatra vyaktyapekṣayā tajjātīyatvam jātyapekṣayā vā  vyaktyapekṣayā
tāvad dhūmāntarameva tajjātīyam  yadi ca tatra citrabhānunānāyattiḥ pramitā tadā
vyabhicārādeva vyāptibahiṣkṛto dhūmaḥ sādhāraṇānaikānto zāta iti kimatra sandigdha
vipakṣavyāvṛttikatvārthaṃ śaṅkāvatāraṇena  apramitāyāmapi vahnayanāyattāvavyabhicārādeva
ki śaṅkayeti cet  adarśanamātreṇa vyabhicārasyābhāvāsiddheḥ yogyānupalabdherevābhāva
sādhane'dhikārāt  tato bahulaṃ sahacāramātre vyabhicārī nāvyabhicārī niścita iti
śaṅkāvakāśaḥ  jātyapekṣayā tu dhūmajāteranyaiva jāti kayācid dravyādipratyāsattyā
sajātīyā tato'bhimatapakṣopanipāte jalādau vyabhicāradaśaṃna muktameva  yuktaścāyameva
pakṣaḥ  dhūme vyāpticintāyāṃ deśakālāntaraviprakṛṣṭaṃ dhūmamekīkṛtyaiva nirṇayaprakramāt
jātyantara eva śaṅkaṣamānadarśanamanurūpam tāvatāpi smṛteranubhavapūrvatvāpracyuteriti 
prathamapakṣādanyatrāvācakaṃ cedamakṣaraṃ tatra cānupayuktamiti yatkiñcidetat 
ajātabādhakotprekṣiṇa saṃśayātmatvamapi bālavilapitameva  bādhotprekṣaṇaṃ
hi niścayātmatayā saṃśaya viruddhamityuktam na hyaniścayaphalaṃ bādhakaṃ vā  tato yatra
sadabhāvaḥ a tatra naḥ saṃśaya iti kathaṃ sarvavyavahāreṣu tadātmakatvam  atha

eva
noṣa buṃdhādhīnatvasya dhūme bādhakamutprekṣate ya iti vivakṣitam ki tu vahnayapratibaddhatvasaṃśaya
'vyāptiniścayasya virodhād bādhaka ukta ityevaṃ neyam  tathāpyutprekṣeteti viruddham 
vikalpanaṃ hyatprekṣārthaḥ na ca saṃśayasyaiva vikalpātmano vikalpanaṃ nāma prastutam 
jananaṃ tu yuktam  tadāpyajātaviśeṣaṇamapārthakam jātasyotpādanārthāsaṅgateḥ  athā
jātamabhūtamasatyamapi śaṅkayamānamanagnyadhīnatādikaṃ prameyaṃ svaviruddhabādhakamutprekṣeta
svakalpanāmātreṇodbhāvayedityarthaḥ tadāpi tadasatyatvaṃ kenacit pramāṇena prasādhya yadyevaṃ
brūyātu sarvaṃ śobheta  na cākrośādanyadasti sādhanamasya sāhasikasya
yadi ca
yathāprasiddhātiriktamabhyūhata evākrośapātratvam tadā darśanādarśanamātraprasiddhe vyāpti 
vāde vipakṣavṛttiśaṅkāmapākartuṃ svābhāvikasambandhādikamabhyūhamānasyāpi kiṃ na tattvam 
tasyāpi vā sambandhasya mānasagrāhyatvabādhaka mindriyagrāhyatvaṃ vadataḥ sarvajñabādhakāni
vā jñeyatvādīni  yathā prasiddhorvasyādiśabdārthabādhakaṃ vā pā  tryādyarthaṃ bruvataḥ kiṃ
vā bhūyo bauddhīyaśaṅkāsannipātaśātanamīdṛśamākrośasādhanamananyaśakyamūhitavato'syaiva
prathamaṃ kṣayagamanamucitam 
J
saṃśayotthāpakasya tadiṣṭamiti cet  nanu saṃśayasthāpi pūrvamajātasyaivotthāpanād
bhraṣṭaḥ tataḥ sādhakabādhakopanītaniścayasyāpyajātasyotthāpanāt kiṃ na duṣṭaḥ  pramāṇa
balānniścayo durlaṅghya iti cet  tadabhāve tarhi saṃśayo'pi durlaṅghaya ityalamativisā
riṇyā kathayā  tataḥ pūrvāparaparāmarśena pramāṇaviṣayādanyatra saṃśayodbhāvanaṃ kathaṃ mohāditya
nunmatto bhāṣate  pramāṇapratibaddho hi niścayo yadi tadabhāve'pi bhavet kimarthaṃ yatnena
pramāṇānveṣaṇaṃ prekṣasya tadvipratipattinirākaraṇāya vā śramaḥ śāstrakārāṇām  tasmāt
pramāṇāpāye niyatamāyātaḥ saṃśayaḥ kathamaniṣṭimātreṇa nirākartuṃ śakyaḥ  yadyapyevaṃ
tathāpi gatyantaravirahāt saṃvyavahāre prāyaḥ sahacāradarśanātū adarśanācca sakṛdapi

na saṃśayaḥ

svargādyarthino vedeśvarādyanuvartanaṃ niyamena vācyam brahmavadhāderapi tallābhaprasaṅgāt

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
āyāte niścayasya siddhatvād gatyantarābhāvo'siddhaḥ b tamantareṇa svābhāvika
sambandhasiddherapyanāśrayatvāt  yattu yatnenānviṣyanta ityādi tatrāpi vyabhicārānve
ṣaṇamevopādhyanveṣaṇaṃ vidmaḥ  vyabhicāramantareṇopādhivyavasthāyā aśakyatvāt  tato
yāvad dhūmadarśanam tāvad vyabhicāraśaṅkayopamṛdya nirūpaṇāparyavasāne gatamanumānenetyukta
prāyam  anyathā yatnenānviṣyamāṇā ityasya ko'rtha  katipayavārāvyabhicāragocarīkaraṇe
hi paratra kīdṛśī nirvṛtiḥ 
yadapi sthādetaditi valgitaṃ tadapi niḥsāram  pramāṇasiddhe hi rūpe svabhāvāva
lambanam  na tu svabhāvavādabalenaiva vasturūpavyavasthā  tad yadi niyata viṣayānvaya
vyatirekagrāhakapratyakṣānupalambhapramāṇasiddhe hetuphalabhāve svabhāvavādaḥ tat kimāyātaṃ
svābhāvikasambandhe  yatra tadutpattipratītisāmagrīṃ hṛdayena dūrīkṛtyānyataḥ sahacarita
dvayāviśeṣapratītau pratītyupāya eva davīyān tatsāmagrathapekṣaṇe ca tadutpattireva sā 
kimāhopuruṣikayā nāmāntarakaraṇena  atrāntare bhūyodarśanajanitasaṃskārasahāyendriyeṇa
grahaṇaparyantaṃ pūrvadūṣaṇenaiva nirastam 
yaccāyaṃ saṃśayasya viśeṣadarśanāpekṣayā
sāmānyadarśanādviśeṣādarśanādviśeṣasmṛteśca
saṃśayaḥ 
vai sū   
iti lakṣaṇakṣati saṃśayamanicchan utkalayati tatra kiṃ lakṣaṇakṣatibhayāt pramāṇāviṣaye
dvayākārabuddhacaiva na bhāvyam utaśvit dvayākāratve'pi nāsau saṃśaya ityabhimatam
atha tattvataḥ saṃśayo bhavatu mā vā vayaṃ tu saṃśayatvena vyavaharāmo'smallakṣaṇakṣayāditi
pakṣāḥ  prathamastāvadasambhavī vikalpollekhitasya rūpasya sādhakabādhakayorekāntasādhana
yorabhāve śvaḥ priyāgamanavārtādivat ki satyametanna vetyubhayāṅgollekhivikalpa
janmano rājājñayāpi niṣeddhumaśakteḥ  śakyante hi kāyavāgvyavahārā anyādṛśe'pi cetasi
balādeva bhayādinānyathā kartum na tu cittavivartaḥ pramāṇāpramāgadvārāyātaḥ  etat
tu syāt  bhūyasaikabhāgasyopalambhāt paripuṣṭa iva so'ṅgaḥ parisphurati ekāntāśaktestvanyo
bhāga kṣīṇa iva tādṛksāmagrīvirahe punarubhayo'pi sādhāraṇaḥ  yathā tatra veśmani
kākaḥ kimasti nāsti veti dvayākāratāpi kāpi nāpaiti  sa eva saṃśayārtha iti
dvitīyo'pyayuktaḥ  anyathā niścayākārābhyāṃ bhrāntisamyagjñānābhyāṃ bhidyamāno
vyāpticarcā
yadi na saṃśayastat kiṃ turīyo rāśireṣaḥ tatastamagṛhṇato lakṣaṇasyaivāyamastu doṣa na
lakṣyamanyathākartuṃ śakyam  ata evāntimo'pi nopayogī  ubhayabhāgāvalambi saṃvedanaṃ
cedekāntakriyāmapekṣamāṇaṃ siddham tāvataiva svābhāvikasambandhāsiddheḥ kimatrabhavataḥ
sandehavyavahārāpekṣayā ityalaṃ bālavāditayā 
mānasadūṣaṇe tu siddhasādhanamevāstu kimatrāpi pariśrameṇa  svabhāvapratibandhe
tu gamakatvaṃ a siddhasādhanameva  sa tu tadutpattilakṣaṇa eveti sthāpitam  evaṃ ca
bhūyodarśanasāmarthyakadarthanāt tatsahāyāni mānāntarāṇi pratyakṣaviṣayasvabhāvaprati
bandhasiddhaye bandhyāni boddhavyāni  viparyayabādhakameva tu pramāṇamanumānamunneyam
tadabhāve vipakṣavṛttiniṣedhasyāśakyatvāt tatputratāyā iva śyāmatve  yat punaratra
annapānapariṇatibhedasyopādherbhāvāt svābhāvikasambandha vaidhuryamuttaram tanna yuktam
āhārapariṇatibhedasyopādhitvaniścayābhāvāt  yathā hi dahanamātrādanindhanānna dhūma
iti dhūmena vaḥ sambandhi indhanamupādhirucyate tathā yadi maitrajanitasyāpi kasyacid
vivakṣitāhārapariṇāmaviraheṇa śyāmatopālapsyate sa upādhiniraceṣyata tadā kimupādhi 
vādena vyabhicārādeva na maitraputratvaṃ gamakamitīyataiva paryāptatvāt  na caivaṃ śakyam 
tat kathamasāvupārdhiniścita  kiṃśvinmaitrasyaiva janmāntarapraṇidhānāt saptāṣṭāpi
dṛśyamānāḥ śyāmatanavaḥ sūnavo na jātā kimatra pramāṇam  tadvat tarhi māturapi

vyāpticarcā
yadā tu dhūme tadutpattireva vyāptisādhanī bhedābhāvāt na tu pārthive

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
bhavavikalpayośca sādhāraṇamiti pratyakṣaviṣayīkṛte hetuphalabhāve mānasavyavahārasvabhāvo'pi

 bhedābhedaparīkṣā 
  namo buddhāya

aprakṛtameva kiñcit 
tatra prathamapakṣe yāveva bhedābhedī pṛthagdoṣajālakavalitau tāvevāmū ekavastu

anyatve'pi taddūṣaṇavad guṇasyāpyananuvṛtteḥ  api nāma bhedapakṣabhāvi pṛthakpratītiprasaṅga
dūṣaṇamabhedamupagacchan parihariṣyāmīti bhede'pyabhedasvīkārastatra bhavataḥ  yadi ca sa
evābhedaḥ pṛthagupalabdhibādhano'dhunāpyupanītaḥ syādevaṃ tatparihāraḥ kevalamekayogakṣema
samāveśāt pramāṇāntarāvṛttimapyākarṣat  tato yadyanyatayaināṃ nākarṣet tata eva
pṛthagupalabdhiniṣedhanamapi na sādhayet  athābhedasya pṛthagupalabdhibādhava phalaṃ na
śabdāntarāvṛttisvābhāvyāt tathāpi dvaitābhyupagamo viphalaḥ  evaṃ bhedapakṣe'pi vācyam 
atha pṛthagupalabdhibādheva phalamabhedasya śabdāntarāvṛttinivṛttistu bhedasyaiva tenāpi hi
saṃbhavinā svakāryamarjanīyameva  evaṃ bhedasthāpi pramāṇāntarāpekṣeva phalaṃ pṛthagupa
labdhibādhā tvabhedasyeti

guṇaḥ  tatredānīṃ bhedena śabdāntaravṛttimātramātanvatā sthātavyam  dvitīye tu kārye

prāyānuvidhānam 
ataeva na dvitīyo'pi vikalpa  astu vaiṣamye'nunayādiḥ sa punarātmopakārāpa

nāsthīyata ityuktaprāyam

vṛttimādhāya yāvat pratibhāsabhedamādhātumupakramate tāvadevābhedenopaniyatatā pratibadhyata

hyekasvabhāvapratibaddhatve yuktamevam  tatrāpi niyato guṇadoṣābhimatakāryaṃkaraṇakramaḥ

cetayata ityupekṣāmarhati  na hi tadicchātiriktamatra kāraṇamākalayāmaḥ  api ca yadā
bhedasya paścād bhedābhyupagamaḥ tadā pṛthagupalabdhi bādhamānasyābhedasya dvitīyaṃ kāryaṃ

bhedābhedaparīkṣā
tvād bhedābhedayorekapratiniyataḥ parihāra svīkāro vetyanibandhanametat  tataḥ pṛthak

na copādherupādhimaṃto bhedenānubhavagandho'pi samasti  vyaktivināśe vā vināśaleśo'pi
na sāmānyasyābhyupeyate paraiḥ 
vyaktirūpeṇeṣyata eveti cet  nanu vyaktirūpeṇeti na nijena rūpeṇeti
vivakṣitam anyathā viśeṣaṇānarthakyāt  nijasyaiva rūpasya bhedābhedacintāyāmayaṃ

pādaprasārikāyā b aparihārāt  pariśramātiśayastvatiricyate āhopuruṣikā

miti 
prayogaḥ yad yanmātranimittaṃ tat tasmin sati bhavatyeva yathā cakṣurādi

vedye yatra hi yanmatiniyamata a syādvā na vā tasya dhī
riṣṭā no'nupalabdhiranyavirahajñāna sthiterāśrayaḥ 
yatra vedyamāne yasya matiḥ syāditi deśakālasvabhāvaviprakarṣāṇāṃ niṣedha  niyame
neti upalambhakāra kāntaravaikalyasya  etena dṛśya viśeṣaṇaprāptasya bhāvajñāna sthitiriti
darśitam  ato na sarvasya niṣedhaprasaṅgaḥ  yatra ca vedyamāne yanmatiniyamena syāt
tasyaiva dhīriṣṭā'nyasya dvitīyasyābhāvaniścaya prabandhākṣepāya kṣameti  etena na virahamātram
