rekidvitīyanāmno viśeṣasiddhiḥ  tathā hi tanubhuvanādyabhijñaḥ kartā nānityāsarvaviṣaya
buddhimānu tatkartustadupādānādyanabhijñatvaprasaṅgāt  na hyevaṃvidhastadupādānādyabhijño
dṛṣṭo yathāsmadādiḥ tadupādānādyabhijñaścāyam  tasmāt tatheti  no khalu paramāṇu
bhedān pratikṣetrajñasamavāyinaśca karmāśayabhedānaparimeyānanyaḥ śakto jñātumṛte tādṛśā
dīśvarāditi jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
vittokastu yathā dhūmadarśanena pakṣadharmatābalāt nikuñjavatitvaṃ vaviśeṣo'vyā
pako'pi pratīyate tathā karturapītyadoṣa iti tādṛgeva puruṣaviśeṣa īśvara b pramāṇa
siddha iti kathamanīśajagadvādino bhagavataḥ pramāṇenāvyāhataśāsanatvamiti 
 īśvaravādādhikāre pūrvapakṣasaṃkṣepa samāptaḥ 
 īśvaravādādhikārai saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam 
vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyāpekṣaprabandhabhīrūṇām 
īśvaravāde dūṣaṇamātrakatheyaṃ samāsena 
iha yadyapi bahulaṃ sahacāramātraṃ kāryasya prayatnavatā darśitam darśitaśca tadabhāve
kacidabhāvaḥ tathāpi pratibandhāsiddheḥ kāryamapi syāt naca buddhimatkartṛpūrvaka mityā
śaṅkā bādhavaidhuryāt kāryaṃ buddhimati sādhye sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttiko hetvābhāsaḥ  na
ca sapakṣavipakṣayodarśanādarśanamātreṇa sādhanasya bhāve sādhyasyāvaśyambhāvaḥ sādhyā
bhāve vā tadabhāva ityevaṃ rūpāyā vyāpteḥ pratibandhaśabdavācyāyā  sādhanaṃ bhavitumarhati
 bhāvivyabhicāradarśaneṣvapi tathopalabdheḥ  kimidamidānīmadarśanamabhāvādeva vyabhicārasya
atha darśanasāmagrīsamavadhānavirahāditi nirṇetumaśakyameva sahacāramātradarśino
vimarśaśīlasya 
ata eva vācaspateḥ svābhāvikasambandhaghoṣaṇamapi śabdapuṣṭimātram tadatiriktārthā
poṣaṇāt  bhūyodarśane hi vyabhicārādarśane svābhāvikavyavasthā  vyabhicārādarśanaṃ ca
vipakṣe'darśanamātramuktaṃ bhavati  yat punaretadupāgheranupalambhena vyabhicārāsiddhiriti tatra
nopādhirnāma dṛśyacihnasthānīyaṃ kiñcidasti yadanupalambho'vyabhicāraṃ vyavahārayet  kiṃtu
vyabhicāradarśanamātreṇaiva tatparikalpaḥ  tadadarśanāt ca svābhāvikatvamiti viśeṣābhāvāt
na svābhāvikavādena kiñcit sādhyena saha bhūyo dṛṣṭo heturvyabhicāre ca na heturitīyataiva
paryāptatvāt  etacca sarva vyāpticarcāyāṃ vivicya kacidarthāntarasya pratibandho nāma
tadutpattimantareṇa sā ca pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanaiveti vyavasthāpitamiti tata evāvadhāryam 
etena śaṅkaravācaspatimatāvalambina pratyuktāḥ 
astu tarhi prayatnavatāpi kāryasya tadutpattilakṣaṇa evaṃ pratibandho dhūmasyeva
vahninā  yathoktaṃ vittokena  tathā hi kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk mṛtpiṇḍadaṇḍa
cakrādiṣu satsvapi kāryaṃ kumbhākhyamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhaṃ tadvyāpārānantaram
upalabhyata iti hetuphalabhāvasiddhau kuto vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ  satyamatra pakṣavipakṣa
vṛttireva na sandehaḥ atra hi pratyakṣānupalambhayogyasvarūpasvīkārādabhivyakto'nupalabdha
puruṣavyāpārairvṛkṣavīraṇādibhirvyabhicāraḥ  pakṣīkṛtāstṛṇādayaḥ na ca pakṣīkṛtenaiva
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
vyabhicāra iti cet na pratikṣiptasya pakṣīkaraṇe nyāyābhāvāt  anyathā anuṣṇo'gniḥ
prameyatvādityādāvapi pakṣīkaraṇameva śaraṇaṃ syāt  tathā hi
sandigdhe hetuvacanād vyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ 
pra vā  
iti nyāya  adhyakṣameva pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogyantarāpekṣayānupalabdhirucyate  a
tato'nupalabdhibādhitamapi pratyakṣabādhitameva  vyavahārasādhanāpekṣayā tu sānumānam 
na cānumāna bādhite'pyanyāvakāśaḥ  sā tarhi dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpannasyaivābhāvaṃ vyavahārayati
dṛśyādṛśyaśarīretarasādhāraṇaṃ ca buddhimattvamiti dṛśyatāniyamānupapatterbuddhimataḥ katham
anupalabdhimātreṇa tṛṇādijanmani niṣedhaḥ  tataḥ sandehāta pakṣīkaraṇaṃ nyāyyamiti
cet  tadetad vikrotagavīrakṣaṇam  vyāptisādhanāyādhyakṣānupalabdhyoravakāśadānādeva
dṛśyaviṣayatāsvīkārasya prasahyāyātatvāt  na hyadṛśye pratyakṣamanvayasādhanamanupalabdhirvā
vyatirekasādhanī bhavitumarhati  tadayaṃ bhede satyanvayavyatirekarūpamadhyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ
hetuphalabhāvamavataranna dṛśyatāmativartituṃ sādhyasya śaktaḥ  dṛśyatve ca niyatatṛṇādinā
vyabhicāra iti sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ 
atha vyabhicāracamatkārādadhyakṣāgocareṇa
prayatnavatā vyāpti gṛhṇīyāt 
gṛhṇātu na tu pratyakṣānupalambhāśrayaḥ śreyānasya  nanu dṛśyādṛśya viśeṣaṇamanapekṣya prekṣā
vanmātreṇa vyāptigrahaḥ  naivam tāvatāpi hi pratyakṣakṛtāyā vyāpteranavakāśa eva 
dṛśyaikasvabhāvaniyatā hi sā kathaṃ dṛśyāvṛśyaviṣavā bhavet  taddhi dṛśyamadṛśyaṃ ca
rūpame kabuddhimatvādidharmānuvṛttāvapi svabhāvaviprakarṣetarābhyāmatyantaṃ bhinnajātiḥ  tataḥ
pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyekajātisvīkāreṇa pravṛttamitaravārtānabhijñaṃ tadviśiṣṭameva sādhāraṇamapi dharmaṃ
vyāpakamādarśayati 
VI
yadyapi deśakāla viprakṛṣṭamapi na dṛśyam tathāpi ta da darśanayogyatayaikajātye
veti svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭasyaiva pratyakṣeṇa parihāraḥ  sarvānyavarjane hi svalakṣaṇaikaparyavasā
nād vyāptireva na syāt dhūmāgnivat kampamārutavañca  yathā hi svapravṛttiyogyajvalad
bhāsurākārapuraskāreṇa pravartamānādhyakṣakṛtā vyāptiḥ saptāciṣi na jaṭharānalasādhāraṇa
rūpaparyavasāyinī anyathā tārṇādibhedavadabhimate'pi rūpe sandihāno na tatsādhyārtha
kriyālābhaikāgrabuddhiḥ pravarteta  pratibandhavaikalyavad vāsati jaṭharyatva ityāmṛśataḥ
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
pravṛttiḥ syāt  yathā vā pallavollāsane samīraṇena vyāptiradhyakṣajakṛtāspṛśyarūpapuraskā
rānnastimitamārutasādhāraṇarūpaparyavasāyinī anyathādyāpi kisalayakampena mātari
śvānamanumāpayan spṛśyaprabhañjanānurūpapravṛttinivṛttī niścayenācaret tathā puruṣe'pi
pratyakṣakṛtā vyāpitāgṛhītiradṛśyarūpaparihāreṇaiva  tasmāt pratyakṣāvyājena yadi
paramiṣṭamātrameva sādhanaṃ nādhyakṣaṃ dṛśyādṛśyasāmānye'pīti vyāpterabhāvāt sandigdha
vipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva 
prayogaḥ yo yaḥ pratyakṣakṛtaḥ b kāraṇatvaniścayaḥ nāsau dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyava
sāyī yathāgnau jaṭharajātajātavedaḥsādhāraṇarūpaṃ pariharan  pratyakṣakṛtaścāsau buddhimatīti
vyāpakaviruddhavyāptopalabdhiḥ  pratyakṣakṛtatvaṃ hi dṛśya viṣayatvena vyāptamadṛśye tasyā
pravṛtteḥ taduviruddhaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviṣayatvam tadvyāptaṃ dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyitvam 
ki ca yadi dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇamavadhūya dhīmanmātreṇa vyāpti vivakṣitā evaṃ sati yadā
buddhimadabhāve kumbhakāryasyābhāvamupadarśayed vyatirekapratipādanāya tadā dṛśyādṛśya
viśeṣaṇarahitacetanamātrasyābhāva kena pramāṇena siddhaḥ dṛśyānupalabdheśyasyaiva
pratiṣedhe'dhikārāt  anyathā tṛṇādinā vyabhicārasyāśakyaparihāratvācca 
na
ca dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhirbuddhimanmātrasya vyatirekabodhasādhanībhavitum
arhati ātyantikaviṣayabhedasya vyaktatvāt  anyathā tṛṇādijanmanyapi dṛśyapuruṣa
viṣayaivānupalabdhistadvayabhicāra sthirīkaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt  na hi lābhe praveśaśchede
niḥsaraṇamiti nyāyyam  tasmād dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpoḍhapakṣe vyāptigrahaṇakāle vyatireka
grahaṇopāyābhāvād avyāpteḥ punarapi vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ  na ca nabhasyubhayābhāva
vibhāvanamupāyo vyatirekagrahaṇasya kāryābhāvasya buddhimadvayāpārābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayā
nupapatteḥ  tadaparakāraṇasākalye hi tanmātrābhāve'bhāvaḥ kāryasya tadabhāvaprayuktaḥ
pratyetuṃ śakyaḥ  yathā trikapañcaka cintāyāṃ cintitam  dvayostu kacinnivṛttimātram
akāryakāraṇabhūtayorapi sulabham 
kiṃ ca buddhimatkāraṇavyāpāravirahāt vihāyasi kāryatvābhāva uta kāraṇamātra
viprayogāditi ko niṣṭaṅkaḥ  tathā ca sati viphala  sakalo yatnaḥ  anvayo'pi hi
kāraṇamātreṇa kāryamātrasya gṛhyatāmutasvit puruṣaviśeṣaṇena kāraṇeneti sandeha eva 
atha dṛṣṭa evāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ dhūme dahanātmavatu  yadyevaṃ dṛśyaśarīra
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
rūpo'pi viśeṣaḥ pratīta eva kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ citrabhānorbhāsurākāravat  sa tarhi
viśeṣaḥ kāryeṇa vyabhicaryaṃta iti cet  vyabhicayaṃtām  kārye'pi kāraṇavad yathā
paridṛṣṭaviśeṣaniṣṭha evānvayo bhavatu ghaṭavat saudhādāvapi dṛṣṭatvāditi kiṃ naśchinnam 
etaccānvayamātraṃ gajanimolitena dūṣaṇamavadhīryābhidhoyate  vastutastu pratyakṣānupa
lambhayorekasyāpi vyāpārāyogānnānvayo na vyatirekaḥ  asti ca kāryatva murvīdharādau
na ca darśanātikrānte kartaryanvayavyatireko spṛśati  tādṛkcetanakṛtetaratvābhyāṃ ca
rāśyantarābhāvād gandhādivadasādhāraṇānekānta eva  tasmānna pratyakṣeṇa kāryamātrasya
vyāptigrahaṇamiti siddham 
a yātāścaivaṃ yadamī pratyakṣānupalambhāviśiṣṭakāryaṃ jātyullekhenaiva kārya
kāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravṛttayo na kāryamātrollekhena  tathā hi pratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttisama
nantaramīdṛśāt jvaladbhāsurasvarūpavastuviśeṣādīdṛśaṃ dhavalimaliptakaṇṭhāmbakavikārakāri
vastu jāyata ityanenākāreṇa hetuphalabhāvavyavahāraḥ sarvāpara
kāryakāraṇajātivyudāsena
viśiṣṭameva jātiyugmamullikhan pravartate  iyameva gatiḥ sarvatra hetuphalabhāvavyavahṛtau
īśvarānurodhāt tu prasiddhanyāyollaṅghanametat  iti paśyāmaḥ 
kaḥ punaratrāparādho yadi tārṇādibhedamudasya vahninā dhūmamātrasyeva bhūdharādi
bhedamapyudasya kāryamātrasya buddhimatā vyāpti pratīyāt pratyakṣam  yathaiva tarhi varhiṣā
kāryajātiviśeṣasya dhūmasyāvāntarasūkṣmajātimātramantarbhāvya vyāptigraho na tu tadvi
jātīyasparśa tathā buddhimatāpyastu vastrādeḥ  yathā vātyantavisadṛśorapi kāryajātī
antarbhāvya bhūtimanmātrasya cetanena vyāpti jighṛkṣasi tathā vahnināpi gṛhṇīyāḥ 
indriyapratyakṣasyaiva hi vyāpāra ubhayatra kathaṃ bhinnāṃ vṛttimāśrayeta  vyabhicāradarśanā
darśanakṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet  tatrttārha darśanādarśanaṃ saṅkalpamanārūḍhaṃ gacchattṛṇa
sparśavadakiñcitkaramiti tadanurūpavimarśenāvaśyabhāvyam  na cāsti 
na hi kaścidagnidhūmādiṣvanvayavyatirekagrāhipratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttau kāryajātiḥ
akhilānalādutpadyata iti saṅkalpamanubhūya bhūyo vyabhicāradarśanāt yato vā kāryāntarāṇi
vahnimantareṇāpyupalabdhānyupalabhyante vā tato dhūma evānena janyata iti niścayaṃ pari
cinoti kiṃtu jhagityeva pratyakṣānupalambhāntaramasmādagnyāderidaṃ dhūmādīti jāti
viśeṣadvayaṃ hetuphalabhāvavyavahārabhājanī kurvannanubhūyate'nusandhānapratyayaḥ  pratyakṣagocare
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
anvayavyatirekayorna kaścid viśeṣaḥ  yadā ca vikalpāntarasthitasya jhagiti kaṇṭakād
vyathetyanupalambhapūrvikādhyakṣa vihitā hetuphalabhāvagrāhiṇī matiḥ tadābhivyakto vyabhi
cāradarśana vimarśavirahaḥ samasamayāsambhavād vikalpānām  tadihāpyasmāt śilpina
idaṃ pṛthubudhnodarādyākā kāryamityavāntarasūkṣmabhedamudasya vyavahāraḥ  yadā tu paṭa
śakaṭādikamapi puruṣādutpadyamānaṃ paśyati tadedamapīdamapi puruṣeṇa janyata iti
matiravisaṃvādinī samudeti 
kiṃ ca vyabhicāro nāma ki siddhāyāmeva vyāptāvanumānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati 
atha vyāptireva mithyeti vyavasthāpayati  atrāpi pakṣe svasāmarthyena sphuratyeva vyāpti
grāhiṇa pramāṇe  yad vā tasyaiva prāmāṇyakṣayamādadhānaḥ adyāpi sarvatra viṣaye niyate vā 
niyate'pi kimiṣṭivaśāt atha pratyakṣasya tatraiva pravṛtteḥ  prathamaḥ pakṣastāvanna yukto
virodhāt  na hi b sādhyāvinābhāvalakṣaṇā ca vyāptirhetoḥ sādhyābhāva saṃbhavakṛta
śvānumānābhāvaḥ saṅgacchate anyatrāpi vyāptāvanāśvāsācca 
evaṃ vyāptigrāhiṇi pramāṇe prāmāṇyādapracyutibhṛti vyāptimṛṣātvabodhanamapya
sambaddhaṃ boddhavyam  sarvatra ca vyāptigrāhiṇa prāmāṇyakṣaye dhūmādagnirapi nānumātavyaḥ
anyasya vyāptigrāhiṇo'bhāvāt  kimidānīṃ śaraṇamīśvarānumānasya bhaviṣyati 
svecchayā ca niyate viṣaye vyāptivihitau pramāṇaṃ varākamudāsīna miti na kaścit
heturaheturvā tattvataḥ dhūme'pi svecchayā vyāptikhaṇḍanaprasaṅgāt  niyata viṣayatvaṃ tu
vyabhicāragocarasyāpi pratyakṣasya katham yāvatā yathā niyatajātipravṛttaṃ vyāptigrāhi
sarvaviṣayamiṣṭam tathā vyabhicāragocaramapi sarvaviṣayamevānyūnānatiriktaśaktitvād
ubhayo  tadekaviṣaya eva vyāptigraho vyabhicāravedanaṃ ceti kimadhunā sādhanamasādhanaṃ
vā syāt  bhavatu vā bhavaduparodhād bādhabodhina pramāṇasya niyataviṣayatvam 
tathāpi na khalu sakṛdeva vyabhicāravatāṃ bādhabodhaḥ kiṃ tu krameṇa  tadā ca vyabhicāriṇā
mapi vyabhicāradarśanamāhatya nāstīti dhūmasya tato viśeṣābhāvāt punarahetutvam hetutvaṃ
vānyasyāpi 
na ca sarvasyānyasya vyabhicāradarśanairdhūme vyāptiviśvāsa iti vācyam  evaṃ hi
purastāda dhūme vyāptigrahaṇānantarameva parvatanitambe dhūmād dahanānumānaṃ na śārdūlāditi
na syāt vyabhicāradarśana vilambāpekṣaṇāt  aśakyaṃ caitadanyatra vyabhicāradarśanairabhi 
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
mate vyāptiviśrāma iti  vyabhicāraviṣayāṇāmadhyanantatvād deśādiviprakarṣavatāṃ
gocarīkaraṇakālāpekṣayā puruṣāyuṣasya kanīyastvāt  tasmād vyabhicāradarśanavanniyata
viṣaya eva vyāptigraho nirapavādaḥ śuddhekādhyavasāyasya vibhāgena pravṛtteḥ  ataeva ca
svābhāvi kavikalpasyaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇe'dhikāro naupādhikasya 
asti hi śuddhaviṣayajanitālocanājñānamātrāpekṣo bālatiryaksādhāraṇo vikalpaḥ 
sa śuddhaḥ svābhāvika iti cocyate yadvaśāt paśavo'pi kṣutpipāsāpraśamādisādhanāni tatraiva
samarthānyavadhārayantaḥ punastadanvitayā tathaiva tatastatra pravartante nivartante vānanvitayā 
asti ca saṅketasmaraṇasacivālocanājñānajanito vikalpa yathā dīpāt kajjalamā
lokayato nīlamidaṃ rañjanādyapayogītyeva vikalpa pūrvadṛṣṭārthakriyāsmaraṇasahāyānubhavabhā
vitastādṛgaupādhika ucyate  na ca tadā nīlavikalpa ityeva pradīpādakhilaṃ nīlamutpadyata
iti prekṣaḥ kaścinniścinoti  kiṃ tu yadeva kajjalāvalokanamātrānurūpavikalpapuraskṛtaṃ
 a vastu kajjalaśabdasaka tayogya jātiyogāt svarūpaviśeṣād vā tadeva pradīpakāryaṃ
vyabhicārālambane coktam 
evaṃ dhūme'pi dhavalamidaṃ vastu varjāyata iti saṅketānusārī vikalpa aupādhika
evākṣipati kāryatvena tuhinādikam  śuddhe tu vikalpe dhūmajātireva parisphuratīti tata
eva tuhinādervyāptau nirāso na vyabhicārālambanaṃ sādhviti boddhavyam  tadvat kārya
vikalpo'pi sarvatra aupādhika eva  apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi svotpattāvandhaḥ  kārya
miti saṅketasmaraṇasahāyādindriyajñānādutpattiriti na hetuphalabhāvavyavahārasyāṅgam 
tato yadyapi puruṣāt ghaṭodayadarśane ghaṭo'yamasmāditi vikalpavat kāryamidamasmādityapi
sulabho vikalpaḥ tathāpi svābhāvikatvābhāvānna tatpuraskṛtasvarūpasya tatkāryatvavyavasthā 
naisargika vikalpa viṣayīkṛtasya tu bhavatu 
nanu śuddhāvasāyagocare'pi vikalpaḥ saṅketasmṛtijanito dṛśyate'yaṃ ghaṭaḥ pauruṣeya
iti nāmollekhāt  tataḥ so'pyaupādhikaḥ prāptaḥ  na tanmātravikalpane smaraṇasya
aprayojakatvāt vācakāṃśollekha eva tasya sāmarthyāt  yadyapi ca vācyavācakā
kārotkalitākhaṇḍavikalpodaya smaraṇasāhāyakena tathāpyapodvāradvāreṇa tanmātre tad
vyāpāra ucyate mṛnmayatvamātre kulālasyeva  jātyantarasamavāyikāryatvadhavalatādi
dharmakalpanaṃ tu saṅketasambandhagrahaṇādiprācīnavyāpārasmaraṇamantareṇa śuddhādhyavasāyasya
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
tanmātrajātyullekhenaiva kṛtārthatvād bālakādivat atastanmātraviṣayaiva pratyakṣakṛtā
vyāptirityanavadyam  tasmād vyāptigrahaḥ pratyakṣakṛto vyabhicārapratyayo vā bhinnaviṣaya
eveti siddham 
evaṃ tarhi vyabhicāradarśanena sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā duḥstheti cet  eva
metad yadi buddhipāṭavaniyamaḥ sarveṣām  mandabuddhistu sādṛśyādinā jātiviśeṣa
pravṛtte'pi pratyakṣa jātyantareṇaikīkṛtya vyāptigrahābhimānādanumānamātiṣṭhamāna paṭunā
pareṇa vyabhicāramādarśya vyāptidurgrahamāpādyate  ataḥ sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā 
yathā dhūme pravṛtte'pi pratyakṣe vyāptigrāhiṇyucchaladbahalarūpamanalavyāptimanusmaran māruto
ddhṛtadhūlipaṭalādanalamanumāpayan vāṣpodayena prasiddhoṣabudhavedhuryeṇa vyabhicāramādayaṃ
vāryate tato'pi kāraṇāt jātiviśeṣaviṣayaiva vyāptiḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti siddham 
yadi hi dhūmaikajātipratibaddha pratibandhabodhamadhyakṣam tadā sādṛśyāpekṣo'nyatra
tadrūpāropaḥ sadṛśāntaravyabhicāreṇa ca vāraṇaṃ yuktam  yadā tu kāryajātau sarvatra
vyāptigrahaḥ tadā kiṃ sādṛśyāpekṣayeti  yadi tarhi jātiviśeṣapratibaddha evādhyakṣeṇa prati
bandhabodhaḥ kathamatyantavijātīyo'pi tīyā api ghaṭakuṭakuḍyādayaḥ sādhāraṇarāgayogino
b haridrādidravyasaṃskāramanumāpayanti  kathaṃ vā kuṭhārādi cchedakriyāyāṃ dṛṣṭa
vyāpāra karaṇamatyanta vijātīyāpi buddhiḥ kriyātvenānumāpayati 
evamatyantavijātīyā api kailāsakuliśādayaḥ sādhāraṇakāryatvādidharmaṃkāḥ
puruṣamanumāpayiṣyantīti cet  naivam vyāpyasya gamakatvāt tadapekṣayaiva sajātīya
vijātīyatāyāścintyatvāt  vyāpyaṃ ca nirvartyavikāryakarmāpekṣayā dvividhaṃ dharmirūpaṃ
dharmarūpaṃ ca  tatra sarvathāpūrvotpattau dharmiṇo vyāptirucyate dhūmādivat  tadā ca
dhūmāntarameva sajātīyam vijātīyamanyad vastu  yadā tu pūrvaṃsthitasyaiva dharmāntaro
tpattivyavasāya tadā dharmavyāptirucyate payasi auṣṇyādivat tadā ca auṣṇyāntara 
meva sajātīyo dharmaḥ nādhunā dharmijāterapekṣā 
evaṃ rāgo'pi ghaṭakuṭādidravyavejātyamavamatya svayaṃ svajātīya kāryāpekṣayaiva
rāgadravyasaṃskārasya gamakaḥ  ataeva tadviśeṣe kacit kuṅkumasya samparka  kacit haridrā
deranumīyate  na caivaṃ pūrvasthite bhūdharāmbhodharādau kāryatvādimātranirvartakaḥ puruṣa
iṣṭaḥ kiṃ tu kumbhādivadapūrvakotpādaka eva  tadā ca dhūme dhavalatādivat kāryatādayaḥ
MONTSERBA AS Cre
jñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvalau
santo'pi jātyantarasamavāyino dharmā vyāpterbahirbhāvādakiñcitkarā eva  tasmād
dharmivastuvyāptigraho na dharmamātra pratyāsattimanurudhyate  nāpi dharmavyāpterdharmiṇaḥ sa
jātīyatām  śuddhekavimarśāpekṣayā ca sajātīyetaravyavasthānamuktam  nāto rāgavaddhami
vaijātye'pi kāryatvādīnāṃ gamakatvam  anyathā pāṇḍudravyādapi havyāśanānumāna 
prasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ vyabhicārottarasya dūṣitatvāt 
indriye tvevamanumānam  yadanthakāraṇasannidhau kādācitkam tat kāraṇāntarā
pekṣam yathā pāthaḥ pṛthvīsannidhāvaṅkaraḥ viṣayamanaskārālokasannidhau ca kādācitkī
buddhiriti svabhāvahetuḥ  anapekṣatve vipakṣe kādācitkaṃ virodhādanavasthāyīti
bādhakāt vyāptisiddhiḥ  yat tadanyadapekṣyaṃ tadindriyamiti vyavasthā tato na kriyā
tvena kāraṇānumānaṃ nāpi pratyakṣaṃ vyāptigrāhi  avaśyaṃ ca svābhāvika vikalpāmukhī 
kṛtajātibhedapuraskāreṇaiva sāmānyagrahaṇameṣitavyamadhyakṣasya anyathā yadā pratyakṣeṇa
vyāptimekāmupadarthyāyaṃ ghaṭa iti saṅketaḥ kriyate tadā kimasau kāryatvādidharmayogi
viśvamāviśati  vyabhicāradarśanena ca niyataviṣayatāmupanīyate  upadeṣṭhaiva vā sarvānya
jātiṣu niṣedhan viṣayaniyame niṣṭhāpayati  atha sāmānyaviṣaya eva nāsau samaya 
evaṃ vācakajātibhede'pi draṣṭavyam  kāryaśabdastu pratyakṣamanapekṣya vikalpamātra
gocarite parāpekṣodayamātre niveśita iti na viśeṣavṛttiḥ  yadi tu so'pi pratyakṣa
vartinyayaṃ kāryaṃ a iti niveśyeta so'pi tatparyāyāntaravānniyatavṛttireva syāt 
tasmāt kāyajātiviśeṣaviṣayīkaraṇameva nisarga pratyakṣasya  yadi ca kāryajātibhede
pravṛttamapi pratyakṣaṃ kāryamātramadhiṣṭhānīkaroti kāraṇe tarhi pravartamānaṃ kāraṇamātrameva
vyāpakamavadhārayatu kasmādupādānādivedana viśiṣṭamavalambate  tato yadi na bhavadabhi 
prāyānurodho'dhyakṣasyobhayatra sāmānyāvalambinā viśeṣāvalambinā vā bhavitavyamanena
sāmānyālambane kāryāt kāraṇānumānamiti kā vārteśvarasiddheḥ  viśeṣāvalambane ca
kāryamātravyāpterasiddheriti  tasmādanubhavād yuktambha viśiṣṭāmeva kāyajāti hetuviśeṣa
vyāptāmupadarśayati pratyakṣamiti 
prayogaḥ  yad yat kāryakāraṇabhāvagrāhi pratyakṣam tad viśiṣṭajātiprati
niyatavyāpāram yathāgnidhūmayoḥ  tathā cedaṃ buddhimatā kāryasya vyāptisādhanamiti sva
bhāvahetuḥ  nāsyānyathāvyāpārāśaṅkayānekāntaḥ kāraṇānupalabdhibādhitatvāt  kāraṇa
bhedo hi kāryabhedasya kāraṇam anyathā sarvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt  na cāsya kāraṇa
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
bhedo'sti viṣayendriyālokādilakṣaṇasamānasāmagrī prabhavatvāditi  dṛṣṭānte sādhya 
śūnyatāśaṅkāyāṃ ca yad yat pratyakṣam tat tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva sāmānyāvalambanam
yathā vyabhicāragrāhi pratyakṣam pratyakṣaṃ ca vyāptigrāhīti svabhāva eva  sa evānekānta
parihāraḥ  buddhimatkāryayorapi vyāptigrāhiṇi dharmiṇyayameva vā prayogaḥ  athavobhaya
trāpi yad yat sambandhagrāhi pratyakṣaṃ tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva yathā vācyavācakayoḥ
sambandhagrāhi ca pratyakṣaṃ kāryakāraṇayorapi pūrvavat  tadayaṃ yadi tattvataḥ kṛtsno'pi
kāryagrāmaḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaḥ tathāpi kāryajātīnāmatyantavilakṣaṇānāmānantyāt
pratijātibhedaṃ ca vyāptigrahaṇāpekṣaṇāt yāvajjātikaṃ kāryaṃ puruṣapūrvakaṃ paricchinnam
tāvata eva tadanumānamāñjasamiti yuktamuktam
siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi 
tathā ca vahvereva dhūmabhasmāṅgārapākapāradotsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛtiṣu kāryeṣu
yatra yatraiva pratibandhasādhakamadhyakṣaṃ pravṛttam tata eva tadanumānam nānyasmāt  evaṃ
devakulakalasaprāsādasyandanadukūlādiṣu vastuvṛtyā pauruṣeyeṣvapi yajjātīyeṣveva puruṣayopa
labdhirāsīt tajjātikādeva kāryāt tadanumānamanumanyāmahe  dhārādharadharādharādijātau
punastadvyāpārānavadhāraṇāt kānumānavārtā jātivaijātyasyātyantikasya sambhavena
vyāpteragrahāta  gṛhītavyāpteśca kāryasyādarśanāt 
krīḍāparvatakādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumā
nāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam 
kiṃ cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyanti cedīśinaḥ
kā vārtā phalasāmyasaṃvidi kuto he toviśeṣa sthitiḥ 
b iti hyanta raślokaḥ 
kīdṛśī punaḥ kāryajāti prayatnavatā vyāptetyāśaṅkaya tasyā apyānantyāt
saṃkṣepārthamucyate yadṛṣṭerarthakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavatīti  tatra ca kṛtabuddhiriti
na sādhanabuddhiḥ nāpyupādānādyabhijñalakṣaṇaprakṛtasādhyabuddhiḥ kiṃ tu kuvindādisvabhāva
sādhyabuddhiḥ  tadabhāvāñca na sākṣādbhavadīyahetvasiddhiḥ prakṛtasādhyasiddhirvā vivakṣitā
kiṃ tu ātyantika vaijātyapradarśana metat  tadddvāreṇa ca hetorasiddhiravyāptirvābhimataiva 
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
tathā hi śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādau kulālādisama śilpibuddhirāvirasti
naṃ malayamakarālayādau  tasyāḥ śilpibuddherbhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamātyantikamantareṇa
ityabhiprāyaḥ  vyāpteragrahaṇe smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśe vā devakulādāvapi na syādiyaṃ samānaṃ
śilpibuddhiḥ  tato yathā dhūmādagnibuddhirbhavantī gardabhādabhavantī dhūmād gardabhasya niyataṃ
jātibhedamāpādayati tatheyamapi pariniścitapauruṣeyabhāvebhyo bhāvebhya kailāsakuliśā
dīnām 
kathaṃ punaranumānābhāva eva pratyetavya iti cet kumbhakārādambhodadambholi
prabhṛtisambhava iti svapne'pi śaṅkāvirahāt  anyathā kuvindapādamardanādanāvṛṣṭikaṣṭam
āviśet na lokaḥ paracakrākrāntikātaro vā kṣitidharajaladhivyavadhamabhilaṣaṃstata
eva nirvṛttimāsādayet  kuvindasthānīyastatrāparo'pekṣyata eveti cet na samāne
kāryajanmani vijātīyakāraṇagaveṣaṇānupapatteḥ kuvindenaiva sādhyasiddheḥ  na hi paṭāntare
api kuvindādaparasyāpekṣā 
asti ca vastraviśeṣe viśiṣṭaśilpino'pekṣeti cet  asti yāvadeva tu
bastrāntareṇaikajātiparāmarśo dṛḍhaḥ ata eva kuvindasyaiva śilpina kalpanam  tadvi
marśābhāve pauruṣeyatāyā eva sandehaḥ  merumandarādayastu na kenacit pauruṣeyeṇaika
pratyavamarśabhājaḥ  tadeṣāmadhyakṣa siddhamatyantavaijātyaṃ śāṭhyādapahṛvānaḥ samānaśilpyanu
mānaviraheṇa svīkāryate  siddhe ca jātibhede yādṛk kāryaṃ kumbhādi puruṣapratibaddhaṃ
siddham na tādṛggarbhārbhakādi  yādṛk cedaṃ na tādṛk puruṣavyāptamiti siddhā asiddhiḥ
avyāptiśca dvayoḥ evaṃ ca sthite prakṛtasādhyabuddhayajananadvārāṇi dūṣaṇāni dūram

tataśca
na hi vayaṃ prakṛtasādhyabuddherabhāvāt kāryatvādihetorasiddhi brūmaḥ  ki tahi 
mandarādau kuvindasamaśilpibuddherabhāvādambarādisajātīyakāryatvāsiddhim 
prakṛtasādhyabuddhivedhuryamiti na kaścid doṣaḥ  kuvindasādhyāpekṣayā ca vyāptigrahaṇa
smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśa eveṣṭa iti na bhūṣaṇavikalpāvakāśaḥ  kṛtakatvamātrapratītistu na
vivakṣitaiva  abhraṣṭasmaraṇānāṃ tāvad bhavatyeva puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ kṣityādiṣviti tu
dūramapakṛṣṭam 
bauddhakṛtasya hi a kṛtabuddhiniṣedhasyāsiddhiḥ prastutā abhidhātum  na ca
sāśakyā kṛtabuddhiśabdena śilpibuddherasya vivakṣitatvāt  puruṣakṛtabuddhibhāvavibhāvanaṃ
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
punaranupayogi  pratīta eva tasmin duṣaṇacinteyam  tatrāpya bhraṣṭasmaraṇānāmityasaṅgatam
atyantavaijātyasiddheḥ sindhvāderanyato na vyāptipratīteḥ smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśasya pari
hartumaśakyatvāt  ata eva jagat kenacit sṛṣṭamiti pralāpamātre ka āśvāsaḥ 
prakṛtasādhyabuddhayāsiddhicodanaparihārādeva va vedeṣvapītyādi pratyādiṣṭam 
yadi tu pauruṣeyavākyāderatyantaṃ vedasya vaijātyamupadarśayet mīmāṃsakaḥ tat kiṃ
samayamātreṇa parājetavyaḥ  na tu tayoḥ svarūpadvāraka śaktidvārako vā kaścid
viśeṣo'sti  tathā ca tat dvayamagṛhītasaṃketasya puraḥ paṭhitvā pratīhi kasya kīdṛśaṃ
viśeṣaṃ vyākurvīta śrotā kiṃ na vā paśyasi garuḍādimantrakṛtaṃ viṣāpākaraṇādi 
tadetadāyātam
tasmāt
eka kāryaviśeṣameva kalayan hetorviśiṣṭaṃ nijaṃ
lakṣyāgneriva kāryamātramamunā vyāptaṃ samutpaśyati 
tajjātīyakameva kāryamaparo nāvaiti tadvetukaṃ
hanta dhvāntaviśeṣa eṣa viduṣāmadhyakṣavastunyapi 
yad vācaḥ puruṣānvayavyatiricostaṃdbhāvabhājaḥ sthitā
nānyasmād vacasaśca vaidikagirāṃ bhedo'sti śakyātmanoḥ 
tulyātīndriyasūcanā ca niyataṃ naikatra cāśvāsanaṃ
vedastena na pauruṣeyapadavīmaprāpya viśrāmyati 
yadi tat kā kathā vicāragocarātītātyantikajātibhedeṣu kumbhādambhoda
dambholiprabhṛtiṣu tajjātiniyatapratīteḥ pauruṣeyatāyāḥ  yadapyanityatāsādhanāyopā
labdham tadapi nyāyabāhyam  pratyakṣeṇa pratibandhabodhādhikāre hi tādṛśī sajātīye
taratvamīmāṃsā  anityatve kṛtakatvamātrasya viparyayabādhakapramāṇādanumānasvabhāvāt
pratibandhasiddhiriti na tatra jātiviśeṣānurodhaḥ  jātiviśeṣānavacchinne tu kṛtakamātre
vyāptisādhanasamarthamasamarthaṃ vā tat pramāṇamiti cintanīyam  śaktau na doṣasparśa 
ata eva tatra ghaṭaśabdabhedena bhedodbhāvanaṃ dṛṣṭāntadāntikavaidharmyābhidhānamiti na
yuktam  yato dharmirūpādākṛṣṭadharmadvayasya vyāptivyavasthāpanād dharmavastveva dharmīti
tadbhedābhidhānasya dharmimātrabheda evārtha jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃ
ihāpi tarhi kāryeṣu dharmiṣu pauruṣeyatvaṃ sādhyaṃ kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti na viśeṣaḥ
kaściditi cet  ucyate kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti ko'sya bhāṣitasyārtha  kiṃ tāvanmukhya
tayā dharmamātre kāraṇasya kuṅkumādereva rāge vyāpārādevamucyate  utasvit kāryena
kārye vyāptisiddheḥ dhūmatvamātraṃ heturitivat  yathā kṛtsno dhūmaḥ sādhyavyāptaḥ tathā
yāvat kāryaṃ tat kṛtsnaṃ puruṣavyāpārajanmakamiti niścayāt  tadetadubhayamapi nirastam 
kṛtakatvamātramanityatvavyāptamiti tu kāyapara eva bhāvanirdeśaḥ yāvat kṛtakaṃ tat
sarvamanityamityayamevārtha  b atrārthe pramāṇabale milite siddhe ca dhvaneḥ kṛta
katve ghaṭa eva kṛtako'nityo dṛṣṭaḥ kathaṃ śabdaḥ syāditi niravakāśamevetyayamevārtho
dharmimātrabhedo'yamityanayā rītyā prakāśyate 
yathā hi svabhāva
hetvadhikāraprastāvāt sādhyasādhanadharmo vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayā
bhinnau vyavasthāpitau tathā dharmyapi śabdādiḥ anyasya taddharmaṇo'bhāvāt  na cānyatra
dharmaṇi kṛtakavastunā anityavastusādhane dhvaneranityatāsiddhiḥ  tasya ca dharmiṇo ghaṭa
śabdabhāvena bhedamāpādayan dūṣaṇamabhidhāya nigṛhyate dharmimātrabhedadvāreṇa prastute tu
kāryahetvabhimānād dhūmasthānīya  kāryarāśiḥ sādhyaśca bhinno'gnivat puruṣaḥ  kevalaṃ
nāgnivat taddeśakāla eva  kiṃ tu janmadeśakāle sannihito niśceyaḥ bhasmakumbhābhyām
ivānalakulālau  tato yathā kulālapūrvo'yaṃ ghaṭo ghaṭatvādityupanyāse'pyutpattikāla
deśasannihitavyāpāra  kulālo niścīyate ghaṭaśca heturvastutaḥ tathā puruṣe'pi sādhye
vastveva heturna kāryatvadharmaḥ tathā sati puruṣavyāptāt kāryād vilakṣaṇaṃ kṣoṇīdharādi
kāryamati vadatā sādhanavaisadṛśyamudbhāvitam na dharmivesadṛśyam  tadā hi tadudayadeśa
kālameva dharmi na ca kalasādikāladeśāt kailāsādikāladeśavesadṛśyaṃ kaścid vaktumupa
krānto yena dharmavai sadṛśyodbhāvanaṃ bhavet 
tasmād dahanarūpamātrād dahanānumānavat sādhanavai sadṛśyodbhāvanametadasiddhim
avyāpti vā darśayituṃ dharmiṇa iti tu viplavaḥ pareṣām  ayamevārtho yādṛk kāryatvaṃ
devakulādau puruṣavyāptaṃ pratītam na tādṛg yugandharādāvityanayā diśopadiśyate 
yajjātīyaṃ devakulādi puruṣavyāptaṃ na tajjātīyaṃ yugandharādītyarthaḥ  atyantavejātyācca
kāryaśabdamātrasāmyamucyate na punarakāryavyāvṛtteḥ kacit nyūnabhāvaḥ  vyāptau tu kārya
tvāderanantarbhāvaṃ brūmaḥ  ataeva sanmātreṇa sāmyaṃ nopayogi mūrtatvādineva dahanā
numāne 
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
mañjaryāstu paryanuyogo'sthānapatitaḥ  ghaṭādijātireva puruṣavyāptā siddheti
vadatānyatra saṃśayamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt  kulālādimanuṣyakṛtabuddhiśca kṛtabuddhiruktā 
tadabhāvaśca jātibhede uttarīkṛtaḥ  sa cobhayasiddhatayā na visarjanānyavakāśayati 
na cātyantikajātibhedamantareṇopapadyata iti niveditam 
evaṃ vācaspaterapi viśeṣagaveṣaṇaṃ kṛtabuddhivaidhuryasyābhidheyaprayojanayoraparijñāna
prayuktamiti veditavyam  yadi hi kṛtabuddhirnāstīti prakṛtasādhyabuddhirnāstīti vivakṣi
tam tadā pratītikalahe'muṣmin kuto viśeṣādanyatra sā bhavati parvatādau tadabhāvānneti
cintyate  yadā tu kṛtabuddhirnāstīti a  samāna śilpikṛtabuddhirnāstītyabhidheyam
tatra ca na vivāda  prayojanaṃ ca kumbhādibhyo'mbhodharāderatyanta vaijātyakhyāpanam 
tadavyaśakyaparihāram  tato gṛhītavyāptikebhyo'tyanta vilakṣaṇāt kathaṃ prakṛtasādhya
buddhirityabhipretam  tadā plavata eva sakalamevaṃvidham  utpattimanmātre ca vyāpti
nirasanāt hantotpattimadityādyuttara kāladaṇḍakhaṇḍitameva  tena ghaṭe dṛṣṭavyāptikasya
ghaṭasajātīyameva buddhimatpūrvakam  yadā tu prāsādādāvapi vyāptigrahastadā tajjāterapi
tatpūrvakatva siddhirityapyuktam 
yaccātha yajjātīyamityāśaṅkaya ki kāryajātīyam  tathā na dṛṣṭamityuttaram
tadapi svābhāvika vikalpāvabhāsina  sāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa vyāptigrahaṇayogyatāsamartha
nāt karthitam  tasmād yadapi aupādhikavikalpapratibhāsināpi rūpeṇa tajjātīya
vyavahāro duṣpariharaḥ vyāptigrahaṇe tu pratikṣiptatvānmahān viśeṣa iti 
ata eva vittokavikalpā api na kiñcit  tathā hi yadyasmadabhiprāyapraśnaḥ
tadā viśiṣṭeva kāryajātirdevakulakalasādilakṣaṇā buddhimāptā yaduṣṭehi parokṣakriya
syāpyanubhūtasajātīyaśilpyanumānam sā na siddhā sindhubhūdharādau  kāryatvamātraṃ tu
na vyāptamityuccaistarāṃ tanvanta evāsmahe  tatra kimebhirvikalpairiti cintaya  yadviśeṣād
viśiṣṭā kāryajāti sa viśeṣa kimanirūpitarūpa evetyapi pāpīya pratyakṣasiddhānāṃ
kāryajātīnāṃ parasparavesadṛśyasyāpahrotumaśakyatvāt  vyāptistu viśiṣṭāyāṃ jātī
bhavatu kāryamātre vetyatra paramāpātato vimantumarhati  kathamanyathā svayamapi vastutva
syāgnikāryatvāsaṃjananaṃ vyabhicāramālambya parihṛtam  vyabhicārabuddhīnāṃ niyatajāti
viṣayatve vivādābhāvādityāvirbhāvitameva  tasmādākārārthakriyāsāmarthyādivedanāt
citrākāre jagati
jyāyasī 
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
niyatamīśvaraprasādādevālaukikamekākāramālokitamasyetyupekṣaiva
yadapi prācīnamupādānodāharaṇamasya kāryamātre vyāptisamohayā tadapi naupa
yikam tatrāpi pratyakṣavyāpārasyāśakyasādhanatvāt
naisargikavikalpaviṣayatvāt
upādānasya dṛśyādṛśyasvabhāvatvācca  tat kimidānīmupādānena kārya rāśervyāptireva
nāsti  āhosvit pramāṇāntaragamyā bhavatviti cet  ubhayatra saṃśayaḥ sato'pi
vyabhicārasya viparyayabādhakānumānasya vānullekhasaṃbhavādidānīmekāntahetorabhāvāt 
tadayaṃ sopādānaṃ sarvotpattiriti sarvatantra siddhānto'virodhādanuvṛttaḥ yāvacca kāryam
ālokayāmastāvadupādānavadevetyavigānena vyavahāro'pi  na ca kāryaparyantabodhaḥ
pṛthagjanasyeti tanīyasāpi viparītāṃśena saṃśayo durvāra  buddheśca buddhirupādānaṃ niścitā
iti vijñānasya vijñānā nyānupādānācca sidhyatīti na virudhyate tato yadi siddhāntā
dapi b tadvyāptivyavasāyo na kācit kṣatiḥ  pratyakṣāt tu mā bhūt kevalamatra
pakṣe'cetanopādānatvaheturekadeśasiddhaḥ śaṅkayeteti vyavasthā  sā cāyātaiva ki kriya
tām  viparyayabādhakapramāṇalābhe tu sāpi na syāt  kevalaṃ pratyakṣeṇa kṛtsnakārya 
vyāptivāde'nudāharaṇamevedam  ataḥ pratyakṣasya jātiviśeṣe vyāpāraniyamaprasādhanād
viśeṣahetvabhāvādityādyapi dhvastam 
yatpunaraparasya' viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsapauruṣam tatrāpi prathamadvitayaṃ
tāvad bādhakaṃ dhūmasyeva siddhāyāmeva tadutpattau tatsādhakapratyakṣānupalambhasya viśiṣṭa
jātyadhikāreṇa pravṛttisādhanād viśiṣṭameva ghaṭādikāryaṃ prati śakyam  evaṃ ca yadi
buddhimantamantareṇa jāyeta sakṛdapi tato na bhavet aniyatahetutve vāhetutvamiti na
kāryamātraṃ prati tasya puruṣādutpattiprasādhanābhāvāt  tataśca tat kāryaṃ yat puruṣapūrvam
ityapi niravakāśam 
nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ svakāraṇāyattasannidheradṛṣṭapariṇāmasahakāriṇaḥ
kāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasya satatamabhāve'pi kāryāṇāṃ kādācitkatopapatteḥ yadapekṣayā nitya
śakterapi īśvarasya śaśtranna karaṇa tvam  ekāvasthāniyame hi kāraṇāntarāṇāṃ pravṛtti
nivṛttisādhanīcchā prārthyeta  sa ca nāsti bījasyocchūnataratamādibhāvavat pariṇāma
 śatānandasyeti prāntalekhaḥ 
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
paramparāparicayasya teṣāmapotumaśakyatvāt  astu vā ekāvasthāniyama īśvarasya
icchāyā api nityatvāt tadavastha kāryāvirāmaḥ anitye tu yadapekṣo'syā kadācid
bhāvaḥ tadapekṣayā kāryagrāmasya yadi syāt kīdṛśo doṣa  kumbhādikāryakrame'pi tarhi
ki puruṣecchayā yadapekṣo'syāḥ kramaḥ tadapekṣa eva kumbhāderapyastīti vaktuṃ śakteḥ 
tadayuktam pramāṇena dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya hetorapohitumaśakyatvāt  prastute tu pramāṇā
bhāvāt kāryakādācitkatāmātramāśritaṃ tadanyathāpyupapatsthata iti kutaḥ puruṣāpatti
niyamaḥ kāryasya 
atha kumbhāde kadācidbhāva puruṣādhīno dṛṣṭa iti kāryāntarasyāpi tatheti
cet  evaṃ tarhi tadeva darśanādarśanamātraṃ vyāptisādhanamāyātam kimatra viparyayabādhako
panyāsaśauṭīryeṇeti tṛtīyamapi nirastam 
yaccocyate kāraṇasannidherdhīdhanādhīno niścita iti tatrāpi tathā darśanamātrā 
śraye etadeva vācyam  viparyayabādhakaṃ ca na kiñciduktam  pratyakṣānupalambhaśaraṇīkaraṇe
ca vātopaghātādimilajjambālabījādisāmagrathā anaikāntikatvādi sarvamākṣepaparihāra
sametaṃ kāryavadavagantavyaṃ sāmagrī viśeṣa eva vyāptiyogya ityetatparyantam  tanna kāraṇa
sāmagrayā puruṣeṇa vyāptisiddhiḥ yato vipakṣe vyāpakānupalambhādasambhava iti caturtha
mapi karthitam 
tāva taiva vācaspaterapi a hṛdayaśūnya pralāpo'pahastitaḥ  yathā hi vi
tatānāṃ tāvadajananabījamuktamavasthāviśeṣābhāvo nāma  yadyapi daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ puruṣā
deva milanamupalabdhaṃ tatprayatnasacivānāṃ ca kāryārambhaḥ tathāpi sarvatra sarvadā vā
tathaiveti niyamayituḥ pramāṇasyābhāvāt kāryotpādavyāpakasyāpi kāraṇasamavadhānasya
buddhimadadhīnatvena vyāptaya siddhestadavastho doṣaḥ  yathā ca kāraṇāntaradaśāviśeṣāśraye 
ṇaiva kāryāṇāṃ kadācid bhāvastathā prakṛtaviśeṣo'pīti pañcamaṃ ca pañcatāmañcitam 
kāraṇamātrāpattisādhanaṃ punaretaditi darśitaṃ śāstre 
etenaiva śaṅkaroktamapi nāpi kaścid viśeṣa ityādi kāvyaracanāmātramā
pāditam pratibandhasādhakapramāṇaparyādānāt  yadyapi ca nirabhiprāyavyāpāratvena prāsā
dādihetubhyo bhūbhūdharādihetūnāṃ na viśeṣastathāpi prayatnavadapekṣānapekṣābhyāṃ yadi syāt
ko doṣaḥ  yathā pārthivatvā viśeṣe'pi lohalekhyatvālohalekhyatve  avaśyaṃ ca nirabhi
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalī
prāyatvāviśeṣe'pi viśeṣa eṣāmeṣitavyaḥ śakteḥ kathamanyathā kāryavaijātyamātyantikam 
tadasau śakti prayatnavadapekṣāve mukhyamapi yadi kṣameta kā kṣatiḥ  kiṃ ca karturapi
karādivyāpāramantareṇa samīhāmātrāt na mūrtakāryasiddhirupalabdhā tamativartamānānāṃ
bhūdharādīnāṃ kā gaṇanā samīhāmātre 
karādayo'pi samīyā pravartyanta iti cet  samīhāpi sanniveśini śayādi
vyāpāravirahe na kiñcitkarītyuktam  tato yayā śaktayā karādivyāpārapāravaśyamapāsya
mahīdharādihetavo nirabhiprāyatve satyapi na kāryakarmaṇi pratihanyante tayā samīhāmapi
nātikrameyuriti ka evaṃ śraddadhīta  na hi dhūmodayakāle ucchaladbahalarūpa vastu vahnī
ndhanajanyatayā sambhāvitamekābhāvaniścaye niścīyamānamanyābhāve'pi na bhāvaśaṅkāyāṃ
niveśayati tādṛgetadapi 
śarīrasvīkāre tu prādeśika kāryānityāne kāsarvajñatvāt sādhu sādhita sudhī
bhirīśvaraḥ  etenaiva vā vyabhicāra  kāryatvādeḥ  na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāmityādivacanād
darśanādarśanamātrādanyamupāyamasya vyāptisādhanāya spṛśati tacca kṛtottaram  yadi ca
darśanādarśanameva śaraṇam tadā yathā samīhāvataḥ kāryakriyā dṛṣṭeti kārye sati samīhā
vato'numānamiṣṭam tathā karādimata eva mūrtakriyā dṛṣṭeti karādivyāpārānupapattau
puruṣasyākriyaiva kasmāt na niścīyate  na khalu kāryahetuvyāpakānupalambhayoḥ prāmāṇye
kaścid viśeṣaḥ  yadi tu darśanādarśanamātramanāsthāya pramāṇāntaramekaniyataṃ syāt
syādekasādhyabuddhiḥ tadabhāve tu pratibandha b eva tayoḥ parasparam na bādhā tulya
kakṣatvāditi prakaraṇasamaḥ parābhiprāyāt 
prayogaḥ yo na svāṅgavyāpāravān nāsau mūrtanirvartanasamartho dṛṣṭaḥ yathā kulāla
eva saṃhṛtakarā divyāpāradaśāyām  nāsti ca svāṅgavyāpāraḥ prakṛte puṃsīti vyāpakā
nupalabdhi  nāśrayāsiddhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyanyāyeneti vastutastarhi dūṣaṇāntarameva yuktaṃ
kaḥ pratihetoravakāśa iti cet na bhūyodarśanasya vyāptisiddhāvana ṅgatvapratipādanārthamasyo
panyāsāt  yadi bhūyodarśanamupāya tadaivamapi syādityutteriti vyāptigrahaprakārāṇām
ayogādanekānta iti sthitam 
astu vā vyāptigrahaḥ kathañcit tathāpi neśvarasiddhipratyāśā phalavatī buddhi
mataḥ sādhyasyaikatvaniyamaniścayābhāvāt  ekatve hi tasya siddhe nityavibhusavaṃjñatva
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
siddhirīśvaravyavahāramāropayet  yadā tu bhinnadeśakālakalitaṃ kāryajātamanekena saṃkhyāti
krāntena kartrā kṛtaṃ sambhāvyeta na tadā vibhutvanityatve svasvaviṣayopādānādimātravedana
siddhau ca ka sarvajñatvam 
atha bahūnāṃ vyāhṛtamanasāṃ vyāpāre kāryasyānutpattirupanyasya vilopādiprasaṅgaśca
syāditi cet  pratyekaṃ vaibhavādiguṇayogādīśvarāṇāṃ vyāpāre syādapīyamāśaṅkā adya
punareko'pi tādṛ na sidhyatītyucyate  arvācīnaśaktayaśca bhūyāṃsa ekamanekaṃ ca kāryam
ārabhya niṣpādayanto dṛśyanta eva  nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenaikena bhāvyam balīyasā
vā sūtradhāravat senānīvad vā  atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvṛttitvāditi cet na
tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcidekasattvādighaṭanā
darśanāt  tatrāpi kaścideva prathamaḥ prayojaka ityapi nāsti anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyā
anivāraṇāt nīcasthāpi prayojakatvasambhavāt 
tasmād bhramaramadhumakṣikāvalmīkajantuvat kṣudraprāṇibhirapaye ke kamainākādikaraṇa
sambhāvanāyāṃ kā vārtā viśvasyaikena kriyāyāḥ  tatrādṛṣṭajanmānastāvat tāvataiva
kṛtārthīkṛtacetanānumitayaḥ kṣitidharādayaḥ  te ca kṣudrajantava upādānamatikṣudraṃ pṛthivyā
didravyamupakaraṇaṃ sukhādisampradānamātmānaṃ sthitisukhādi ca prayojanaṃ jānanta eva
valmīkajantuvat pravarteran  siddhe ca nāvaśyamadhiṣṭhāyakā dṛśyeran vicitraśakti
karmākṣepāt svabhāvaviprakarṣād vā  ye'pi dṛṣṭajanmāno vṛkṣādayaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ tatra
cintaiva nāsti  adṛṣṭapuruṣavyāpārāstu ye bindhyayugandha rādiparisaradbhāvāste'pi piśā
cādiprakārairadhiṣṭhātṛbhirasaṃkhyaiḥ kartṛmanta iti kaḥ sarvavedī bhavatu  deśakālayośca
bhinnā evepri ka vibhutvanityatve  na caivaṃ śaṅkāyā a bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti vastubala
pravṛttamanumānam 
i
nanu
caivaṃ tāvad bhavadbhirapi na svīkṛtameva  etāvaccātikaṣṭataraṃ kalpayato varam
īśvarakalpanaiva lāghavāditi cet  satyam yadi kalpanāmātretaranyāsaḥ tadā bhavadupa
nyāsameva puraskariṣyāmaḥ  yāvat punaranumānavyājaṃ na varjayasi tāvadavaśyamasmākaṃ
dṛḍhanirūpaṇābhiyogaḥ  atha kṣudraṃrasaṃkhyanirmitā narmaṃdādaya iti dunoti cetaścet 
ekenāśarīreṇa nirmitā iti suṣṭhutarām  tasmāt pramāṇameva sarvato balavad yathā sthā
payati tathārthaṃsthitiḥ  ataeva tad dṛḍhaṃ nirūpyate  na ca kṣudreṣvanurodhaḥ kaścit 
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
kṣudrairakṣudrai radṛśyaiḥ samānaśaktibhiradhikaśaktibhiḥ svatantraiḥ pradhānasammataikaikajantusanāthāpari
mitayūthairvā sthūlāṇukaikāne kasvakāryabhāgopādānādimātravedibhiḥ ṣaḍgatiparyāpannaiḥ kṛto
bhavatu bhuvanasanniveśaḥ eka eva tu kartā'sya mā bhūt 
nāpi bauddhastathānupagamāt tato hetuvyāvṛttiḥ ekato'pi vyāvṛttiprasaṅgāt 
na ca vastubalapravṛtte'numāne paropagamāpekṣā  upagamamātrasya tyāgenāvirodhāt  tadevaṃ
buddhimanmātre sādhye upādānādyabhijñatālakṣaṇaviśeṣanāntarīyakatayā sākṣādupādānādya
bhijñakartṛsādhanād vābhimatasiddhinaikāntiko sarvaṃkāryakriyāyā ekakartṛtvāsiddheḥ 
upādānādyabhijñamātrasādhane ca vaiphalyam bhāratādikathāvat  tataḥ sādhanāntarā
bhāvādasmādeva sarvajñādiguṇavataḥ siddhiriṭeti tadapekṣayaiva dūṣaṇamabhidhānīyamanekānta
lakṣaṇamiti sthitam 
ato yāvatīmarthaṃgatimityādi durlaṅvayam  sādhyasāmānyapratibandhākṛṣṭatve'pi
viśeṣasya siddhi sādhanādhīnaiva tadekaparatayā sādhanopanyāsādanyasādhanābhāvācca 
bauddhasyāpi hi nairātmyasiddhiḥ sādhanādhīnaiva  yadi hi nairātmyatyāge'pi kṣaṇabhaṅga
sādhanaṃ caritārthaṃ bhavet tadā kiṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhane nairātmyasiddhiḥ syāt  bhavatastu
sārvajñyādisiddhimuddhūyānyathāpyupādānādyabhijñānalakṣaṇo viśeṣa upapāditaḥ 
nātmopanyāsapūrvako'nvayo dṛṣṭānte pradarśyata iti anupayuktam  sākṣāt tadanvayadarśane
api tannāntarīyakatvaṃ sādhyasāmānyasya darśayitavyameva  taccaikatvena sakalakriyādhārasya
vyāpterabhāvādaśakyam 
ataeva
etenaiva vācaspatyo'pi sārvajñyasādhanābhinayaḥ prativyūḍhaḥ  siddhe tu sarvajñe kartari
karturekatvanirūpaṇaśramo'smākamanuyogītyuparamyate  yadapyayaṃ vyatirekiprayogamāha
tadapyekatvāniścayādeva dūṣitam anityāsarvaviṣayabuddhitve'pyupādānādivedanasambhavasyopa
pāditatvāt 
vittokasamādhāne tu dhūmāddharādharāyoga vyavacchedavat agneḥ pañcavarṇaśikhākalā
patāyā apyanumānaprasaṅgaḥ  nātra sāmarthyamiti cet  tatrāpi pakṣāyogavyavaccheda eva
sāmarthyāt  pṛthvībhṛti prayatnavataḥ siddhāvapyekatvāniścayāt ka sarvavedanasiddhiḥ 
b  nanu dūdhaṇukasyāpi kāryatvāt kartā tadupādānaparamāṇudarśī niyamena
eṣitavyaḥ  na ca māṃsacakṣuṣastathā bhavitumarhanti  anyathā kimasmadābhiraparāddhaṃ yena
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
tathā na bhavāmaḥ  tadavaśyaṃ kartātīndriyadarśī svīkriyamāṇo neśvarādanyo yuktaḥ  tadapi
yatkiñcit  na hi māṃsacakṣuṣ'pi sarvasādhāraṇaṃ karaṇasāmarthyam asmadatyantamapakṛṣṭānāmapi
gṛdhrādīnāmindriyapāṭavātiśayadarśanāt  kṣodiṣṭhānāmeva ca keṣāñcit paramāṇudarśanamapi
syāt karmaśaktiviśeṣāt yathā pipīlikānāmasmadagocaragandhāṇugrahaṇam  ca
tanmātrasūkṣmamīkṣamāṇairdeśakālaviprakṛṣṭasyāpi sūkṣmāntarasya grahaṇam sakalasthūlasya vā 
tanna tāvataiveśvarasiddhipratyāśā 
na
evaṃ tarhi bhavatu paramāṇodarśanasambhāvanā sakalakṣetrajñatatsamavetadharmādharmāśaya
viśeṣāṇāṃ tu katham  na kathañcit  na hi kāryakriyā kṣetrajñasvarūpādiparijñānenāpi vyāptā
kulāladṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭā kiṃ tu sampradānopakaraṇavedanadvāreṇa tadākṛṣṭiriṣyate  sā cāśakyā
sāmarthyānupapatteḥ uktakrameṇāpi tanmātravedanasya caritārthatvāt  karmaṇi svasyābhipreya
māṇatvena sampradānatāyā durvāratvāt yathā svasmai mandiraṃ karotīti  anyathā tenaiva
vyabhicāraprasaṅgaḥ sampradānajñānāpekṣāyāḥ 
anumīyamānastatrāparaḥ sampradānavedī bhaviṣyatīti cet na vyabhicāradarśanena
kartuḥ sampradānajñānanāntarīyakatvāsiddheranumānavārtāvirahāt  na cānumīyamānāpekṣayā
tasyā kartṛtvam  evaṃ hi kulālasyāpyakartṛtvaprasaṅge vyāptigraha virahāt tadavastho'numānā
nudayaḥ  tasmād yad yadavaśyaṃ sampradānajñānāpekṣaṃ kartṛtve svātmāpi sampradānameṣitavyaḥ 
na ca paramapi sampradānaṃ vyavahāraprasiddhamuddhūya kṣetrajñarūpamasau jñātumīśaḥ karmāśayabhedārthopa
karaṇaśabdasaṃgṛhītānapi  tato yathā kulālastāna vidvān daṇḍacakrādivedanenaivopakaraṇajñaḥ
tathānumīyamānā api jantavaḥ svakīyakaramukhādijñānenāpyante bhaviṣyanti 
tat kutastyametat kṣetrajñarūpatadīyadharmādharmāśayabhedaparijñānam  athāśarīrasya ka
svāṅgavyāpārasaṅgatiḥ  aśarīrasya siddhisaṅgatirapi kīdṛśī  ekatve hi siddhe śarīrī
prādeśiko na sarvakarmaṇi samartha iti sāmarthyādaśarīrisiddhipratyāśā ekatvaṃ ca duḥsādha
mityuktam  na cāśarīratve'pi daṇḍacakra karamukhādyupakaraṇānupapatteḥ pāriśeṣyāt karmāśaya
bhedajñānenaivopakaraṇajñānaniṣṭheti sauṣṭhavāya  dikkālasamavāyāderapyupakaraṇasaṃgṛhītasya jñānena
tajjñatāmātrasya kṛtārthatvāt 
kaḥ punarasau viśeṣo yatastadavasthasya digādijñānenaivopakaraṇajñatā  a na
dharmādharmādijñāneneti  ubhayajñānenaiva bhavatviti cet  tadayuktam  nahi yāvadupakaraṇaṃ
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃ
tāvat kartrāvaśyaṃ jñeyamiti dṛṣṭam  na ca digā dijñānenaivopakaraṇa vittistadavasthasyeti
niścayaṃ brūmo yato viśeṣaparyanuyogaḥ kiṃ tūpakaraṇāntarasambhavānna pāriśeṣyaviśrāntiḥ
atretyucyate  tato yathā parāparakartṛṣu daṇḍacakrāditurīvemādyupakaraṇavirahaparamparāyām
anyānyairupaka raṇairdharmādibāhyai rupakaraṇajñatāsthiti rupalabdhā tathā kimadyāpyastu  uta
dharmādīnādāyaiveti sandeha eva  yadi punaranyadupakaraṇaṃ na syāt pāriśeṣyavyākhyānaṃ
śobheta  abhyudayaniḥśreyasamārgādisandehe ca kiṃ tādṛśā tena kartavyamīśvarābhidhānena
dhanavirahiṇeva 
tasmādaśarīritve'pi na dharmādijñānākṛṣṭiḥ kiṃ punastadasiddhau  mā bhūdupakaraṇatayā
dharmādervedayitā niyamena kāryatayā bhaviṣyati yataḥ kartā kāryarūpādivedaka sa ceśvara
ityapi niḥsāram  dānahiṃsādikaṃ hi kurvantastad vedayanta eva svarūpamātreṇa na tāvatā
ta eveśvarāḥ  na cānyaḥ kāryena tadvedī siddhaḥ  dharmādharmatvena tu niścayaḥ tatkāriṇo'pi
nāvaśmbhāvī kumbhakāravat  tatkāriṇāṃ tarhi tattvena niścayābhāvāt tattvaniścayaḥ kāryatvāt
kartāramīśvarameva sannidhāpayedityapi nāsti  dharmādharmatvaniścayo'pi hi samīcīnaḥ
sandigdhasattāka eva vartate  kathaṃ tataḥ pratyāśā  anirastaviparyayāśaṅkasaṅkalpasvabhāvastu
bhūyasāmāgamadvāreṇa devajātismarādisvīkārācca teṣām apyasti leśena samyakkarmaphala
sambandhabodhaḥ  na ca tāvataivaiśvaryaparyāptiriti 
tadevamīśvarāsiddheḥ sakalajanmināṃ śubhāśubhakarmāṇi nopakaraṇam kiṃ tu kāraṇānyeva
lokavaicitryasyeti dhīmatāmupādeyaḥ prathamaślokārtha iti 
 īśvaradūṣaṇaṃ samāptamiti 
 vārtikasaptaślokī 
sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu 
iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā   
siddhaṃ yādgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat 
sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate   
vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ 
na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādivadbhutāśane   
anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit 
ghaṭāde karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ   
sādhyenānugamāt kārye sāmānyenāpi sādhane 
sambandhibhedād bhedoktidoṣaḥ kāryasamo mataḥ   
jātyantare prasiddhasya śabdasāmānyadarśanāt 
na yuktaṃ sādhanaṃ gotvād vāgādīnāṃ viṣāṇavat   
vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā 
tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarva sarvasya sidhyati   
pramāṇavārtike prathame'dhyāye  īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam 
karmanirmita vaicitryamanīśaṃ yo jagajjagau 
praṇamāmi pramāṇena tamavyāhataśāsanam 
nityapramāṇapratiṣedhasiddhau yadapramāṇatvamanityabhāve 
vibhāvayannāha kṛtī tadaṃśe vimohadaṃśāpaha eṣa mārgaḥ 
svayaṃ nirasyāpi parasya sādhanānyasaṅgatau vārtikakārakīrtane 
na nirvṛtiścet punarasya varṇanāda varaṃ hi tadvarṇanayaiva vikramaḥ 
yad yat kāryaṃ tat tad buddhimatpūrvakam yathā ghaṭaḥ  kāryaṃ ca mahīmahīdharādi 
yad vā yad yat na buddhimatpūrvakaṃ tat tanna kāryam yathā ākāśam  kāryaṃ ca
tarugirisāgarādītyarthataḥ kāryahetuḥ  evamacetanopādānatvam arthakriyākāritvam
svārambhakāvayavasanniveśa nāviśeṣavattvam sthitvā sthitvā kāryakarmāṇi pravṛttidharmakatvaṃ
ca prayojyamiti kathamucyate

anitye'pyapramāṇateti 
etacca nityānityayoḥ sādhāraṇameva b  sādhanam  anityatāprakramaṇe tu
parasya pramāṇaparyeṣaṇā pravarteta  tadupanyāsanidānatvamātreṇānityaśabdānuvādaḥ  na punaḥ
asāvanitya eva bhagavān asmābhiriṣyate  tathā hi 
eko vibhuḥ sarvavidekabuddhisamāśrayaḥ śāśvata īśvarākhyaḥ 
pramāṇamiṣṭo jagato vidhātā svargāpavargāthibhirarthanīyaḥ 
atrocyate  kimebhireva hetubhirupadiṣṭaguṇagaṇāgārapuruṣātiśayasādhanamano
ratho'tha hetvantarabalāt  tatra na tāvadādyaḥ pakṣaḥ  tathā hi yat sādhanaṃ yāvatīmartha 
gati vyāpnoti tatastāvatyeva sidhyati nārthāntaram  na hi yāvānicchayā vyāpto'rthaḥ
tāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam  api tu yāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam tāvato'rthasya
tannimittā siddhiḥ  na ca kāryatvādi cetanapūrvakatvena vyāpyamānamapi tadekatvādi
niyatāṃ matimutpādayituṃ śaktam tadviśeṣaṇe vyāpterevāpratīte anyathā viparītarūpa 
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
niścayasyāpi prasaṅgāt  na hi dahanasāmānyena vyāptaṃ dhūmamupalabhya kaścid visphuratpañca
varṇaśikhākalāpakamanīyamanalamanumātumīśaḥ 
nanu tathāpi deśakālaviśeṣa viśeṣaṇamanumimīta eva pakṣadharmatābalāt evaṃ
bhūdharādāvapi buddhimadadhiṣṭhānādhīnaṃ kāryatvamupalabdhavato'bhimatasiddhiradhikaraṇasiddhānta
nyāyena bhaviṣyatīti cetna sāmarthyānupapatteḥ  yathā hyetaddeśakālena vahninā
janyamānasya na taddeśakālatvamiti dhūmādyanumāne sāmarthyam na tathā cetayiturekatva
sarvajñatvādikamantareṇa tarūṇāṃ vāsaniveśādyanupapattimākalayāmaḥ  tataḥ pakṣadharmaṃtā
balāt kulālādī tadutpādanasamarthatvasiddhirapi bhavantī nābhimataṃ viśeṣamavalambitum
alam 
nanu yadi bhūdharādinirmāṇasamartha siddhaḥ kimaparaṃ prārthyate  tat kimidānīm
apariniṣṭhitavācyarūpeṇa vācakamātreṇa parituṣṭiḥ  na hyevamabhimataprastutavastusiddhiḥ 
utpādanavyāpāro hi notpitsukāryaṃ prati niyataprāgbhāvitvamātrādatiriktaḥ  sa cācetana
sādhāraṇo buddherapi naikasarvagatvādiviśeṣapratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ  tato vivakṣitasādhyā
pekṣayā vacanamātrasiddhayā na kiñcit 
kaḥ punarevaṃ pratijānāti sarvajñapūrvakā  parvatādaya iti  api tu buddhimaddhetukā
ityāśaṅkaya sādhanenāntarupahasannāha
sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu 
iṣṭasiddhiriti 
sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇakarmanirmito hi samasto vasturāśiriṣyate  karmaṃ cācetana
svabhāvamiti sakalajñāna
hetavo'sidhyantaḥ sindhubhūdharādayaḥ kimaniṣṭamasmākamāvahantīti
bhāvaḥ  tanmātrasādhyābhiprāye ca virodhāsiddheḥ sādhanopanyāsavaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ  tasmāt
upāttaviśeṣa evānena a sādhya  na ca tatra sādhanasāmarthyamityuktam  astu
tarhi sādhanāntarādeva tathā siddhiriti dvitīyapakṣāpekṣayā niścayābhāvamudbhāvayannāha
asiddhirveti 
na pramāṇāntaraṃ na vā hetvantaramasti yato'yaṃ niścayaḥ syādityarthaḥ  athavā
atīndriyatvenādhyakṣāsaṃbhavādanumānamabhyarthanīyam tadarthaṃ ca sarvaṃ hetumadhikṛtyāha
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānam
asiddhirveti 
uktānumānato hi prativādisādhāraṇasarvaṃkṛccetanamātre siddhe'pi viśeṣaśaṃsī
na kaściddheturyo na svarūpāsiddho'nyatra sattāyāḥ tanmātrasattātirekiṇi dharme'numānasyānava
sarāt  sattā tu kṣaṇabhaṅgaśaṃsinīti nityaikatvāpekṣayā āha
asiddhirveti 
viparītasiddhirityarthaḥ  adharmādivat paryudāsena nitye'pi hi parasādhanavad
dūṣaṇasyābhimatatvāt prastāvamātraphalatvādanityokteḥ  vyāpitvāpekṣayā anekānta
madhyāha
asiddhirvā dṛṣṭānta iti 
vyāptittrasya paramārthato'bhāvādeva dṛṣṭānte darśanābhāvānna tena kasyacid dharmasya
vyāpti sidhyatītyuktaṃ bhavati  sarvabodhasya tu bhāve'pi na vyāpakatvapratītiḥ 
kuta ityāha
dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā
iti arvāgdarśanena viśeṣaniṣṭhatayā vastuto niścetumaśakyatvāt  tasmādupagītaguṇasya
yathoktasādhanebhyo na sākṣānnādhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyena nāpi sādhanāntarāt siddhiḥ
iti siddhaḥ sādhakapramāṇavirahaḥ  tadviśeṣavirahiṇi viṣṭasiddhiriti 
athavā kāryatvādihetuṣūpanyasteṣu sādhyasāmānya viśeṣabhāvena vikalpa iti
siddhirasiddhiyāha  tatra karmavāditāprasiddhayā siddhasādhanaṃ vyaktamitya siddhinibandhanaṃ
viśeṣe'nugamābhāvamādarśayannāha
asiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā
iti sādhyasyeti prakṛtam  tatra vibhutvādipratyanīkadharmaṇa kulālāderavivādena siddheḥ
asiddhiriṣṭasya dṛṣṭānte  atha dehātiriktabhāgasyānisargaduvibhāvasya vaibhavādikamiṣṭam
iti matistathāpi saṃśayo'stu kimidānīmatra nirbandheneti bhāvaḥ 
sāmānya siddhasādhyateti
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalī
tasmāt sādhyavikalpātsandigdhasādhyadharmatvād vā na dṛṣṭānte sādhyena kāryatvādervyāpti
riti viśeṣasyāsiddhereva anekāntastu hetudoṣaḥ 
nanu dhūmānugame'pi
viśeṣe'nugamābhāvaḥ sāmānye siddhasādhyatā 
iti samāno nyāyaḥ tadanayornaikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamanyad veti  niyataṃ cet  na samī
cīnamālocitam  tathā hi na tāvadviśeṣasiddhimavadhūya prāmāṇyamanumānamanubhavatīti
siddham  sa tu viśeṣaḥ pakṣāyogavyavacchedamātralakṣaṇastadatiriktaśca saṃbhavati yathā
agniratra dhūmāt evaṃrūpo vā  tatra prathamāpahnave syādanumānasyāpalāpaḥ tanmūlatvād
atiriktasiddherapi  na cāsau tathānvayānusaraṇamantareṇāpi nirasituṃ śakyaḥ  pakṣadharmo
hi yatpratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ sa tena dharmiṇamaviyuktamanādarśayan svarūpasattayaiva b
viyujyeta yadi paraṃ kāryahetvadhikāreṇa kālādyapekṣātiricyate  dvitīya siddhistu
tanmātrasādhyeti tajjanyaviśeṣagrahaṇanāntarīyakatayānvayānusaraṇamantareṇābhavantyapi
nānumānāpalāpāya prabhavati tadviśeṣavirahiṇā dharmeṇāyogavyavacchedasiddhathāpi
tasyāścaritārthatvāt  anumānaviśeṣāpalāpastu syāt yathā kaścit pañcavarṇaśikhaṃ
śikhinamanumātumabhipretya vahniratra dhūmāditi sādhane pareṇa siddhasādhanānanugamābhyām
abhiyujyamānastarhi dhūmamātrocchedeneha cānumānamapi na syāditi bruvāṇa śobheta 
na tvanumānoccheda eva syāt tadaiva dahanasāmānyānumānasya tena pramāṇīkriyamāṇa
tvāt  tasmāt
pakṣāyogavyavacchedamātrabhedena dūṣaṇam 
iṣṭasiddhabanvayābhāvāvatirikteṣu dūṣaṇam 
naito dūṣaṇatve'dūṣaṇatve vā niyatau viṣayabhedena tu dvayī sthitiriti matam 
tadvadihāpi jaladhibhūdharādī buddhimadadhiṣṭhānāyogavyavacchedamaṅgīkṛtya vivakṣitaviśeṣā
ntarāpekṣayā to dūṣaṇamudbhāvayataścitrakāntiśikhānumānoccheda eva prasañjayitumāñjasaḥ
nānumānocchedaḥ  tato'numāna viśeṣāpekṣayā naikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamaprāmāṇyaṃ veti yuktaṃ
na sāmānyena 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam 
nanu cādyāpi bhedo'nvayamanapekṣyaiva siddha iti bhedāntare kaḥ pratirodhaḥ  na vai
niranvayā kāpi siddhirasti  sāmānyānvaya eva tu taṃ viśeṣamanākṛṣya nāvasthātuṃ
śaktaḥ  na caivaṃ viśeṣāntare'pi tasyāvaśyaṃ śaktiriti śakyam yathopavarṇitaṃ prāk
anyathā pañcavarṇaśikhādyanumānasya durnivāratvāt  atrāsaṃbhavādikṣepaṇameka cittatvādi
mati puruṣe'pi samānam  tādṛganumānodgārastatrāpi samānaḥ  tasmādatireka viśeṣa
śaṃsināvaśyamanenānvayaḥ pradarśanīya iti tadabhāvādanekānta eva  buddhimanmātrasādhane
ca siddhasādhanamiti sthitam 
syādetat  buddhimāniti na caitanyamātravān api tupādānādyabhijñaḥ prayatna
vān vābhimataḥ tena cānvayo ghaṭādikārye siddha iti bhūdharādāvapi kāryatvamupalabhya
mānaṃ tādṛśameva kartāramupasthāpayatīti noktobhayadoṣaḥ  tathā hi tadupādānādyabhijña
ityeva sarvajñaḥ deśakālaniyataśca na tadbheda upādīyamāna kāryagrāmanirvartanasamartha syāt
iti nityatvavibhutvādayo'pi taddharmāḥ siddhā iti cet  seyaṃ chinnamūla viṭapasya
phalabhogapratyāśā  ekatve hi siddhe siddhireṣāṃ guṇānām anyathā bhinnadeśakālasya
kāryasthānekakṛtau saṃbhāvyamānāyāṃ kasya vaibhavādayaḥ svasvavyāpāraviṣayamātravedanācca
kasya sārvajñamiti 
ekatve siddhe  a  sādhyamaśeṣamākṛṣyeta na ca tanniścaye kiñcinnibandhanam
asti  na ca kṣityādinirmāṇasamartha siddha ityekavacanaprayogapatanāt tatsiddhiḥ
pratibandhābhāvāt  pratibandhe vā siddhaikatvaḥ paraḥ kathamenamupekṣeta  jātyapekṣayā tu
syādapīti na nirbandhaḥ aparāparadhūmapramitasyeva vahnaḥ  na ca vicitre'pi citrakarmaṇi
sajātīya rekhādyanugamā dekakartṛsiddhivat kāryabhedeṣu guṇaviśeṣānugamāt tadekatvasiddhiḥ
tathāvidhasya kasyacidanugatasyaivānupalabdheḥ  upālabhyamānaṃ ca kāryatvavastutvādi naikatva
sādhanaṃ citravadeva  guṇāntarasaṃbhave'pi hi sadṛśa eko vā karteti sandeha eva kiṃ
punastadabhāve'pyekaniścayaḥ  niyatamidamabhitticitrakarmaiva yadabhedāniścaye sarvajñatvādi
vyavasīyata iti 
itarastvāha eva tvamapi kāryotpattyaivāvagantavyam  katham  bahūnāṃ vyāhata
manasāṃ svātantryeṇa parasparavirodhena mitha svānukūlābhiprāyānavabodhena yugapat kāryā
nutpattiḥ utpannasya vilopanādiprasaṅgaśca syāditi jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
atra cintyate bahubhiḥ karaṇe yugapat kāryānutpattiriti bhinnakālānāṃ bhinna
deśānāṃ kāryānutpattirvivakṣitā ekasyaiva vā mahāvayavinaḥ kṣitidharādirūpasyeti pakṣaḥ 
tatra naikatrāpyanekena karaṇe utpattivirodhaṃ paśyāmaḥ  yathā hyekasya pravṛttistathānyeṣāmapi
syād valmīkavat  kiṃ prayojanamabhisandhāya teṣāṃ pravṛttiriti cet  na vicitravṛtti 
tvānmanasāṃ pravṛttinibandhasya viśeṣaniścāyanāśakteḥ  anyatheśvarasyaiva kimabhi
pretyeti cintānirbandho nirvoḍhuṃ na śakyaḥ  śakyo vā anyeṣāmabhipretādibādhyatā
vadhāraṇapaṭīyasām na mṛduprakṛterīśvarasya 
nāpi bahūnāṃ parasparavyātiniyama upapādayituṃ śakyaḥ valmīkaukasāmekārambha
darśanāt  puruṣāṇāmahamahamikayā saṃbhāvyata eva taditi cet  sadvivekino hyeka
kāryārambhiṇaḥ santyapīti tathāvidhairaparairapyatipracuratarairekasya krameṇa sthavīyasaḥ karaṇe
saṃbhavini ko'smākaṃ nareṣvanurodha  nāpi yugandharāderyugapanniṣpattiḥ vanacidupalabdhā
yata ekasyaiva kasyacicchakti saṃbhāvyate  na cāhamahamikayā puruṣeṣvapi vyāghāta 
niyamaḥ śakyanirvāhaḥ parasparāvyāghātena puruṣasya virodhadvayasyānupapatteḥ  tasmāt
saṃbhāvanāmātrametat na pramāṇavartma ityupanyāsamarhati nānekeneṃka mainākāde karaṇa
miti samayamātrānusmṛtirvā 
nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenekena bhāvyaṃ balīyasā sūtradhāravat senānīvad vā
atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvatitvāditi cet  b na tatrāpi niyamā
bhāvāt svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcideka se tvādighaṭanādarśanāt 
tatrāpi kaścideva pradhāna prayojaka ityapi nāsti anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyā
nivārakābhāvāt apradhānasyāpi vā prayojakatvasaṃbhavāt  na tāvataiva prādhānyaṃ
lokavirodhāt  kiṃ ca sūtradhārasthānīyāparimitaikaikajanasanāthaiḥ sārthairaparimitaireva
khaṇḍaśaḥ sthūlārambhasaṃbhave'pi kā nāma kāmasiddhiḥ  etena valmīkajantuṣu mukhyopa
nyāsaḥ pratyuktaḥ 
api ca yathekahṛdayānuvartibhiranekairabhinirmīyamānasya prāsādasya sukhopadhānā
vayavasanniveśaviśeṣa upalabhyate na tathā visaṃsthūlasthūlaśilājālakaliteṣu kula

bādhya 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam
āgamā dekatvasiddhistahi iti cet  so'yaṃ sannipātāpannasya sapai rakṣābandha
vidhirabādhaka eva bauddhānadhikṛtyāgamavicāraikacaturacetasaḥ  yadi hi parīkṣāgamagrahaḥ
tadāyameva parīkṣākāla iti kastadanurodho'dhunaiva  atha parīkṣānapekṣaḥ tadāpi tata
evābhimata

lābhaḥ 
yadapya yameva vādī prāmāṇyamāgamānāṃ samarthayan na hyapramāṇatve samastāśramiṇāṃ
saṃvādo nāma tasyāpramāṇatve kasyacidaprāmāṇyabodhena visaṃvādasyāpi saṃbhāvyatvāt
saṃvādaniyamasya ca pramāṇeṣveva pratyakṣādiṣūpapatteriti nāpramāṇāni ṛgyajusāmāni
samastāśramiṇāṃ saṃvādijñānasādhanatvāt pratyakṣādivadityādi pañcālakaṃ paṭhati tadapi
śiṣyasamitāvevopayujyate  tathā hi saṃvādo nāma pramāṇāntarasaṅgatirarthakriyā vā
syāt na ca tadubhayamapi

tula saiva   
ityādivākyārtheṣu svargasādhanāgniṣṭomādau vā kasyacit saṃbhavati 
āśramiṇastāvad yathaikasya eko vibhuḥ śāśvataḥ sraṣṭā jagato'stīti matiḥ
tathānyasyāpi  tadanurūpānuṣṭhānaṃ ceti cet  sā punareṣāṃ matistadekāgamaprabhavā tādṛga
nyaprabhavā vā ākasmika vikalpamātrarūpā vā syāt na tu pratyakṣānumānarūpā anā
śramiṇāmadhyavakāśaprasaṅgāt pratyakṣādeḥ puruṣāntarai a anaparādhāt  āgamāśrayaṃ
tu jñānamatato'nādṛtavato na syāt bhavāntarābhyāsavāsanāvaśād vā saṃbhavet
nānyasyeti yuktam  tatredaṃ svatantratayā na pramāṇam satyasati vā vastuni saṃbhavinaḥ
abhyāsāt prasūteḥ  tadāgamaprabhavatvena pramāṇāntarasaṅgatiruktā bhavati tādṛkprabhava
tvāt tasyāpyaprāmāṇyāt  tadasiddhaṃ yadasiddhena sādhyata iti nyāyaḥ

jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
tādṛksamayānusmaraṇamātrametadevambhūtaḥ kaścidastīti  kiṃ ca āśrama ityapi darśanamātraṃ
vidmaḥ tataśca samastāśramiṇāmiti viśeṣaṇāsiddhiḥ bauddhadigambarāde saṃvādāsiddheḥ 
katipayasaṃvādaśca viparītamate'pyastīti nopanyāsaḥ saphalaḥ  ataeva visaṃvādasyātyanta 
nivṛttirasiddhā yataḥ prāmāṇyamavatiṣṭheta abhimatamāśramiṇāṃ tvanādikālapravṛttasamāna
saṃmohasāmarthyādapi syāditi yatkiñcidetat 
tasmādekatrāpi

tadā ta eva

adhyavasāyaḥ 
prabhāvātiśayasahāyāpekṣāyāṃ ki śilpena  na tadantareṇa tasya śaktiriti

iṣṭasyā kartṛtvasya siddhirasiddhirvā asiddhireva upayogābhāvāt 
na hi narakādinā tāvat kaścidupayogaḥ saṃvittyānuṣṭhātuḥ sukhopakaraṇamātra

ādhāsyanti  yadi paraṃ tanmārgamaviduṣāṃ tadupadeśa evānugrahakaraḥ atastadarthaṃ mārga
sākṣātkaraṇābhyāsa eva śreyāniti vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyābhyāṃ nābhyāsaḥ  tarhi pratiparamāṇu
jñānābhyāse'pi kathaṃ tadvad vā sarvakaraṇe'pi na kṣatirityāha sarvasarvavidi
dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā
iti upayuktasarvajñapakṣasya mukhyatayā vakṣyamāṇatvāt  athavā vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyayostatra
saṃśayo nābhāvaniścaya ityarthaḥ  uddeśaścānyatropadarśanamiti na pareṇa saha sāmyam 
tataḥ prakṛtahetubhyaḥ prayatnavatāṃ siddhāvapi na kṣatiriti 
nanu prayatnavatā jantujātena janitā gandhamādanādaya iti bhavatāmaniṣṭameva tataḥ
prakārāntarābhāvenānekato nivartamānaḥ prayatnavāneka eva sakalakāryakartā sidhyan sarvajña
tvādikamapi pratyujjīvayatīti cet  naitadasti vastupratibandhānupapattericchāyāḥ tat
kṛtāyā anekato nivṛtterasādhanatvāt  yadi ca kathañcidasau na svīkurute svīkārayituṃ
tarhi caraṇamadanādinārādhanīya  prativādīti
nāyaṃ nyāya  svatantrasya prasaṅgo'pi na saṅgataḥ 
prasaukyamapāye'sya na hyanekatvamīhitam 
viparyaya paryavasāyivyāpāratvāt tasyeti 
nanūbhayathāpi tāvat parasyāniṣṭameva na hi sattvalokaḥ sakalo'pi prayatnadvāreṇa
kāraṇamiṣyate api tu cetanālakṣaṇakarmādhipatyamātreṇa tataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaṃ
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
kāryatvamekamanekaṃ vā prayatnavantamantike dadhānaṃ sādhanamaniṣṭasyaiveti cet  tat kimi 
dānīṃ parāniṣṭamātrasiddhaye sādhanamupanyastam kiṃ nu svasādhyasiddhaye  tatra ca pareṣṭa
siddhirasiddhirvātmana iti na a  kiñcit sādhanopanyāsaphalamiti vaktumāha
sthityā pravṛttyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā

yatpunaruktam
viśeṣe'nugamābhāva

iti  asiddhiriti vartate  ayamabhiprāyaḥ  na prakṛtameva ghaṭapiṭharādikāryamekena

ekena yatnavatā dṛṣṭakāryāṇāmanvaya iti  athavā kulālo nāmaikaḥ kaścidasti bhūta
bhautikasaṃvittirāśirayaṃ kumbhakārādiprajñaptiviṣayaḥ karacaraṇasamudāyo veti  vastutaḥ
kenaikena karaṇaṃ kumbhāderupalambhagocara ityarthaḥ 
atha kimanena nirbandhena  yādṛśa eva kaścidekavyahāragocaro dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśaḥ

saṃśayo'thavā
iti  sādhyasyeti śeṣaḥ  kulālavat saṃghātamātratayā kāryatvasanniveśādibhāve'pi prayatna 
vatkartṛpūrvaṃkatvasyābhāvāt etadabhāve'pi vā tasya bhāvāt  tatrāpyanyatkārakeṣṭī
vā anavasthānādapratipattiḥ 
nanu cācetanasvabhāvaḥ svayamutpattau paraṃ cotpādayituṃ prayatnavantamapekṣate  sa tu
svayameva tathāvidhabuddhayādhāra iti kimapareṇa  na hi jaḍā ghaṭādayaḥ prakāśamapekṣanta
iti prakāśenāpyaparaḥ prakāśo'pekṣitavya ityasti niyamaḥ  tataḥ keyamanavastheti 
evaṃ tahi kulālasaṃjñita eva prayatnavān buddhīndriyādikalāpaḥ kathamaparamapekṣate 
tasmāccetano'cetano vā kalāpaḥ svabhāvenaivāparacetanamapekṣya jāyate janayati vetyupa

parihāreṇa sthitimanubhaveyuḥ  tathāvidhādhiṣṭhānasvīkāre tu svabhāvaviprakarṣādanupa

rabdhamityāstāṃ tāvat
tat kimanena nirbandhena  nirbaṃndhe vā virodhyadhyakṣasthūladoṣāvatāraprasaṅgāt
tathāpyasiddhirveti viparītasiddhiryojayiṣyata iti sāntargarvo gajanimīlitenaiva vāḍava
dhīrya yathaivānena sarvakāryotpattau nimittakāraṇamīśvaro gṛhītaḥ tathainaṃ saṃbhāvya cetana
syāpi cetanāntarāpekṣāyāmanabasthānabhī rostenaivāvyabhicārānāśritya saṃśayamāha  atha
prayatnavānapi kulālo na svaśarīre kiṃ tu kumbhādau tataḥ svaśarīrasiddhaye kiṃ na
paramapekṣeta  tarhīśvarābhimato'pi parakaraṇaprayatnavān na svaśarīra eva svātmani
kāritravirodhāditi kiṃ na paramapekṣeta  na cāpekṣate  tato yadarthakāri kāryādi vā
tatpratiyatnavadadhiṣṭhitamiti tattenaiva vyabhicārīti saṃśayasiddhiḥ 
nanu tasya śarīrameva nāstīti kuto'nekānta eṣaḥ  tadetat prakaraṇavismaraṇa
phalam  tathā hyanvayopadarśanasamīyā kulāle sāṃvṛtamekatvamaṅgīkṛtya tādṛksāṃvṛtaika
puruṣanirmeyatvaṃ jagato bhavataiva svīkṛtamityayamasmākamavakāśaḥ  yadi tu vāstavameva

nanu tathāpi tādṛśaḥ
sādhyasyāsiddhau kena vyabhicāra siddhau ca vyabhicāraḥ
kiṃ kariṣyati  vyabhicārādasiddhireveti cet  asiddhau tahi vyabhicāro'pi nāstīti
kuto'siddhiriti siddhiriti vā vyavatiṣṭhate  kāryatvādeśca vastudharmasya vastusanneva dharmī

tatrābhyupāyaḥ kāryāṅgam
