saṃbhavāt  tasmānnidarśanaṃ nāma gṛhītavismṛta pratibandhasādhakapramāṇasmaraṇadvāreṇaiva
hetāvupayogi na svasannidhimātreṇa 
saca pratibandho dvārāntareṇa vā gṛhīto vihāyasā smaryeta svādhikaraṇapramāṇa
prasiddho vā  tatra tāvat prathamakalpanamapāstaṃ prāgeva dṛśyaśarīropādhinā dhīmātreṇa
vā kāryatvāderghaṭāvapi pratibandhagrahaṇopāyāpāyāt  caramaṃ cāsaṃbhava tathā hi
yadi nāma vyogni dvayanivṛttirupalabdhā tathāpyekābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayāyogādanyābhāve
viśvarūpasya ca tatrāvṛtteḥ kasya kena saṃbandhabodha syāt  karabhagardabhāderapi b
kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaprasaṅgācca  anyatrānvayadarśana sahāyasya tathā pratītiriti cet 
nanu sahadarśana mevānvayārthaḥ tacca kadācit karabhāderapyastīti sādhvī vyavasthā 
sa ca buddhi
na sahṛdarśanamanvayasyārtha ki tvekasaṃbhavaprayukto'nyabhāvaḥ 
matkāryatvayorasti nānyatreti cet  na tadbhāvaprayuktatvaṃ nāmāparabhāvasya na tadvyāpārāt
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalī
prāgabhāvinaḥ sattālābhādanyaḥ prāgabhāvaśca nānupalabdhivyāpāramantareṇeti pratyakṣānupa
lambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekayoniścaye saṃśayoṃ nāma kīdṛk hetuphalasthitāviti tatpratīti
pratibandhasmaraṇameva vihāyasā vidhīyata iti prathamapakṣa evāyam 
kiṃ ca kimidamīśvare'nujo vivṛttāvivṛttāviṣkaraṇamātramatrabhavataḥ uta prati  vandī
kṛte  dhūmānumāne'pi saiva gatiḥ ekatrobhayasaṃbhavamupalakṣyāntarīkṣe ekavyāpāranivṛttau
anyanivṛtterupalakṣaṇād vyāptigraha iti  yadyeṣa eva nyāya tadā tadicchatāmanibandhanaḥ
prakṛtapradveṣaḥ kevalamevaṃ vilayatā dahanānumānamapi hāritaṃ dūratarā tu prakṛtasiddhiḥ
uktakrameṇa gardabhenāpi tasya prasaṅge vahnāvapi hastakatyāgāt  yadā tu gatyaṃntara mapi tatra
prakṛtāsaṃbhavi saṃbhavi tadā kuto vandīkaraṇaṃ śaraṇam 
evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāraḥ tadatiprasaṅgabhayādevāśrīyate na tu sa eva
samaya iti cet  evaṃ sati bhavataiva kimayamatiprasaṅge bharo datto neti kośapānaṃ
kartavyam yo hi pratyakṣānupalabdhī vihāya vihāyasi vavyāpāranivṛttyā dhūmanivṛttim
ādāya vyāptimabhidhatte taṃ prati yathā vastumātrasyāpi tatra vyāpāroparamāttenāpi
vyāptisiddhiḥ syādityatiprasaṅgaḥ tathā yo'pi pratyakṣānupalabdhīruddhūya tadyogyapuruṣa 
viśeṣavyāpāraviraheṇa vyomani ghaṭādikāryatvanivṛtti darśayitvā tena vyāptimasya
manyate taṃ prati puruṣamātrasyāpi tatra nivṛttyā tenāpi vyāptiḥ tathā kāryāntaratvasyāpi
nivṛttyā tasyāpi syāditi vyaktamatiprasaṅgamātrametat na nyāya iti paśyāmaḥ 
dhūme gardabha divyabhicāradarśanāśa vastumātreṇa vyāptiriti yuktam puruṣamātrasya
tu vyabhicārānupalabdherna damatiprasaṅgamātrodbhāvanaṃ bhaviṣyati  naivaṃ samānanyāyānām
ekatra bādhakadarśanamanyatrāpi śaṅkāmutpādayati  yadi hi vihāyasi ubhayanivṛttidarśanaṃ
pratibandhasādhakaṃ bhavet vastudhūmayorapi na bādhyeta tatra tu bādhyamānamanyatrāpi katham
ekāntāvasāyasādhanaṃ syāt  na ca pakṣīkṛte neva vyabhicāra ityapi na pakṣīkaraṇaṃ
mantraprabhāvaḥ kiṃ tu vyāptigrāhakadārḍhyam  tacca yadi nabhasi ubhayābhāvamātram tadā
tatra bādhakādhigaterastaṃ dāḍhamiti satyapi a  pakṣīkaraṇavyabhicārāśaṅkā na
nivartata iti 
vyomāsti vyatirekabhūmiriti ced dhūmasya dhūmadhvajād
utpattāvapi ki sa eva samayo nātiprasaṅgodayāt 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
yadyevaṃ bhavataiva kiṃ vinihito nātiprasaṅgetara
stasmin bādhavilokanaṃ punarihāpyārekamākarṣati 
iti saṃgrahaḥ 
tasmāt nākāśe dvayanivṛttyā vyāptisiddhiḥ siddhavyāptikayostvabhāvadarśanaṃ
gṛhītavyāptismaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt  na ca vyāptigrāhakaṃ kiñcidupapadyata ityuktam  tasmāt
anvayamātrabhāve'pi vyatirekābhāvādanekānta eveti sthitam  vastutastu vyatirekavadanva
yo'pyasya durlabha eva  yasya hi pratyakṣāgocaratayā abhāvaprayuktaḥ kāryābhāva iti
pratyetumaśakyaṃ tasyānvayo dūrotsārita eva pratyakṣagrāhyatvāt tasya  pratyakṣaṃ hi paridṛśyamāne
vastuni deśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi svapravṛttiyogya
mevāntarbhāvya vyāptimavakalpayet na svabhāva
viprakṛṣṭamapīti uktaprāyam  tataścānvayamātraṃ gajanimīlitenāvadhīrya vyatirekābhāvenaiva
duṣaṇamuktam  vastutastu nānvayo na vyatireka iti prayatnavanmātre sādhye kāryatvamasādhā
raṇameveti vā darśayitumāha
saṃśayo'thavā
iti  pratyakṣādiyogyāpekṣayā sādhāraṇānaikāntikam caitanyamātrāpekṣayā asādhāraṇam
ityartha  nanu śarīropādhibuddhikṛtaṃ kārya sidhyat buddhimātrakṛtaṃ sidhyatyeva śiśapākṛtamiva
vṛkṣakṛtam viśeṣe sāmānyānapavāditi kathamucyate'nvayābhāvaḥ  evaṃ sati vyatireko'pi
tadapekṣayā syāditi cet  kā no hāniḥ buddhimati kāryahetoranvayavyatirekavattvābhyupaga
māditi  uktamatra evamanvayavyatirekakalpane jāṭharacitrakā digatenāpi rūpeṇa dhūmādanumi
tamagni saṃśayāno nābhimataikāgracittaḥ pravarttatetyādi 
api ca na tatra saṃbhavītyeva pratyakṣeṇa yatkiñcidvastuno rūpaṃ kāryasya vyāpakam
avadhāryate api tvadhyavasāyāpekṣayā  adhyavasāyaśca puruṣeṇa kṛta eva iti buddhimatā
veti viśiṣṭa viṣaya eva pravartate tādṛśyeva puruṣādiśabdasya rūḍhe  na tu karādivyā
pāranirapekṣeṇa caitanyamātreṇeti caitanyamātraṃ sadapyudāsīnamanvayagrahaṇakāle'dhyava
sāyasya viśeṣonmukhenaiva pravṛtteḥ sāmānyaśabdatve'pi vā prakṛtaviśeṣamākṣipyaivāgni
vyāptivat  sa cādhyavasāya pratyakṣavyāpārānusārī tadyogyameva rūpaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt
na tu tadayogyamapi jāṭharādivat tārṇādivacca evaṃ puruṣeṇāpi vyāptī kasyacit
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
śarīropādhividhurasya buddhimātrasya tadayogyasya pratikṣepaḥ syādeva  apratikṣepastu kharvādi
bhedasyaiya  ayameva nyāyaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣeṇānvayagrahaṇe 
b athāṅgārasaṅgādagurukhaṇḍajanitaṃ dhūmamupalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣayogyatayā
indhanādyantareṇāpi tadanvayaprasaṅga iti cet  tatkimidānīṃ pramāṇaviṣayapratiniyamam
anādṛtya yatra kacit pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ yena kenacidanvayaṃ pratyetviti vivakṣitam  evaṃ
sati hetumadābhāsavyavasthāvilopāt sarvasya sarvasiddhiriti pratiniyatasādhanānveṣo
viphalaḥ 
atha pratyakṣeṇa svayogyamullaṃghyāpi vyāptigṛhītetyucyate  tadasiddham  yadāpi
pratyakṣaṃ svapravṛttiyogye'pi vastunyavāntarabhedāpekṣayā sāmānyamudāsayadanvayaṃ pratipadyate
tadā kaiva kathā svapravṛttyayogyasyātyantaṃ vijātīyasya  na cāsmākaṃ pakṣa pratyakṣayogyeṇa
sarveṇa vyāptiriti kiṃ tu pratyakṣayogyeṇaiva tatkṛtā vyāptiriti  anyathā gardabhādibhirapi
dhūmakumbhāderevānvayaprasaṅgaḥ  kimataḥ param  kathaṃ punaratrāvāntarabhedāpekṣa eva vyāptigraho
na darśanayogyatāmātrāpekṣaḥ  vikalpastu vāsanāprabodhamātrārthamapekṣitapratyakṣādisannidhira
niyatodayākāratayā na pratiniyataṃ viśeṣamāveśayitumarhatīti 
satyam ataeva vyatirekasādhanyā anupalabdheravatāraḥ  tatra yathā vahni 
puruṣābhyāṃ dhūmakumbhayoranvayādhyavasāye sahāyatāmanupalabdhi pratipadyate pūrvasthitiranyata
utpattiranyata āgamanamiti tridhā bhinnasaṃbhavavyatirekaṃ sādhayantītarathānupayogāt
tathā yadi gardabhānvaye vedanamātrānvaye vā pratipadyeta syādeva tābhyāmapi vyāptiḥ
nānyathā yato na pratyakṣamātraṃ vyāpti pratipadyate nāpyanupalambhamātraṃ kiṃ tu pratyakṣānupa
lambhāvanyonyasahāyāviti nirṇītaṃ śāstre bahuśa  asmābhirapi trika pañcaka cintāyāṃ
kiñciditi 
na ca gadaṃbhādyanvaye tasyāḥ sāhāyakamasti  etena dhūmaviśeṣāpekṣayānupalambha
vyāpārābhāvo vyākhyāta iti naivavādini kaścit paryanuyogaḥ  yastu pratyakṣa gocare'pi
tatkṛtāṃ vyāptimupavarṇayati tasya tadviṣaya eva vyāptigrahaviraha iti duḥsthā vyavasthā 
tataśca tasyaivāsau paryaṃnuyogaḥ  tasyāpyanupalabdhivyāpārābhāvānneti cet na yataḥ
pratyakṣa yogye'pi tatkṛtavyāptivādino'nupalambhavyāpāravirahe'pi tatkṛtavyāptimicchataḥ
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
kaḥ pratiroddhā  yadi hyasya vrīḍā syādapratyakṣayogya eva tadvayāpāraṃ kathaṃ varṇayet 
athopādānādividā prayatnavatā kāraṇadarśanādeva gardabhasya nirāsaḥ kimatrānupalabdhyā 
evaṃ tarhi dṛśyamānenaiva vyāptimupavarṇayan  na ca darśanapathātikrāntena na ca
śarīropādhi vyavadhūya caitanyamātramupalabdhaṃ kacit  yadi ca darśanabalādeva vyavasthā
caitanyamātrādhiṣṭhitaṃ śarīraṃ kumbhādi janayat dṛṣṭameveti na gardabhenānvayavirodhaḥ tat
kathamanupalabdhiapratikṣepa  vyāpakagatā sāmānyadharmā eva vyāptau sādhakāḥ
itareṣāṃ vyabhicāradarśanenānyatra śaṃkāvakā śā  deva na gardabhenānvaya iti cet  nanu
vyabhicāradarśana miti tadabhāve'pi bhāvadarśana mityanupalabdhivyāpārābhāve'sādhanatvam
upanīyamānamanupalabdhereva sādhanāṅga niścaye vyāpāraṃ paridīpayati 
yadi ca viśeṣe vyāpāraśaṃkākula sāmānyamanusarati bhavān upādānādya
bhijñamapi viśeṣamapahāya caitanyamātreṇa gadaṃbhasādhāraṇena siddhasādhanayogyena tato'pi
vā sāmānyena kāraṇamātreṇa vyāptimabhidhattām  evaṃ hi sati sarvathā dūrīkṛtaḥ
śaṃkāvakāśaḥ syāditi  etāvattu sāmānyamavamanya upādānādyabhijña viśeṣe sthitirna
tu tadapyavajñāya yathādṛṣṭa iti kimatra sāmarthyamanyatra jāḍyāt  pratyakṣānupalambhavādi
śaṃkāvakāśini
nastu yāvati yādṛśi sāmānye pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāro na tatra śaṃkā
cana vyāpāra iti nāsī kacana svayamicchayā vyāptimupanayatyapanayati vā pramāṇenaiva
samarpaṇāditi na doṣaḥ 
nanu so'pi hetumātrakṛtaṃ vā kāryagrāmaṃ bruvan pratyakṣayogye'pi pratyakṣavyāpāropa
lambha ki na paśyati  paśyatyeva viparyaṃyabādhakādāgamācca tasya tadābhyupagamāt 
pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ tu śarīraviśeṣādhika eva cetasi sa pramāṇayati  icchāyāmapi
karādivyāpāroparame kāryābhāvāt taddvāreṇaiva kulālādivyapadeśaviṣayasya samudāyasya
pratyakṣatvavyavahārāt  na tviyaṃ gatiḥ prayatnasacivacittamātre  tadāpyanumānādanvayaḥ
pratyeṣyate  na ca pratyakṣasyaiva kaścidanurodhaḥ  upalambhānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatireka
niścayaḥ kartavyaḥ  sa copalambhaḥ pratyakṣarūpo'numānarūpo veti nātra nirbandhaḥ 
atra cintyate  kiṃ tadeva śarīropādhikaṃ cittaṃ prayatnavañcittamātraśabdenābhi
matam utānyat  tattve kimanumānena pratyakṣasiddhau vivādābhāvāt  tena cānvaya
vyatirekau siddhau kāryamātreṇa ca tadvyabhicāro vyaktaḥ  anyatve liṅgābhāvadoṣaḥ
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
bhāṣaṇāde kāryastha śarīriṇaiva caritārthatvāt  na ca tenānumitenāpi vyāptiḥ svī
kriyate vyatirekāniścayāt pūrvavat  evaṃ tarhi bahiṣāpi dhūmasya vyāptinaṃ deśakālā
vasthāniyatena kiṃtu vahnimātreṇa  tacca dṛśyamānādanyenaiveti vikalpe vyabhicārādi
doṣa sādhāraṇa iti tādagviśeṣavirahiṇā sāmānyena vyāptirvaktavyā 
tathehāpīti cet  evamapi jāṭharādigatenāpi rūpeṇa vyāptiprasaṅgo dhūmasya 
tasmānna sāmānyamityeva vyāptāvadhikriyate nāpi viśeṣa ityeva pratikṣipyate b 
dhūmānumānasyaivocchedāt abhimate śikhani pravṛttisandehāt  tato yadi na sveccheva
saṃgrahaparicchedasādhanī tadā pramāṇavyāpāramanviṣya vyavasthāprakrame kiñcit sāmānyaṃ
svīkārapravṛttenāpi pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣiptamarthādeṣitavyam yadviśeṣātikrameṇa nāsyāvatāraḥ 
yathā jvaladbhāsurākāra pātikrame dhūmavyāptigrāhiṇa  kiñcittu pratyakṣasvīkṛtam
apyanupalabdhi pratikṣipati pīṭharādivat sāmarthyāt 
sā hi dahanābhāve kāryābhimatābhāvaṃ sādhayantī dahanabhāvaprayuktatadbhāvavibhā
vanādayogavyavacchedena tatkāryaṃtā sādhanapravṛttāpyanyasya hetutāṃ sādhayatyeva yadabhāve
svayaṃ na vartate  anupalambhapūrvake tu pratyakṣa prāgbhāvādibādhana pravṛttayānupalabdhyānekavastu
rūpasattvābhāve'bhāvasiddhau yadekavastusvabhāvasannidhau sannidhiradhyakṣeṇa pratīyate prāgapi
tadabhāvaprayuktābhāvavibhāvanāt taddhetubhāvasādhane yadapravṛttiyogyatayā pratikṣiptam
adhyakṣeṇa tatpratikṣiptameva 
tato na jāṭharāderanvayaḥ  nāpi kāladeśadaśā bhedabhinna svabhāvapratikṣepaḥ
sarva pratyakṣa svajanmayogyatayā svīkārāt  nāpyanupalabdhyā sā hyatādṛvasvabhāvā
bhāve'bhavantī tadvijātīyahetutāṃ pratikṣipatīti yuktam na tu tasyaiva anyathā tadā
śrayaṇaveyarthyāt  nanu deśādibhinnasvabhāvābhāve'vyayaṃ dhūmo dṛṣṭaḥ na deśādibhinnasyā
pyekākāra
pratyavamaśaṃpratyayena paridṛśyamānarūpeṇa sahakīkaraṇāt darśanāyogyasvabhāvād
anyatra  ataeva vahnimātraśabdābhidheyaṃ tadeva paridṛśyamānayogyādbhedākṛṣṭāvapyabhedāva
bhāsāt 
nanu deśādiviprakṛṣṭamapyadarśanayogyameva  satyaṃ kevalaṃ kadācit kacit  sva
bhāvaviprakṛṣṭaṃ tu satyatyanta vijātīyatayā svīkāraparihārayorbhedena vṛttinaṃ virudhyate 
tato yathānumānavādinā sāmānyamanusaraṇīyamavyāptimasaṃbhavaṃ vā parihartu tathā
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
dṛśyaviśeṣāpekṣayātiriktasāmānyamapi parihartavyamativyāptiparihārāya evaṃ sati yathā
darśanāyogyavahvisāmānyaparihāreṇa tadyogyāvāntarasāmānyena vyāptirekatvavyavasthā ca
yuktā na prayatnavanmātreṇa pratyakṣa pratikṣiptatvāditi 
tatra vyāmohāt pramāṇāntareṇānvayamicchan tattvānyatvābhyāṃ paryaṃnuyujyate 
dahane tu tatpakṣeṇaiva samādhirityuktam  tasmāt pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptijighṛkṣāyāṃ
a tadyogyasāmānyāpekṣāyā ghaṭaviṭapādau dṛṣṭānta iṣṭasya siddhirasiddhiśceti sādhāraṇā
naikrāntikatvaṃ kāryasya  caitanyamātreṇa tu tadayogyenānvayavyatirekayorekasyāpyaniścayāt
'sandigdhānvayavyatirekatvaṃ vaktuṃ yuktamuktam
saṃśayo'thaveti 
siddhaya siddhayoriti prakaraṇāt  tābhyāṃ bhāvābhāvāvuktau  yathāha  upalabdhireva
sattā anupalabdhirasatteti  tataḥ kāryatvādisādhanavati dharmiṇi dṛṣṭānte sādhyatveneṣṭasya
prayatnavanmātreṇa sasvāsattvasandehāt tadadhiṣṭhānānadhiṣṭhānābhyāṃ ca sarvasaṃgrahādekatānvaya
vyatirekānupapatteryuktamasādhāraṇānakāntikatvam 
nanu tathāpyanekānto'pyastu anvayamātraṃ kimiti pratikṣipyate kāryotpattī
buddhereva vyāpāradarśanāt  jāṭharasādhāraṇenāpi rūpeṇa tarhi dhūme'nvayaprasaṅgaḥ dahana
vyāpāradarśanāt  tataśca tadapekṣo vyatireko'pi syāditi prācīnadoṣaḥ  pratyakṣapratikṣepastu
sādhāraṇaḥ 
nanu jāṭharādyabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvānna prācīnadoṣaḥ satyapyanvaya iti cet  kailāsa
karaṇakauśala vikalenāpi kalasasya karaṇaṃ kiṃ na kīrtyate  atha karaṇakauśalasāmānye 
nānvayo'tra  tatrāpi dāhakamātreṇeti na vyaktayupakṣepeṇa kiñcit  jātyapekṣayā tu
tadānyadāpīti kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvaḥ  atha dāhakatvamātraṃ paridṛṣṭaviśeṣād bhinnāṃ
jātimāsthāya vyabhicāra ucyate tadā tadapekṣayānvayo'pi kutaḥ pratyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭāyā
eva jāte radhigamāt  anvaye vā punavrvyābhicārānupapatteriti 
yatpunaḥ sajātīyena pratyakṣataḥ pratibandhaniścayamāśaṃkya na hi sarvatra samāna
jātiranumīyate pratyakṣaśca yasmādasamānajātiḥ apratyakṣadha rūpādivyaktibhiranumīyate
cakṣurādigrāmaḥ tathā candramasaḥ pṛthivyāśca parabhāgādhobhāgāvityuktam tadapi
pāpīyaḥ  tathāhi na tāvad vyāptiśūnyamanumānam vyāptiśca sāmānyena sāmānyasya
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloṃ
bhavantī kathamasamānānumānamanusaheta  tathā ca sā dvidhaiva pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ viparyaya
bādhakād vā  ubhayathāpi dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭasajātīyasyaivānumānam  anyathānyajātīyena dharmeṇa
vyāptimupādāyānyajātīyamanuminotīti mahatī prekṣā 
sāmānyato dṛṣṭānumāne'pi hi yadeva gatisāmānyamanyasthāna prāpti nibandhanamupalabdham
tadevādhikaraṇāntare niścīyata iti kathaṃ vijātīyadharmānumānam  athādhārabhedāpekṣayā
sāmarthyasādhyamavāntarabhedamabhipretyocyate tadanuktasamam  na hi kaścit anumānavādo
tanmātreṇa viśeṣamanicchan b phalinamanumānaṃ samarthayitumīśaḥ  yadi ceśvarānumāne'pi
tādṛśo vyāptiḥ syāt tanmātra viśeṣa siddhayā ceṣṭasiddhiḥ syāt kastatra matsaramācaret 
na ca tanmātraviśeṣāpekṣayā na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyata iti vaktuṃ yuktam
kacidasamānajātyanumāne'pi tathocyate tanmātraviśeṣaśca sarvatrānumāne'sti  viśeṣato
dṛṣṭasya sāmānye'pi tadeva niścīyata iti tadapekṣayā na sarvatra tadevānumīyata iti vaktavyam
bhedādhiṣṭhānatvāt samānajāticintāyāḥ 
tat punaraprakṛtameva  sa tu na sarva pratyakṣo'numīyata iti  yadi prakṛtamagnivat
pratibandhagra he pramāṇamadhikṛtyocyate tadā pratyakṣasyaiva sarvatrānumānam anyatrāpadiṣṭapramāṇa
pravṛtteḥ  atha viparyayabādhakāpekṣayā tadā na vaktavyaṃ na kaścidviśeṣo'gnisādhanāt
īśvarānumānasyeti  anityasādhanāditi tu vaktumucitam  atha kāryahetutāmātreṇaivam
ucyate tadā kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pratyakṣānupalambhasādhana eveti sa eva doṣaḥ  na ca
viparyayabādhakaṃ kiñcidastīti carcitameva  deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgaśca hetumātrāpatti sādhaya
tyapi  tasmāt prakṛtaprameyānavagāhanāt lavata etat na sarvaḥ pratyakṣo'numīyata iti 
anumānakālāpekṣayā tu sarva parokṣa evānumoyate na ca tatra kācid vimatiḥ
ityanuktasamam  indriyaṃ tu na sākṣād buddheranumātuṃ śakyam pratibandhāgrahaṇāt  buddhikāryaṃ
tu keṣucit satsvabhāvābhāvavattatirikta kāraṇasāpekṣatāmāvahatīti tādṛśīndriyaghoṣaṇā 
tatrārādiṣu dṛṣṭajātīyameva sāpekṣatvaṃ yathā sādhyate tathā parabhāgādhobhāgāvapi
ghaṭādikāryeṣu  avagaikasāmagrī pratibaddhau sāmānyato dṛṣṭāvevānumoyete iti sādhyaśūnya
mudāharaṇamapi ityalaṃ bahunā  athavā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpyate kāraṇa 
viśeṣeṇa tu kāryaviśeṣa eveti nyāyaḥ  adhyavasāyamātrato vā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryaviśeṣa
iti pravādaḥ  tatrāyaṃ kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpta mitibruvāṇaḥ
pramāṇāvaṣṭambhena nāma prasiddhimullaṅghayet 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam
tacca pramāṇaṃ vyāptisādhakaṃ dvividhameva pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ vā viparyayabādhakaṃ vā
anayoḥ pratyakṣānumānasvabhāvatvāt anyato niścayāyogāt  tatra tāvaduktakrameṇa
kāryasāmānyasya
no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśād vyāptiḥ samastasya ca
pratyakṣānupalambhato na tadatajjātīyabhedaspṛśaḥ 
prāgbhāvādiniṣedhapūrvakatayā dhūmādivajjanmadhī
ranvetīdṛśamīdṛśāditi yataḥ sāmānyabhedadvayam 
idamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhamasyopalambha upalabhyata ityevaṃ a  hi
pratyakṣānupalambhayorvyāptigrahaṇakramaḥ  tatredamityekajātīyatayā eka pratyavamarśapratibhāsi
dhūmādikamanekakāryajātyantaravyudāsenānekakāraṇajātyantaravyudāsena cāsyeti vahnayādeḥ
ityarthaḥ  tataḥ kāryakāraṇayoḥ pratyekaṃ tajjātīyetarayoritaretarato bhede parāmarśapūrvikā
pravṛttiḥ anyathā sāmathvaiyarthyābhyāmanupayogāt 
tathā hyakāryarāśivyavacchedena vā kāryāntaravyavacchedena vā idametad bhāvā
bhāvānuvidhāyītyavadhāryeta  ādye pakṣe etāni vastuni etanniyatāni ityayamartho
netadvastviti ekākāravirahādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteḥ  nanu kāryatvādinā sāmānyena
idamiti kāryaṃ sanniveśo vetyādi vaktuṃ śakteḥ asiddhametaditi cet  ucyate ih
bhāvābhāvavidhānabuddhidvidhā saṃbhavati dharmiviṣayā dharmaviṣayā ca kāryasya nirva
vikāyabhedena dvaividhyāt  tatrādyā sarvātmanotpattiniścayamupādāya dharmiṇameva viśiṣṭā
kārakroḍīkṛtaṃ kāladeśādibhedabhinnamapi svabhāvamanta rbhāvyai kapratyavamarśād viṣayī
karotīti tadviṣayetyucyate  sa hi saṃbhavinamapyatadākārabhedavirodhinaṃ dharmaṃmudāsayati
dhūmādiṣu dhavalatādivat 
yatra punaravasthitasyaiva dharmiṇo dharmāntaramudayamāsādayati tatra dharmamātrasyaiva
hetubhiranvayavyatirekāviti dharmaviṣayetyucyate  sā punarākāramevodāsayantī dharmamātram
adhiṣṭhānīkaroti rāgādivat  na hyākārakriyādivaijātyamatyantamanubhavantaḥ paṭakūṭādayaḥ
sādhāraṇa rāgayogino gṛhītasāmarthya rāgadravyāntarayogamanumāpya tṛpyanti 
prathamā
 tvākāraśaraṇaiva sarvātmanotpatteḥ  yathaiva hi viśiṣṭākāroparaktaṃ vastu kutaścidupajāyate
tathaiva tadvalotpannenendrijñānenānubhūyānantaraṃ vikalpadvāreṇa vyavahāragocarīkriyata itijñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
kathamākāraparihāra  ataeva dhūmakumbhādivyaktirekatrānupalabhyaprabhavā upalabhamānasya
anyatra tadaiva yadyuktibhedena vyāptisiddhistatraiva tatkāraṇāvasāyo jāyate nānyatra
vyabhicāradarśanādarśanamapekṣyāpi  anantaraṃ tvākāramudāsayet kevalaṃ vyavasthite dharmaṇi
dharmamātrodayadarśinaḥ 
na ca vyavasthite kumbhādau kāryatvādidharmamātrotpattirīkṣyate kṣitidharādau
vābhyupeyate yenākāramanādṛtya rāgavattanmātrameva hetumanumāpayet  sanniveśastarhi sthita
eva tadātmani kumbhakārāditi cet ta drāgapi saṃsthāna vinākṛtāyā mṛdo'nupalabdheḥ 
atha tādṛśasyābhāva eva pūrva yaḥ kumbhaprajñaptigocara iti cet  tadeva saṃsthānaṃ tarhi
puruṣāditi na tāvanmātravyāptiḥ
tathāpi yadi saṃsthānasāmānye puruṣakriyā 
haridrādravyayogo'pi b varṇamātra vidhāyakaḥ 
nanu tathāpi na pūrvasiddhadarśanamityeva vyaktyantare gṛhyamāṇāyā vyāptervyāghātaḥ
tadvalātvanumānameva tatretyanantarameva samarthitam  na ca tāvatā varṇamātraṃ kusumbhasaṃbhava
sādhanasādhu vyabhicārālambanaṃ tu durbalamiti kimatra prāptam 
guṇe'pi dravyavat tasmāt sajātīyaparigrahaḥ 
tatpūrvasiddhe'pyanumā na varṇāt kuṅkumasya ca 
tanniyataviśeṣāpari hi rāgādapi kutaḥ kuṅkumānumā  davīyasī tu varṇa
mātrāt  varṇavacca saṃsthānasyāpi vicitrameva vaijātyamanubhavaviṣayaḥ  tadanayorekatra
jātiniyamena vyāptivyavasthānamaniyamena vā vyaktau vyabhicāro naikaniyataḥ  tasmād
varṇavadanekajātini saṃsthāne'pi tattvaṃ sāmānyamanuvartamānamapi vyāptigrahād bahirbhūtam
eva  evamarthaṃkriyāpi pūrvamasati vastuni puruṣāditi vaktumaśakyam  sarvasāmarthya 
virahiṇaḥ prāgabhāvaprasaṅgenāpūrvotpattiprāpteriti viśiṣṭe vārthakriyāpi puruṣānvayavyati
rekānuvidhāyinīti siddham 
tasmādevaṃvidhā dharmaviṣayāpi vyāptibuddhirna sāmānyamanudhāvati  yadā tu
kārya hetvadhikāreṇa dharmiviṣayeva tadā yathāparidṛṣṭākārārthakriyāsāmānyaṃ samāśritya
yathā kāraṇe pratiniyatasvarūpasāmānyena vyāpakatvāvasāyinī tathā kārye'pi prati
niyatākā sāmānya puraskāreṇeva vyāpyatvāvasāyinī samakṣabuddhiriti na sandehaḥ 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
anyathā kāryavat kāraṇe'pi buddhimadādiviśeṣavyudāsena pravṛttimatī matiḥ kimabhimatam
upanayet  tasmāt kāraṇavat kārye'pi tathābhūtākāra
viśeṣamevamayamavasātumarhati 
tatredānīṃ tadākārabahirbhūteṣu bhūtalādiṣu sadapi kāryatvamabhidhīyamānamanupayukta
meva dharmaviṣayahetuphalagrāhipratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā dharmamātrasāmyasyākiñcitkaratvāt 
na hi tadevākārārthakriyādirūpaṃ tatsāmyonmīlanaheturvā  tadanena sāmyaṃ na kiñcidarthaṃ
puṣṇāti agauṇakāryaśabdapravṛtteranyatra  sa hi saṅkalpaniveśinyudayārthamapekṣitapara
vyāpāramātre artha akārādikamudāsya kṛtasamaya iti na tasya vyāghātaḥ  upapattyanta
reṇa vyāpakatayā yaḥ pratīto dharmaḥ tatraiva nāśavatpratyakṣavyāpāra eva tu svodayasamaya
parisphuradākārādisādṛśyamapekṣate deśādikṛtabhede tu vesadṛśyāvasāya iti na
virodhaḥ 
tasmādekakāra ṇa virahāt pratyekaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhāpekṣāyāmetāni vastūni
etatkāraṇānugāmīnītyanenaivākāreṇa vyāptiniścaya  kārya  kevalamadyāpi na vyakti
kāryenopayoga iti sarvakāryaprakāre vekaika viṣayo'vatiṣṭhate  sa a cāśakyaḥ
kramayaugapadyābhyāmayogāt  tathā hi na tāvat sakṛdeva teṣāmanvayaḥ sarvaprakāropanipāte
darśanasya draṣṭurevāntardhānaprāpteḥ  vyatireko vā śakyaniścaya aśakyaparihāratvāt
keṣāñcidādhārālokaśarīrādīnām 
nāpyekena narāyuṣā kṣamamidaṃ sarvaprakārekṣaṇaṃ
kāryasyāntaviyogataḥ katipayāpekṣāsu kātsnyaṃ kutaḥ 
na khalu bhūyaso'pi bhāgasyābhividhibodhe nirvṛttiḥ na hi tadapi yadyat kāryaṃ tattadevam
iti śakyamabhidhātum etāvaditi tu syāt 
yatpunarekatra pravṛtto vicāra sarvabhāvāṃstathābhāve vyavasthāpayatītyucyate
tatsādhāraṇākārapravṛttimadhikṛtyākṛtyādivyudāsena pramāṇāntarāvalambanāt  pratyakṣa
vyāpāra eva hyekajātigrahaniyama uktaḥ  nanu tatrāpyavāntarānekabhedasaṃbhavādayamevam
ityabhidhātumaśakteranāśvāsaḥ  atra vā bhedatiraskāreṇa dhūmādijātyantaramavalambya
saṃvyavahāre kāryatāmāśritya jātyanta reṣvapi kīdṛśo doṣa iti cet  na vayaṃ svecchayā
kaścida tiraskurmaḥ puraskurmo vā kāmapi jātim  adhyakṣapūrvakastu saṃkalpo yathā
arthānupasthāpayati bhedenābhedena vā tathā hetuphalabhāvavyavahāramavatarāmaḥ  sa tujñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalī
prakṛtiviśeṣamāsādya yadi sūkṣmasthūlabhāvena bhedeṣvabhibhūtisāmarthyāsāmarthyābhyāṃ bhinatti
vṛttim kimatra kaiścitakartavyaṃ tadvivartastu cintyaḥ  tatra
dhūmo'vāntara bhedavatyapi yathā jātyantarāpohitaṃ
sārūpyaṃ viṣayīkaroti hṛdayaṃ ki kāryamātre tathā 
eka saṃsthānādyanugamānanugamayoḥ pratyātmavedyatvāt nāparamatra prārthyate nirṇaya
nibandhanam anyathā ca vyapadeśārthakriyāviniyogādisaṃkaraprasaṅgaḥ  tasmānna kacit
kāraṇe sarvakāryaprakāraṇāṃ krameṇa yaugapadyena vā adhyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavā vyāptirupa
pādayituṃ śakyeti kimābhyām  ata evaṃmukhena sarvakāryavyāptivādinaḥ svābhiprāya
nivedanamātrametad vartmani sthāṇūpadeśaghoṣaṇavat  tathā ca sati icchāmātraṃ sādhanam
astviti sphuṭamanayorapārthaṃkatvam  tasmādābhyāmata idamiti matiḥ kāryāntaravyava
cchedenaiva bhavantīna kārya mātragocarokara gasaṃvādamāsādayati  tato niścayamupādānādi
vido'panudannāha 
I
saṃśayo'thaveti 
pareṣṭasiddhirna parasya bādhane prasādhane vedanayatnamātrayoḥ 
ananvayo'bhīṣṭaviśeṣasādhane vipakṣasandehasahaṃ tu sādhanam 
sādhye ca dṛśye vyabhicāra eva dṛśyaṃ na cenna vyatirekasiddhiḥ 
na cānvayo'pi vyatirekavad vā vyāptirviśeṣeṇa na cetarasya 
 keciditi mātṛkāyām
 dvitīyaḥ khaṇḍaḥ 
evaṃ sati satyapi vyāptiraśakyaniścayā saṃbhāvyata iti kimatra sāmpratamiti
b cet  paśya
kāryaṃ tāvadanekajāti janakaścaiko jaḍo vīkṣate
nānābhedavato na caikaniyamajñāne'nyabhede'pi tat 
yadyajjātikame kahetuviditaṃ tattattadaṅgaṃ tato
naivaṃ cedatisañjanaṃ na ca mataḥ sādhyopame'yannayaḥ 
na hi nānāprakārakāryaṃjananaṃ nāma prayatnavatyeva niyatam vahnayāderapi vividha
sāmagrīmadhyamadhyāsīnasya dhūmabhasmāṅgārāṅgatāpapākapāradotsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛti
vicitrakāryakriyādarśanāt  yadi paraṃ prayatnavato'dhiṣṭhānenetyatra vivādaḥ na caikasya tatra
niyame jñāte kāryāntare'pi niyamajñānamupapadyate yathoktaṃ prāk  tato yāvantaḥ prakārā
ekahetavo niścitāḥ tāvantastasya hetoścetanasyetarasya vā sādhanaṃ yujyante  anyathā
stimitendhanasakhena śikhinā gṛhītadhūmavyāptiraparicitatatkāryaṃbhāvairbhasmādibhirapi
dahanamanuminuyāt  na caivaṃ tasmāttajjātibhedo vyakto vyāptigrahaśca pṛthak pṛthagapekṣya
māṇo yatra kacittadgrahaṇena yena kenacidanumānamunmūlayati 
kaḥ punarevamāha yatra kacidgṛhītavyāptiryena kenacidanumimītāmiti ekadharmānu
vṛttivirahe hetorevābhāvāt  na hi tadā bhasmasādhanamavyāpteḥ  nāpi dhūmo'siddheḥ 
kuṭakūṭādau kāryatvamevānyadharmānanuvṛttāvapyanumāne vartamānaṃ hetu syāditi cet  na
kāryatvasyāpi prāgavyāptevistareṇa sādhanāt  tatra yathā kulagiriḥ kulālavyāpārakāle
svabhāvavaikalyādikalitaniyamaḥ tathā sadapi kāryatvaṃ prāmāṇyapravṛttyā dhūmajanmanīva
rāsabha iti pramāṇena vyāptigrahavirahe na kaścidviśeṣaḥ  tadayaṃ ghaṭādau kāryaviśeṣe
gṛhītavyāptiḥ sarvato na kāryatāmātreṇa vā vyāpakamanumātu  na tu vyāptigrahaṇasādhana
vyavasthayobhinnādhikaraṇatāmatikrāmatīti kathamatiprasaṅgopālambhaparihāra 
tasmānnaikadharmānuvṛttimātreṇopayogaḥ  kena vā dhūmasaṃbhavinaḥ kāryatvavastutvādayo
bhasmani bhasmasādeva kṛtā  santo'pi vyabhicāriṇa iti cet  nanu savyabhicāro
vyāptiviyogādeva vyāptau tadgandhasyābhāvāt  sa ca vyāptyabhāvaḥ kāryatvenāpi
avajita iti tatrāpi vyabhicāro dunivāraḥ  āhtyādarśanaṃ tu viprakarṣādapi syāt 
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalo
na tāvatā tadabhāva eva tanmūlabhūtāyā avyāptestādavasthyāt  yadi tu vyāptāveva
savyabhicāraḥ tadā nitarāmavyāptāvityalaṃ mithyābhiniveśena  tad yadyapi sādhāraṇa
dharmā tanmātraṃ vyāptimanādṛtya sādhanamiṣyate kiṃ na bhinna evaṃ bhūdharādisādhāraṇaṃ dharmam
anādṛtyetyatiprasaṅgastadavasthaḥ
nāpyayaṃ nayaḥ sādhyasamānīkṛte kalasādāvapyasti tatrāpi yathāyathā pratisara
śarābodañcanādiṣu kumbhakārakṛtimupalabhāmahe a tathātathaivamapīdamapyanena sṛjyata
iti pratiyantaḥ paricitakriyebhya eva prakārebhyastadvayāpāramavadhārayāmaḥ anyathā
taddoṣānativṛttiḥ  tasmād yadi paramārthataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyaka evāyaṃ sakalaprakāra
kāryagrāmaḥ tathāpi svayamakiñcitakara iti pramāṇavṛttyapekṣayā
siddhaṃ yādṛgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat 
sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate 
iti  yadṛṣṭerakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavati śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādivat sanni
veśādi
pra vā  
taccāsiddhamityākṛtam 
tādgeva yadīkṣyeta tannagādiṣu dharmiṣu 
yuktaṃ tatsādhanādasmādyathābhīṣṭasya sādhanam 
nanu bhavatyevāsmākaṃ sarvatra pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhiḥ sā sādhyabuddhirevānumānam
iti niyamaḥ kathañcit kasyacittatrāpyabhāvāt  kiṃ ca kṛtabuddhiriti kāryamātra
buddhirvā puruṣamātrabuddhirvā  yadi kṛtamātrabuddhiḥ sā bauddhasthāpi siddhā sindhubhūdharā
diṣu  sāvayavatvācca tadārambhasaṃbha vitvameva kṛtatvam  atha pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhi 
sā sādhyabuddhirevānumānamiti cocyate tatastadabhāvānnānumānamiti kathamucyamānaṃ
nopaplavate 
yadāha naca vyāmohāt kasyacit sādhyabuddhayabhāve hetorasiddhatādoṣaḥ sarvānu
māneṣu tadbhāvaprasaṅgāditi  yadapīdamucyate tādṛkkāryatvādi niṣiddhamacalādiṣviti
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
tatrāpi na kāryatvādinā kailāsakalasādeḥ kiñcidviśeṣamupalabhāmahe  āha ca nāpi
kaścidviśeṣaḥ kṣityādihetūnāṃ prāsādādihetubhyo yenāmī nirabhiprāyāḥ santaḥ prayatna
nirapekṣā  pratiniyamavatā ca vyāpāreṇa tadvantaḥ syuḥ na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāṃ prayatnavatā
karaṇadharmāṇāṃ kriyāsu svātantryamupalabdhipūrvam sarvatra buddhimadadhiṣṭhiteṣveva prāsādādi
prasavopalabdheriti 
atrocyate neyaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ siddhāntābhiniveśavāsitabuddhīnadhikṛtya kīrtitā
kiṃ tu saṃvyavahārapragalbhapuruṣamātrāpekṣayā  tasya ca pūrvapratītapratibandhasmaraṇavataḥ
kāraṇaparāmarśave mukhyābhāve bhavatyeva devakulādau tādṛśī buddhinaṃ tu malayamakarālayādī 
tadanayorasyā dhiyo bhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamavyavasthāpya sthātuṃ prabhavataḥ dhūmadvaya 
darśane'pi tathābhāvaprasaṅgāt  iyaṃ ca kāmaṃ sādhyabuddhireva kaḥ punarenāmetadvato'numāna
nibandhanamāha tadabhāvād vā bhūdharādau tadabhāvam  kiṃ tu jātibhedamātropalakṣaṇārthamasyā

smaraṇavānna vā  ādye pakṣe tasyaiva nācalādau puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ kulālānumānasyāpi
prasaṅgādityupapāditam  tatkathamabhraṣṭadarśanānāṃ tadbhāvaniyama  tata eva vicitraṃ
jagadityādimatirapi na vyāptigrahasmaraṇabalāt kiṃ tu darśanāntaraprabhavapravādavaśāt
tamaśṛṇvatāmabhāvāt viparītavādavat 
vyāptivimūḍhānāṃ tvityādi siddhasādhanaṃ ca  udāharaṇamapi pāpīya kṛta
buddhayabhāvasya jātibhedamātropadarśanaparatvāt  na ca vādiprativādyapekṣayā tadbhāvābhāva
cintetyuktam svayaṃ vā abhiniveśenānyathāpi saṃkalpasaṃbhavāt  pratyakṣāpekṣayā tu
vyāvahārikādhikāreṇa cinteyam  tasya cāviditavedādisaṃketasya vaidikavākye
tatpraticchandena ca racitamaparaṃ śṛṇvato nipuṇamapi nirūpaya iścintaya tāvat kīdṛśo
viśeṣāvasāyaḥ kalasakuliśādivat sarvaprakārāṇāṃ puruṣaiḥ kāraṇadarśanāt pratyakṣa
svabhāvānāṃ śabdānāṃ pratyakṣabhedakalpane dhūmādiṣvapi prasaṅgāt  tataśca
yadbhāvaḥ puruṣānvayavyatiricostadbhāvabhājaḥ sthitā
nānyasmād vacasaśca vaidikagirāṃ bhedo'sti śakyātmanoḥ 
tulyātīndriyasūcanā ca niyataṃ taikatra cāśvāsanaṃ
vedastena na pauruṣeyapadavīmaprāpya viśrāmyati 
yadi tadā ko'vakāśastadbhāvasya pratyakṣamahāvejā  b  tyeṣu śailādiṣu 
tadetadāyātam
CALOR
na ca laukikavaidikavākyayorvejātya saṃbhave samayamātreṇa parājetavyo mīmāṃsakaḥ 
na ca pratyakṣākṣiptavyāptikaṃ vākyatvameva tatra śaraṇam  kṛtakatve tu yaduktaṃ tadapi
cintitaṃ cintayiṣyate cānantaramiti  nanu tathāpi tadvyāpte'pi kārye kāryatvādi dṛṣṭam
itaratrāpīti yathā ghaṭādi prayatnavannāntarīyakam tathā pṛthvīdharādyapi syāditi cet 
nanūktamatra kāryatvādi vidyamānamapi tatrāśakyavyāptigrahatayodāsīna meveti tenābhidya
mānādapi kāryāntarānna yatnavataḥ sparśo'pi labhyate kevalaṃ kāryaṃ kāryamiti śabda
mātramabhidyamānamavaśiṣyate  tad yadi tadeva dvārāntareṇa śaraṇīkṛtamāyuṣmatā tatra
sākṣād dūṣaṇāśravaṇāt tadā tadapi kākabhakṣaṇaprāyamityādarśayannāha 
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
eka kāryaviśeṣameva kalayan hetoviśiṣṭaṃ nijaṃ
lakṣyāgneriva kāryamātramamunā vyāptaṃ mudhā manyate 
tajjātīyakameva kāryamaparo nāvaiti taddhetukaṃ
hanta dhvāntaviśeṣa eṣa viduṣāmadhyakṣavastunyapi 
eka ma
vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ 
na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśane 
 pra vā   
etena yadapyuktaṃ nāpyatra śabdasāmyādacetanopādānatvasya samāropeṇa sādhya
siddhiḥ anityatvādinā kṛtakatvādiṣviva pratyāsatterihāpi vāstavatvāt  na ca
jātibhedo dharmiṇordharmayoḥ sarvatra vāstavīṃ pratyāsatti bhinatti kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ
śabdaghaṭajātibhedena pratyāsatterabhāvaprasaṅgāditi  tadapyanavakāśam  na hi nagādāva
cetanatvasya sopādānatvasya samāropaṃ brūmaḥ  tanmātraṃ tu vyāptibahirbhāvādasatkalpamiti 
yadi cānyadevācetanopādānatvaṃ cetanāpekṣi siddhamanyadeva cācalādau dṛśyata
iti kiṃkṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet  upādhikṛtaḥ  kina bhinnadharmiṇordharmayorapīti
cet  na vaiṣamyāt  acetanopādānaṃ dhūmasthānīyaṃ kāryahetvabhimānāt na ca kaścittasya
dharmibhedādbhedamāha  yadā tvacetanopādānatvādacalādī cetanāpekṣatvaṃ vivakṣitam tadā
dhūmatvena dhūmo vahnimānityevaṃprāyā sthitiḥ  evaṃ ca sati dhūmadvaye dhūmatvayorbhedaḥ
prasañjanīya iti kathaṃ sāmyam  evamevāstviti cet na bhidyamāno hyupādhirupādhi
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānam
mantamapi bhindyāt  bhedaścaikapratyavamarśabahirbhāvalakṣaṇo na dhūmamupādhi spṛśati yena
svagataṃ bhinattu yathā kumbhāmbhodharādiracetanatvopādānatvamityacodyametat 
nanu na dṛṣṭastāvaddharmibhedena dharmabheda iti cet  yadrūpapuraskāreṇa pratibandha
sādhaka pramāṇavṛttistasyābhede bhidyamānāpi dharmijātirabhinnavadābhāsamānā na bādhikā 
tadbhede tu tadgataṃ dharmāntaramabhidyamāanamapi bhinnavadābhāsamānaṃ na sādhaka miti
nyāyaḥ  anyathā jaladharāthināpi kumbhakārasya paryeṣaṇāprasaṅgaḥ  tadapāyespi vihāyasi
balāhakodayadarśanānneti cet  na tatprabhavasyaiva ghaṭasyeva tasya maruto kṣepaḥ kiṃ na
saṃbhāvyate  atha ca vāridhāritvamātramubhayatra dṛṣṭamiti yathā tatra saṃjñābhedamātrabhedo
vyavasthāpyate tathātrāpīti yuktam  pratibandhaniścayo hi pramāṇaviṣayasvabhāvaniyame sati
bhavati tadviruddhāniyamarūpaṃ ca sādhāraṇatvam 
pramāṇapratibaddho hi niścayastadviṣayasvarūpollaṅghe'pi bhavan pramāṇāpramāṇasādhyaḥ
syāt  na caivam tasmānnānekāntaḥ  nāpyasiddhiradhyakṣavyāpārānusārāt  tadiha
pāṇḍutvasyāgnivyabhicāro dṛṣṭa iti dṛṣṭāntasya sādhyaśūnyatāniṣedha eṣaḥ  ata eva
nānumāna miti pratibandhābhāvādaniścayaphalamidamubhayatra  na tu siddhavyāptikayordahana
pāṇḍutayorvyābhicāreṇa sādhanavaidhuryam vyāptisiddhāvanumānāpavādasyāśakyasādhana
tvāt vyabhicārasyaivāyogāt  sarvopasaṃhāravatī hi vyāptiḥ tadbhāve tadbhāvaḥ kathaṃ
syāt 
tato'yamarthaḥ  yathā pāṇḍutvānnāgnimattve'numānaṃ tasya tatrāpratibandhāt  sa
ca vyabhicāreṇābhivyaktaḥ  anyathā tatrāpyanumānamaṅgīkṛtyaiva svasthamāsīt  sa ca
vyabhicāra pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpetarasādhāraṇaṃ dharmaṃ sarvamapratibaddhatve niyatamādarśayatīti
yathoktasādhāraṇatvākṛṣṭādapratibandhāt  tathaiva yathā kāryatvādimātrādapi na cetanādhiṣṭhānānu
mānamiti  ato vyabhicāradarśanamupakārakameva parasya  tasmāt pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpa
parāmarśāt tathāvidhopādhikameva kāryatvādisādhanaṃ dhiya iti siddham  tathāvidhasya ca
vāstava eva pratyāsattibheda iti saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇamāpatitam 
tena dharmijātibhedasya dharmabhedakatvaṃ siddhamapīti kathaṃ sarvatra tanniṣedha  atha
sarvatraiva yadbhedakatvaṃ tanniṣidhyate kacidabhedakatvamapītyartha tadā siddhasādhanam  uktaṃ
hi pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpāpekṣayā tadubhayavyavasthānamiti  tathā ca sati bhedasthitirevajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
kṛtakatvādisparśaṃścāparibhāvakatayā kriyate  na hi tatrāpi pratyakṣabalād vyāptirupapādayituṃ
śakyā kiṃ tu viparyayabādhakānumānāt tadabhāve'nanumānasyeṣṭatvāt 
tato'bhūtvābhavanābhidhānadharmamātrasya bhūtvābhavanena dharmeṇa vyāptisādhakaṃ dharmiṇo
yadi jātibhedamudāsayati dhūmasyāgninā vyāptisābdhakameva mahānasādi tadā prastute
kimāyātam yatra pratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā jātibhedaniṣṭheva vyāptigṛhītirītiriti  yadi tu
prakṛte'pi kāryavastustomagatāḥ kāryatvādaya eva dharmāḥ pratītavyāptayaḥ syuḥ tadāyaṃ na
doṣaḥ  kevalamupāyaprakāradvayasyāpyayogādayukteva vyāptiriti darśitam  tatra viparyaya 
bādhakapramāṇaparicayasteṣāmasaṃbhavo bauddhagandhereva kasyacit tathā yatnadarśanāt  na ca
prakṛte vaktuṃ śakya iti tatrāsthāmavadhūya  pradeśāntare ca
nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vetyādinā
pra vā  
karaṇamātre viśeṣatyāgena kāryamātra pratibandhaṃ viparyayabādhakabalena sūcayato nirvṛti vidadhāno
bhagavān vārtikakāraḥ parasya darśanādarśanamātreṇa vyāptivādinaḥ tadyogapratipādane pratyāsa
pratyakṣānupalambhabalāvalambanamavalokayan tadāhṛtya dūṣayituṃ jātibhedakṛtaṃ dūṣaṇamudbhāvayatīti
veditavyam  tasmāt pratyakṣavyāpārāvadheyajātibhedasyātyantaṃ vyaktatvāt saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇī
kriyamāṇamapyakiñcitkaramityuktam 
athavā astu ghaṭādyapekṣayā kṣoṇīdharādīnāṃ jātibhedo yataḥ 
siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi
ucyeta  krīḍāparvatādayastu pauruṣeyāstadekajātibhavāḥ taiḥ sahaikahetavaḥ kiṃ na
bhavanti  tato'yamarthaḥ yo yaḥ śailaḥ sa sarva pauruṣeyo yathā krīḍāśaila śailaśca kailāsa
iti  evaṃ kulyāmahāsarovaraprabhṛtayo nadīsamudrādīnāmudāharaṇānyūnīyānī tyā
śāha
ayamarthaḥ
vastubhede prasiddhasyetyādi
krīḍāparyaṃta kādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumā
nāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam
ki cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyantyamī cennagāḥ
kā vārteśvarasādhanasya kimihopāttaṃ samāptaṃ ca kim 
jātibhede siddhe'dhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyānusāra pūrayedapi pratyāśām abhede tu tadapi
nirāspadam  na hi sajātīyakumbhāntare tadvijātīyasya nirmātuḥ siddhirityanubhavāt
abhyupagamād vā bhinnaiva jātiranayorna samānaṃ hetumāvahati saṃjñāmātrasāmye'pīti 
kaḥ punarayaṃ niyamo ya ukta prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigraho nānyathetyāśaṅkayāha
anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit 
ghaṭāde karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ 
pra vā  
iti  na hi sudūramanusaratāpi sa kaścitpratibandhasādhana vidhilaṃbdhavyo yaḥ kumbhakāreṇa
mṛnmayamātravyāptiprasaṅgaparihārakārī prayatnavatā kāryamātravyāpti sādhayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ 
kumbhakāreṇa hi kāryamātra vyāptisādhanāya prabhavatastadviśeṣa mṛnmayasya sāṃdhane kaḥ śakti
vyāghātaḥ  astu vā prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigrahaḥ  yattūktam
no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśādityādi
tato'nyathā bhaviṣyatīti āśaṅkaya jaladharārthinā kumbhakāraparyeṣaṇāprasaṅgamuktameva
prakārāntareṇa a  saṃbhāvayantāha
anyathetyādi 
yadā hi bādhātmakoddeśenāpi pravartamāna  sāmānyenaiva vyāpti sādhayati tadā
kuto mṛnmayāt kulālānumānaṃ kuryāt kāraṇamātrasya siddhe  yadāpi pratyakṣāpekṣayā
hetuviśeṣeṇa kulālena karaṇavyāpāropadheyaviśeṣasya kumbhādikāryaviśeṣasya vyāptistadāpi
kutastatprasaṅgaḥ  yadāpyadhyavasāyamātrāpekṣayā sāmānyena viśeṣasya tadāpyayaṃ dūrataraḥ 
evaṃ tu vyavasthāto'nyathāvyāptigrahaṇe viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya bhavatīti kathaṃ mṛnmayāt
kulālānumānamaprasaṅga  tatkāryakumbhādyapekṣayā atyantavisadṛśādapi prasaṅge kathaṃ
kiyatāpyaṃśena pratyāsannāt na syāt  tathā caivaṃ sajātīyādapyavāntarabhedānusāri
pratyakṣavyavasāyāpekṣayā nānumānaṃ pratibandhāniścayāttadā kaiva vārtā vijātīyād 
atyantavijātīye dṛṣṭavyāptikasyeti daṇḍāpūpanyāya eṣa iti darśayituṃ mṛnmayagrahaṇam ZA PRVNAREA PO
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
nanūbhayathā vyākhyāne'pi vyabhicārādeva nānumānaṃ tatkathamatiprasaṅga iti
cet  uktakrameṇopakāraka eva vyabhicāro'smākaṃ na bādhakaḥ  tathāhi pramādvayavyā
pārātikrame'nantaraprakārabahirbhāva vā pratijñāta pratibandhaniścayābhāvasādhaka eva
vyabhicāra iti  api ca vyabhicāro nāma sāmānyena gṛhītāyā vyāpteniyataviṣayā
pekṣayā vighātamātanoti atha vyāptigrahaṇameva tanna bhavatīti vibhāvayati atha
satyapi vyāptiprasa re'numānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati ataevābādhita viṣayatvamapi liṅgalakṣaṇam
ākhyātamiti pakṣāḥ 
tatra prathamapakṣe sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ anyatrāpi tadvalādeva sādhyapratyāśā sā ca
niścitāpi khaṇḍitā kaciditi anyatrāpi śaṅkānivṛtteḥ tata eva tadgrahaṇavaiyarthyāt 
dvitoye tu na viśeṣaścetane  yathā hi kumbhakāreṇa kāryasāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa
vyāptirgṛhītā vyabhicāreṇa durgṛhītā vyavasthāpyate tathā cetanyamātreṇāpi tatrāpi
pratyakṣavyāpāre viśeṣābhāvāt 
tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyāmeva vyabhicāreṇānumānamapāsyata iti mahīyasīyam ayoga
paramparā  kevalamatra pakṣe etadāpatitaṃ yadīdamatra sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ vyabhicarya na sthitaṃ tadā
sādhyaṃ sādhayatīti  etacca sādhyavidhuraṃ sarvārthasākṣātkāriṇo nānyaḥ kartuṃ śaktaḥ  sa hi
ya eva dharmī tathāvidhamadhyamadhiśayito na bhavati tameva vā vyabhicāragocaratayā anumāna
bhājanīkaroti sarvavipakṣānīkṣaṇe tu tanmadhya eva kadācideṣo'pi sthāditi śaṅkā'nivṛtteḥ 
tasmādukta eva nyāya āśrayaṇayogyo vyabhicāraśca vyāptidurgrahaṇameva sādhayatīti kārya
mātravyāptiḥ prakṛtakā raga viśeṣeṇāsaṃbhavinyeva sādhuriti 
gṛhītāyāṃ vyāptau yadi vihatirāśvāsaviraho
graho nāsau vyāpteb yadi ca na viśeṣo matimati 
abādhāpekṣāyāṃ na sakalavipakṣekṣaṇamṛte
nirātaṅkastasmāna khalu phalamātre grahavidhiḥ 
iti saṃgrahaḥ 
ki cādāya samastavastuviṣayāṃ vyāpti punaścenmatā
tattajjātiṣu bādhakakramavaśātsvavyāpyatattat sthitiḥ 
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
tattajjātiṣu sādhakakramavaśādunnīyate kiṃ na sā
yenāyāsakaśaktisaṃśayapadaṃ santo viśantīdṛśam 
ityantaraślokaḥ 
aparigaṇito nāma vastuvyāpāraviṣayo'parigaṇitatamastvaviṣayaḥ  tatra ka
evamanātmīyakāryajātinikarasya pratyekaṃ vyabhicārān dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā svakāryaṃjātiṣveva
niyantuṃ hetumapāravyāpāra pārayate  tathā ca sati yasyaiva sākṣādanīkṣito vyabhicāraḥ
tadeva tasya gamakamāśaktam  tadā śaṅkāsaṃbhavānneti cet  na kacidatīndriye tarhi
niścayamayaṃ kuryāt  yajjātīyoddeśena pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ sāmānya viṣayamavasthāpitaṃ tatra
kaḥ sandeha iti cet  evaṃ tarhi parāparatadīyavyāpyajātiṣu tathaiva saṃśayapravṛttipratyanīka
pramāṇavṛttyanusaraṇe āyātastṛtīyapādāpatito'rthaḥ  tasmānna kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā
kāryamātrasya vyāptiḥ pratyetuṃ śakyeti
siddha yādṛgityādi
siddhāntaḥ 
athavā yaduktaṃ na śarīranirapekṣaprayatnavanmātreṇa kāryasya vyāptiḥ pratipattuṃ pāryate
pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣepāt tādṛśasyetyādi tadevopasaṃharati 
siddhamiti
yāvṛkṣo'sau śarīrādiyogī adhiṣṭhātā ceti  śeṣaṃ subodham  tādṛśaśca pratyakṣabādhādi
doṣaviṣaya ityākūtam  nanu śarīravatyapi cetanatvaṃ dṛṣṭamitaratrāpi saṃbhavati iti yathā
śarīriṇā vyāptaṃ kāryādi sidhyati tathābhimatenāpi ityatrāpi prāguktanyāyāt saṃjñā
mātrādavaśiṣyamānāt sādhanamanorathamunmathnannāha vastubhede kumbhādau prasiddhasya
kulālāderyo vācakaḥ śabdaśca tana iti tanmātrādabhidyamānasyābhimatasya pramāṇavyāpārā
pekṣayā dūrīkṛtasya na yuktānumitiriti vyāptābhimatād vastuna iti prakṛtamarthāpanaṃ vā
kathamivetyāha
pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśana iti 
ayamabhiprāyaḥ yadi śabdamātrasāmyenābhidyamānasyānumānaṃ śabdasāmyenābhidya
mānādapi pāṇḍumna kiṃ na dhūmadhvajasyānumānam  atha tatra viśiṣṭa kāryasvabhāvāpekṣamjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
adhyakṣamanyavyāpti pratikṣipatīti nānumānamucyate tathā cetanamātrapratikṣepeṇāpi
pratyakṣaṃ ki na tadanumānaṃ nirasyati  etena yadā daśyamapi kāryāntaraṃ tiraskaroti
pratyakṣaṃ tadā keva kathā dṛkpathātiriktasya cetanamātrasyeti  astu tāvad vyāpyā
pekṣayā vibhāga eva loke tathaiva pratīteḥ anyathātiprasaṅgācca 
vyāpakāpekṣayā tu yadyeṣa niyamo na syāt ko doṣa ityāśaṅkhyā pūrvoktameveti
prasaṅgaṃ bhaṅgayantareṇa taruṇayati anyathetyādi  valmīkasyeti valmīkajantorityarthaḥ 
tatkṛtiriti ghaṭādikṛtiḥ  a ayamarthaḥ yadi viśeṣeṇāpi vyāptimavasāya cetana
mātraṃ sāmānyamanumātavyam tadā kumbhādikaraṇasya kulāle niyatasya cetanamātra paryaṃ
vasitatvāt ghaṭāderapi valmīkajantuḥ kartānumeya syāt yathāhi kumbhādeḥ kumbhakāreṇa
vyāptigrahaṇe caitanyamātreṇāviśeṣāt tasyāpyanumānamevaṃ valmīkaukaso'pi caitanyenānyā
viśeṣāt kiṃ nānumānam  yadā ca śarīriṇā vyāptigrahe śarīriṇo'pyanyasya pratikṣepaḥ
tadā kā vārtātyanta visadṛśasyeti  na cātra bahutvenopayogaḥ ekātmano'pi cetanyād
iti valmīkasyeti nirdeśaḥ  etena dhūmāderapi jāṭharāderanumānākṣepo vyaktaḥ  vyabhi
cāracarcāyāṃ ca pūrvavat sarvamāvartanīyamiti 
yaduktaṃ prayatnavatā yadvaghāptaṃ sanniveśādi tanna siddhaṃ sindhubhūdharādau yacca siddhaṃ

pra vā 
yat punarastaṃ gate'pi vastunyākārāntarabhāji vā sthirākāratayā bhāvanā
yasya nirālambanatvamāpāditaṃ sarvasya tadapi vastubhāvanāpakṣe śobhate na vastudharmaṃ
bhāvanāpakṣe  vastudharmāṃśca kṣaṇikatvādayaḥ saṃsāraverāgyāt sphuṭībhāvabhājo bhāvayitu
mupakrāntāḥ  athaikatra pramāṇapariśuddhe'pi bhāvanājanitaveśadyasya vastuni visaṃvāda
saṃdarśanādanyatrāpi ka āśvāsaḥ pramāṇapariśuddhimantareṇāśvāsa he torapyasyābhāvāt
tasyāśca saṃvādaniyatāvasāmarthyāt  tanna sthirāsthiraviṣayatvena viśeṣāt  asthiraṃ
hi vastu pradhvaṃsavikārābhyāṃ grasthata iti na saṃvādaḥ a vastudharmāstu
kṣaṇikatvādayo na kadācidvicchidyanta iti tadviṣaya sphuṭībhāvaḥ sarvadā sālambana
eva 
nanvetadapi na yuktam  na hi kṣaṇikatvādikaṃ nāma kiñcidasti vastu satve vā
tadeva nityamāsaktamiti sarvamayatnaśīrṇam  avastutve ca tadeva nirālambanatvam  tasmād
bhavanmate'pi kṣaṇikatvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikā eva bhāvarāśayo'parāmṛṣṭabhedāḥ bhedāntaratiraskāre
ṇocyante  tathā ca sati kṣaṇikatvabhāvanetyapi kṣaṇikapadārthasārthabhāvanetyevārthaḥ  tāvatā
tānyeva vastūni bhāvyamānāni sphuṭībhavantīti sa eva doṣaḥ  athābhinnānyapi kṣaṇikatvā
doni bhinnānīva tāvatpratibhānti  tathāpyadhyavasāyād vastugatānyeva bhāvyanta iti na

mevākāro bhāvanāyāḥ

tathāpi na tasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ tattvamātratātparya paryavasānāt  tattvabhāvanaiva hi sphuṭībhavantī

yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam
naiṣa doṣaḥ dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭībhāvamaspṛśato'pi dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvadarśanāt 
kevalaṃ vastupratyāsatyanapekṣya na sphuṭasphuraṇamiti syāt  sphuṭībhāvo'pi tasya tadviṣaya
sannidhau yatnamanapekṣya jhagiti tajjñāne tattadākārasphuraṇaṃ nāma vastuprattyāsatyapekṣā tu
na kṣīyate dharmatvādeva priyatvādivat  tathā hi nimbarasādau tāvat priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ
sphuṭībhavadṛṣṭam  naca nimbādeḥ sa dharma iti tadbhāvanayā nimbādyapi svajanmadeśasthaṃ
rasanāprasaṅgi vā sphuṭaṃ sphuradasti yāvanna viparyayabhāvanābhiyogaprakarṣaḥ  na ca sphuṭībhūtaṃ
priyatvamapi taṭasthamupalabhyate nimbādyanubhavamanapekṣya kiṃ tu yadā yadā nimbādyanubhava
tadā tadā jhagiti priyatvamanubhavaviṣayaḥ na prāgivodvejakamanubhayaṃ vetyeṣa eva dharma
sphuṭībhāvārthaḥ 
yathā hi kāminyādivastuni sphuṭobhūte'pi na yathā samayasiddhastattvasphuṭībhāvaḥ
tathā tattvabhāvanayāpi na vastusphuṭībhāva ubhayo parasparāvyabhicāre'pīti kīdṛśo
doṣa  atha na bāhyadharma priyatvamasādhāraṇatvād bhāvanādheyatvācceti cet  kasya
punarayaṃ dharmo'stu priyatvādiḥ pratyātmavedyatvenāpahnotumaśakyaḥ  jñānasya b cet 
bāhyasya priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ jñānasya sphuṭībhavatīti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ  utkṛṣṭamidaṃ nimbā
diti bhāvanākāro'pi na tajjñānamutkṛṣṭamiti  athāpi jñānasyaiva priyatayā sphuṭībhāve
na jātu kaścidapriyamanubhavet  na hi bahiriva jñānamapi kādācitkasannidhānam 
jñānasyāpi kasyacideva priyatvavyaktiriti cet  kikṛtaḥ punarayaṃ vibhāga  yadyabhyāsa
kṛtaḥ yatraivābhyāso bāhye tatraiva bhavatu  tadanapekṣāyāṃ kasyacidapi pratyāsattiviprakarṣā
bhāvānmanomātramadhiṣṭhānībhūtamiti na kaścidviśeṣaḥ 
bā tu viśiṣṭajātinimbādikamabhyāsaviṣayīkṛtamiti nātiprasaṅgaḥ  jñāna
mapi tarhi bhāvitanimbagocarameva pratyāsannamiti viśeṣaḥ  evaṃ tarhīdamāyātam yadvastu
kenacid rūpeṇa bhāvyate tadvastu vihāya tatpratyāsannasya sphuṭībhāva iti kāminīṃ bhāva
yatastatpratyāsannasya pitrādereva sphuṭībhāvaprasaṅgo na kāminyāḥ  atha viṣayasya viṣa
yiṇā jñānena saha viśiṣṭeva kācitpratyāsattiḥ  evamapi nimbe priyatayā abhyasyamāne
tajjñānaṃ priyatayā sphuratīti nimbādikaṃ prāgvadapriyameva bhavet  tato yathā sarpādāva
priye parihārāṅgatayā tanniścayaḥ priya eva na sarpādistathedamapīti kṛtaṃ bhāvanayā 
atha bhāvanābalāt priyākārameva tadviṣayaṃ jñānamupajāyata iti kalpanā  evaṃ
sati nimbarasaḥ priyo bhāvyata iti tadviṣayajñānameva priyākāraṃ bhāvyata ityāpannam 
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalī
sphuṭābhatāpi tasya tadviṣayopanidhau tadgrāhijñānasya jhagiti yatnamanapekṣya priyākāra
sphuraṇam na viṣayasyaivāsannihitasya sākṣādbhāvaḥ  evaṃ kṣoṇīdharādayo'pi kṣaṇino
bhāvyanta iti tadviṣayajñānameva kṣaṇikākāraṃ bhāvyata iti  tasyāpi sphuṭībhāvo
bhūdharādisannidhau tadgrāhakasya kṣaṇikākārodayo na bhūdharāderasannihitasyāpi sphuṭī
bhāvaḥ  iyameva dharmaṃbhāvanā śabdārthaniṣṭheti na prastutavastukṣatiḥ 
vastutastu priyatvaṃ nāma sukhakaratvam  tatra yadviṣaye yasya priyatvabhāvanā
taccittasantānaṃ bhāvanāpariṣkṛtamupādānamupādāya sa viṣaya sahakārī sukhamutpādayatīti
sthitau na sarvaṃ priyatvam  tatra prīṇakatvaṃ tu tasyaiva dharmaḥ sarvaṃ ca pratīti na doṣaḥ 
sa cābhyāsādeva  evaṃ kṛpādiṣvapi mānaseṣu dharmeṣu yojyam  duḥkhinamuddharāmīti
duḥkhiparoddharaṇabhāvanāyāḥ sphuṭībhāvastadviṣayasannidhau jhagiti tat jñānaṃ tadanurūpā
nuṣṭhānaprasavahetuḥ  evaṃ śucikapālabhāvānāyāmapi naṃrghuṇyasphuṭībhāvo nāma karpūropa
sarpaṇe veditavyaḥ  na tu saṃbandhinaiva pratyāsannanetareṇa vā sahasphua rattā 
yathoktaṃ sarvajñasiddhau
labdho bodhadayādibhistvatiśayastadgocaropasthitau
naivaṃ yatnamapekṣate svarasataḥ pratyātmamunmīlati 
tasmāt kṣaṇikatvadharmābhyāse'pi prakarṣagāmini yāvadanubhavitavyamanena tāvat
truṭya pamasmadādidarśana vilakṣaṇameva  yathāsmākamatyantasadṛśe'pi bhinna deśapaṭutara
bhedānukāri darśanaṃ vikalpaśca jhagityeva tathā syāt anuṣṭhānaṃ vā tadanurūpam evaṃ
yoginaḥ kṣaṇabhedini bhāvadvaye darśana vikalpau  sthairyādibhramodbhavarāgādikalaṅkānaṅkitaṃ
cāsya ceta iti iyatī tasya sphuṭābhatā 
nanu paribhāṣāmātrametat iyatyeva tasya prakarṣagatiriti  tathādṛṣṭatvāditi
nottaram  yadyapi dṛṣṭamevaṃ tathāpi tāvataiva sthitiriti na śakyaṃ prastute  kadācidati
ricyamānaḥ prakarṣo viṣayeṇaiva saha sphuṭayediti pūrvadoṣaśoṣaḥ  priyatvādāvapi ca
kadācidanyaiva niṣṭheti cet  bhavatviti bhāvanayā abhimatāṃ sthitimullaṅghaya sphuṭī
bhāvaśaṅkā  yastu prekṣāpūrvakārī svārtha parārthaṃ vā bhāvanābhiyuktaḥ tasya tāvataiva
kṛtārthatvaṃ jātamiti kimiti śramāntaramāviśet anarthakatvādanartha karatvācca  yathā

yoginirṇaya karaṇam
taiva pākaprakarṣaparyaṃntavyavahāraḥ tathā prastute'pīti na kaściddoṣaḥ  tadevaṃ yadyapi dharmiviṣaya
bhāvanāyā sphuṭībhāvo visaṃvādasaṃvāsī sthairyaviparyayādviṣayasya tathāpi na yathoktadharmaṃgoca
rāyāstadāśaṅkati sthitam  yadyevamanucitaḥ kāminīdṛṣṭānta iti na codyam bhāvanāyā
veśadyamātra nidarśanasya vivakṣitatvāt  ata eva vārtikama
ghṛṇāvairāgyarāgavat
ityāha 
tattarhi yogijñānamindriyajñānādbhinnamabhinnaṃ vā  kiṃ cātaḥ  abhedapakṣe na yogi
jñānaṃ nāma pratyakṣabhedaḥ indriyajñānenaiva saṃgrahāt  na ca bhāvanopaskṛtasantānasya tathodayād
bhedavyavasthā rasāyanādisaṃskārāpekṣayāpi pratyakṣāntaravyavasthāprasaṅgāt  bhedapakṣe ca
bhāvanāsaṃbhavaṃ kṣaṇikatvasākṣātkārijñānamanyadanyatheti sādhvī śuddhiḥ indriyajñānasyāpi
tadavasthāyāmasthairyaṃsākṣātkaraṇe kṛtaṃ yogijñānena  na ca tasyākasmikaḥ kṣaṇikatvabodhaḥ 
bhāvanogata vaiśadyasya hi tadbodhaḥ  na cendriyajñāne bhāvanā api tu manasaḥ  tāmantareṇāpi
sākṣāt kriyālārbhe ca bhāvanāvaiyarthyam 
kiṃ ca bhinnakālaṃ vā tadvayamabhinnakālaṃ vā  tatrābhinnakālatvamanupapannam 
indriyajñānopanītasya hi dharmiṇa kṣaṇikatā sākṣātkartavyā bhāvanābhāvinā'nubhavena 
anyathā dharmiṇaṃ dharmaṃ ca svātantryeṇa b sākṣātkurvato dharmidvārakaṃ dūṣaṇamanivāryam 
niveditametat 
na ca dharmabhāvanāyā vastusākṣātkāravyāpāro nimbādivaditi
tasmādindriyajñānagocarādadhika eva tattvasākṣātkāra iti prathamamindriyajñānaṃ dharmigrāhi
paścānmānasaṃ kṣaṇikatāgrāhīti niyataḥ kālabhedaḥ  kālabhede ca prācīnāpekṣayā paścimasya
gṛhītagrāhitvādaprāmāṇyamekārthatve  bhinnārthatve tvindriyajñānagocarādanyatra pravartamānaṃ
svātantryeṇa dharmiṇamupasthāpayatīti na ca prācyadoṣānmuktiriti 
atra brūmaḥ  prathamapakṣe tāvanna vastudūṣaṇam tādṛkpuruṣa viśeṣasya sādhyasya
siddhatvāt  vyavasthādūṣaṇamapi nāsti sādhyatayaiva tādṛśādaśa viśeṣasya lokātikrānta
rūpatve tatsādhanaviśeṣapratipādanāya pṛthagjanasādhāraṇendriyajñānād bhedena nirdeśāt 
na cendriyajñānaśabdena koṣṭhaśuddhayā rasāyanādijanitaviśeṣasyeva saṃgrahamātreṇa śāstra
sāphalyam  ata evāñjanādikṛtaviśeṣāpekṣayāpi na bhedanirdeśa lokātikrānta
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
rūpasya viśeṣasyābhāvāt  prayojanāpekṣayā hi bahulamekaprakārasaṃgrāhyasthāpi prakārabheda
nirdeśa iṣyata eva yathā saṃprayuktasaṃskāraskandhasaṃgṛhītayorapi vedanāsaṃjñayoḥ vikalpa
saṃgṛhītasyāpi kliṣṭamanojñānasya  tasmānnendriyayogijñānayorabhedapakṣe tāvaddoṣaḥ  tadeva
dharmirūpāpekṣayendriyajñānaṃ dharmāpekṣayā yogijñānaṃ yathā dharmipratyakṣameva niṣedhāpekṣayā
nupalabdhi 
bhedakapakṣe'pi na tāvat sthairyetarasphuraṇakṛtopālambhasaṃbhava indriyajñānenāpi
vastu sarvātmanā gṛhṇatā truṭyadrūpasyaiva grahaṇāt  adhyavasāyo'pi pūrvaṃ durlabhaḥ sa
saṃprati bhāvanābalāvalambinā manasā āsāditapāṭavena ghaṭita iti viśeṣaḥ 
nanvindriyasyāpi taddaśāyāṃ niratiśayaviśeṣalābhād dūrasūkṣmādyanubhava ko nivārayati
bāhyayogivat tiraścāmapi kutaścit karmākṣepānmātrayā tathopalabdheḥ  vidyamānānāṃ
ca kṣaṇānāmavaśyaṃ vaisadṛśyamaṇīyo'pi saṃbhavi anyathā sarvātmanā sādṛśye tattva
prasaṅgāt  tat tathāvidhasūkṣmabhedāvadhāraṇadhūryeṇākṣavijñānenaiva sādhyasiddheranarthakaṃ
yogijñānam 
etena duḥkhānātmādisākṣātkāro vyākhyātaḥ  puruṣavapuṣā cendriyamantareṇa
bhavitumaśakyamiti yogijñānamanutpādanīyamastu  tadapyayuktam  na hi saṃbhāvanā
mātropanītaṃ netrabalamavalambya saṃvyavahāriṇā prekṣeṇa pramāṇaparāyaṇo mārga parihatu
śakyaḥ  tadabhyāsasahakārikameva vā tathāvidhendriyaśaktisādhanamityaparihāryeṇa yogijñānena
samānakakṣatāyāmapi indriyajñānasya na kaścid doṣaḥ  vaiyarthyaa mekasyeti cet 
katareṇa punaḥ svakāraṇopanidhānadharmaṇoranayoḥ svavyāpāravaiyarthyabhayānnivartitavyam
bojādiṣvivāntyakṣaṇaprāpteṣu 
aprāmāṇyamekasyāstviti cet  bījādiṣvapyekasyākāraṇatvamastu  sarveṣāṃ
samānasāmarthyānāṃ katamadekamakāraṇamavasthāpayituṃ śakyamiti cet  paricchedabalavato
jñānayorapi kimekamapramāṇīkriyatām  parasparāpekṣayā mā bhūdubhayamapi pramāṇamiti cet 
bījādiṣvapi naikamapi kāraṇatvamastviti samānam  gṛhītagrāhitvaṃ nāma nāstyeva  tarhi
doṣa iti cet na kālabhedena tasya svīkārāt  gṛhītagrahaṇaṃ hi taducyate na gṛhyamāṇastha
yathā kṛtasya karaṇasvīkāre'kārakatvam na tu kriyamāṇakaraṇe bījādivadeva  tasmādabhinna
kālapakṣe naiṣa doṣaḥ 
OVER
yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam
nanu tathāpyā kāradvayasphuraṇaprasaṅga iti cet  satyam satyajñānākārastāvaddhanta
samānadeśaḥ anyathā bhramatvaprasaṅgāt  atastāvākārāvapratighau kayā rītyā sphurata iti
ko nirṇetuṃ kṣamaḥ dāha
acintyā yogināṃ gatiḥ
pra vā  
iti  tasmād dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt kimivāniṣṭaṃ kimiva vā na doṣa ityubhayorapi nāvasaraḥ 
samasamayatayā tarhīndriyajñānānapekṣāyāṃ svātantryadoṣa uktaḥ kathaṃ parihartavyaḥ  indriyāpekṣayaiva
parihariṣyata iti nottaram  tadā hi tadapīndriyajñānameva syāt tadvyāpārānuvidhānāt 
na yogijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit 
tadvaramekameva svīkṛtamiti na bhedapakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ  naivam tathā hi mā bhūdindriyā
pekṣā  vīkṣaṇaṃ tu yathā svasāmarthyānurūpāṃ yogyadeśāvasthitimapekṣya svavijñānajanane
pravartate tathā manaindriyamapi pravartiṣyate aprāpyakāritāyā ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇatvāt
arthavattāyāśca manaso'pi tadānīmiṣṭatvāt  pṛthagjanasantānasya tu na tādṛśī śaktiḥ
yato netraśrotravanmano'pi tādṛṅmaryādayā yogyadeśasthamarthasahakāriṇamāsādya vedanam
utpādayediti nātiprasaṅgaḥ  taddaśāyāṃ tu śrutinayanayoriva manaso'pi kiyavareṇa
viṣayasannidhivyavastheti ka evaṃ pramātuṃ kṣama  kevalametāvaducyate yāvattena śakyam
adhigantuṃ svākārārpaṇasahaṃ sahakāri vastu tāvaditarajanāsādhāraṇatruṭyadrūpatayā tasya
gocarībhavati  tathā ca sati vastvākāro vastukṛta eva na bhāvanājanita iti na
visaṃvādaśaṅkā 
nanu cakṣurādestāvadvarataragocarīkaraṇe dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ manasastu nendriyātikrameṇa
sarvaviṣayasyeti cet na paracittajñānādīnāṃ saṃbhavāt  tadapi neṣṭamekeṣāmiti
cet  adṛṣṭamātreṇa pratikṣepāyogāt  upāyābhāvāditi cet  upāyābhāve'pi
nānupalambhamātrādanya upāya  tasmād yadyevaṃ syāt tadā yogi bnāmindriyamano
jñānayorbhedapakṣe'pi na nirvāha ityupakṣepārthaḥ  nirvāhastvanyathā'pi darśita eva evaṃ
ca sati kālabhedapakṣe'pi na doṣaḥ yadi sā prathamaṃ manojñānavṛttiḥ yadi
cendriyapathātikrameṇa vṛttiḥ  indriyajñānaṃ tu tasya tadapekṣayā prāmāṇyavirahe'pi na
vyathayatītyalaṃ vistareṇa 
jñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvalo
tadevaṃ yogijñāne tattvabhāvanādhikārādarthākāro'rthakṛta eva  bhāvanayā punastadīya
santāne netra ivāñjanaviśeṣeṇa śaktiratiśayavatī kācidarpitā yayetarajanāsādhāraṇaṃ
darśanamasya  yathoktaṃ prāk  yadi tarhi viṣayajanyameva yogijñānamatītānāgataparijñānasya
kā vārtā  tadetatprastāvānavagāhanasya phalam  upayuktasarvajñādhikāreṇa hi vastudharmabhāva
nopakṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ  na sarvasarvajñapakṣāpekṣayā tato'tītānāgatamapratīyamānamapi na bādhakam 
tāvataiva duḥkhanirodhasiddheḥ parasmai ca niṣkampadeśanāvatārāt 
yat punaḥ kaṇikāyāṃ kṣaṇikāditattvabhāvanādvāreṇa taddharmiṇāṃ samastavastūnāmeva
bhāvanayā tadākārajñānotpādanātsākṣātkaraṇamutthāpya dūṣaṇamabhidhīyate yogijñānasya
tadavadhoraṇīyameva vārtikabhāṣyādivādabahirbhāvāt  anyathārabdheva nityaduḥkhādibhāvanā
sā ca sarvasarvajñatvamevārpayatoti yadyabhipretaṃ syāt kathaṃ yatnenotthāpya tatparihāro
vārtike
nāsmābhiḥ śakyate jñātumiti santoṣa iṣyate
ityādinā bhāṣye ca  yadi punastadavasthāprāptau nirāvaraṇāntaḥkaraṇasya kāruṇyātiśayāt
sarvākāraparārtha prārthanaparatayā sakalagocaracāriṇi cetasi ciravirūḍhotsāhasya tādṛgupāya
viśeṣādhigamo bhaviṣyati yamanutiṣṭhataḥ pratiparamāṇu sarvavastuviṣayaṃ yathādeśakālaṃ pratyava
sthānukāri sphuṭataraṃ jñānamudīyāt  tadā na tāvadvastuvyabhicārakṛtaṃ visaṃvāditvam nāpi
nirālambanatvam vastūnāmeva pratibhāsanāt 
athotpattisārūpyābhyāmālambanavyavasthā
bhinnakālaṃ kathaṃ grāhyamiti ced grāhyatāṃ viduḥ 
hetutvameva yuktijñā jñānākārāpaṃṇakṣamam 
pra vā 
iti vacanāt tataḥ sārūpyamekama kiñcitkaramiti kathamanālambanatvaparihāra 
tadayuktam tat khalu lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthagjanāpekṣayā bahirathaṃ prati samasamayabhāvinā
nupakāryeṇa jñānena grahaṇaniṣedhaparam tathā prastāvāt  tattvatastu yadeva yatra pratibhāsate
tadeva tasyālambanamucyate  yathendriyapratyakṣe bāhyamanyatra svākāraḥ pratibhāsavaśāt
yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam
pratyakṣasya grahaṇāṃgrahaṇe iti hi prathamaparicchedavṛttiḥ  tatra bāhyasya pratibhāso nāma
tadākārotpattimātram  tathā hi bahivicchinnākārodayasaṃvedanamātrādidaṃ dṛṣṭamiti
bhavati  na khalu tatsaṃkalpakāle utpattiraparāpekṣyate a tasyāḥ paścānniśceyatvāt
phalaprāptayā vā abhyāsena vā  sa ca tadākārodaya indriyapratyakṣe'rthād bhrame viplavāt 
vikalpe vāsanātaḥ  tatrārthajanye saṃvādo'nyatra viparyayo bahirapekṣayā svarūpe sarvatra
saṃvādaniyamāt  tato'bhipretasaṃvāde vedane tadutpattimantareṇa na saṃvādo nāpi tādrdhyamiti
tatra tadutpattiprārthanā  ataeva tadākārataiva prāmāṇyam sārūpyatadutpattī ca saṃvedyalakṣaṇa
mityubhayamavirodhi 
yatra tu bhāvanāviśeṣabalādeva devatādhipatyāt satyasvapnavadarthākāramarthayāthātmya
nāntaroyakaṃ jñānam tatra na kiñcit tadutpattyā  yad vārtikam 
 rūpādeścetasaścaivam aviśuddhadhiyaṃ prati 
grāhya grāhaka cinteyamacintyā yogināṃ gatiḥ 
iti  tasmād bāhye pṛthagjanasya sārūpyotpattibhyāṃ vedyasthitiḥ yoginaḥ sārūpyamātre
ṇāpi  svarūpe yogyatāmātreṇaiveti nyāyaḥ  'bhāvibhūtayostahi yadi svarūpasphuraṇaṃ
vartamānataiva syāt 
pra vā  
atha svarūpamasannihitaṃ jñānameva tadākāramiti nirālambanaṃ niyamena tadapi
nāsti  yasmādasannihite'pyarthe bhāvanābalāñcet taddeśakālānukāri vijñānaṃ kathamanā
lambanam  sphuraṇarītiviśeṣeṇa tu kālabhedavikalpodayāt tadanurūpānuṣṭhāne niyatatvāt
tatprāpteḥ  yadbhāṣyam
yathā sa dṛṣṭaḥ śaradādikālayuktastathā tasya na bādhitatvam 
iti  yadvā saṃcityeva kālabhedabhāgivasturūpapratītaye
bhedādhyavasāyaḥ  yathoktam
yad yadicchati vai boddhum
pra vā bhā  
samādhisamāpattervyutthāne kāla
ityādi  krameṇa tvanābhogamapi jñānamavirodhi  jñānamātrasya tattvataḥ sphuraṇācca na
 tula ratna niba pṛ   ta sa  
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauṃ
vartamānatāprasaṅgaḥ yathā nirākāravāde vastusvarūpasyaiva sphuraṇāditi  yadyapi ca
vartamāne'pi jñānākārasyaiva sphuraṇaṃ tathāpi vartamānatayaivādhyavasāyastatra  evaṃ
dūrāsannādibhede'pi veditavyam  tatra yathādhyavasāyaprāptau niyamena saṃvādāt prāmāṇyam
anyadā viparyayaḥ yathā svapnakāminyādau  pratibhāsvargasādhanāgniṣṭomādivikalpe ca
bhāvinaḥ spaṣṭarūpasya pratibhāsābhāvādeva na cintā  na ca tatra prekṣavyāvahārikasya
prāptiniyamaniścayo'sti 
prastute'pi ko niścaya iti cet  kasya punaratra niścayaścintyate tasya tadanyasya
vā  yadi tasya tadā yathābhyāsāt parito nirastavibhramāśaṅka sādhanajñāne pṛthagjanasya
tathā yogino'pyatyantābhyāsād bhāvibhūtādipratibhāsa kena vāryate  athānyasya
tadedamāyātam  yāvadanyasya na prāmāṇyabodhastāvanna pramāṇam  yāvacca na pramāṇaṃ
tāvannānyasya prāmāṇyabodho'bhrānta iti na kiñcitpramāṇaṃ syāt  tannābhiveśapāravaśyena
kiñcit  tasmādupāyaviśeṣab sacivabhāvanābhedasyāhatyāsphuraṇāt tādṛsiddhāveva
saṃśayo na tu siddhe'pi nirālambanatvādidoṣairupadravaḥ śakyaḥ 
yacca vikalpena bāhyasyāgrahaṇe'pyadhyavaseyatayā sphuṭībhāvamāśaṃkya yadanumānena
gṛhyate yaccādhyavasoyate te dve'nyanivṛttī na vastunī svalakṣaṇāvagāhitve'bhilāpasaṃsagaṃyogya
pratibhāsānupapatterityāha tadapyasaṃbaddham  tathā hi yathā tathā vā bauddhasiddhāntagandhena
vyavahāraḥ kāminyākāravikalpabhāvanavat kṣaṇikākārasyāpi paryante viśadopādeyakṣaṇa
prasavastu dunivāraḥ  yadi punarīdṛgapohasthitiḥ kṣaṇika vikalpaikatalpaśāyinī na kāminyādi
vikalpamanvetītyupapādayiṣyasi tathaiva grahīṣyāmaḥ  na cādhyavaseyamavastunivṛttimātraṃ vā 
dharmottare'pi hi mate svalakṣaṇamadhyavaseyamiti sthitiḥ 
nanu vahniḥ pratoto mayetyadhyavasāyākāraḥ  tatra ca svalakṣaṇasphuraṇamiti
sāhasam vikalpādhyavasāyayorekārthatvāt  satyam na tu tatra sphuratīti tāvatā
svalakṣaṇamadhyavasitamucyate  asphuraṇe tarhyabodhāt kathamavasāya  sphuraṇe'pi prati
bhāsa evāsau kathamadhyavasāyaḥ  na ca pratibhāsādhyavasāyāvadhyekārthau  pratibhāso
hi sākṣāt sphuraṇamasphuraṇe'pi pravṛttiviṣayīkaraṇamekavyāvṛtyullekhasāmarthyādadhyavasāyo
bhāṣyamataḥ  ato yadanurūpamanuṣṭhānaṃ tadadhyavaseyam pratibhāsamānarūpānanupraviṣṭameva 
tacca kacidāropitamātram  kacivasturūpam  prakṛtaṃ tu pramāṇavyāpārasvīkārād vastu
rūpameveti kathamucyate nivṛttimātramavastu vādhyavaseyamityāstāṃ tāvadanārabdhanirbaṃndhaḥ 
yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam
pratibhāso'pi vikalpe vyāvṛttākārasya na vyāvṛttimātrasya yadyanubhavānusāraḥ  sarvadā
yad vā tad vā rākṣasādi pratibhāseta  bhāvanayā punaradhyavasitākāreṇa pariṇati
abādhyā tatrāropitamātre'dhyavaseye nirālambanatvam  sati tu tadevālambanaṃ yathānantara
muktam 
yattvāha arthaṃsyālambanapratyayatvaṃ vijñānaṃ pratīndriyāpekṣatvena vyāptam  taccā
smāt svaviruddhopalabdhyā nivartamānamālambanapratyayatvamapyarthasya nivartayatīti tatrā
vyāpaka viruddhopa
lambanapratyayatvendriyāpekṣatvayorvyāpyakabhāvamaprasādhya
pramāṇena
labdhi sphuṭayatīti mahadvaidagdhyam  tathā darśanāditi cet  darśanā darśanameva hi
pramāṇīkṛtya sthīyatām kimevaṃvidhapramāṇopanyāsavyasanena  tasmādindriyamana
pekṣyāpi yadyālambanabhāvaṃ bhāvaḥ svīkuryāt na bādhakamutpaśyāmaḥ  athātroktameva na
khalvindhanaviśeṣo dhūmaheturiti vināpi dahanaṃ sahasreṇāpi saṃskārairdhūmamādhatte  tadā
dhāne vā samastakārya hetvanumānocchedaprasaṅgaḥ  tasmāt jñānamapīndriyasāpekṣādarthād
utpattidharmakam 
pratyālambanabhāva
indriyavyāpāravirahe ca samastā la parakāraṇasannidhāvasannidhīyamānasattākaṃ
tatpratibaddhaṃ siddhamiti kathamindriyānapekṣyasyārthasya svavijñānaṃ
iti cet  etadapi paracittajñānasaṃbhavena prativyūḍham  iṣṭāśca paracittavedinaścārvāka 
mīmāṃsakavyatiriktaiḥ  cārvākāderapi sandehānnāparā gatiḥ  sandehe ca vipakṣādekānta
vyāvṛtterayogaḥ  nanu jñāna kāryasyendriyāpekṣā niyamādeva nānyatra sandeho dahanāpekṣa
dhūmavat  yadyevaṃ rūpajñānasya vīkṣaṇāpekṣaṇe yādṛśī sāmagrī sā na saṃcaraṇaviśeṣasya
caraṇāpekṣaṇe kalayāpi hīyate tat kathaṃ na dhūmadṛṣṭāntaścaraṇavirahiṇāmuragādīnāṃ
gamananiṣedhāya prabhurabhūt  kathaṃ vā karādivyāpārasaṅga sāvegamantrodgāraparamparā
sādhyamekeṣāṃ viṣaśamanādikāryaṃ samādhimātrādanyasya  na caivaṃ dhūmo'pi kacidindhane
dahanānapekṣodayo dṛṣṭo yato'trāpi tathā śaṅkayeta 
tasmād bahirbhuvo bhāvā yathā hetuphalabhāvenopalambhabhāja te tathaiva niyata
vṛttayaḥ  cittasantānasya tu vicitrakarmābhisaṃskārasāmarthyād vicitra eva vivartaḥ 
atastadāśrayakāryamekatra yāvadapekṣaṃ tāvadapekṣamanyatrāpīti na niyantuṃ śakyam  tat
kathaṃ paracittavedanāderabhāva eva  yadi ca dhūmavadanalamanapekṣya nendriyaṃ buddhiḥ tadā
svaviṣaye'pyutkarṣaghoṣaṇāvīkṣaṇādīnāṃ dīnaiva syāt  tathā hi yāvaddeśaṃ dahanendhanādijñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
dhūmādisādhanamupalabdhaṃ na tāvaddeśātikrame samartham  evaṃ yāvaddeśe'smākaṃ viṣaye
ndriyādivedanamutpāditavat kathaṃ tadatikrame gṛdhrādīnāmutpādayet  utpādane vā nendhana
dahanādikakṣāṃ kṣamate cittasantānāśrayā sāmagrī  nāpi dhūmakakṣāṃ buddhiḥ

 advaitabinduprakaraṇam 
iha bahirarthābhiniveśino manoratho yad yathā pratīyate tat tathā saditi

ghaṭādaya iti svabhāvahetuḥ  nātrāsiddhiḥ grāhakāṅgād vicchinnena tarjanīnirdeśayogyena
puro'vasthāyinā rūpeṇa ghaṭādyākārasya pratibhāsādhyavasāyābhyāṃ kroḍīkaraṇāt  tathā
hyayaṃ ghaṭo nāyaṃ ghaṭa iti pratītiḥ pratyātmavedyā sarvapuruṣāṇāmavyutpanna saṃketānāmapi
saṃjñāviśeṣollekha vimukhastadanurūpa evāntarjanya  bālo'pi sukhasādhanaṃ stanamavalokya
tadabhimukhe karamukhe prahiṇvan bahiravasāyasacivamātmānamātanoti  tataśca vyatiriktena

saṃbhavasya darśitatvāt  viparyayavyāptasya ca viruddhasya tadasaṃbhavāt

keśoṇḍūkapratītau vā taimirikasya ataḥ sādhāraṇatvameveti bādhakagrastatvena tatpratīteḥ

tathā vyavahāravirahaḥ syāt tadā tadanyāpekṣaṃ syāditi sādhyasya tadvayavahārayogyatvasya

advaitabinduprakaraṇam
kena punavijñānasya nīlākārotpattiniṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ tatsādhanāya sādhanānavadhānaprasaṅgāt 
tasmānna parokṣamasadeveti dvayavādino yuktam 
na cāyamabhyupagamo'pyasyeti nātra nirbaṃndhaḥ  pramāṇābhāve prameyābhāvamicchato'pi
hi na parokṣasya sarvathābhāva evābhimataḥ api tu sannavaśyaṃ kasyacitpramāṇasya viṣaya syāt
stokāntareṇeti b anyathā 'satsaṃprayoge satīndriyāṇāṃ puruṣasya buddhijanmetyavācyaṃ
syāt jñānāt prāk sato virahāt  sa punarabhyupagamo na nyāyya iti kimanena tanmātrasya
vivakṣitatvādityalaṃ vistareṇa 
vikāryapakṣe tu yasya jñānasya yo vikāryo'rthaḥ sa grāhya iti vyavasthāyāṃ śokādino
pahatāyā buddhevikāryamindriyamapi grāhyaṃ syāt malina mukhacchāyādayo vā  duḥkhajanito'sau
vikāra iti cet na upahatākārasaṃvedanādanyasya tasyānupalabdheḥ  nirloṭhitaṃ caitacchāstra
ityalaṃ prayāsena  atha naitādṛśo'tiśayaḥ prameyasya jñānāt kiṃ tarhi prakāśarūpasyotpattiriti
cet  atrāpi pakṣe ekagocaraḥ sarvagocaraḥ syāt  tadīyajñānanivṛttau tadrūpanivṛtteranya
sthāpyadarśanaprasaṅgaḥ 
anyasthāpi tadupāyayogānnevamiti cet  tasyāpi nivṛttajñānasya tatprakāśa
prasaṅgaḥ  tajjñānanivṛttau tadrūpānivṛttāvapyeṣa eva doṣaḥ  na hi kulālaprayatnaparihṛtāyā
mṛdastameva prati ghaṭībhāvaḥ  dahanādvā dahanopadhāyakameva prati ghaṭasya gaurabhāvaḥ  evaṃ
tarhi upakāritvamapi svarūpamasya sarvasādhāraṇaṃ syāt na caivam  tato yathā ghaṭatvena
sādhāraṇo'pyeṣa nārthaṃkāriṇā rūpeṇa tathā prakāśarūpeṇāpi na sthāditi ko'yaṃ prasaṅgaḥ 
athopakāryaviśeṣopakāritāsya sādhāraṇī  puruṣaviśeṣāpekṣaprakāśatāpyasya sarvasādhāraṇīti
samānam 
na samānam  upakāritvaṃ hi nāma sākṣādupakāraḥ pravṛttiyogyatāmātraṃ vā
abhimataṃ syāt  tatra yogyatāmātraṃ sarvasādhāraṇamiti na tatra vivādaḥ  prathamapakṣe
tu upakāralakṣaṇa kāryakarmaṇi sahakāribhāvo'sya yathaikatra tathānyatrāpi ki na syāditi
codyārthaḥ  na cāyaṃ nyāya avyavadhānādyapekṣatvāt  tato yatsantānavartinaḥ upādāna 
syopanidhiḥ tatraiva sāhāyakamasyeti kathaṃ vyavahitādau puṣṭiḥ  tathā yadi prakāśa
ityapi kāryāntarajananadvāreṇa vyavahāra iṣṭaḥ syāt tadā syādapyevam  yathāhureke
 tula jaiminisū   jñānaśromitranibandhāvalo
buddhilakṣaṇavyaktijanakatvameva tasya vyaktatvamiti  tadā hi yasyaiva buddherupādānaṃ samanantara
saṃkhyātaṃ nopanipātabhāgi sādhanāntaraṃ vā tasyaiva nāsau sahakāradānavirahād vyakto yuktaḥ 
dūṣaṇāntaraṃ ca tatrāpi vakṣyāmaḥ 
na caivaṃ yujyate jñānāt prakāśarūpasyaiva viṣayasyotpattirityetasya pakṣasya
vicintyamānatvāt  kāryāntaradvāreṇa tu vyaktavyavahāre na tatastathotpanna iti prakṛta
kṣatiḥ  tathotpattau durvāra sādhāraṇatva prasaṅgaḥ  upakārakatvamapi hi yāvadeva bhinna
santānavati sukhādijanakatvaṃ tāvadeva tadapekṣayā a sādhāraṇam  yadā tu sukhādi
rūpatvamevābhyupagamyeta tadā ka sādhāraṇatvaniṣedhāya prabhuḥ  nanu tathāpi yadekasya

śātādiḥ paramo'thaveha nihitaṃ nīlādya vidyāvaśā
citrākārakamekameva yadi vānākāramevāthavā 
teṣāṃ ca balābalacintāyāḥ ka idānīmupayogo bahirarthaṃsādhanābhiniveśena
prayuktasādhanasya  tasmāt pratyātmavedyatvādisiddhayathoktavijñānarūpasya ghaṭākārasya
vijñānāntarasaṃmatād bhedasādhane na kiñcitphalamiti vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ  nanu na pratyātma
vedyo ghaṭākāra  sarvasādhāraṇatvāt tataḥ svaprakāśaḥ sannapi sādhāraṇatvādarthaṃ evāyaṃ
tato'pyabhedena pratītirvyavahārasādhanī prayukteti cet na sādhāraṇatvasyāpi prāgeva

api tu prakaraṇāpatnamiṣṭamaprakāśasya prakāśakavyāpāreṇa prakāśasya sato ghaṭādeḥ
prakāśakād bhinnatvam na ca tathā siddhiriti sādhanavaiyarthyādasādhanāṅgavacanaṃ vādino
nigrahasthānam  naivaṃ vā tathāpi suptataimirikādipratibhā sairanekāntaṃ ko nivārayati 
sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam 
iti cet 
sarvatrālambanaṃ jñānaṃ deśarūpānyathātmakam 
ityapi tarhi vaktuṃ śakyam 
ityantaraślokau 
kathaṃ grahaḥ svarūpasya parasthāpi kathaṃ grahaḥ 
buddherātmani bhinne vā vyāpāravirahaḥ samaḥ 
savyāpāre ca nirbhāti yathānyatra tathātmani 
dīpavad vyavahāro'yamaśakyāpahno dhiyaḥ 
tasmād yathānyathākhyātīti matiḥ tathā
abahibahirākāramanīlaṃ nīlarūpataḥ 
jñānameva na bhātīti sapathairyadi nirṇayaḥ 
kimatra bījaṃ vyasane jñānasyārthātmano'pi kim 
pradeśa niyatakhyātau codyametad dvayoḥ samam 
āntaropaplavastatra śaktibhedayuto
yadi 
khyāyate heturatrāpi sa vaktuṃ kiṃ na śakyate

advaita binduprakaraṇam
sadanyathā vibhātīti deśabhede'stu sā gatiḥ 
kālabhede tvasattvena prathanaṃ kathamanyathā 
jīvannaṭo'nyathā nāma khyātīti na mṛto'pyalam 
cittameva tataḥ sarvatrānyathā khyātumarhati 
tato'nyathākhyātipakṣe'pi nānekāntaparihāraḥ  kālabhede'pi nātyantamasanneva
svakāle satvāditi cet  pratibhāsakāle'satastasya kālāntarasattāmātraṃ kopayogi  yatra
yasya svasattopadhānenopayogo na sa tatra cirātītaḥ kṣamaḥ yathā dagdhaṃ bījamambaraṃ vā aṅkure
kālimni vā  svasattopadhānena copapadyate'rthaḥ pratibhāsa iti viruddhopalabdhiḥ yato
vinaṣṭasyāpi śaktisaṃbhavaḥ  svasattopadhānena copayoga iti viruddhau dharmo  ihātītamapi
kuśūlasthaṃ bījamare paramparayopayujyate na tu svasattopadhāneneti viśeṣaṇaṃ tadartham 
pratibhāsamānaścārthaḥ pratibhāse svasattopadhānenaiva upayukto vaktavyaḥ na paramparayā  pratibhāso
hi tasya dharmo vā kāryaṃ vā syāt  tatra dharmatve sahabhāvaḥ  kāryatve svasattānantaryaniyama
iti na kṣaṇenāpi vyavadhistadbhāvaṃ sahata iti svasattopadhānenaiva pratibhāse arthasyopayogaḥ
siddhaḥ  tadabhāvāccātītaḥ prakāśitumaśakyaḥ 
tataḥ
prakāśamāno'yamasanneva prakāśate 
atītatvāt svasattāyā upadhāna vibhūtitaḥ 
tadabhāve'pi bhāse ca bhāsaḥ prāpto'sataḥ punaḥ 
svavācaiva yataḥ sattvasyābhāve bhānamicchati 
tadavaśyaṃ bahirathaṃpakṣe'pi bhrāntijñāne b duṣpariho'satkhyātipakṣaḥ  astu
vānyathākhyātirubhayathāpi jñānavivarta eva sadṛśastasya sattvādaniṣṭimātreṇa nivārayituṃ na
śakyate iti vyāpterabhāvādanekānta eva bhedena pratīyamānatvaheturbhedavyavahārasiddhāviti
sthitam  nanu bhrānteṣvevaṃbhāve'pyanubhave kimāyātam  tataḥ abhrāntatve satīti
viśeṣaṇasyābhimatatvāt nānekānta iti cet na bādhakādhīnā hi bhrāntisthitiḥ tasya
coktenaiva krameṇātrāpi siddhatvāt  tathā hikerte
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
svayaṃ
prakāśādvijñānādasādhāraṇarūpataḥ 
bhinnatve paravedyaḥ syādartha sādhāraṇastathā 
na caivamupapanno'yaṃ niyamaḥ proktayuktitaḥ
tataḥ keśādivat kumbho jñānādbhinnaḥ kathaṃ bhavet 
yaddharmavyatireke na yato dharmavyavasthitiḥ 
anvayastasya dharmasya tato bhedaṃ nirasyati 
tadayaṃ
bāhyatvalakṣaṇa sādhāraṇāsvaprakāśarūpatvaviruddho'sādhāraṇasvaprakāśatārūpo
dharmaṃ upalabhyamāno ghaṭādiṣu tadbhāvamapākarotīti bādhaka sāmarthyāttathāpratītirbhrāntireva
vṛttameva cedaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇaṃ notprekṣāmātreṇeti nātiprasaṅgopālambhaḥ yadapi vijñānavādī
pramāṇayati
yad yat prakāśate tat tad vijñānaṃ svapnadṛṣṭavat 
prakāśate ca nīlādiḥ svabhāvo heturityayam 
tadāpyayaṃ prabandho'stu pratibandhasya siddhaye 
jñānānvayavikalpānāmavakāśaśca
dūrataḥ 
svaprakāśamasāmānya vijñānamiti saṃmatam 
tadrūpeṇa prakāśasya vyāptiścānyairatatkṛte 
prakāśate ca nīlādi nānyeneti svayaṃ yadi 
prakāśate svayaṃ nātaḥ pareṇeti na kiṃ matiḥ 
dṛṣṭo'pi bhedavyāpāraḥ prastute yadi nocitaḥ 
adṛṣṭaḥ sthāpyabhede tu bhavadbhiḥ kalpyate katham 
tu'
nanu prakāśabhedī yaḥ svayamityādi dṛśyate 
tatrāpi nātmani vyāptasvabhāvastu tathocyate 
evaṃ prakāśate buddhiḥ svayamityapi gamyatām 
khe svayaṃ śūnyatā yadvat paravyāpāravāraṇāt 
advaitabinduprakaraṇam
tathātmavyāpṛtibhrāntibhraṃśanāya paraśrutiḥ 
na vyāpāravaśā vṛttistadrūpaṃ tu tathā tadā 
yathā nirlepamākāśaṃ prakāśaṃ ca svayaṃ tathā 
asādhāraṇametañca pūrvameva samarthitam 
tataḥ prakāśatā nāma sādhāraṇyaparakriye 
sarvatra tulyadoṣatvānnirākṛtya vyavasthitā 
tābhyāṃ virodho yuktyāto labdhastādrūpyanirṇayaḥ 
tasmādviparyaṃye hetorvirodhādeva na sthitiḥ 
prakāśatā ca siddheti jñānarūpāḥ śitādayaḥ 
taddbāhyarūpapratyāśā pratyāśaiva hi kevalā 
yadi svarūpamākārāścitra taika dhiyaḥ katham 
bhedaḥ pratyaṇu vā buddheḥ tathā nānyonyavedanam 
mithastathāpi vā vittī bāhyavallakṣaṇakṣatiḥ 
bhede'pyevaṃ dhiyasteṣāṃ prakāśaghaṭanā katham 
athaivameva nirbhāsaḥ svasantānadhiyo dhiyā 
alīkākārarāśervā ko'parādhī bahilarbhuvaḥ 
alīkavedane kiṃ ca prakāśaṃ ca na cāparam 
ato vipakṣasāmānyo hetuḥ saṃśayasādhanaḥ 
alīkamanyatvetīdaṃ  vyāvṛttyantaramīritam 
tasya sandehavattve'pi prakāśe jñānatā sthitā 
evaṃ prakāśamānasya jñānatve pratipādite 
kacit sarvatra vā vādādalīkatve'pi bodhatā 
jñānameva tataḥ satyamalīkaṃ vā bahinaṃ tu 
bahirapyastu vā vastu prakāśasyāstu bodhatā 
SETTIERT
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
bhedābhedavikalpo'pi na prakāśasya bādhakaḥ 
na vā yathoktasādhyena vyāpteriti kimarthaṃkaḥ 
pareṇa parasaṃvitti yo'bhimanyeta taṃ prati 
śeṣaṃ syādapi doṣāya brūmaḥ svapne'pi na tvidam 
ekānekatvavirahāt niḥsvabhāvamidaṃ jaḍam 
yathā tathā na kiñcittaṃ sattaikasya kathaṃ tataḥ 
prakāśamānaṃ nīlādi jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā 
iti prakaraṇe'smābhirbuddhive heturucyate 
tatraikānekaviraho yadi dharmāntarārpakaḥ 
kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tāvatāpi nīlāderjaḍatā na hi 
sattāyāṃ nanu siddhāyāṃ jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā 
asatturaṅgaśṛṅgādi na hi tattve'numīyate 
tathāpya prastutamidaṃ sattācintāviyogataḥ 
siddhāyāmeva sattāyāṃ viśeṣaścintyate yataḥ 
sattāyāṃ saṃśaye'pyasmāt sacced vijñānameva tat 
tataścādūṣaṇākhyātirasattāsiddhibādhayoḥ 
prasiddhimātrarūpeṇa dharmitvānnāpyanāśrayaḥ 
anyathā niḥsvabhāvatvahetorapyāśrayaḥ katham 
tasminna bhāvamātraṃ cet jñānatāmātramatra ca 
bāhyavastutvasiddhistu dvayorapi virodhinī 
vastutopādhibodhatvaṃ sādhyamatra tvayeti cet 
bodhatvamātra prastāve viśeṣa kuta īdṛśaḥ 
jñānatvaṃ vastutāvyāptaṃ tadabhāve bhavenna cet 
viruddhāvyabhicāraḥ ka doṣo yadvāstu vastutā 
advaitabinduprakaraṇam
kiṃ ca prakāśamātrātmavyatiriktānyathāthavā 
sattā niṣeddhayābhimatā niḥsvabhāvatvahetunā 
niṣedhe vyatiriktāyā na prakāśātmavāraṇam 
asyaiva vāraṇe kena vāraṇādhyakṣabhāsinaḥ 
anumānaṃ pramāṇatvād bādhakaṃ yadi kasyacit 
pratyakṣamapi tadbhāvāt sādhakaṃ kiṃ na kasyacit 
avaśyamante'dhyakṣasya prāmāṇyamanumāśrayet 
prakāśamātrarūpe ca nānumāpekṣamakṣajam 
athāyamanumānasya viṣayo'kṣadhiyo'paraḥ 
prakāśarūpe'dhyakṣatvādanumāvasaraḥ kutaḥ 
atha pratyakṣasiddhaṃ yanna tasyeva nirākriyā 
vyāvṛttibhedaḥ kaścātra vicārāsahatā yadi 
vijñānasyaiva dharmo'stu śaśaśṛṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ 
arthaśaktiviyoge vā dharmo'stu dhiya eva saḥ 
arthaśaktiviyogaśca vicārāsahtā ca sā 
jñānasyaiva na bāhyasyetyayate kimataḥ param 
prakāśasyaiva cinteyaṃ tadgandho'pi bahinaṃ hi 
tannāgaśṛṅgasāmye'sya siddhe ki na kṛtārthatā 
bahivaṃdavabhāseṣu prajñaptā rūparāśitā 
saṃskārādvedanāsaṃjñe b abhinne kiṃ na bhedi te 
mūlamevāprakāśasya duḥsthaṃ sattāvyavasthiteḥ 
prakāśarūpasya sato dharmāntaramabādhakam 
prakāśasyāpi taddoṣād yadi sattā davīyasī 
aprakāśo'pyasattāyāḥ kimanyat sādhayiṣyati 
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
asattaivāprakāśasya prakāśasya tu nātmanā 
tenaivāsattvamityuktaṃ kalpite na tu yujyate 
prakāśamānasya punaḥ prakāśādeva satyatā 
abhāvo'vasitenaiva keśasyāpi jaḍātmanā 
prakāśasaṃmatasyāpi nīlāderata eva hi 
satyamarthakriyaivoktā tāṃ vinā na bhidā dvayoḥ 
kriyāmātrānubandhācca vijñānasyāpyanityatā 
kriyā'bhāvo yadā tvasmin sattā mukhyaiva bhāsanāt 
na kṣaṇitvaṃ tadā tasya sattvaṃ ca vyabhicāyaṃtaḥ 
sattvamarthakriyārūpaṃ sādhanaṃ tanna duṣyati 
na vā tasyāpyanityatvaṃ parihṛtya daśāntaram 
tatkṣaṇasyaiva saṃvitteranyathā na bhidā kacit 
kāryakāraṇabhāvo'yamāyātastahiṃ cennanu 
sāṃvṛtasyāniṣedho'tra kṣaṇitāpyasya sāṃvṛtī 
tattvato nityarūpaṃ cet saṃvṛtāvapi yanna sat 
anityapratiṣedhācet tathāpyasthāgatiḥ kutaḥ 
bhāvaṃ kañcit puraskṛtya bhedābhedāvudīrayet 
deśakālādibhedena svavinmātre tu kaḥ kramaḥ 
svarūpaṃ buddhiraparairna yauti na bhinatti ca 
svaparapravibhāgo hi dhiyo yācitamaṇḍanam 
anyasyāvācyatā nāma svabhāvabhāvaśaṃsinī 
tadeva rūpaṃ tattvasya taccādvaite pratiṣṭhitam 
paraṃ hi vidvan niyataṃ niyataṃ pratipadyate 
anyathā vittimātreṇa na pravṛttinivartane 
advaitabinduprakaraṇam
prathamaṃ grāhakākāro bhinatti grāhyamātmanaḥ 
rūpana tathā grāhyāntarādapi 
advaitamevetarathā tadabhāve bhidāṃ dyati 
bhedābhedau tato dvaite niyato nādvaye tathā 
yāvacca svapnabodhāya kālabhedaṃ parāmṛśet 
dhīvikalpāntareṇeyaṃ kṣayeṇa grasyate'nyavat 
tasmānna nityatā nāma tattvato na ca saṃvṛtiḥ 
kṣaṇitātattvayoge'pi gṛhyatāmanumānavat 
citraikavyavahāro'pi bhedāpohaparo mataḥ 
ekānekaviyukto hi prakāśaḥ kevalo'tra san 
sarvaṃśaktiviyuktena prakāśana satāpi kim 
śakyabhāvānna kāryaṃ syāt svarūpaṃ tu ke gacchatu 
prakāśasyāpi rūpaṃ cet vicāreṇa na labhyate 
vicāramanumāṃ vidmona sā pratyakṣabādhanī 
guñjānala viparyāsau bādhyate'kṣakṛto'pi cet 
pararūpe bhramānnākṣaṃ svarūpe bhrāntatā kutaḥ 
' pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ ced vicārāvasaro hṛtaḥ 
bruvatā niyataṃ kiñcit sādhyaṃ vā bādhyameva vā 
tatrāyukti bruvāṇasya ślāghā sadasi kodṛśī 
nānumāyāḥ parā yukti ki siddhaṃ tadanādare 
svīkṛtā tena setyasmāt tanmatyā bodhanaṃ yadi 
abādhane'syāḥ svīkārāttaddhiyāabodhanaṃ katham 
sādhyaṃ na kiñciditi cet bādhāyā api sādhyatā 
sāpi neti vaco vyarthaṃ praśnamātre'pi kiṃ phalam

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
phalaṃ yadi giraḥ kāpi nānyat taccāvabodhanāt 
vācaḥ pratyāyane śaktā nākṣadhūmādi sundaram 
yadi hetuphale saṃvṛttadbhāva kena gṛhyatām 
phalācca hetudhīrnūnaṃ na ced vyarthā vratādayaḥ
yo'pi tāpādito'bhyeti candanaṃ na hutāśanam 
vaktuṃ kiñcidanāśritya sajñānaṃ tuna vartate 
vastu kiñcidupanyasya nyasyante yadi yuktayaḥ 
śāstre pakṣagrahaḥ kiṃ na nacettat kena gṛhyatām 
mokṣamārgaṃ yadā pṛṣṭo vyākuryāt śūnyabhāvanām 
bodhayan śūnyatāṃ tarhi garhetpakṣagrahaṃ katham 
tasmāt saṃvṛtimāśritya sādhyaṃ sādhanamasya vā 
durvāramiti durvāra pramāṇasya parigrahaḥ 
'saṃvṛttau mānamiṣṭaṃ cet vicāro'pyeṣa saṃvṛtiḥ 
saṃvṛtāvapi neṣṭaṃ ced bruvan jetā yathā tathā 
yathā hetuphale saṃvṛttathā saṃvādidhīrapi 
anumāmicchato'dhyakṣaṃ neti ko'pyeṣa niścayaḥ 
svavedane vivādaścet na saṃvṛtyaiva sādhanāt 
tasmādaparamārthatve'pyāttā vittiḥ prādhikā 
saṃvṛtiścet ka niṣkarṣaḥ paramārtho'stu tāvatā 
tataśca saṃvṛtāveva sāṃvṛtaṃ tyajyate katham 
tatprakāśānvayaḥ sattāvyavahāro'stu cetasaḥ 
na prakāśo na vā śaktiryasya tena tulā katham 
tato vicārāsahatādidharma
